##

MAT 1:1 Kakaɗ tǝghǝr kǝ hulfa Yesu Kǝristi, zǝra Dauda kwa ghǝravaan ndakwani zǝra Ibrahim.
MAT 1:2 Ibrahim wa yaa Ishaku, ya nǝ Ishaku kǝ Yakuba, ya nǝ Yakub kǝ Yahuda ard zaraabahaana.
MAT 1:3 Ya nǝ Yahuda kǝ Ferez ard Zera. Babbaatǝr Tamara. Ya nǝ Ferez kǝ Hezron, ya nǝ Hezron kǝ Aram,
MAT 1:4 ya nǝ Aram kǝ Amminadab, ya nǝ Amminadab kǝ Nashon, ya nǝ Nashon kǝ Salmon.
MAT 1:5 Ya nǝ Salmon kǝ Bowaz, ɗaaga babbaan Rahab. Ya nǝ Bowaz kǝ Obed, ɗaaga babbaan Rut. Ya nǝ Obed kǝ Yesse,
MAT 1:6 ya nǝ Yesse kǝ Tlǝkes Dauda. Ya nǝ Dauda kǝ Saluman, ɗaaga babbaan Betshaba, kwandza uusa Uri wura.
MAT 1:7 Ya nǝ Saluman kǝ Rehobowam, ya nǝ Rehobowam kǝ Abija, ya nǝ Abija kǝ Asa,
MAT 1:8 ya nǝ Asa kǝ Yehoshafat, ya nǝ Yehoshafat kǝ Yoram, ya nǝ Yoram kǝ Uzziya,
MAT 1:9 ya nǝ Uzziya kǝ Yotam, ya nǝ Yotam kǝ Ahaz, ya nǝ Ahaz kǝ Hezekaya,
MAT 1:10 ya nǝ Hezekaya kǝ Manasse, ya nǝ Manasse kǝ Aman, ya nǝ Aman kǝ Yosiya,
MAT 1:11 ya nǝ Yosiya kǝ Yekoniya ard zaraabahaan sartakwa hutsavtǝra nǝ uudah damma Babila kiyava ɛɛva.
MAT 1:12 Tǝhalakwa lanngavtǝrda nǝ iitǝr damma Babila, kaa yigayig nǝ Yekoniya kǝ Shayeltiyel, ya nǝ Shayeltiyel kǝ Zerubbabela,
MAT 1:13 ya nǝ Zerubbabel kǝ Abihud, ya nǝ Abihud kǝ Eliyakim, ya nǝ Eliyakim kǝ Azor,
MAT 1:14 ya nǝ Azor kǝ Zadok, ya nǝ Zadok kǝ Akim, ya nǝ Akim kǝ Eliyud,
MAT 1:15 ya nǝ Eliyud kǝ Eliyazar, ya nǝ Eliyazar kǝ Mattan, ya nǝ Mattan kǝ Yakub,
MAT 1:16 ya nǝ Yakub kǝ Isuvu zhiila Maryam, Maryam wa yaayig kǝ Yesu kwa ɗahav dǝ Kǝristi.
MAT 1:17 Baɗǝm nǝ hulfaatǝr ciigǝt tǝ Ibrahim dat Dauda, hulf kǝlawa tar uufaɗa, ciigǝt tǝ Dauda damma sarta kwa hutsavtǝra nǝ yaa Izraˈila damma Babila kiyava ɛɛva, hulf kǝlawa tar uufaɗa, ciigǝt ma sarta ɛɛvǝr ma Babila da tǝ sarta yiga Kǝristi, hulf kǝlaawa tar uufaɗa.
MAT 1:18 Wan nǝ ɗuuli yava nǝ Yesu Kǝristi. Ma sartǝn ndza ɓǝlghara nǝ Isuvu kǝ dzǝgwambǝr kǝ Maryam babba Yesu. Lakuti kǝsgaan kiyava uusa, kaa dlǝghǝgadlǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ huɗ tǝdvad Shǝɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 1:19 Nahabi nǝ Isuvu jambuwaan kǝ tsǝgar zhǝru mataataka uudah biya, aɗaba uuda jiirjiir nǝ iina. Kaa ɓaa dabariya tagwav kǝ iin dǝ vakaiy ma ɗyamɗyamǝra.
MAT 1:20 Masartǝn ba ndzǝgaan nǝ iin ba dzamaghǝra, kaa tlǝgaraatlǝg zǝrɓǝlga Yaazhigǝl ma sǝnnga, aiyama taa kǝ iina, “Isuvu zǝra Dauda, gǝdzbi kǝ kǝssa Maryam kiyava uusagh biya, aɗaba huɗɗǝn dǝvakai nǝ iinna dǝga Shiɗkwa Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 1:21 Da yigaan kǝ zǝra, agha da farva kǝ ɗaag Yesu, aɗaba iin wada katta uudahaan sagal ma haipahaatǝra.”
MAT 1:22 Dzǝghardzǝg wanahaan baɗǝm mbakyarvad righǝvant nǝ dǝgiti tagada nǝ Yaazhigǝl tǝdvad tlayang taakiya,
MAT 1:23 “Pakwara dǝghwa da dlǝghgaan kǝ huuɗa, da ya kǝ zǝra, da fǝvarva ɗaag Immanuela.” Dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ Immanuela, “Daadamazhigǝl ǝmtaɗ dǝ kǝmiyamma.”
MAT 1:24 Ciyit ba nǝ Isuvu ma haara, kaa gatǝgaan kǝ iin kǝ dǝgiti taga nǝ zǝrbǝlga Yaazhigǝla. Kaa kǝsguukǝsǝg nǝ Isuvu kǝ Maryam nal kǝ uusaana.
MAT 1:25 Farabi kǝ dzaghǝr biya, bamma tǝhala kwa yaa nǝ iin kǝ zǝraana, farva kǝ iin kǝ ɗaag Yesu.
MAT 2:1 Tǝhalakwa yava nǝ Yesu ma kǝssa Bitalahami ma larda Yahudiya ma zamana Tlǝkǝs Hirudus, kaa sagat kǝ lii sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgit tǝghǝr kwadladl dagat damma Wurshalima.
MAT 2:2 Kaa ndavǝg kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Mǝr nǝ tlǝksa Yahudahǝn kwa yavan ni? Aɗaba kǝmnda nǝghǝga kwadladlaan sagat dǝ sǝga, iin wa kǝmaa sagau nǝmnd sa ɓagarnǝs kwatnahǝra.”
MAT 2:3 Cinngha ba nǝ Tlǝkǝs Hirudus ǝndkwana, kaa ba uushig kǝ ghǝrana, baz uudaha Wurshaliim baɗǝmma.
MAT 2:4 Kaa dzahgantdzahǝg kǝ iin kǝ maalmaalah ma zhiila kǝsuufah ard lii tsaga adzahadzaha Muusa, ndavtǝru kǝ iin kǝ vakavaki da yaav dǝ Kǝristina.
MAT 2:5 Am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Ma kǝsa Bitalahamiya, malarda Yahudiya. Aɗaba vinda bandkwah nǝ tlayanng taakiya,
MAT 2:6 “ ‘Kǝgh Bitalahami ma larda Yahud ndakwani, agha ǝnkykwah bi nǝng ma lii kwara Yahud biya. Aɗaba da sagal ma kǝgh nǝ dadda kwarga, kwada piya uudahar Izraila.’ ”
MAT 2:7 Kaa ɗahtǝrǝtɗahǝg kǝ Hirudus kǝ lii sǝrgasǝrg kǝ dǝgitǝn damma dlǝmmbaava, kaa nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg kǝ iin vakaatǝr kǝ kalkala sarti nǝghara nǝ iitǝr kǝ kwadladlǝna.
MAT 2:8 Kaa ɓǝltǝrǝtɓǝlǝg kǝ iin damma Baitalahami amaa, “Damdǝg ndan ndavamndavǝg bad hǝnkal kǝ vakavaki dǝ zǝriina, tǝhala kwama tlamaraatlǝga, am saas am tagǝwana, ghǝravar ndakwani ǝn dagal da ɓagarnǝs kwatnaha.”
MAT 2:9 Ghyǝngara ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ cinnga ǝlbǝga tlǝkǝsna, kaa dagalaatǝr kǝ iitǝra, dlaɓa ka dagal kǝ iitǝr gata kwadladlǝn nǝghara nǝ iitǝr tǝvuukwatǝra, tangw da vakavakǝn ghaca nǝ iin tǝghǝr kǝ zǝriina.
MAT 2:10 Nǝghara ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ kwadladlǝna, kaa hwaɗag kǝ iitǝr ba vaivaiya.
MAT 2:11 Daragha ba nǝ iitǝr damma hǝnyahiina, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ zǝriina ard babbaan Maryam, ar kǝla kǝ ghunj tǝvuukwana ar ɓaganǝs kǝ kwatnaha. Tǝhalakwaha, ar palna kǝ kadlangngahaatǝr ar vǝlar kǝ adawana ard tǝrshan lubban ard mur.
MAT 2:12 Kaa gwiyaghǝra daas kǝ iitǝr damma kǝsaatǝr tǝ ɗuuli tlǝrna, aɗaba ɓǝlatǝraaɓǝlǝg nǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ magi ma sǝnng taakiya, aa gwiya darbi daa da vak Hirudus biya.
MAT 2:13 Daral ba nǝ iitǝra, kaa tsǝgwatsug kǝ zǝrbǝlga Daadamazhigǝl vak Isuvu ma sǝnnga amaa, “Ciiga, kǝsantkǝsǝg kǝ zǝrna ard babbaana ǝmndǝramǝmndǝrǝg damma haaya Masara. Ndzamandzǝg vaakwaha, bamma tagankuratag lakuti am gwiyaghǝra saasa, aɗaba da gatǝgaan nǝ Hirudus kǝ zǝrǝn kiyava tsǝgaana.”
MAT 2:14 Kaa ciig kǝ Isuvu kavǝɗa, kǝsant kǝ zǝrna ard babbaana, kaa dagal kǝ iin damma haaya Masara.
MAT 2:15 Ndza kǝ iin vaakwaha tangwa damma sarta kwa ǝmtsa nǝ Hirudusa. Kwana dzǝghaar mbakyarvad righǝvant nǝ dǝgiti tagada nǝ Yaazhigǝl tǝdvad tlayanng taakiya, “Ɗahanant saa ma Masar kǝ zǝrara.”
MAT 2:16 Nǝghaaka ba nǝ Hirudus taakiya, ɗyamɗyamǝr wa marararda lii sǝrga dǝgitna, kaa badza ǝrviɗmahuɗ kǝ iin ba vaivaiya. Kaa ba ɓǝlgantɓǝlg kǝ iin kǝ uudah da ciɓa zaraa ghwalvaha kwama Bitalahami baɗǝmma ard kǝsahaanǝn hǝrz dǝ iina, ciigǝt tǝ zǝr vuunj dat zǝra hǝi buwa, kalkal dǝ sartǝn tagarar nǝ lii sǝrgasǝrgǝn kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ zǝriina.
MAT 2:17 Ma sarta kwahiin wa righavant nǝ dǝgiti tagavda tǝdvad tlayang Irmi taakiya,
MAT 2:18 “Cinngavacinng nǝ huulǝg ma Rama, huulǝga badzǝga ǝrviɗmahuɗ ba vaivaiya, kats Rahil wa tuug mbakyarvad zarhaana, lawalǝg baz fa ǝrviɗya aɗaba zarhaani ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝga.”
MAT 2:19 Tǝhala ǝmtsǝga Hirudusa, kaa tsugwatsug kǝ zǝrɓǝlga Yaazhigǝl vak Isuvu ma sǝnng ma Masara,
MAT 2:20 amaa, “Ciiga kǝsantkǝsant kǝ zǝrna ard babbaana, gwig da damma haaya Izraila, adaba lii gata tsa shifǝga zǝrna, ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝga.”
MAT 2:21 Kaa ba ciig kǝ iin kǝsant kǝ zǝrna ard babbaana, kaa daas kǝ iin damma Izraila.
MAT 2:22 Cinngha ba nǝ iin taakiya Arkilayus zǝra Hirudus guyugwig kǝ daddaana, kwara larda Yahuda, kaa gǝdzǝg kǝ gwuya daas da vaakwaha. Bǝlavara ba nǝ magi ma sǝnnga, kaa kyǝha daas kǝ iin damma Galili.
MAT 2:23 Kaa dagal kǝ iin ndza ma kǝsiin kwa ɗahav dǝ Nazarata. Righavant ǝndkwan nǝ dǝgiti tagara nǝ tlayangah taakiya, “Da ɗahav dǝ uuda Nazarata.”
MAT 3:1 Ma hǝnngahaatsa, sǝghalsǝg nǝ Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝg da taa ǝlbǝg maraw ma tǝghala ma larda Galili,
MAT 3:2 taakiya, “Pǝlampǝlǝg kǝ ghǝra aɗaba tlǝksǝra Daadamazhigǝl ba hǝrza.”
MAT 3:3 Kwan wa ndza taga nǝ tlayang Ishay kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝrǝna, taakiya, “Mǝng nǝ uud ɗaag ma tǝghala, amaa, ‘Ɓadlamarnaɓadlǝg kǝ ɗuul kǝ Yaazhigǝla, am ɓadlarna kǝ ɗuulaan ba ndǝɗɗa.’ ”
MAT 3:4 Sǝɗavi tsǝguv nǝ Yuhwan ɓagava dǝ guja adlugwama, dǝga ndzǝɗa huɗaana ɓagava dǝ hǝluwa. Dǝgzǝgaana ndza ayayuwa ard yuwa mamma.
MAT 3:5 Kaa ba sagau kǝ uudaha Wurshslim ard uudaha larda Yahudiya baɗǝmma, baz lii ma lardǝn dǝ Zaagha Judan da vakaana.
MAT 3:6 Kaa tagaan kǝ iitǝr kǝ haipahaatǝra, ɓagtǝra kǝ iin kǝ tsuufǝg ma Zaagha Judan.
MAT 3:7 Nǝgha ba nǝ iin kǝ Farisah ard Sadukiyah ba ɗyak da vakaan kiyava ɓagtǝr tsuufǝga, kaa amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kuram faɗǝga ghavalahaan dǝ gurna! Warwaa ghudkura harɗa ngǝdlgarwa kǝ dlaɗa Daadamazhigǝlǝn sagauni?
MAT 3:8 Ɓagamɓag kǝ dǝgitahi da mardamarg taaki pǝlamapǝlǝg kǝ ghǝra.
MAT 3:9 Tsam bi kǝ kusǝgh taakiya, ‘Ibrahim nǝ daadamnd biya.’ Ən tagkurtaga, virɗigaravirɗig nǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ zarh kǝ Ibrahim dǝ kwanahaan kǝ akuraha.
MAT 3:10 Bavǝtbǝg nǝ hiil tǝ suuha uufa, badǝm nǝ uufi lawalǝg kǝ yazǝr marawa, ghudvars ɓǝlǝvdǝm damma kaara.
MAT 3:11 “Ən ɓagkur dǝ yu nai kǝ tsuufǝg kiyava mara taaki pǝlamapǝlǝg kǝ ghǝra, mǝng nǝ dadda kwa jakwaraajig dǝ ndanngǝr da sagau tǝ halara, tlanalbi nai aanji kǝ kǝssa kimbakaan biya. Da ɓagkur dǝ Shǝɗkwa Daadamazhigǝla, ard kaar nǝ iin kǝ tsuufǝga.
MAT 3:12 Kuwa bǝgaan bamma dǝvaana, da bǝggrzha kǝ hǝiyaana, da hutsǝdaan kǝ hǝiyaan damma kuvǝraana, da haars kǝ kaar kǝ hyahya dǝ kaari maay ǝmtsǝg biya.”
MAT 3:13 Sagha ma kwahiin kǝ sart nǝ Yesu saama Galili, kaa dagal kǝ iin damma zaagha Wurdǝn kwakyarvad ɓagara nǝ Yuhwan kǝ tsuufǝga.
MAT 3:14 Naha tsǝharvatsǝg nǝ Yuhwana, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Kai ndakwi mana naa magha ɓagwi nǝng kǝ tsuufǝga, agha sagau ndar dlaɓ nǝng sa vakari?”
MAT 3:15 Ngugharangu nǝ Yesu amaa, “Aandz bandkwah ndakwana, aɗaba kalkalaan righvant nǝ dǝgiti naag nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.” Kaa haigaranthaig kǝ Yuhwana.
MAT 3:16 Tǝhalakwa ɓagavara nǝ tsuufǝg kǝ Yesu, bad sagalaan ma yuwa, kaa wurgǝtwurg kǝ ghǝrazhigǝla, dlaɓa kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ Shiɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl saay da tǝghǝr kǝ iin band garava kakura.
MAT 3:17 Kaa cinngvacinnga nǝ ghai sii ma ghǝrazhigǝl taakiya, “Kwana iin nǝ zǝrara, ǝn waigaana dlaɓa ǝn cinngaan kǝ ǝmtakǝraan ba vaivaiya.”
MAT 4:1 Ngal langaan nǝ Shiɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl kǝ Yesu damma tǝghala, kiyava fǝshgaan kǝ Shatanaha.
MAT 4:2 Tǝhala kǝsgaana Yesu kǝ adǝla hǝng kwul uufaɗ ard vang kwul uufaɗa. Tǝhalakwaha kaa njǝkǝnjiig kǝ waiya.
MAT 4:3 Kaa sagau kǝ Shatanaha, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Magha ba zǝra Daadamazhigǝla, nǝdalnǝg ci kǝ akurǝn kǝ bruudiya.”
MAT 4:4 Kaa ngwangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Vindavavindǝg ma kakaɗ Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, “ ‘Dǝgzǝg kalti bi wa hǝkya shifǝga uudbiya, bamma ǝlbǝgahi sagal vak Daadamazhigǝl baɗǝmma.’ ”
MAT 4:5 Kaa lanngaan kǝ Shatanah kǝ Yesu damma Wurshalima kǝss ɗyak caccuwanacaccuwana. Ngal lanngdit dat ghǝra vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 4:6 Aiyama taa kǝ iina, “Magha ba zǝra Daadamazhigǝla, dzǝvǝg ndan daaya. Aɗaba vindavavindǝg taakiya, “‘Da tagarta nǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ zǝrɓǝlgahaan, ar da tsǝkǝs kǝ dǝv haik kǝ tsǝgaan kǝ shigahagh tǝ akura.’ ”
MAT 4:7 Ngugharangug nǝ Yesu, taa kǝ iina, “Vindavavindǝg dlaɓ taakiya, ‘Fǝsh bi kǝ Yaazhigǝl Daadamazhigǝlagh biya.’ ”
MAT 4:8 Ngal gwiya lanngaan nǝ Shatanah damma ghǝra aghw ba kyakkwa, kaa margardmarg kǝ iin kǝ tlǝksǝraha duni ard ndangǝrahaatǝr baɗǝmma.
MAT 4:9 Aiyam nǝ shatanah taa kǝ iina, “Ən vǝlakvǝlǝg kǝ kwanahaan baɗǝmma akwama kǝlghakǝlǝg kǝ ghwunj tǝvuukwara, agha ɓagwǝs kǝ kwatnahǝra.”
MAT 4:10 Ngugharangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Yagh vaakwan Shatanaha, aɗaba vindavavindǝg taakiya, “ ‘Ɓagarɓag kǝ kwatnahǝr kǝ Yaazhigǝl Daadamazhigǝlagha, ba iin pall wagha da ɓagarnǝs nǝng kǝ kwatnahǝra.’ ”
MAT 4:11 Kaa dagalaan kǝ Shatanaha, kaa sagau kǝ zarabǝlga ar mǝlaruwa.
MAT 4:12 Cinngha ba nǝ Yesu taaki viyavǝtviig nǝ Yuhwana, ngal dagal kǝ iin damma Galili.
MAT 4:13 Ɗuwars kǝ iin kǝ Nazarat kaa dagal da ndzǝga ma Kafarnahum, kwandza tǝvǝgh kǝ yuwahaiya, tǝ ghaala dǝ larda Zebulun ard Naftali.
MAT 4:14 Tǝdvadkwan kǝ ɗuul wa righǝvant nǝ dǝgiti tagada nǝ tlayang Ishai taakiya,
MAT 4:15 “Larda Zebulun ard larda Naftali ma Galili, larda lii ar Yahudah biya. Lardǝn hǝrz dǝ yuwahayin tangw damma gyilga zaagha Wurduna.
MAT 4:16 Uudahi ar ndzǝgama gurtla nǝgharanǝghǝg kǝ parakrakǝr ba vaivaiya, lii ndzǝga ma shiɗkwa ǝmtsǝg dlaɓa, sǝghawisǝg nǝ parak da tǝghǝr kǝ iitǝra.”
MAT 4:17 Ciigǝt tǝ kwahiin kǝ sart wa fǝgharzha nǝ Yesu kǝ taa ǝlbǝg maraw taakiya, “Pǝlampǝlǝg kǝ ghǝra aɗaba tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝl ba hǝrza.”
MAT 4:18 Tǝ ɗuula dagal nǝ Yesu tǝvǝgh kǝ Yuwahaiya Galili, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ zarha baabah buwa, Siman kwa ɗahav dǝ Bitrusa, ard zǝra babbaan Andrawusa, ar ɓǝla amshiya vaiya kilfatǝr ma yuwahaiya, aɗaba ar lii vaiya kilf nǝ iitǝra.
MAT 4:19 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gatamkwagatǝga, ǝnda nǝkurdalnǝg kǝ lii vaiya uudah da vakara.”
MAT 4:20 Batwatsǝra ar ɗuwars kǝ dǝgaha vaiya kilfaatǝra, kaa gata Yesu kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 4:21 Tǝghǝrdǝga dagala, kaa gwuya nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ zarha baabah buwa, Yakuba ard zǝra babbaan Yuhwana zarha Zabadi. Ar ma pɛrayu ǝmtaɗ dǝ daddaatǝr Zabadi, ar ɓadla amshiya vaiya kilfatǝra, kaa ɗahtǝrǝt kǝ iina.
MAT 4:22 Batwatsǝra kaa ɗuugarsɗuug kǝ iitǝr kǝ pɛrayuwaatǝr ard daddaatǝra, kaa gata Yesu kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 4:23 Gwaivagwaig nǝ Yesu ma Galili baɗǝmma, tsagtǝr dǝgit ma guda dzugwazhigǝla, dlaɓa taa ǝlbǝg marawa tlǝkǝsǝra Daadamazhigǝla, mbahǝgaan dlaɓ aanji hulfa kwar kǝ kuzaha, ard lii yang biya.
MAT 4:24 Cinngalcinng nǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ iin baɗǝmma ma haaya Suuriya. Kaa ba lanngaan kǝ uudah kǝ lii dǝ kuzah baɗǝmma, ard lii yangbiyah shahshaha, ard lii hǝɓa dlaɗa, ard makwayaha, ard lii ciɓǝg nǝ Shatanah baz lii ǝmtsamtsan nǝ vǝgh mbahavtǝrambahǝg baɗǝmma.
MAT 4:25 Kaa gatǝgaan kǝ dzahava uudah ba ɗyaka ma Galili, dlaɓa ard lii ma larda Dikafulis ard Wurshalima, ard lii ma larda Yahudiya baz lii gyilga zaagha Wurdǝna.
MAT 5:1 Nǝghgha ba nǝ Yesu kǝ dzahava uudah baɗyaka, kaa dagat kǝ iin damma ghwaa, cǝhura kǝ iina. Kaa ba dagau kǝ mbǝrzahaan da vakaana.
MAT 5:2 Ngal farzha kǝ iin tsagtǝr dǝgita.
MAT 5:3 “Ar dǝ bark nǝ lii sǝrgasǝrg kǝ hǝtsǝgalhǝtsǝgaatǝr ma gata Daadamazhigǝla, aɗaba tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl dǝgaatǝra.
MAT 5:4 Ar dǝ bark nǝ lii dǝ badzǝga rǝviɗmahuuɗa, aɗaba da tagǝvtǝrtag nǝ dzǝgwagha.
MAT 5:5 Ar dǝ bark kanadiyaha, aɗaba ar da gwigaan kǝ duniya.
MAT 5:6 Ar dǝ bark nǝ lii kǝma ɓa dǝgiti naag Daadamazhigǝla, aɗaba ar da baghǝga.
MAT 5:7 Ar dǝ bark nǝ lii mara zhuwadaala, aɗaba da marvǝtǝrmarǝg nǝ zhuwadaala.
MAT 5:8 Ar dǝ bark nǝ lii caɗaɗ nǝ ǝrviɗmahuda, aɗaba ar da nǝghǝganǝhǝg kǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 5:9 Ar dǝ bark nǝ lii fa gabǝra, aɗaba da ɗahvǝtǝrɗahǝg dǝ zarha Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 5:10 Ar dǝ bark nǝ lii hǝɓa dlaɗ kwakyarvad ɓa hɛrǝrra, aɗaɓa tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝla dǝgaatǝra.”
MAT 5:11 “Am dǝ bark nǝ uurama, akwama ar ɗaava kuram nǝ uudaha, ar vǝlkur kǝ dlaɗa, dlaɓa ar ɓagkura kǝ dǝga kǝlaadǝrah shahshah mbakyarvad kaiya.
MAT 5:12 Dlayamdlaiga am hwaɗag ba vaivaiya, mbakyarvad am da tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ dǝgshigaru baɗyak ma ghǝrazhigǝla. Aɗaba vǝlartǝr bandkwah nǝ uudah kǝ dlaɗ kǝ tlayanngahi sarǝv lakuti kǝskurama.
MAT 5:13 “Kuram nǝ iizha duniya. Akwama maadlai nashnash nǝ iizh biya, da gwiya gwivdaa ndar nǝ nashnashani? Maadlai tlǝraan biya, bamma ɗivda dagala, hapǝna nǝ uudaha.
MAT 5:14 “Kuram parak duniya. Akwama favafǝg nǝ kǝs tǝ gavala shiɓvǝna biya.
MAT 5:15 Maay mbiyav nǝ kaara jahuramba humbvara kǝghai biya, bamma hǝrtǝvǝt tǝ dǝga hǝrtǝgaan vakavaki da ba parakrak kǝ uudahi hǝnnyah baɗǝma.
MAT 5:16 Bandkwah dlaɓa, parakaruwa aandz ba pǝripǝri tǝvuukwa uudaha, kiyava nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ dǝgitah marawi am ɓag nǝ uurama, ar da fǝgaarafǝg kǝ Daadaruwi ma ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 5:17 “Tlatlam bi taakiya sanhi mbakyarvad ǝn kalarwut kǝ Adzahadzah Musa ard tsaga tlayanngah nai biya, sanhi mbakyarvad ǝn righanta.
MAT 5:18 Ba jiirjiir wan tagkurtaga, lakuti ghyǝng nǝ zhigǝla ard haaya, maay nǝ dǝgit aanji ba hǝɗikǝn ma vindǝga Adzahadzaha Muus kwada nig biya, bamma righavantrighǝg baɗǝmma.
MAT 5:19 Mbakyarvad kwaha baɗǝm daddakwa kǝladakǝlǝg aanji ba pal ma adzahadzahahaan hǝɗikǝnna, tsagtǝru dlaɓ kǝ kǝla adzahadzahahaan kǝ uudaha, da ɗahav nǝ iin daddakwa ǝnkykwah ma tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝla. Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa gatǝgaan kǝ adzahadzahiina, dlaɓa tsagartsag kǝ uudaha, da ɗahav nǝ iin dǝ uud maamal ma tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 5:20 Ən tagkurtaga, akwama jamtǝruubi kǝ lii tsaga adzahadzaha Muus ard Farisah dǝ jiir biya, am dǝgaa bi damma tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝl biya.
MAT 5:21 “Cinngamacinng ndza tagavtǝrdatag kǝ daadijaharu taakiya, ‘Tsǝbi kǝ shifǝg biya, baɗǝm daddakwa tsǝga shifǝga, da tǝvartǝg nǝ shariya.’
MAT 5:22 Aiciya ǝn tagkurtaga, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa nguɗa ǝrviɗmahuɗ dǝ zǝraabaana, da tǝvartǝg nǝ shariya. Daddakwa ɗahgarva zǝraabaan taakiya maay nǝ dǝgiti agha tuukvakai biya, da lanngav damma guda ta shariya, dlaɓa daddakwa ɗahgarva zǝraabaan dǝ dlaga, dlaiyaan ɓǝlǝvdǝm damma kaara faiya.
MAT 5:23 “Kwakyarvad kwaha, akwamagha ɗiya baiku tǝ bagadiya kyulǝga, kaa dzamnadzamǝg kǝskǝgh taakiya hǝkyakahǝkyig nǝ zǝraabagh ma ǝrviɗmahaɗaana,
MAT 5:24 faffǝg kǝ baikuwaghǝn tǝvuukwa bagadi ndana, dǝga agha ɓaga kǝ gabǝrǝr dǝ zǝraabagh bazǝngwa. Ka sagau kǝskǝgh da ɗiya baikuwagha.
MAT 5:25 “Akwama da ɗiya ghunjagh nǝ uudana, ɓag kǝ gabǝrǝr dǝ iin tǝ watswats tǝghǝrdǝg lakuti damma guda ta shari. Akwama maay ǝndkwah biya, da langaklang davak alkali, alkali dlaɓa da langaklang davak yaa dela, ar ɓǝlkadǝm ma guda bǝrfina.
MAT 5:26 Bak jiira wan tagaktaga, lakuti sǝkadasǝg nǝ uud vaakwaha, bamma pǝlghapǝlǝg kǝ kwaɓi gatak nǝ uud baɗǝmma.
MAT 5:27 “Cinngamacinng ndza tagavdatag taakiya, ‘Ɓagam bi kǝ gwaragwar biya.’
MAT 5:28 Aiciya ǝn tagkurtag, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa vazǝna dǝkhǝra, dlaɓa kaa kǝmgaan kǝ iina, ɓagaaɓag kǝ gwaragwar dǝ vakai ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaana.
MAT 5:29 Akwama fǝkaa kǝ ɓa haip nǝ gyiya dǝvaakaffagha, tǝdatǝɗǝga agha ɓǝldana. Ngulǝm maay ba nǝ uuɓiya vǝghagh pal tǝghǝr kwada ɓǝlǝvdǝm nǝ vǝghagh baɗǝm damma kaara faiya.
MAT 5:30 Akwama fǝkaa kǝ ɓa haip nǝ dǝvaakaffagha, ghwudaghudǝga agha ɓǝldana. Ngulǝm maay ba nǝ uuɓiya vǝghagh pal tǝghǝr kwada ɓǝlǝvdǝm nǝ vǝghagh baɗǝm damma kaara faiya.
MAT 5:31 “Tagavdatag dlaɓ taakiya, ‘Daddakwa tagwavatagw dǝ uusaana, barari ghudara kǝ kakaɗa tagwavǝgh dǝ iina.’
MAT 5:32 Aiciya dǝgiti ǝn tagkurnaiya in taakiya, akwama tagwavatagw nǝ uudan dǝ uusaan kwakyarvad haipa gwaragwar biya, fadǝmfǝg ma ɗuula ɓa gwaragwara. Baɗǝm daddakwa kǝsguukǝsǝga, ɓa ba gwaragwar dǝ iina.
MAT 5:33 “Gwaastaana, cinngamacing tagavtǝratag kǝ daadijaharu taakiya, ‘Kǝldabi kǝ lanngiyagh biya, bamma agha righant kǝ langiyi tǝghara nǝnng kǝ Yaazhigǝla.’
MAT 5:34 Aiciya dǝgiti ǝn tagkurnaiya in taakiya, zambi kǝ ngwaɗǝg ba linnglinng biya, aanji dǝ ghǝrazhigǝl biya aɗaba vaka ndzǝgana Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 5:35 Zambi dlaɓ kǝ ngwaɗǝg dǝ haay biya, aɗaba vaka fa shiga Daadamazhigǝla, bi dǝ Wurshalima aɗaba iin nǝ kǝssa Tlǝkǝs ɗyaka.
MAT 5:36 Zǝbi dlaɓ kǝ ngwaɗǝg dǝ ghǝragh biya aɗaba agha nǝdalbi kǝ guja ghǝragh aanji pall kǝ maɗukwa bi gyangw biya.
MAT 5:37 Dǝgiti ɓagaaɓaga kǝ maraw kǝ taga iin taakiya, ‘Aana,’ bi ‘Əndkwah biya’, majuujig ma kwana, aasǝgal vak shatanaha.
MAT 5:38 “Cinngamacinng tagavdatag taakiya, ‘Gyiya dlakulva gyiya, tlǝrɗ dlaɓa dlakulva tlǝrɗa.’
MAT 5:39 Dǝgiti ǝn tagkur naiya, akwama naa ɓa dǝgit ghwaɗ nǝ uudan tǝ kǝgha, ɓagarbi kǝ uushav biya, ma ɓǝlakaɓǝlǝg nǝ uudan kǝ mahupeng tǝ uumǝla dǝvaakaffa, agha guyarant ghyaba kwah palla.
MAT 5:40 Akwama ɗiyakaaɗiig nǝ uudan kǝ ghunnj kwakyarvad kǝskava kǝ angyuwagha, agha vǝlar baz amugdiyagha.
MAT 5:41 Akwama fakaafǝg nǝ gwarǝɗ kǝ dagala mil palla, dǝgdagal ǝmtaɗ dǝ iin kǝ dǝga mil buwa.
MAT 5:42 Akwama ghalaaghalǝg nǝ uudan kǝ dǝgit vakagha, agha vǝlara. Dlaɓa ma sǝghǝvsǝg nǝ uudan sa kǝla gǝmau vakagha, piyarda biya.
MAT 5:43 “Cinngamacinng tagavdatag taakiya, ‘Waig kǝ zǝraabagha, agha ɗuwant kǝ tlǝghumagha.’
MAT 5:44 Aiciya, ǝn tagkurtaga, wayamwaig kǝ tlǝghumaharuwa, dzǝgwamtǝrdzǝgw kǝ zhigǝl kǝ lii vǝlkur dlaɗa
MAT 5:45 Tǝdvad ɓakwan wam da nǝg nǝ uuram kǝ zarha Daadaru kwama ghǝrazhigǝla, kwa fǝgara kǝ faci kǝ ɓa parakrakǝr tǝghǝr kǝ yaa dadda jiira ard lii ɓa kǝlaadǝra, hyitǝrhyig dlaɓ kǝ yu kǝ yaa dadda jira ard yaa dadda kǝlaadǝra.
MAT 5:46 Akwamam waiya ba lii waiya kuram nǝ uurama, auci nǝ dǝgshigi am da tlǝkǝna nǝ uurami? Aanji lii dzaha hadam ndakwi ar ɓagaan bandkwana.
MAT 5:47 Akwamam tagtǝr bak zaraabaharu nǝ uuram kǝ uusa, auci gǝrgǝraru dǝ kyalma uudahi? Aanji kǝrdiyah ndakwi ar ɓagaan bandkwaha.
MAT 5:48 Mbakyarvad kwaha, namalnǝg kǝ yaa dadda jiira band Daadaru kwama ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 6:1 “Famfǝg kǝ hyǝmiya aa nal bi nǝ gata Daadamazhigǝlaru kǝ dǝga nǝgha gyi biya, aɗaba ma ɓagamaɓag ǝndkwaha, am da tlǝkna bi kǝ dǝgshigaru vak Daadaruwi kwama ghǝrazhigǝl biya.
MAT 6:2 “Mbakyarvad kwaha, akwamagha da vǝlgar dǝgit kǝ uuda, kutbi ma ghai bandkwa ɓag nǝ muniyah ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝl ard dǝ ɗuulah kiyava dlǝbǝvtǝrǝt biya, ba jiirjiira wan tagkurtaga, cauwaracaug kǝ dǝgshigaatǝr ba ma kwahiina.
MAT 6:3 Akwma agha da mǝlgaru kǝ dadda kwa maay dǝ vakai biya, aa sǝrabi nǝ dǝvaa ghyaɓagh kǝ dǝgiti ɓag nǝ dǝvaa kafagh biya.
MAT 6:4 Aɗaba dǝgaha jiirjiiri kwa ɓagha nǝnng shiɓashiɓana, nǝghǝganǝghǝg daadagh baɗǝm kǝ dǝgitah ɓagha nǝng shiɓashiɓana, da vǝlakvǝlǝg kǝ dǝgshǝgagha.
MAT 6:5 “Akwamam da dzǝgwazhigǝla, ɓagam bi ǝndkwa ɓag nǝ muniyah biya, aɗaba ar naaba dzǝgw vaka ghacgan kǝ zhigǝla ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝla ard barama ɗuula kiyava nǝghtǝrnǝghǝg kǝ uudaha. Ba jiir wan tagkurtaga, tlarkǝnatlǝg kǝ dǝgshigaatǝra.
MAT 6:6 Akwamagha da dzǝgwazhigǝla, dǝg daadama gudagha, agha hǝdarduwa. Agha dzǝgwa kǝ zhigǝl kǝ Daadaghi kwa nǝghva biya, Daadaghi kwa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ dǝgiti ɓagav shiɓashiɓana, da vǝlakvǝlǝg kǝ dǝgshigagha.
MAT 6:7 “Akwamam dzǝgwazhigǝla, gwayamars bi ǝnd lii sǝrgabi kǝ Daadamazhigǝl biya, aɗaba ar tlatla taaki ma dzǝgwaradzǝgw kǝ zhigǝl tlaɗɗa da cinngtǝrnuu ǝndkwah nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 6:8 Ɓagam bi ǝnd dǝgaatǝr biya, Aɗaba sǝrgasǝrg nǝ Daadaru kǝ dǝgiti am naag nǝ uuram lakuti am ghalgaana.
MAT 6:9 “Dzǝgwamdzǝgw kǝ zhigǝl ǝndkwana. “ ‘Daadamnd kwama ghǝrazhigǝla, aa fǝvaarafǝg nǝ ɗaagagha,
MAT 6:10 tlǝksǝragha aasasǝga, dǝgiti agha naag nǝng aa ɓagvǝnaɓag ma duni bandkwa ɓagav ma ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 6:11 Vǝlkǝmndvǝlǝg kǝ dǝgzǝg haniina dlaɓa ba kǝlahǝnga.
MAT 6:12 Ɓǝshkǝmndanaɓǝshig kǝ haipahamnda, bandkwa kǝm ɓǝshtǝr nǝmnd kǝ lii ɓagkǝmnd haipaha.
MAT 6:13 Langkǝmnd bi da vaka fǝshig biya, katkǝmndkatǝg vak Shatanaha.’
MAT 6:14 “Aɗaba ma ɓǝshamtǝrnaɓǝshig kǝ lii ɓagarkura haipa, Daadaruwi ma ghǝrazhigǝl ndakwi da ɓǝshkurnaɓǝshiga.
MAT 6:15 Akwama ɓǝshamtǝrnaa bi kǝ haipahaatǝr kǝ uudah biya, da ɓǝshkurna bi dlaɓ nǝ Daadaru kǝ haipaharu biya.
MAT 6:16 “Akwamam da kǝsa andǝla, badzam bi kǝ huɗvǝgaru ǝnd kwa ɓag muniyah biya, ar badzǝda kǝ huɗvǝgaatǝr kiyav sǝrvan taakiya ar kǝsa andǝla, bak jiirjiira wan tagkur naiya, tlarkǝnatlǝg kǝ dǝgshigahaatǝra.
MAT 6:17 Akwamagha kǝsa andǝla, agha barda kǝ huɗvǝgagha, agha massa kǝ wal tǝ ghǝragha,
MAT 6:18 aɗaba aa nǝghvaakai taakiya agha kǝsa andǝl biya. Daadaghi kwa nǝghǝva biya, dlaɓa kwa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ dǝgǝti ɓagav shiɓashiɓana, da vǝlakvǝlǝg kǝ dǝgshigagha.
MAT 6:19 “Dzahamar bi kǝ alman kǝ ghǝraru ma duni biya, vakavaki da badzǝdabadzǝg nǝ agatla ard kwalaviyavi biya, ɗlaɓa ard vakavaki da dǝgaadǝg nǝ gǝlah ar ghǝluwa.
MAT 6:20 Bammam dzaharu kǝ alman kǝ ghǝraru ma ghǝrazhigǝla, vakavaki da badzǝda bi nǝ agatla ard kwalaviyavi biya, dlaɓa vakavaki da dǝgaa bi nǝ gǝlah ar da ghǝlu biya.
MAT 6:21 Aɗaba vakavaki da almanagha, dzamaghǝragh ndakwi ba vaakwaha.
MAT 6:22 “Gyiya band kaara jahurammb nǝ iin kǝ vǝgha, akwama ba lapi nǝ gyiyahagh, baɗǝm nǝ vǝghagh da ba parak ba vaivaiya.
MAT 6:23 Akwama yang bi nǝ gyiyahagh biya, baɗǝm nǝ vǝghagh ba gurtla. Akwama nalnǝg nǝ paraka vǝghagh kǝ gurtla, ba jiirjiira da ba ɗyak ba vaivai nǝ gurtlǝna!
MAT 6:24 “Maay wa ɓagarnǝsɓag kǝ kwatnahǝr kǝ dadda hǝnyahah bu biya, bi ɗuwant kwa palla, nahant kwa palla, bi hǝkyina kǝ palla nenna kǝ palla, ɓaga bi taakiya am nahant kǝ Daadamazhigǝla am nahant kǝ kwaɓ biya.
MAT 6:25 “Mbakyarvad kwaha, ǝn tagkurtaga ndavam bi kǝ dǝgiti am da zǝgaru nǝ uuram kǝ shifǝgaru biya, ard dǝgiti am da hǝɓǝg nǝ uuram biya, dlaɓa ard ɗuuli am da tlǝkǝna nǝ uuram kǝ sǝɗav dat vǝgharu biya. Mbats juu bi nǝ shifǝg kǝ dǝgzǝg biya? Nii juu bi ha nǝ vǝgh kǝ sǝɗavahi?
MAT 6:26 Vazamvazǝg kǝ ɗiikah ndana, ar maay riig biya, ar maay ghuda hǝi biya, ar maay dlaɓ dzaagaan damma kuvǝr biya, bakǝvakwaha gǝltǝrgǝlǝg Daadaruwi kwama ghǝrazhigǝla, jamtǝru bi nǝ uuram kǝ iitǝr dǝ ndangǝr biya?
MAT 6:27 War ma kuram mbakyarvad dzama dǝgiti tǝ ghǝraan fǝgarnaafǝg kǝ hǝnngah aanji ba hǝɗikǝn kǝ ghǝraani?
MAT 6:28 “Aujilbǝg kǝskuram dzama sǝɗavi am da nguɗǝg nǝ uurami? Vazamvazǝg kǝ ɗuuli ghubarǝg nǝ kwadladlah ndana, ar maay ɓa tlǝra aanji haa sǝɗav biya.
MAT 6:29 Bakǝvakwaha ǝn tagkurtaga, aanji Saluman ma ndzǝgana ndangǝraan ndakwi tapghǝnai kǝ caɗvacaɗǝg ǝnd palǝraatǝr biya
MAT 6:30 Aitsaa, akwama caɗnacaɗǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ kazhakwa tǝghal ǝndkwana, kwar mǝng haniina dlakadur ɓǝlvǝtǝrdǝm damma kaara, kyakaɗaava kuram ha wada vǝlkur bi nǝ iin kǝ sǝɗav hi? Kuram lii hǝtsahǝtsan fadghǝrna.
MAT 6:31 “Mbakyarvad kwaha, ndavam bi taakiya, ‘Auwa kǝm da zǝg nǝmndi?’ Bi ‘Auwa kǝmnda hǝɓɓǝg nǝmndi?’ Bi ‘Auwa nǝ dǝgiti kǝmnda nguɗǝg nǝmndi?’
MAT 6:32 Aɗabad kwaha lii sǝrga bi kǝ Daadamazhigǝl biya, iitǝr lii gata kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitah baɗǝmma. Sǝrgasǝrǝg nǝ Daadaru kwama ghǝrazhigǝl taakiya am naagaan kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitaha.
MAT 6:33 Gatamgatǝg kǝ tlǝkǝsǝra Daadamazhigǝl ba zǝnngwa, ard dǝgiti naag nǝ iina. Da vǝlkurvǝlǝg kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitah baɗǝmma.
MAT 6:34 Mbakyarvad kwaha, ndavambi kǝ dlakadur biya, aɗaba dlakadur sagau bad dlaɗaana, dlaɗa hinan ndakwi tlaltlǝg kwakyarvad haniina.
MAT 7:1 “Tar bi kǝ shari kǝ uudah biya. Akwama ɓaghiniɓaga, ar da taktǝg nǝ uudaha kǝ shariya.
MAT 7:2 Aɗaba hulfa shariyi am tǝgar nǝ uuram kǝ uudaha, da tǝkur bandkwah nǝ uud kǝ shariya, kuwǝn am kurgar nǝ uuram kǝ uudah dǝ vakaiya, da kurkur bad vakai nǝ uuda.
MAT 7:3 Aujilbǝg agha vaza zǝr afǝsafǝsa dǝga dakari ma gyiya zǝraabagh kwal fataaɗ kǝskǝgh tǝ gugyǝmba dakari ma gyiyaghi?
MAT 7:4 Agha tagar ndar kǝ zǝraabagh taakiya, ‘Ən sǝkadasǝg kǝ zǝr afǝsafǝsa dǝga dakarǝn ma gyiyaghǝn,’ mbats kǝgh ndakwani gugyǝmba dakar wa ma gyiyaghi?
MAT 7:5 Kǝgh muunina, kǝsdakǝsǝg kǝ gugyǝmba dakarǝn ma gyiyaghǝn ndana, kiyava nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝskǝgh ba caɗaɗɗa lakuti agha da kǝsa zǝr afǝsagǝsa dǝga dakarǝn ma gyiya zǝraabaghǝna.
MAT 7:6 “Vǝlamtǝr bi kǝ ghǝgyah kǝ dǝgiti caccuwanacaccuwanan biya, aɗaba ar da gwiyav ar tahkurdana. Vǝlamtǝr bi dlaɓ kǝ jindararu kǝ ghavzah biya, aɗaba ar da hapgaana.
MAT 7:7 “Ghalamghalǝga, da vǝlǝkurvǝlǝg nǝ uuda, gatamgatǝga, am da tlǝkǝnatlǝga, ngadlamngadlǝga, da wurkurwurǝg nǝ uud kǝ ghaiya wakyagha.
MAT 7:8 Aanji kwar kǝ dadda ghalǝga vǝlvarvǝlǝga, aanji kwar kǝ dadda gatǝga tlǝkǝnatlǝga, aanji kwar kǝ dadda ngadla wakyagha da wurvarwurǝg nǝ wakyagha.
MAT 7:9 War ma kuram daadaha, akwama ghalaaghalǝg nǝ zǝraan kǝ bruudi, vǝlar kǝ akuri?.
MAT 7:10 Nii ma ghalaaghalǝg nǝ zǝran kǝ kilfa, vǝlar kǝ ghaval dlakulvaan hi?
MAT 7:11 Akwama kurami dangw huɗaharu am sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ vǝlǝga dǝgit maraw kǝ zarharuwa, kyakaɗava daadaruwi ma ghǝrazhigǝli kaci wa da vǝltǝr bi kǝ dǝgitah maraw kǝ lii ghalǝgan biya!
MAT 7:12 “Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgitahi am naag nǝ uuram ɓagkura nǝ uudaha, kuram ndakwani ɓagamtǝrɓaga. Aɗaba kwan wa tagada nǝ adzahadzaha Muus ard tlayanha.
MAT 7:13 “Tamtǝg kǝ ghaiya wakyaghǝn jǝghwna, aɗaba ɗuula daas da vaka ǝmtsǝga ba bahahha, dlaɓa kwanǝn kǝ ɗuula ba tsalalla. Lii tǝgaana ar ba dyaka.
MAT 7:14 Ɗuula tlǝkǝna shifǝga. Ba jǝghwa nǝ iina, dlaɓa dladlaɗ nǝ tǝgaana. Lii tǝgaana ar maay ɗyak biya.
MAT 7:15 “Famfǝg kǝ hyǝmmi tǝ tlayangaha fiidfiida kwar sahasagaw da vakaru dǝ garava tughaha, ma huɗmahuɗa ar jagajagaan band ghǝgyaha tǝghala.
MAT 7:16 Am da nǝghǝtǝraakanǝghǝg tǝdvad tlǝrahaatǝra. Cagvacag nǝ zarha inabi tǝ uufa takka? Nii cagvacag ha nǝ zǝra ghǝgyiv tǝ zaz hi?
MAT 7:17 Bandkwah dlaɓ makwar kǝ uufi marawa yaa ba zǝr marawa, uufi ghwaɗa, ya zǝr ghwaɗa.
MAT 7:18 Maay nǝ uufi maraw ya zǝr ghwaɗ biya, dlaɓa uufi ghwaɗa yiga bi kǝ zǝr maraw biya.
MAT 7:19 Baɗǝm nǝ uufi maay ya zǝr maraw biya, aa ghudvarsghudǝga, ɓǝlvdǝm damma kaara.
MAT 7:20 Mbakyarvad kwaha am da nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg kǝ tlayanngaha fiidfiid tǝdvad tlǝrahaatǝra.
MAT 7:21 “Ɗǝm bi dadda kwa taa kǝskai ‘Yaazhigǝl, Yaazhigǝl’ da daas damma tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl biya, bamma dadda kwa ɓagaaɓag kǝ dǝgiti naag nǝ Daadar kwama ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 7:22 Daghuvala ta shariya, ar da tagwatag nǝ uudaha baɗyak taakiya, ‘Yaazhigǝl, Yaazhigǝl, tagamnda bi kǝ ǝlbǝg maraw ma ɗaagagh biya? Lagwamndada bi kǝ shatanah ma ɗaagagh biya? Ɓagamda bi kǝ dǝgaha jappǝr baɗyak ma ɗaagagh biya?’
MAT 7:23 Tǝhala kwaha, ǝnda tagtǝrtag taakiya, ‘Ən sǝrkur bi ba dǝm biya. Yagham vakar kǝlaadahaana.’
MAT 7:24 “Mbakyarvad kwaha baɗǝm daddakwa cinnghacinng kǝ ǝlbǝgara, dlaɓa ɓagaan kǝ tlǝr dǝ vakaiya, da nǝg band dadda dabari kwa ndǝraa vǝgyaan tǝ akurna.
MAT 7:25 Hyiyaa ba nǝ yuwa, kaa righǝtrighǝg nǝ zaagha kǝla saasa, fǝɗ ndakwi tsa saas dat hǝnyahiina, bakǝvakwaha dlǝghana biya, aɗaba ndǝrava tǝ akura.
MAT 7:26 “Baɗǝm daddakwa cinnghacinng kǝ ǝlbǝgara, dlaɓa ɓagaa bi kǝ tlǝr dǝ vakai biya, ba kalkal dǝ dlagǝn kwa ndǝraa hǝnyahaan tǝ sǝghǝla.
MAT 7:27 Hyiyaa ba nǝ yuwa, righǝtrighǝg nǝ zaagha, fǝd ndakwi tsa saas dat hǝnyahiin, kaa dlǝga, dlagaadlag bafakya.”
MAT 7:28 Ghyǝnga ba nǝ Yesu tagtǝr kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, kaa ba ɓa jappǝr kǝ uudah dǝ tsagaanana.
MAT 7:29 Aɗaba tsagatǝr band daddakwa dǝ ndzǝɗa, gǝrgǝr dǝ tsaga lii tsaga adzahadzaha Muusa.
MAT 8:1 Sahi ba nǝ Yesu sii ma aghwa, kaa gatǝgaan kǝ uudaha baɗyaka
MAT 8:2 Kaa sagau kǝ dadda vǝc da vakaana, kǝla kǝ iin kǝ ghunj tǝvuukwaana amaa, “Yaazhigǝla, ma haighanthaiga, mbǝkwimbǝga.”
MAT 8:3 Kaa vǝlla dǝv kǝ Yesu tapǝna kǝ dadda vǝcna amaa, “Haiyananthaiga, mbambǝga.” Batwatswatsǝra, kaa mbǝgambǝg kǝ iina.
MAT 8:4 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Faffǝg kǝ hyǝmmiya tagar bi aanji kǝ war kǝ dǝgiti aa dzǝgardzǝgǝn biya, dǝg mardamarǝg kǝ ghǝragh vak zhiila kǝsuufa, agha vǝlda kǝ baiku bandkwa tagada na adzahadzaha Musa. Ɓagnaɓag kwana kiyava fadghǝr kǝ dlamakǝlaawa taakiya mbǝghambǝga.”
MAT 8:5 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu damma Kafarnahum, ngal dagau kǝ tlauja Rum maamal da vakaan da ghalgaan taakiya,
MAT 8:6 “Yaazhigǝla, kwatnahar hǝngan hǝnyah ǝmtsamtsan nǝ vǝgha, hǝɓa dlaɗ ba vaivaiya.”
MAT 8:7 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Ən dagau da mbǝgaana.”
MAT 8:8 Kaa ngugwamgug kǝ tlauj maamalna amaa, “Yaazhigǝla, tlanal bi nai kǝskǝgh kǝ sagau sa vǝgyar biya, tagdatag ba kǝ ǝlbǝg kalti kwatnahar da mbǝga.
MAT 8:9 Aɗaba kai dǝghǝrar ndakwani ǝn mazhangyil kǝ kwarǝga uuda, mǝng dlaɓ tlaujah mazhangyil kǝskaiya, ǝn tagardatag kǝ pallaatǝr taakiya, ‘Dǝga,’ kaa dagauwa. Kwatlǝrǝn dlaɓ ǝn ɗaagantdaaga taakiya, ‘Sawa,’ sagauwa, Akwama taganartag dlaɓ kǝ kwatlǝrǝna, ‘Ɓagnaɓag kǝ dǝgit ǝntkwaha,’ kaa ɓagaana.”
MAT 8:10 Cinngha ba nǝ Yesu ǝndkwaha, kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ iina, aiyama kǝ lii gatǝgaana, “Ən tagkurtag kǝ jiira, tapanna bi kǝ tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ uud dǝ fadghǝr ǝndkwan ma Izrail biya.
MAT 8:11 Ən tagkurtaga, baɗyak nǝ uudah ar da sii dǝ sǝga ard sagat dǝ sǝga ar da cihurgan ǝmtaɗ dǝ Ibrahim ard Ishaku ard Yakub vaka za kaffa hwaɗag ma tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 8:12 Aɗaba uudahi ɓadlavtǝrna kǝ iitǝr nǝ tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla, da ɗiivtǝrdǝm damma gurtla, vakavaki ar da tuug nǝ iitǝr ard ghwada dǝv dǝ tlǝrɗa.”
MAT 8:13 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ tlauja maamalǝna, “Dǝgdaasa, da ɓagakɓag nǝ uud mbakyarvad fadghǝragha.” Kaa mbǝg nǝ kwatnaha nǝ iina batwatsǝra.
MAT 8:14 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu da vǝgya Bitrusa, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ babba uusa Bitrus ɓǝlgan njǝkǝn fǝɗa.
MAT 8:15 Tapǝna kǝ iin kǝ dǝva uusiina, kaa mbǝgambǝg kǝ iin tuuk kǝ fǝɗiina, ngal ciiga ɓagtǝra kǝ dǝgzǝga.
MAT 8:16 Ɓǝlaa ba hwaasa, kaa sǝdǝvsǝga kǝ uudah kǝ lii ciɓǝg shatanah baɗyak da vak Yesu, tagada ba ǝlbǝg kalti, ngal sagal shatanahahaan ma vǝghaatǝra, mbahǝnan baz lii yangbiya.
MAT 8:17 Tǝdvad kwan wa righavant nǝ dǝgiti tagavda tǝdvad tlayang Ishay taakiya, “Kǝsakiyamaarakǝsǝg kǝ kuzahamiyama, dlaɓa kǝskiyamaaran kǝ yangbiyahamiyama.”
MAT 8:18 Nǝgha ba nǝ Yesu kǝ uudah baɗyak faɗǝga tǝghǝr kǝ iina, ngal tagartag kǝ iin kǝ mbǝrzahaan maraa dzǝva dagal dat ghyaba kwah kǝ ghaiya yuwa haiya.
MAT 8:19 Ngal sagau kǝ dadda tsaga adzahadzah da vakaana, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Dadda tsaga dǝgita, ǝn gatakgatǝg badǝm vakavaki agha dagal nǝnga.”
MAT 8:20 Ngugharangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Mbayakaha ar da afkahaatǝra, ɗiikaha dlaɓa mǝng vakavaka hǝnnganahaatǝra, Zǝra Uuda maay vaka hǝnnganan biya.”
MAT 8:21 Am nǝ pall ma mbǝrzahaan taa kǝ iina, “Yaazhigǝla, ǝn dǝgaadǝg ndan ǝn hǝɗnan kǝ daadara.”
MAT 8:22 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Gatkwagatǝga, aa hǝɗarhǝɗǝg lii ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝg kǝ zaraabahaatǝri ǝmtsaraǝmtsǝga.”
MAT 8:23 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu damma pɛrayuwa, kaa gatǝgaan kǝ mbǝrzahaana.
MAT 8:24 Kaa ciig kǝ ghabag ard fǝɗ ma yuwahaiya, fǝgharzhafǝg baz yu ghubǝɗa saas damma pɛrayuwa, Yesu dlaba hǝnahaara.
MAT 8:25 Kaa dagau kǝ mbǝrzahaan ar ciyanta, am nǝ iitǝra, “Yaazhigǝla, katkǝmndkatǝga wakǝm tǝ ɗuula ǝmtsǝga.”
MAT 8:26 Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Aujilbǝg kǝskuram gǝdzǝg ǝndkwani, kuramǝn dǝ fadghǝr hǝɗiikǝna?” Kaa ciig kǝ iin cagara kǝ gyi kǝ fǝɗǝn ard ghubǝɗǝga yuwa, kaa kyaɓalǝgakyaɓalǝga.
MAT 8:27 Kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ mbǝrzahaana, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Hulfakwar kǝ uud wana, baz fǝɗ ard ghubǝɗǝga yu ar cinngarnucinngni?”
MAT 8:28 Tsǝgwa ba nǝ Yesu ma haaya Garisaha, kaa sagau kǝ uudah bu kwa ciɓtǝr shatanah sa vak Yesu, gǝdzǝvtǝrgǝdzǝg ba vaivaiya, aɗaba ar ndzǝga bamma gǝtlaha, maay wa ta kwahiin kǝ ɗuul biya.
MAT 8:29 Kaa huulǝg kǝ iitǝr ar taakiya, “Au lambagh dǝ kǝmnd Zǝra Daadamazhigǝli? Agha sa vǝlkǝmnd dlaɗ ba sart ndakwani ɓagaa biya?”
MAT 8:30 Mǝng nǝ maandala agyaragyara ghavzah ar piig kǝ dagalaatǝra.
MAT 8:31 Ngal ba ghalgaan kǝ shatanahaan kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Akwama sǝghkǝmndadasǝga, ɗiikǝmndarsɗiig damma gyǝɗya ghavdzahaana.”
MAT 8:32 Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Damdǝg ciya,” Kaa daas kǝ iitǝr damma ghavzahiina. Baɗǝm gyǝɗya ghavzǝn kaa ǝmdǝra daay kǝ iitǝr bawatswats damma yuwahaiya, ngal ruug kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 8:33 Kaa ǝmndǝra daas kǝ lii piya ghavzahaana. Daragha ba nǝ iitǝr damma kǝssa, kaa tagaan kǝ iitǝr kǝ dǝgitahi dzǝghaar dǝ lii ciɓtǝr nǝ shatanahǝn baɗǝmma.
MAT 8:34 Ngal sagal kǝ uudah ma kǝsiin baɗǝm da tlǝgaraa Yesu. Nǝghara ba nǝ iitǝra, kaa ghalgaan kǝ iitǝr maa ɗuwars kǝ lardaatǝra.
MAT 9:1 Kaa daas kǝ Yesu damma pɛrayuwa, ngal dagal tǝghǝra yu damma Kafarnahum, kǝssi ghubara nǝ iina.
MAT 9:2 Kaa sagau kǝ uudah dǝ daddakwa ǝmtsamtsan nǝ vǝgha hǝngan tǝ kǝjja, nǝghǝgha ba nǝ Yesu kǝ fadghǝratǝra, aiyama kǝ daddakwa ǝmtsaǝmtsan nǝ vǝghǝna “Zǝrara, ndavbiya, ɓǝshakanaɓǝshǝg nǝ uud kǝ haipahagha.”
MAT 9:3 Cinngara ba nǝ lii tsaga adzahadzaha ǝndkwaha, kaa takǝvatag kǝ iitǝr mataatakaatǝr taakiya, “Kwanǝn kǝ uuda badza ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝla!”
MAT 9:4 Nǝghakanǝghǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ dzamaghǝraatǝra, amaa kǝ iitǝra, “Aujibǝg am dzama kǝlaadǝr ma ǝrvidmahuɗaruwi?
MAT 9:5 Kwar wa tsaftsaf kǝ taga, taakiya, ‘Bǝshakanaɓǝshǝg nǝ uud kǝ haipahagha nii ciiga dǝgdagalhi?’
MAT 9:6 Ən naagaan am sǝran taakiya Zǝra Uuda dǝ ndzǝɗa ɓǝsha haipah ma duniya.” Kaa amaa taa kǝ daddakwa ǝmtsamtsan nǝ vǝghna, “Ciig kǝssǝg kǝjjagha dǝg daas dahǝnyaha.”
MAT 9:7 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa ciig kǝ uudanǝna, ngal daas kǝ iin da vǝgyaana.
MAT 9:8 Nǝghara ba nǝ dzahava dlamakǝlaawa ǝndkwaha, kaa gǝdzǝg kǝ iitǝra, ar gala Daadamazhigǝla kwa vǝlgar hulfa kwan kǝ ndzǝɗ kǝ uudaha.
MAT 9:9 Ɗughars ba nǝ Yesu kǝ vakavaka kwahiina, kaa nǝghǝganǝhǝg kǝ iina kǝ uuda nǝ iin kwa ɗahav dǝ Matiyu cihurgan vaka cauwa hadama. Am Yesu taa kǝ iina “Gatkwagatǝga” ngal ciig kǝ iin kaa gatǝgaana.
MAT 9:10 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa za kaf kǝ Yesu ma vǝgya Matiyu, ngal sagau kǝ lii cauwa hadama ard yaa dadda haip ba ɗyaka ar cihuran buud za kaf kǝ iitǝr dǝ iina ard mbǝrzahaana.
MAT 9:11 Nǝghǝra ba nǝ Farisiyah ǝntkwaha, ngal am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Aujibǝg kǝ dadda hǝnyaharu za kaf ǝmtaɗ dǝ lii cauwa hadama ard yaa dadda haipi?”
MAT 9:12 Cinngha ba nǝ Yesu ǝntkwaha, aiyama, “Lii yanga maay lambatǝr dǝ dadda mba uud biya, bamma lii yang biya.
MAT 9:13 Damdǝg tsagamtsag kǝ dǝgiti tuuk vakai wanǝna, ‘Zhuwadaal wan naag nai vakaruwa kyulǝgg biya.’ Sanhi da ɗaa lii jiir bi nai biya, sanhi mbakyarvad yaa dadda haipa.”
MAT 9:14 Kaa dagau nǝ mbǝrzaha Yuhwana dadda tsuufǝg davak Yesu, am nǝ iitǝra, “Aujilbg kǝskǝmnd ard Farisiyah kǝm kǝsgaan ka andǝla, kwakyarvadau kǝ mbǝrzahah ar maay kǝsgani?”
MAT 9:15 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ar badzǝgaan nǝ tsaghwaha zhiila ghuula kǝ ǝrvidmahuɗ ma bar ǝmtaɗ dǝ zhiila ghuula? Da sagau sarta kwa da kǝsav zhiila ghuula dagal vakatǝra, ar da kǝssǝg ma kwah sarta nǝ iitǝra kǝ andǝla.
MAT 9:16 “Maay wa ghudgǝtghudǝg kǝ daala sǝɗav tlappant tǝ ǝnghura sǝɗav biya aɗaba da tǝhgaan kǝ ǝnghura sǝɗav na, tǝhgaana, da jǝguujǝg kwa ndza wura.
MAT 9:17 Maay wa ɗiya daala yuwa inabi damma ǝnghura ambǝla hǝllu biya, akwama ɗiyavdǝmɗiiga, ciɓgaan kǝ ǝnghura ambǝla hǝllwuna, ɗiya dagal nǝ yuwa inabiya badzǝgaan kǝ ambǝla hǝlluwa. Daala yuwa inabi ɗiyav bamma daala ambǝla hǝlluwa tǝvad kwah wa da ɗiigal bi nǝ iin biya dlaɓa ciɓǝgai nǝ ambǝla hǝllu biya.”
MAT 9:18 Ma sarta taa kwanǝn kǝ Yesu, kaa sagau nǝ maala ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝla da vakaana, kǝla kǝ ghuunj tǝvuukwana, amaa, “Dǝghwar aa ǝmtsǝga ba ndakwana, asǝg tapnatapǝg da ciiga.”
MAT 9:19 Kaa dagal kǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan gata uuda nǝ iina.
MAT 9:20 Mǝng nǝ uusiin viigaan kǝlawa tar buwa kǝla avǝza, ka dagau kǝ iina gyilga Yesu tapǝna kǝ ghaiya sǝɗavaana.
MAT 9:21 Amaa ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaana, “Akwama tapannatapǝg aanji ba ghaiya sǝɗavaan kaltiya, ǝn da mbǝga.”
MAT 9:22 Gwiyavǝt ba nǝ Yesu kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝga, aiyama, “Ndav bi dǝghwar biya, fadghǝragha mɓakanambǝga.” Batwatsǝra, kaa mbǝga kǝ uusina.
MAT 9:23 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu da vǝgya maala ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝlǝna, kaa nǝhganǝhǝg kǝ iin kǝ lii fǝrta faakila ard dzahava dlamaa kǝlaaw ar tuuga.
MAT 9:24 Aiyam nǝ Yesu, “Ciyamciig vaakwana, ǝmtsabi nǝ dughwiin biya, hǝnnahaara.” Kaa ɓagar ghuɓasǝga nenneg kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 9:25 Lagwavtǝrda ba nǝ uudah da gyǝmala, kaa daas kǝ iina hǝkyinan kǝ dǝva dughwiina, ngal ciiga.
MAT 9:26 Kaa cinngalcinng nǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ iin aanji taakwara.
MAT 9:27 Ɗughars ba nǝ Yesu kǝ vakavak kǝ iina, kaa ba gatǝgaan kǝ gulfah buwa ar ɗaag bad halavuwa ndzǝɗaatǝr ar taakiya, “Zhukǝmndaalazhug, Zǝra Dauda!”
MAT 9:28 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu damma kwatlǝrǝn kǝ hǝnyaha, kaa daas kǝ gulfah bu da vakaana, aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Famdǝghǝrtfǝg taakiya ǝn mbǝkurambǝga?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Aana, Yaazhigǝla.”
MAT 9:29 Tǝhala kwaha, kaa tapǝna kǝ iin kǝ gyiyahaatǝra aiyama, “Tǝdvad fadhǝraruwa, mbǝkurmbǝg nǝ uuda?”
MAT 9:30 Ngal wurǝg kǝ gyiyahaatǝra, tǝhala kwaha ka ɓǝltǝra nǝ Yesu kǝ magi ba vaivaiya amaa, “Tagamarbi aanji kǝ war biya.”
MAT 9:31 Daral ba nǝ iitǝra, kaa ba kutǝgaan kǝ iitǝr kǝ ǝlbǝgǝn tǝghǝr kǝ iin aanji takwar ma lardiina.
MAT 9:32 Ar tǝ ɗuula sagala, kaa sǝvardǝvsǝg nǝ daddakwa mamghant nǝ shatanaha kǝ Yesu.
MAT 9:33 Savda ba nǝ Satanahna, kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ uuda nǝ iin kǝ taa ghaiya, kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ dzahava dlama kǝlaawa, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Ba dǝm tapavnai kǝ nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ hulfa kwan kǝ dǝgit ma Izrail biya.”
MAT 9:34 Aiyam Farisiyaha, “Abi lagw dǝ ndzǝɗa maala Shatanah nǝ iin kǝ shatanaha.”
MAT 9:35 Tǝhala kwaha, kaa gwaivagwaig kǝ Yesu ma kǝssaha ard gǝdzǝr kǝssaha, tsagtǝrtsag ma guda dzugwazhigǝla, tagtǝr ǝlbǝg maraw tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝkǝsǝra Daadamazhigǝla, mbahtǝran dlaɓ kǝ uudahi dǝ kuzah shahshaha ard lii yang biya.
MAT 9:36 Nǝgha ba nǝ iin kǝ dzahava dlamaa kǝlaaw baɗyaka, kaa zhutǝrdalaazhuuga. Aɗaba ar hǝɓa dlaɗa maay wa mǝltǝrumǝlǝg biya, ar band tughwahǝn kwal dadda piiga.
MAT 9:37 Aiyama taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Tlǝra ghuda hǝi ba ɗyaka, dlaɓa lii ɓa tlǝra ar ba ǝnkykwahha.
MAT 9:38 Mbakyarvad kwaha, ghalamghalǝg kǝ dadda guhha maa dzǝgaraa kǝ lii ɓaa tlǝra, maraa ghudara kǝ hǝiya.”
MAT 10:1 Kaa ɗahtǝrantɗahǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝlaawa tar buwa. Vǝlatǝrvǝlǝg kǝ ndzǝɗa lagwa shatanaha ar mbaha kuzah shahshaha ard lii yang biya.
MAT 10:2 Wan nǝ ɗaagaha mbǝrzah kǝlaawa tar buna. Dǝga zǝnngwa iin nǝ Siman kwa ɗahav dǝ Bitrus ard dǝ zǝra babbaan Andrawus ard Yakubu zǝra Zabadi ard zǝra babbaan Yuhwana,
MAT 10:3 ard Filigus ard Batalomi ard Tuma ard Matiyu dadda cauwa hadama ard Yakubu zǝra Halfa ard Taddiyus,
MAT 10:4 Siman kwa naagaan kǝ za vukwa kǝsaana, ard Yahuda Iskariyoti kwa zuu langiya Yesu.
MAT 10:5 Ɓǝlatǝrǝtɓǝlǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝlaawa tar buna, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Dam bi davak lii ar Yahudah biya, ɗlaɓa dam bi damma kǝssa Samariyah biya.
MAT 10:6 Dlakulva kwaha damdǝg da vak tughaha uudaha Izraila kwa zaharazahǝga.
MAT 10:7 Damdǝg tagamtǝrtag kǝ ǝlbǝg marawa taakiya, ‘Tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla hǝrzǝthǝrzǝga.’
MAT 10:8 Mbahamtǝrmbahǝg kǝ lii yang biya, ciyamtǝrciig kǝ lii ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝga, mbahamtǝrmbahǝg kǝ magyagulfaha, lagwamlagw kǝ Shatanaha. Tlamkǝna ba gyaagyaana vǝlamtǝrvǝlǝg ba gyaagyaana.
MAT 10:9 Kǝsam bi kǝ adawana, aanji agwalɛl, aanji vǝrzhagan ma ambǝlaru biya.
MAT 10:10 Kǝsam bi kǝ ambǝl mam dagal biya, aanji sǝɗav buwa, aanji kimbak aanji zad biya, aɗaba dadda ɓa tlǝra dlaikǝndlaig nǝ dǝgshigaana.
MAT 10:11 “Baɗǝm nǝ kǝsa ard gǝdzǝr kǝssahi am dǝgaa nǝ uurama, gatamgatǝg kǝ uuda jiirjiir am ndzan ma vǝgyaana tangw damma sarti am da ciig nǝ uurama.
MAT 10:12 Akwama damaghan da hǝnyahiina, tagamtǝrtag taakiya, ‘Gabǝrǝr tǝghǝr kǝskurama.’
MAT 10:13 Akwama uudaha jiirjiir wa ma hǝnyahiina, gabǝraruwa aa ndzandzǝg tǝghǝr kǝ iitǝra, akwama uudaha jiirjiir biya, gabǝraruwa gwiya saa kǝskurama.
MAT 10:14 Baɗǝm daddakwa lawalǝg kǝ dlǝgha kurama, ard cinnga ǝlbǝgaruwa, pangamdapang kǝ alagwat tǝ shigaharuwu akwamam da ɗuwa kǝsaatǝra.
MAT 10:15 Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, da zhuvtǝrdaala kǝ uudaha Sadum ard Gumara tǝghǝr kǝ uudaha kǝssiin daghuvala ta shariya.
MAT 10:16 “Wan ɓǝlkurɓǝlǝg band tuughwah ma taataka ghǝgyaha tǝghala, mbakyarvad kwaha ndzamandzǝg ba ɗyamɗyam band ghavala, dlaɓa am nal kalaliyah band kakuura.
MAT 10:17 Famfǝg kǝ hyǝmmi dǝ uudah aɗaba ar da langkurlang damma guda ta shariya, ar da ɓalkura kiiɓ ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝlaatǝra.
MAT 10:18 Ar da langkurlang da tǝvuukwa maamaalah ard tlǝkǝssah mbakyarvad kaiya, kiyava taa ǝlbǝg maraw kǝskuram tǝvuukwatǝra ard tǝvuukwa lii ar yahudah biya.
MAT 10:19 Akwama langarkurdalanga, ndavam bi kǝ dǝgiti am da tag nǝ uuram biya, ard ɗuuli am da tag nǝ uuram biya, aɗaba da vǝlkurvǝlǝg nǝ uud kǝ dǝga tagga.
MAT 10:20 Aɗaba kuram bi wada taaghai biya, shǝɗkwa Daadaru wa da taaghai mbakyarvad kurama.
MAT 10:21 “Zǝraaba da za lanngiya zǝraabaan da tsǝvana, daada da za lanngiya zǝraana, zarha ar da ciitǝrant kǝ yaatǝra da ciɓǝvtǝrana.
MAT 10:22 Uudah baɗǝm ar da naakur bi mbakyarvad ɗaagara, dlaɓa baɗǝm daddakwa ghacaghacig dat ghalaana, da tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ katǝga.
MAT 10:23 Akwamar vǝlkur dlaɗ ma kwatlǝrǝn kǝssa, ǝmndǝraǝmdǝrga damma kǝssi tǝvuukwa, jiira wan takur naiya lakuti am tsǝgarvaratsǝg kǝ kǝsaha Izraila baɗǝmma, da saaya nǝ Zǝra Uuda.
MAT 10:24 “Daddakwa tsaga dǝgit vak kǝ uuda jiguubi kǝ dadda tsagar dǝgit biya, jiguubi dlaba nǝ kwatnah kǝ dadda hǝnyahaan biya.
MAT 10:25 Tlǝgaltlǝg nǝ dadda tsaga dǝgit vak kǝ uuda, nal band dadda tsagar dǝgita, dlaɓa kwatnah band dadda hǝnnyahaana. Akwamar ɗaag dǝ Baˈalzabul kǝ dadda hǝnnyaha, ar da ɗaatǝr dǝ kwa juujig kǝ Baˈalzabul kǝ uudahi ma hǝnnyahiina.
MAT 10:26 “Mbakyarvad kwaha, gǝdzamtǝr biya, aɗaba maay nǝ dǝgiti hǝɗahǝdan kwa da maay wurav biya, dlaɓa maay nǝ dǝgiti shiɓashiɓan kwa da sǝrvaaka biya.
MAT 10:27 Dǝgiti taagankur nai magurtla, tagamtag bat ɓalaɓala, dǝgiti cinngama nǝ uram da gǝlagǝla, tlǝhamtlǝhǝg tǝ ghǝra guda.
MAT 10:28 Gǝdzam bi kǝ lii tsǝgatsǝg kǝ vǝgha biya aɗaba ar maay dǝ ndzǝɗa tsa shifǝg biya, gǝdzamgǝdzǝg kǝ dadda kwa tsǝgatsǝg kǝ vǝgh ard shifǝg ma kaarafaiya.
MAT 10:29 Maay kwan vǝlav nǝ caakwah bu tǝ kwaɓ pal biya? Bakǝvakwaha maay aanji pallǝratǝr ɓǝladagal da tǝ haay kwal sǝrga bi kǝ daadaru biya.
MAT 10:30 Baz guujaha ghǝraharu ndakwani kǝdlakǝdlana.
MAT 10:31 Mbakyarvad kwaha, ndavam biya, jamujig nǝ uuram kǝ caakwah baɗyak dǝ ndanngǝra.
MAT 10:32 “Baɗǝm daddakwa haiyakuthaig kǝskai tǝvuukwa uudaha, kai ndakwi ǝn da haiganthaiga dǝ iin tǝvuukwa Daadar kwa ma ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 10:33 Aiciya, badǝm daddakwa haiyakut bi tǝvuukwa uudah biya, kai ndakwani ǝn da haigant bi dǝ iin tǝvuukwa Daadar kwa ma ghǝrazhigǝl biya.
MAT 10:34 “Tlatlam bi taakiya sanhi kwakyarvad ǝn vǝlkur kǝ gabǝrǝr nai damma duni biya, maaya, sanhi kwakyarvad ǝn vǝlkur kǝ gabǝrǝr biya, ba tagwazhatagwazha.
MAT 10:35 Sandi tagwazhatagwazha, adaba “ ‘zǝra da ɓa dau dǝ daddaana, dughwa da ɓa dau dǝ babbaana, ghuul dlaɓa dǝ ɓa dau dǝ jikkan uusa.
MAT 10:36 Uudaha hǝnnyahaan kǝ uudan war da ɓa dau dǝ iina.’
MAT 10:37 “Badǝm nǝ daddakwa waiya daddaan bi babbaana tǝghǝr kǝskaiya, tlǝgal bi kǝ nǝg kǝ dǝgar biya. Dlaɓa baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa waiya zǝraan bi dǝghwaana tǝghǝr kǝskaiya tlǝgal bi kǝ nǝg kǝ dǝgar biya.
MAT 10:38 Badǝm nǝ daddakwa kǝsǝghanti kǝ tlaɓahǝrtǝgaan ngal gata kai biya, tlǝgal bi kǝ nǝg kǝ dǝgar biya.
MAT 10:39 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa naa kata shifǝgaana, ɓǝlgaan dagala. Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa ɓǝlda shifǝgaan kwakyarvad kaiya aa fǝgabadfǝga.
MAT 10:40 “Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa dlǝghakuradlǝghǝga, dlǝghakwidlǝghǝg kǝskaiya, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa dlǝghakwidlǝghǝga, dlaghaadlǝghǝg kǝ daddakwa ɓǝlkwadi kaiya.
MAT 10:41 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa dlaghaadlǝghǝg kǝ tlayanga kwakyarvad tlayang nǝ iina, da tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ dǝgshiga tlayanga. Dlaɓa badǝm nǝ daddakwa dlaghaadlǝghǝg kǝ uuda jirjira kwakyarvad uuda jirjira nǝ iina, da tlǝkǝnatlǝga kǝ dǝgshiga uuda jirjiira.
MAT 10:42 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa vǝlgar kuwa yu lǝmcikcik kǝ pall ma lii hǝɗiikǝn kwakyarvad mbǝrzar nǝ iina, ǝn takurtaga da pilwai nǝ dǝgshigaan biya.”
MAT 11:1 Ghyǝnga ba nǝ Yesu kǝ tagtǝr dǝgitah kǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝlaawa tar buwa, kaa dagal kǝ iin damma kǝsaha Galili da tsagtǝr dǝgitah ard taa ǝlbǝg maraw kǝ uudaha.
MAT 11:2 Ma sarta kwahiina Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝga ndza ma guda birfǝna, cinngha ba nǝ iin kǝ dǝgitahi ɓag nǝ Yesu, kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ iin kǝ mbǝrzahaan da vakaana.
MAT 11:3 Ar ndavaru taakiya, “Kǝgh wagha da saayin nii, kǝm paka kwatlǝrǝnhi?”
MAT 11:4 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gwiyamagwig daas am tagar kǝ Yuhwan kǝ dǝgiti amaa nǝghǝga nǝ uurama, ard dǝgiti amaa cinnga nǝ uurama.
MAT 11:5 Gulfaha ar nǝghǝganǝghǝga, ghurɗikaha ar dagala, yaa dadda vǝca mbahavtǝrambahǝga matanngaha ar cinngacinnga, uudahi ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝga ciyavtǝrǝtciiga, dlaɓa tagǝvtǝrtag nǝ ǝlbǝg marawa kǝ talagaha.
MAT 11:6 Dǝ bark nǝ daddakwa tǝrɗa bi tǝ ɗuul mbakyarvad kai biya.”
MAT 11:7 Ar tǝghǝrdǝga ciya dagal nǝ mbǝrzaha Yuhwana, kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ Yesu kǝ taa ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ Yuhwan vak dlamakǝlaawa, “Au wamaa dagal nǝ uuram da vazǝgaan ma tǝghali? Amaa da vaza kazhakwahaanǝn tlaɗtlaɗǝn kwa gajag nǝ fǝɗ na?
MAT 11:8 Au kaci wa damal nǝ uuram da vazǝgaani? Daddakwa caɗva ma sǝɗav marawna? Udahi ndzǝga ma vǝgya tlǝkǝsa iitǝr wa nguɗa sǝɗavah marawa.
MAT 11:9 Au kaci wa damal nǝ uuram da vazǝgaani? Tlayannga? Ən tagkurtaga, juujig vavvaan kǝ tlayannga.
MAT 11:10 Kwan wa vindava nǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr taakiya, “ ‘Ən da ɓǝlgaan kǝ zǝrɓǝlgar tǝvuukwagha, kwada ɓadlak ɗuul lakuti agha da saaya.’
MAT 11:11 “Ən tagkurtag kǝ jiira, ma huɗa uudah kwa yaa nǝ ǝnghwasaha, maay wa juujig kǝ Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝg dǝ ɗyakǝr biya. Bakǝva kwaha, daddakwa ǝngykwah ma tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl juujig kǝ iin dǝ ɗyakǝra.
MAT 11:12 Cigǝt ma zamana Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝga damma kwanǝn kǝ zamana, tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl hǝɓa ba dlaɗ ma dǝva kǝlaadaha, lii vǝlgar dlaɗɗiina, iitǝr wanaa pǝrɗa tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl bad ndzǝɗa.
MAT 11:13 Aɗaba adzahadzaha Muusa ard kakaɗa tlayanngaha baɗǝm tagardatag kǝ tlayanngǝr tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl lakuti saay nǝ Yuhwana.
MAT 11:14 Dlaɓa akwamam haiyamanthaig dǝ kwanǝna, Ili wa ndza tagavda nǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr taakiya da saayna, iin nǝ Yuhwana.
MAT 11:15 Dadda kwad hyǝmmiya, aa cinnga.
MAT 11:16 “Ən da gǝrǝg dau nai kǝ kwanǝn kǝ zamani? Ar band zarhah cihurgan tǝ ɓala kasukwa ar ɗaa ghǝrahaatǝr ar taakiya,
MAT 11:17 “ ‘Kǝm fǝrtǝkura kǝ faakila, lamwalǝg kǝ shakalga, kǝm ɓǝlkura kǝ ǝngsa taa dzǝgwagha, lamwalǝg kǝ tuuga.’
MAT 11:18 “Sahi ba nǝ Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝga maay zǝgaana maay hǝɓǝgaan biya, aiyam nǝ uurama, ‘Shatanah wa ma vǝghaana.’
MAT 11:19 Sahi ba nǝ Zǝra Uuda zǝgaana hǝɓǝgaana, ar taakiya, ‘Wayam dadda tlǝhuɗa ard dadda hǝɓa kya, tsaghwa lii cauwa hadama ard yaadadda haipaha.’ Bakǝvakwaha nǝghvaakanǝghǝg nǝ dabariya Daadamazhigǝl tǝdvad tlǝrahaana.”
MAT 11:20 Kaa cagtǝraacag nǝ Yesu kǝ gyi kǝ kǝsahi kwa ɓagaa nǝ iin kǝ dǝgaha jappǝr baɗyaka, aɗaba pǝlar bi kǝ ghǝr biya.
MAT 11:21 “Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ sǝkǝgh Korazin! Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ sǝkǝgh Betsaida! Akwama ɓagava ma Taya ard Sidun nǝ dǝgaha jappǝrahaanǝn ɓagavǝna vakaruwǝna, ma pǝlara bawur kǝ ghǝra. Maa tsǝgwarǝvtsǝgw kǝ akacakaca ar kutǝr kǝ aftsa.
MAT 11:22 Aici wan tagkurtaga, daghuvala ta shariya da zhutǝrdaala kǝ Taya ard Sidun nǝ Daadamazhigǝla tǝghǝr kǝ sǝkurama.
MAT 11:23 Kǝgh Kafarnahuma! Magha tlǝg nǝng da fǝkaarafǝg nǝ uud damma ghǝrazhigǝla? Maaya! Da fǝkaara bi nǝ uud biya, agha dii ba kǝ kaara faya, akwama ɓagava ma Sadum nǝ tlǝra jappǝrahaan ɓagav ma kǝsaharuwǝna, maa ba ndzǝgaan gwastaana.
MAT 11:24 Aiciya wan tagkurtaga, daghuvala ta shariya, da zhuvardaala kǝ Sadum tǝghǝr kǝskǝgha.”
MAT 11:25 Ma sarta kwaha wa tagaa nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ən tagak uus Daada, Yaazhigǝla ghǝrazhigǝl ard duniya, aɗaba shiɓǝghtǝrvashiɓǝg kǝ dǝgitahaanǝn kǝ lii dǝ dabariya ard lii sǝrgasǝrga, kaa martǝrdamarǝg kǝskǝghǝg kǝ zǝr zarhaha.
MAT 11:26 Bandkwah, Daada, aɗaba kwan nǝ dǝgiti ɓagakaɓag kǝ marawa.
MAT 11:27 “Badǝm nǝ dǝgitaha, vǝlghwavǝlǝg nǝ Daadara. Maay wa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ Zǝriin biya bamma Daada. Dlaɓa maay wa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ Daadiin biya, bamma Zǝriina ard kwa haigant Zǝriin marardana.
MAT 11:28 “Asamasǝg sa vakara, baɗǝmaru lii kuɗaralkuɗǝga ard lii sǝpa kadlannga, ǝn kǝskuraran am tlǝkkǝna kǝ diyakuɗǝga.
MAT 11:29 Cinngamcinng kǝ dǝgiti ǝn tagkur naiya, bandkwa bǝlvar nǝ zuuki ma kungy kǝ kawa uusǝga, am tsagaan dlaɓa vakara. Aɗaba kaiya ǝn kalaliya ǝn maay naaghǝr biya, dlaɓa am tlǝknatlǝg kǝ gabǝr ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaharuwa.
MAT 11:30 Aɗɗaba zuukiyara ba tsaftsafa, kadlanngahara maay ɗǝmɗǝm biya.”
MAT 12:1 Daghuvala faciya ngiiga Yahudaha, ghudadagal nǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan ma guha hǝiya, ngal fǝgharzafǝg nǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ kala ghǝra hǝiya ar zǝggaana aɗaba njǝtǝr waiya.
MAT 12:2 Nǝghara ba nǝ Farisiyah ǝndkwaha, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ Yesu, “Zharga, mbǝrzahagh ar ɓa dǝgiti dzah kǝ ɓagaan daghuvala ngiiga.”
MAT 12:3 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Mbats karantamabi kǝ dǝgiti ɓagaa nǝ Dauda ard lii ǝmtaɗ dǝ iin ma sartakwa ndza njitǝr nǝ waiy biya?
MAT 12:4 Kaa daas kǝ iin damma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla kǝsant kǝ iin kǝ bǝruudi kwa favtǝra ba kǝrkangyǝkwa kǝ zhiila kǝsa uufah zuwa, vǝltǝr baz lii ǝmtaɗ dǝ iin kwa dzah zǝgaan kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 12:5 Nii karantamabi ha ma Adzahadzaha Muus kwa kǝlarda nǝ zhiila kǝssufah kǝ adzahadzaha ngiig ma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, mbats nal bi kǝ haip kǝ iitǝr biya?
MAT 12:6 Ən tagkurtaga, wan nǝ daddakwa juujig kǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl vaakwana.
MAT 12:7 Akwamamaa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ ǝlbǝgahaan kwa taakiya, ‘Zhuwadaal wan naag naiya, kyuulǝg biya, mamaa maay ghaza daddakwa maay dǝ haip biya.’
MAT 12:8 Aɗaba Zǝra Uuda iin yaazhigǝla faciya ngiiga.”
MAT 12:9 Kaa ɗugarsɗuug kǝ Yesu kǝ vakavakintsa, ngal daas kǝ iin damma guda dzǝgwazhigǝlatǝra.
MAT 12:10 Ndza mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin ǝmtsamǝmtsan nǝ dǝv vakwahiina, kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu, taakiya, “Haighanthaig nǝ adzahadzah mbǝvna nǝ uuda daghuvala Faciya Ngiiga?” Ndavararu kwakyarvad ar tlǝkǝna kǝ iin dǝ haipa.
MAT 12:11 Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Akwama mǝng nǝ daddakwa dǝ tuugh pal makurama, ma dahi damma afǝkka daghuvala Faciya Ngiiga, mbats maay kǝsgaan nǝ dadda tuughǝn sagat biya?
MAT 12:12 Abi ndanng ba nǝ uud tǝghǝr kǝ tuugha. Mbakyarvad kwaha kalkalan ɓagvǝna nǝ harǝr daghuvala Faciya Ngiiga.”
MAT 12:13 Aiyama taa kǝ uudanena, “Vǝlǝg kǝ dǝvaagha.” Kaa vǝlgaan kǝ iin kǝ dǝvaana, ngal mbǝg kǝ dǝvaan bandkwa pallna.
MAT 12:14 Kaa dagal kǝ Farisah da diya sawariya ma taatakatǝra tǝghǝr kǝ ɗuuli ar da tsǝg nǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu.
MAT 12:15 Nǝghǝghaaka ba nǝ Yesu ǝndkwaha, ngal ɗuugarsɗuug kǝ iin kǝ vakavakiina, kaa gatǝgaan kǝ uudah badyaka, mbahtǝra kǝ lii yanng bi baɗǝmma.
MAT 12:16 Ɓǝltǝra kǝ magi taakiya, aa tagarar bi aanji ǝndwar biya.
MAT 12:17 Tǝdvad kwan wa righavant nǝ dǝgiti tagada nǝ tlayang Ishaya taakiya,
MAT 12:18 “Wan kwatnahar kwa kǝsanaaka naiya, ǝn waigaana, ǝn cinngaan kǝ ǝmtakǝraan ba vaivaya. Ən da righǝgaan dǝ shǝɗkwara, iin wada tagtǝr ǝlbǝga shariya jiir kǝ uudaha.
MAT 12:19 Da maay ɓala agajaw bi taa ǝlbǝg dǝ caagyi biya, da cinngvabi nǝ ghaiyaan tǝ ɗuul biya.
MAT 12:20 Da maay kǝla ghuvi hǝrzh kǝ kǝlǝg biya, da maay ǝmtsa kaara jahurambi kwa hǝrz kǝ ǝmtsǝg biya, bamma da fǝgharaafǝg kǝ jira zuu kǝ fiira.
MAT 12:21 Fantara uuda dǝgshiga ba tǝ ɗaagaana.”
MAT 12:22 Kaa sǝdǝvsǝg nǝ uudah kǝ makwai kwa mamghant nǝ shatanaha dlaɓa gulfa da vak Yesu, ngal mbǝnan kǝ iin kǝ uuda nǝ iina, farhza kǝ taaghai kaa nǝghǝganǝgha.
MAT 12:23 Kaa ɓa japǝr kǝ dlamaa kǝlaaw baɗǝmma, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Aitsa Zǝra Dauda bi wan kwanya?”
MAT 12:24 Cinngara ba nǝ Farisiyah ǝndkwaha, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Abi lagw dǝ ndzǝɗa Baˈalzabul tlǝkǝsa shatanaha nǝ uudanǝn kǝ shatanaha.”
MAT 12:25 Nǝghaakanǝghǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ dzama ghǝraatǝra, aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Baɗǝm nǝ tlǝksǝri tagwazhatagw hutsǝg buwa ar ɓa tlǝghum dǝ ghǝrahaatǝra, kwanǝn kǝ tlǝksǝr da zǝlma biya, bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ kǝsa bi hǝnnyah ma tagwazhatagw hutsǝg buwa, ar ɓa tlǝghum dǝ ghǝrahaatǝra da badzǝga.
MAT 12:26 Akwama lagwan nǝ shatanah kǝ shatanaha, ɓa uushav dǝ ghǝraana, da ɓag ndar kaci nǝ tlǝksǝraan kǝ ndzǝɗi?
MAT 12:27 Akwaman lagw dǝ ndzǝɗa Baˈalzabul nai kǝ shatanaha, mbǝrzaharuwum? Ar lagw dǝ ndzaɗa wari? Mbǝrzaharuwa wa da tǝkur shari tǝghǝr kwanǝnna.
MAT 12:28 Akwaman lagw dǝ ndzǝɗa Shiɗkwa Daadamazhigǝla nai kǝ shatanaha, mbats tlǝksǝra Daadamazhigǝla sǝghawiisǝg da tǝghǝr kǝskurama.
MAT 12:29 “Maay wa dǝgaadǝg da vǝgya dadda ndzǝɗ hutsavarvan nǝ almanan biya, ba zǝnngwa bamma takwasavant nǝ dadda ndzǝɗǝna, lakuti hutsǝvarvahutsǝg nǝ almanana.
MAT 12:30 “Daddakwa maay ǝmtaɗ dǝ kai biya, tlǝghumar nǝ iina, dlaɓ daddakwa mǝlghwad bi kǝ dzahgaan biya, kwazǝg bad kwazǝga.
MAT 12:31 Mbakyarvad kwaha, ǝn tagkurtaga, da ɓǝshivtǝrnaɓǝshig kǝ uudah aanji hulfa kwar kǝ haip ard badza ɗaaga kwa ɓagara nǝ iitǝra, aiciya, daddakwa badza ɗaaga Shiɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl da ɓǝshvarna biya.
MAT 12:32 Akwama tagadatag nǝ uudan kǝ ǝlbǝga nennig tǝ Zǝra Uuda da ɓǝshvarnaɓshiga, aiciya, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa nǝnna Shiɗkwa Daadamazhigǝla da ɓǝshvarna bi ba dǝm biya.
MAT 12:33 “Uuf marawa yaa zǝr marawa, uufi ghwaɗa yaa ba zǝr ghwaɗa, ma kwar kǝ uufa nǝghvaakanǝghǝg tǝdvad zarhaana.
MAT 12:34 Kuram faɗǝga ghavalahaan kǝlaadahna, am da tag ndar nǝ uuram kǝ dǝgitah maraw kuram ndakwani am kǝladahi? Abi, dǝgiti ma ǝrviɗmahuɗ wa tag nǝ ghaiya.
MAT 12:35 Uuda jiira ba jiir wa sagal ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaana, uudi kǝlaada ba kǝlaadǝr wa sagal ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaana.
MAT 12:36 “Ən takurtaga, baɗǝm nǝ ǝlbǝgah ghwaɗ kwa tagarda nǝ uudaha, ar da tagaan daghuvala ta shariya.
MAT 12:37 Aɗaba tǝdvad ǝlbǝgahagh wada tak nǝ uud kǝ shariya, bi da maay nǝ uud ghazakghazǝg biya, bi da ghazǝka nǝ uuda.”
MAT 12:38 Am kyalǝma lii tsaga adzahadzah ard Farisiyah taa kǝ Yesu, “Dadda tsaga dǝgita, makǝmaa naagaan magha markǝmndadan kǝ dǝga sǝrga.”
MAT 12:39 Ngwatǝrangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Uudaha zamana ar kǝlaadaha, dlaɓa ar za lanngiya Daadamazhigǝla. Ar gata maa marǝvtǝrda nǝ dǝga sǝrga, maay watlǝrǝn kǝ dǝga sǝrgi da marǝvtǝrmarǝg biya, bamma dǝga tlayang Yunana.
MAT 12:40 Bandkwa ɓagaa nǝ Yunan kǝ hǝng hǝkǝrɗ baz avǝɗ baz faci ma huɗa kilfa. Da bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ Zǝra Uud da ɓa hǝng hǝkǝrɗ baz avǝɗ baz faci ma kusǝgha haaya.
MAT 12:41 Daghuvala ta shariya, uudaha Neneva ar da ciig ǝmtaɗ dǝ uudaha zamana, ar martǝrda kǝ uudaha zamanǝn taakiya ar ghazaghazana, aɗaba pǝlara mbakyarvad ǝlɓǝg marawǝn tagada nǝ Yunan nǝ iitǝr kǝ ghǝra. Wan ci, nǝ daddakwa juujig kǝ Yunan vaakwana.
MAT 12:42 Daghuvala ta shariya, da ciig nǝ tlǝkǝssa Sheba uusa ǝmtaɗ dǝ uudaha zamanǝna. Martǝrdan taakiya ghazaraghazǝga, aɗaba ghǝravaana sal vaka bǝtky sa cinnga dabariya Salumana. Wan ci, daddakwa juujig kǝ Salumana vaakwana.”
MAT 12:43 “Akwama salsǝg nǝ Shatanah ma vǝgha uuda, kaa gwaiyav kǝ iin gata vakavaka ɗiyakudǝg tlakǝna biya, aɗaba maay nǝ yu vakavaka kwahiin biya.
MAT 12:44 Ngal ba tagan taakiya, ‘Ən guya daas da vakavaki sanal naiya.’ Akwama guyaagwig daasa, tlǝgharaatlǝg kǝ hǝnyahǝn maay aanji ǝndwar biya, dlaɓa hyaɗahyɗana ɓadlaɓadlana.
MAT 12:45 Kaa dagal kǝ iin dzǝgdaan kǝ kwatlǝrǝn kǝ shatanah uuɗiffa kwa jaruujig kǝ iin dǝ kǝlaadǝra, kaa daas kǝ iitǝr ar ndzan vaakwaha. Tǝhalakwaha ndzǝgana uudanǝna, da jǝguujig kǝ ndzǝganaanǝn ndza wurǝn kǝ badzǝga. Da bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ uudaha zamanǝn dǝ kǝlaadǝra.”
MAT 12:46 Tǝghǝrdǝga tagtǝr ǝlbǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ uudaha, kaa sagau kǝ babbaana ard zarha babbaan ar ghacan gyimala, ar naa taaghai dǝ iina.
MAT 12:47 Am nǝ uuda nǝ iin taa kǝ Yesu, “Wai baabagha ard dǝ zarhabaabagh ar ghacga gyimala, ar naa taaghai dǝ kǝgha.”
MAT 12:48 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ uudanǝnna, “War nǝ baabara ard zarha baabarni?”
MAT 12:49 Kaa maraa mbǝrzahaan kǝ iin dǝ dǝva aiyama, “Wan nǝ baaba ra ard zaraabahar vaakwana.
MAT 12:50 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa ɓa dǝgiti naag nǝ daadar kwa ma ghǝrazhigǝla, iin zǝraabara, ard dǝghwa baabara ard baabara.”
MAT 13:1 Ba daghuvala kwahiin kǝ faciya, kaa sǝgalsǝg nǝ Yesu hǝnyahiina, ngal dagal kǝ iin cǝhuran tǝ ghaiya yuwa haiya.
MAT 13:2 Kaa faɗav kǝ uudah baɗyak sa tǝghǝr kǝ iina, mbakyarvad kwaha kaa daas kǝ iin damma pɛra yuwa cǝhurana. Kaa ghacgaghacǝg kǝ uudah tǝ ghaiya gardza.
MAT 13:3 Kaa tagtǝrtag kǝ iin kǝ dǝgitah baɗyak dǝ garava, amaa, “Mǝng dadda riig kwa dal da riiga.
MAT 13:4 Riig nǝ iina, kaa ɓalgalɓalǝg kǝ kyalǝma hulf dat ɗuula, kaa caguucag kǝ ɗiikaha.
MAT 13:5 Kyalǝm ɓalal dat caccahǝlaw vakavaki maay nǝ haay ɗyak biya, kaa laghǝr ba watswatsa aɗaba maay nǝ haay ɗyak biya.
MAT 13:6 Ghwut ba nǝ faciya, ngal fuug kǝ iitǝra, aɗaba baharabi kǝ tlali vaivai biya, kaa ghulǝg kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 13:7 Kyalǝm ɓalal damma takka, kaa ghwubararaa nǝ takka, tsarva kǝ ɓǝlauwa.
MAT 13:8 Kyalm ɓalal dat haay marawa, kaa ya zǝr dǝrmǝkka, kyalǝm kul ǝngkwaha, kyalǝm dlaɓ kul hǝkǝrɗa.
MAT 13:9 Dadda kwad hyǝmiya cinngaana aa cinnga.”
MAT 13:10 Kaa dagau kǝ mbǝrzah davakaan ar ndavaru taakiya, “Aujibǝg agha tagtǝr bad garav kǝ ǝlbǝg kǝ uudahi?”
MAT 13:11 Kaa ngutǝraangug kǝ Yesu, amaa, “Haiyakuranthaig nǝ uud am sǝra kǝ dǝgiti shǝɓashǝɓan ma tlǝkǝsǝra Daadamazhigǝla, kiyava iitǝra vǝlavtǝr biya.
MAT 13:12 Aɗaba baɗǝm dadda kwad dǝgita, da fǝvarnaafǝga baɗyaka, dlaɓa da jǝguujig tǝ iin ba vaivaiya, dadda kwa maay dǝ vakai biya, da kǝsvarǝvkǝssǝg aanji ba hǝɗikǝni dǝ vakai nǝ iina.
MAT 13:13 In wan tagtǝr nai kǝ ǝlbǝg dǝ garavna, “ ‘Aanji ar vazǝgaana ar nǝghǝga biya, aanji ar cinngaana, ar cinnga biya dlaɓa ar nǝghǝgaaka biya.’
MAT 13:14 “Righǝtrighǝg nǝ tlayangngǝra Ishaya tǝghǝr kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “ ‘Am da cinngaana am da cinngaaka biya, am da vazǝgaana, ba dǝm am da nǝghǝgaaka biya.
MAT 13:15 Aɗaba uudahaan ba dǝkdǝk nǝ ǝrvidmahuɗaatǝra, ar cinnga ba dlah dǝ hyǝmiyahaatǝra, dlaɓa ar hǝɗardu kǝ gyiyahaatǝra. Maa maay ǝndkwah biya, maraa nǝghǝganǝg dǝ gyiyahaatǝra, maraa cinngacinng dǝ hyǝmiyahaatǝra dlaɓa maa nǝgharaakanǝghǝg ma ǝrvidmahuɗaatǝra ar pǝla kǝ ghǝra ǝn mbǝtǝrnana.’
MAT 13:16 “Bark nǝ gyiyaharuwa aɗaba ar nǝghǝganǝghǝga, dlaba hyimmǝyaharu ar cinngacinnga.
MAT 13:17 Bak jiira ǝn tagkurtaga, tlayangaha ard uudaha jirjira ba ɗyaka, naharnahǝg kǝ vazza dǝgiti nǝghama nǝ uurama, nǝghara biya, ard dǝgiti cinngama nǝ uurama, cinngara biya.
MAT 13:18 “Wan nǝ dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ garava dadda riigna.
MAT 13:19 Badǝm dadda kwa cinnghacinng kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksǝra, dlaɓa nǝghaaka biya. Kaa sagau kǝ shatanaha ghǝldan kǝ ǝlbǝgǝn sagal ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaana, kwanǝn kǝ hulfa iin wa ɓalal dat ɗuula.
MAT 13:20 Hulfǝn ɓalal dat caccahǝlawna, iin garava uudahanǝn cinngaracinng kǝ ǝlbǝgna, dlaɓa dlǝgharadlǝghǝg bad hwaɗǝga.
MAT 13:21 Aɗaba baabi kǝ tlali biya, fadghǝraan ba dǝga sart hǝɗiikǝna, sǝghǝv ba dlaɗ kwakyarvad ǝlbǝgiina, kaa tagwzhatagw kǝ iin dǝ fadghǝrana.
MAT 13:22 Hulfǝn kwa ɓalal damma takkǝna, iin garava uudi cinnghacinnga kǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝla, dzama kadlannga duniya ard hyahǝra, tsǝgharvatsǝg kǝ ɓǝlauwa yaa bi kǝ zǝr biya.
MAT 13:23 Hulfǝn riyava tǝ haay marwna iin garava dadda kwa cinnghacinnga kǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝla dlaɓa nǝghǝghaakanǝghǝga, ngal yaa kǝ zǝra, kwana dǝrmǝkka, kwana kul unkwaha, kwana kul hǝkǝrɗa.”
MAT 13:24 Vǝlatǝrvǝlǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ kwatlǝrn ke garava, amaa, “Da gǝrav nǝ tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl dǝ uudi riiya hulf maraw ma guhaana.
MAT 13:25 Ma sartǝn hǝnna haar nǝ uudah baɗǝmma, kaa dagal kǝ dadda tlǝghuman riiyars kǝ dlǝgh miizhangyil hǝiyina, ngal dasaana.
MAT 13:26 Ghubara ba nǝ hǝiya yaak kǝ zǝra, dlǝgh ndakwani ghubaraghubarga.
MAT 13:27 “Kaa sagau kǝ kwatnahahaan ar tagar kǝ dadda hǝnyahaatǝr taakiya, ‘Dadda hǝnyaha, mbats hulf maraw bi wa riigha nǝng ma guhaghǝn biya? Aa sǝga ndar ka ci nǝ dlǝghi?’
MAT 13:28 “Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, ‘Dadda tlǝghum wa ɓagaa kwaha.’ “Aiyam nǝ kwatnahaan taa kǝ iin, ‘Agha naagaan kǝm taɗdan kǝ dlǝghahaana?’
MAT 13:29 “Amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, ‘Taɗam biya, aa nali vaka taɗa dlǝgh kǝskuram am taɗdan baz hǝi biya.
MAT 13:30 Aɗuwamtǝrɗuug aa ghubararghubarg ba ǝmtaɗ tangw damma sarta ghuda hǝiya, ma kwah kǝ sarta ǝn da tagtǝrtag nai kǝ lii ghuda hǝiya ar da farzha aghwa dlǝgha ar ngwaɗant aɗagwal aɗagwala hǝvars kaara, dzahvant nǝ hǝiya ɗiivǝdǝm damma kuvǝra.’ ”
MAT 13:31 Vǝlatǝrvǝlǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ kwatlǝrn kǝ garava, amaa, “Tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla band hulfa zǝra mastad kwa riiya nǝ uudan ma guhaana.
MAT 13:32 Iin wa mishish ma hulfah badǝmma, akwama ghubaraghubarga, juguujig kǝ dǝgitahi riiva ma ɗyaghar baɗǝmma kaa nǝg kǝ uufa, kaa ɓa vǝgyahaatǝr kǝ ɗiikah tǝ dǝvahaana.”
MAT 13:33 Gwiya vǝlatǝrvǝlǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ kwatlǝrn kǝ garava amaa, “Tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla band yista kwa kǝɗghant nǝ uusiin dǝ taasa ahupi hǝkǝrɗa, kaa uushigǝtuushig kǝ ahupiyin baɗǝm dǝ yistina.”
MAT 13:34 Tagatǝrtag nǝ Yesu kǝ dzahava uudah baɗǝm kǝ dǝgitah dǝ garava. Maay nǝ dǝgiti tagatǝr nǝ iin kwal garav biya.
MAT 13:35 Tǝdvad kwan wa rǝghvant nǝ dǝgiti tagada nǝ tlayang Ishaya taakiya, “Ən da tagaan kǝ ǝlbǝg dǝ garavaha, dǝgiti ndza shǝɓashǝɓan gwil fǝgarzha duni, ǝn da tagaana.”
MAT 13:36 Kaa ɗutǝrǝsɗuug nǝ Yesu kǝ dzahava uudaha, kaa daas kǝ iin da hǝnyaha. Ngal tlǝgaraatlǝg kǝ mbǝrzahaana, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Tagkǝmndtag kǝ dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ garava dlǝgh ma guhna.”
MAT 13:37 Kaa ngutǝrangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Dadda kwa riiya hulf marawa, iin Zǝra Uuda.
MAT 13:38 Guhna iin nǝ duniya, hulf marawna, iin zarha tlǝksǝra Daadamazhigǝla. Dlǝghna iitǝr zarha shatanah.
MAT 13:39 Dadda tlǝghumǝn riiya dlǝghna, iin shatanaha. Sarta ghwuda hǝina, iin ghyǝnnga duniya, lii ghuda hǝiya iitǝr nǝ zarhaɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 13:40 “Bandkwa dzahav nǝ dlǝgh hǝvars nǝ kaara, da band kwah daghuvala ghyǝnnga duniya.
MAT 13:41 Da ɓǝlgaan Zǝra Uud kǝ zarhaɓǝlgaana, ar da dzahaant baɗǝm kǝ dǝgitahi fǝgara uudah kǝ ɓa haipa, baz lii ɓa tlǝra kǝlaɗǝr baɗǝmma, ar da lagwtǝrda dagal ma tlǝksǝraana.
MAT 13:42 Ar da ɗiitǝrdǝm damma kaara faaya, vakwaha ar da tuuga ar da ghwada dǝv dǝ tlǝrɗa.
MAT 13:43 Tǝhalakwaha ar da mbiig band faciya nǝ uudaha jiirjiira ma tlǝksǝra daddaatǝra. Dadda kwa dǝ hyǝmiya cinngaana aa cinnga.
MAT 13:44 “Tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla band almani kwa shiɓavǝna ma guuha, kwa tlǝkǝna nǝ uudana ngal gwiya shiɓnanna, mbakyarvad ɗyakǝra hwaɗaga kaa valǝt kǝ dǝgahaani dǝvakai nǝ iin baɗǝmma, ngal sǝgwa kǝ guuhiina.
MAT 13:45 “Gwastǝna, tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla band zǝra kasǝkwa, kwa gata akura ndannga.
MAT 13:46 Tlǝkǝna ba nǝ iin kǝ akurǝn ndanng pal ba vaivaina, ngal valǝt kǝ dǝgahaan baɗǝm sǝgwa kǝ iina.
MAT 13:47 “Gwastǝna dlaɓa, tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla band amshiya vaiya kilfa kwa ɓǝlavdǝm damma yuwahaiya, vaiyitvaig kilfah shahshaha.
MAT 13:48 Righǝt ba nǝ iina, ngal tǝɗdatǝɗǝg kǝ yaa dadda vaiya kilf dat ghaiya gardza, ar dzǝraakan kǝ kilfahi marawa, ar ɗiivǝdǝm damma alghwa ɗiivǝdan nǝ wa maraw biya.
MAT 13:49 Da band kwah daghuvala ghyǝnnga duniya, ar da sagau nǝ zarhaɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝla, ar da tagwtǝrzha kǝ kǝlaadah sagal ma uudaha jiirjiira.
MAT 13:50 Ar da ɗiitǝrdǝm kǝ kǝlaadah damma kaara faiya, vakavaki ar da tuug nǝ iitǝra ar ghwada dǝv dǝ tlǝrɗa.”
MAT 13:51 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Nǝghamaakanǝghǝg kǝ kwanahaan baɗǝmma?” Kaa ngug kǝ iitǝra takiya, “Aana.”
MAT 13:52 Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Mbakyarvad kwaha baɗǝm dadda tsaga adzahadzaha kwa nalnǝg kǝ mbǝrz ma tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla, band dadda hǝnyaha kwa sadda daala almana ard ǝnghura alman vaka fǝgaana.”
MAT 13:53 Ghyǝnng ba nǝ Yesu tagtǝr dǝgitah dǝ garava, kaa dagalaan kǝ iina.
MAT 13:54 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu damma kǝssana, kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ iin tsagtǝr dǝgit kǝ uudah ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝlaatǝra, kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ iitǝra, ar taakiya, “Aa tlǝkǝna mǝr nǝ uudanǝn kǝ hulfa kwan kǝ dabari ard dǝ ndzǝɗa ɓa tlǝraha jappǝrni?
MAT 13:55 Zǝra kafintini wan kwan biya? Babbaani wa ɗahav dǝ Maryam biya? Zarhaababani nǝ Yakuba, Isuvu, Siman ard Yahud biya?
MAT 13:56 Dughwaha babbaan bi wa ǝmtaɗ dǝ kǝmyamǝn biya? Tlakǝnamǝr kaci nǝ iin kǝ kwanahaan baɗǝmmi?”
MAT 13:57 Kaa badzǝg kǝ ǝrvidmahuɗatǝra. Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Bamma kǝsaana ard hǝnyhaan wa maay nǝ tlayanng dǝ ndanng biya.”
MAT 13:58 Ɓagaa bi nǝ iin kǝ dǝgaha jappǝr ɗyak vakwah biya, adaba ar maay dǝ fadghǝr biya.
MAT 14:1 Ma sarta kwah wa cinngha nǝ Tlǝkǝs Hirudus kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu.
MAT 14:2 Amaa taa kǝ kwatnahahaana, “Kwan kǝ uuda, Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝg waa ciigǝt ma gǝtlaha, iin waa tlǝkǝna nǝ iin kǝ ndzǝɗa ɓa dǝgaha jappǝrahaana.”
MAT 14:3 Aɗaba ndza viyǝtviig nǝ Hirudus kǝ Yuhwana, takwasanta, ɓǝldǝm damma guda bǝrfin kwakyarvad Hirudiya, uusa zǝra babbaan Filigusa.
MAT 14:4 Aɗaba ndza tagartag nǝ Yuhwan kǝ Hirudus taakiya, kalkalaan bi kǝ iin kǝssa Hirudiya biya.
MAT 14:5 Bakǝvakwaha nahanahǝg nǝ Hirudus kǝ tsa Yuhwana, ndza gǝdza gyiya uudaha, aɗaba haiyaranthaig nǝ uudah taakiya tlayanga nǝ iina.
MAT 14:6 Sǝgha ba nǝ sarta ɓa kwaanda Hirudusa, kaa shakalǝg kǝ dughwa Hirudiya tǝ vuukwa ghulabaha, fǝgharaafǝg kǝ Hirudus kǝ cinnga ǝmtaakǝr ba vaivaiya.
MAT 14:7 Tǝgharatǝg kǝ langyiya baz zǝgara gwaɗǝg taakiya, da vǝlǝgarvǝlǝg kǝ dǝgiti ghalǝg nǝ iin baɗǝmma.
MAT 14:8 Ngal diigaradiig nǝ babbaan kǝ sawariya dǝgiti da tag nǝ iina, amaa, “Aa vǝlwavǝlǝg nǝ uud kǝ ghǝra Yuhwan dadda Tsuufǝg bandakwan ma kwatama.”
MAT 14:9 Cinnguu bi nǝ tlǝkǝs kǝ ǝmtakǝra ǝlbǝgiin biya, aɗaba mbakyarvad ngwaɗǝgi zaa nǝ iin tǝvuukwa ghwulabahaana, ngal tagaan kǝ iin taaki aa vǝlvarvǝlǝg nǝ dǝgiti naag nǝ iina.
MAT 14:10 Ɓǝlant kǝ uud damma guda bǝrfina ghudva ghǝr tǝ Yuhwana.
MAT 14:11 Sǝvdaa nǝ ghǝraan ma kwatama, vǝlǝvar kǝ dughwiina, kaa lanngardaa kǝ iin kǝ babbaana.
MAT 14:12 Kaa sagau kǝ mbǝrzaha Yuhwana ar kǝssant kǝ tlǝwa vǝghaan ar hǝɗǝnana, tǝhala kwaha ngal daagal kǝ iitǝr ar tagar kǝ Yesu.
MAT 14:13 Cinngha ba nǝ Yesu ǝndkwaha, kaa daas kǝ iin damma pɛra yuwa, ngal dagal da vakavaki maay aanji ǝndwar biya, ndzan ba daghuvaana. Cinngara ba nǝ uudaha, kaa sagal kǝ iitǝr ma kǝssahaatǝra, ngal dagal kǝ iitǝr gatǝgaana.
MAT 14:14 Sǝghal ba nǝ iin ma pɛra yuwa, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ uudah ba ɗyaka. Ngal zhutǝrdaalazhuuga, dlaɓa mbǝhtǝra kǝ lii yang bi ma iitǝra.
MAT 14:15 Dǝm ba faci kǝ ɓǝladaaya, kaa dagau kǝ mbǝrzahan da vaakana, am nǝ iitǝra, “Kwan kǝ vakavaka maay aanji ndǝwar biya, dlaɓa hǝrz faci kǝ ɓǝladaaya. Ɗutǝrsɗuug kǝ uudaha kiyava dagal kǝ iitǝr damma kǝsah ar gatu kǝ dǝgzǝga.”
MAT 14:16 Aiyama nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Maay nǝ tlǝra dagalaatǝr biya. Vǝlamtǝrvǝlǝg nǝ uuram kǝ dǝgzǝga.”
MAT 14:17 Am nǝ iitǝra taa kǝ iina, “Dǝgiti vakamnd vaakwana, ba bǝruudi dlǝɓa ard kilf bu kaltiya.”
MAT 14:18 Aiyama, “Anakam da vakara.”
MAT 14:19 Ngal tagtǝrtag kǝ iin kǝ uudah aa cahwararacahwarǝg tǝ kazhakwa, kaa kǝsgantkǝsǝg kǝ iin kǝ bǝruudi dlǝɓ ard kilf buwa, dzǝgant kǝ iin kǝ ghǝraan damma ghǝrzhigǝla, tagar kǝ uus kǝ Daadamazhigǝla. Tǝhalakwaha, lahǝna kǝ bǝruudina vǝltǝr kǝ mbǝrzahana ar tagwtǝrna kǝ uudaha.
MAT 14:20 Baɗǝmmaatǝr zaruuzǝga tlatǝrtlǝga, ar dzahaant nǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ ghwadǝgahaani tǝmaatǝmga, righantrighǝg kǝ alghw kǝlaawa tar buwa.
MAT 14:21 Uudahi zaruuzǝga tamaha ghwalvah alfu dlǝɓa, maay ba nǝ zǝrha ard ǝnghwasah biya.
MAT 14:22 Bad ghyǝngaatǝr waha, kaa fǝtǝraafǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ mbǝrzahaan damma pǝra yuwa, kiyava dagal kǝ iitǝr zungw tǝghǝr kǝ iin dat ghyaba kwah kǝ gardza, aɗaba paka salama uudah nǝ iina.
MAT 14:23 Tǝhalakwa salamada nǝ iin kǝ uudaha, ngal dagat kǝ iin da dzǝgwazhigǝla ma aghw ba daghuvaana, ɓǝlgharaaɓǝlǝg baz avǝɗ vaakwah ba daghuvaana.
MAT 14:24 Ma kwahiina sarta ndza ma taataka yuwahaiya nǝ pɛrayuwa, kaa tsǝgaan kǝ fǝɗ kǝ ghubǝɗǝga yu dat pɛrayuwa, aɗaba ndza ba gyar nǝ fǝɗ dǝ pɛrayuwa.
MAT 14:25 Tamaha karfe hǝkǝrɗa avǝɗa, kaa happa dagal kǝ Yesu tǝghǝra yuwa da vak mbǝrzahaana.
MAT 14:26 Nǝghara ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ iin happa dagal dǝ shig tǝghǝra yuwa, kaa gǝdzǝg kǝ iitǝra. Ar hulǝg mbakyarvad dladlawa ar taakiya, “Dadda kwa sǝgal tǝ afka.”
MAT 14:27 Bat watsǝra, kaa tagtǝrtag kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ndavam biya, ba kaiya, gǝdzam biya.”
MAT 14:28 Kaa ngug kǝ Bitrus amaa, “Yaazhigǝla, akwama ba kǝgha, ɗaakwaɗaag sa vakaagh tǝghǝra yuwa.”
MAT 14:29 Aiyam nǝ Yesu, “Asǝga.” Kaa sagal kǝ Bitrusa ma pɛrayuwa, farzha kǝ dagal tǝghǝra yuwa da vak Yesu.
MAT 14:30 Nǝghǝgha ba nǝ iin kǝ fǝɗ ciyǝtciig bad ndzǝɗa, kaa gǝdzǝg kǝ iina aɗaba fǝgharzhafǝg nǝ yu kǝ ndǝgaana. Kaa huulǝg kǝ iin amaa, “Katkwakatǝg, Yaazhigǝla.”
MAT 14:31 Bat watsǝra kaa vǝlǝgaan kǝ Yesu kǝ dǝvaan viyita, aiyama “Kǝgh dadda hǝtsahǝtsan nǝ fadghǝrna, aujilbǝg agha ɓa ndawndawi?”
MAT 14:32 Daragha ba nǝ iitǝra damma pɛrayuwa, kaa kyaɓalgakyaɓalǝg kǝ fǝdna.
MAT 14:33 Kaa ɓagarnǝsɓag nǝ lii ma pɛrayuwǝn kǝ kwatnahǝr kǝ Yesu, ar taakiya, “Bak jiijiira agha Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla.”
MAT 14:34 Dzǝvara ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ yuwa haiya, ar tsugwa ma Janisarat.
MAT 14:35 Nǝgharaaka ba nǝ uudaha kǝsiin kǝ Yesu, kaa bǝla ghai kǝ iitǝr damma kǝsahi tǝghǝr kǝ iitǝr baɗǝmma, ar sardǝv kǝ lii yang bi badǝmma.
MAT 14:36 Kaa ghalgaan kǝ iitǝr maa ɗuutǝrnaa kǝ lii yang bi maraa tapnan aanji ghaaya sǝɗavaana, baɗǝm lii taparnatapǝga mbaharambahǝga.
MAT 15:1 Tǝhalakwaha kaa sagau kǝ kyalǝma Farisiyaha ard lii tsaga adzahadzah sagal ma Wurshalim da vak Yesu am nǝ iitǝra,
MAT 15:2 “Aujilbǝg kǝ mbǝrzahagh ar kǝlla dǝga daadijaha tlǝvuukwahi? Aɗaba ar maay bara dǝv lakwti ar da zaa kaf biya.”
MAT 15:3 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kuramǝm, aujilbǝg kǝskuram am kǝlla adzahadzaha Daadamazhigǝl kwakyarvad dǝga daadijahawi?
MAT 15:4 Am nǝ Daadamazhigǝla, ‘Faarafǝg kǝ daadagh ard baabagha,’ dlaɓa ‘Baɗǝm dadda ɗaava daddaana bi babbaana, barari tsavva.’
MAT 15:5 Kuram am tsagtǝrtsag kǝ uudah taakiya, akwama mǝng nǝ uudani dǝ dǝgit kwada mǝlgaru kǝ daddaana bi babbaana, ngal tagaan taakiya, ‘Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgiti mammaa da tlǝkǝna nǝ uuram vakara, fanarafǝg kǝ Daadamazhigǝla.’ Mbakyarvad kwaha fǝghaara bi kǝ daddaan ard babbaan dǝvakai biya.
MAT 15:6 Mbakyarvad dǝgaha daadijaruwa, namdalnǝg nǝ uuram kǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl kǝ dǝga lakǝra.
MAT 15:7 Kuram muuniyahaana! Mbats ba jiir nǝ tlayanngǝrǝn tagada nǝ Ishaiya tǝghǝr kǝskuram taakiya,
MAT 15:8 “‘Udahaana, ar fǝkwara bat vaa ghai kalti, ǝrviɗmahuɗaatǝr bitky dǝ kaiya.
MAT 15:9 Ar ɓaggwa ba gyaan kǝ kwatnahǝra, ar tsaga adzahadzaha uudah tǝghǝr kǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝla.’”
MAT 15:10 Ɗahatǝrǝtɗahǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ dzahava uudah da vakaana, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Cinngamcinnga am nǝghaakana.
MAT 15:11 Dǝgiti daadamma ghaiya kǝ uud bi wa fǝgara kwadlambǝr kǝ uud tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl biya. Bamma dǝgiti sagal ma ghaiyaana.”
MAT 15:12 Kaa sagau kǝ mbǝrzahaan da vak Yesu am nǝ iitǝra, “Agha sǝrgasǝrg taaki aandzaa badzgalbadzǝg nǝ ǝrviɗya Farisiyah sarta kwaraa cinnga nǝ iitǝr kǝ ǝlbǝgna?”
MAT 15:13 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Baɗǝm nǝ riigi kwa riiya nǝ Daadari ma ghǝrazhigǝl biya, da taɗava.
MAT 15:14 Aaɗuwamtǝrɗuuga. Ar gulfah nǝ iitǝra, lii taɗa gulfaha. Akwama gulf wa taɗa gulfa, ba bǝrkuɗaatǝr ar mbǝɗa daay damma afǝka.”
MAT 15:15 Aiyam nǝ Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Tagkǝmndtagg kǝ dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ garavna.”
MAT 15:16 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Mbats gwaastǝn nǝghamaaka biya?
MAT 15:17 Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgiti zǝguu nǝ uuda, ba zǝnngw da bak ghaiyaana, kaa damma huɗaana, tǝhala kwaha kaa sagal ma vǝghaana.
MAT 15:18 Dǝgiti aa sagal ma ghaiya uuda, aa sǝgal bamma ǝrviɗmahuɗaana. Iin wa fǝgara ndzǝgaana kwadlambǝr kǝ uud tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 15:19 Aɗaba sagal bamma ǝrviɗmahuuɗ nǝ dzama dǝgit ghwaɗa, ndǝ tsa sifǝga, ɓa gwaragwara, ɓa gǝlla, shiida fiida, ard badza ɗaaga.
MAT 15:20 Kwanahaan wa fǝgaraa ndzǝgaana kwadlambǝr kǝ uud tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝla, za kaf kwaal bara dǝv bi wa fǝgaraa ndzǝgan kwadlambǝr kǝ uud tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl biya.”
MAT 15:21 Ɗughars ba nǝ Yesu kwahiin kǝ vakavaka, ngal dagal kǝ iin damma larda Taya ard Sidon,
MAT 15:22 Kaa huula saas kǝ uusa yaa Kanˈana, amaa, “Zhukwadalaazhuug, Yaazhigǝla, Zǝra Dauda. Mǝng nǝ dǝghwar kwa vǝlgar nǝ shatanah kǝ dlaɗ ba vaivaiya.”
MAT 15:23 Tagghar bi nǝ Yesu aanji ndau biya, kaa ba sagau kǝ mbǝrzahaa da ghalgaana, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Lagwarslagw kǝ uusna, aɗaba gata kǝmyamma dlaɓa mbakiyammbǝg dǝ huulǝga.”
MAT 15:24 Ngwatǝrangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Ɓǝlakwadi mbakyarvad tughwaha Israˈilǝn zaharazahǝgǝn nǝ uuda, mbakyarvad uudahi tlǝrǝn biya.”
MAT 15:25 Ngal sagau kǝ iin kǝlla kǝ ghunnj tǝvuukwana amaa, “Yaazhigǝla, mǝlwadmǝlga.”
MAT 15:26 Aiyamaa, “Kalkalaan bi kǝ kǝsvant nǝ kaffa zarh ɓǝlǝvtǝrda kǝ ghǝgyah biya.”
MAT 15:27 Amaa, “Aana, bandkwah, Yaazhigǝla, aanji ghǝgyaha ar cagaan kǝ pashpasha kaffi ɓalgal vaka zǝg kǝ dadda hǝnyahaatǝra.”
MAT 15:28 Kaa ngugarangugg kǝ Yesu amaa, “Uusǝna, fadghǝragh ndzǝɗandzǝɗana, tsakatsǝg nǝ uud kǝ puutagha.” Bat watsǝr kaa mbǝgambǝg kǝ dǝghwaana.
MAT 15:29 Ciyit ba vaakwahiin nǝ Yesu kaa ta ghaiya Yuwa haiya Galili. Ngal dagat kǝ iin dat kungula aghwa, cǝhurana.
MAT 15:30 Kaa sagau kǝ uudah baɗyak da vakaan dǝ ghurɗikaha, gulfaha, lii ǝmtsamtsan nǝ uuɓiya, makwayaha, ard uudahi tlǝrǝn baɗyaka, ar ɗiitǝra tǝvuukwana. Ngal mbahtǝrana.
MAT 15:31 Nǝghgha ba nǝ uudah kǝ makwayah ar taa ghaiya, lii ǝmtsamtsan nǝ uuɓiya, uuɓiyatǝr nalnǝg balapiya, ghurɗikah ar dagala, gulfah dlaɓ ar nǝghǝganǝghǝga. Kaa galla Daadamazhigǝla yaa Izraˈila kǝ iitǝr baɗǝmma.
MAT 15:32 Tǝhala kwaha, ngal ɗahtǝrǝtɗahǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ mbǝrzahaan amaa, “Ən ɓa zhuwadaala kwanǝn kǝ uudaha, hǝngah hǝkǝrɗ wan kwana ar ba ǝmtaɗ dǝ kaiya, ba kwal dǝgzǝga. Ən naay kǝ ɗutǝrǝsɗuug daas dǝ wai biya, aɗaba haik ɗiya haar kǝ iitǝr tǝghǝrdǝga.”
MAT 15:33 Am nǝ mbǝrzah taa kǝ iina, “Da tlǝvkǝna mǝr nǝ dǝgzǝgǝn da tlǝtǝraara kǝ uudahaan ma tǝghal vaakwani?”
MAT 15:34 Kaa ndavtǝruundavǝg kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ɗummba bruudi ngwɛn wa vakaruwi?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Uuɗiifa ard mishish kilf hǝɗiikǝna.”
MAT 15:35 Kaa fǝtǝraafǝg kǝ iin kǝ dlamakǝlaaw cahwargan tǝ haaya.
MAT 15:36 Kǝsant kǝ iin kǝ ɗummba bruudi uuɗiifǝn ard kilfna, tagar kǝ iin kǝ uus kǝ Daadamazhigǝla lahnana. Vǝltǝr kǝ iin kǝ mbǝrzahaana, kaa vǝltǝr nǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ uudaha.
MAT 15:37 Baɗǝmaatǝr zaruuzǝga, tlatǝrtlǝga, kaa dzahgantdzahǝg nǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ ghwadgahaan ar rɛghant kǝ alǝghwah uuɗiifa.
MAT 15:38 Uudahi zaruuzǝga, tamaha damma ghwalvah alfu uufaɗa, maay ba nǝ ǝnghwasah ard zarh biya.
MAT 15:39 Salamada ba nǝ iin kǝ uudaha, kaa damma pɛra yuwa, ngal dagal damma haaya Magadan.
MAT 16:1 Sarǝvsǝg nǝ Farisiyaha ard Sadukiyah da vak Yesu kiyava fishǝgaan kǝ iitǝra, kaa ghalgaan kǝ iitǝr ma martǝrdan kǝ dǝga sǝrǝg kwa da mara taakiya, sǝghhi vak Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 16:2 Ngutǝrnaguga, amaa, “Akwama ɓǝlaaɓǝlǝg nǝ hwaasa, ma nǝghǝmanǝghǝg kǝ zhigǝla ba kyanga, am tagaan taakiya da maraw nǝ kǝs dlakaduura.
MAT 16:3 Akwama nǝghamanǝghǝg kǝ zhigǝl ba kyanga dlakaduur wur ciyitciig nǝ ghabaga, am tagaan taakiya, ‘Da hyiyav nǝ yuwa hiinanna.’ Am nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg tsau kǝ ndzǝgana zhigǝla. Ɗǝmakurvaa ndar kaci nǝghǝgaaka ndzǝgan kwanǝn kǝ zamani?
MAT 16:4 Uudaha zamana ar maay dǝ jiir tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl biya, dlaɓa ar kǝladaha. Ar nagan mara nǝgha kǝ dǝga sǝrga, da maay marvǝtǝrmarǝg nǝ watlǝrn kǝ dǝga sǝrǝg biya, bamma dǝga sǝrǝga Yunana.” Kaa ɗuutǝrsɗuug kǝ iin ngal dagalaana.
MAT 16:5 Daral ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan dat ghyaba kwah kǝ gardza yuwa haiya, mbats viyaatǝraviig nǝ kǝsa bruudiya.
MAT 16:6 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Famfǝg kǝ hyǝmiya, dlaɓa am fǝgaan kǝ taaɗ tǝ yista Farisiyah ard Sadukiyaha.”
MAT 16:7 Kaa fagarzhafǝg kǝ iitǝr tagaan ma taatakatǝr taakiya, “Mbakyarvad kǝsyamant bi kǝ bruudi nii?”
MAT 16:8 Nǝghghaaka ba nǝ Yesu ǝndkwana, aiyama, “Kuuram lii hǝtsahǝtsan nǝ fadghǝra, aujilbǝg am taaki am maay dǝ bruudi biyi?
MAT 16:9 Mbats gwastǝn nǝghamaaka biya? Viiyakuraviig nǝ ɗuuli gǝlantǝrǝt nai kǝ uudah alfu dlǝɓ dǝ ɗummba bruudi dlǝɓa? Alghwa ngwɛn wa dzahamant nǝ uurami?
MAT 16:10 Nii ma sarta kwa gǝlantǝrǝt nai kǝ uudah alfu uufaɗ dǝ ɗummba bruudi uudifna, alghw ngwɛn wa dzahamant nǝ uurami?
MAT 16:11 Aujibǝg nǝghǝghaamaka bi taakiya ǝn tag tǝghǝr kǝ bruudi bi nai kǝ ǝlbǝgǝn biyi? Amaaya, famfǝg kǝ hǝnkal tǝ yista Farisiyaha ard Sadukiyaha.”
MAT 16:12 Tǝhalakwah wa nǝgharaaka nǝ mbǝrzahaan taakiya, tagtǝr taaki aa farfǝg kǝ hǝnkal tǝ yistin kwa ɗiiyav ma bruudiyin biya, mbats tagtǝr taakiya aa farfǝg kǝ hǝnkal dǝ tsagaana Farisiyaha ard Sadukiyaha.
MAT 16:13 Sǝghal ba nǝ Yesu damma larda Kaisariya Filibi, kaa ndavtǝrundavǝg kǝ iin kǝ mbǝrzahaana, amaa, “War nǝ Zǝra Uud mar tagaan nǝ uudahi?”
MAT 16:14 Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Kyalm ar taakiya Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝga, kyalmah ar taakiya, tlayanga Iliya, kyalmah dlaɓa ar taakiya Irimiya bi pal ma tlayangaha.”
MAT 16:15 Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kuramǝm ǝn war nai mam tlǝg nǝ ghǝraruwi?”
MAT 16:16 Kaa ngwangug kǝ Siman Bitrusa taakiya, “Kǝgh nǝ Kǝristi, Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla kwa dǝ shifǝga.”
MAT 16:17 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Agha dǝ bark nǝng, Siman zǝra Yunana, aɗaba uud bi wa markada kwanǝn biya, aa markada nǝ Daadar ma ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 16:18 Ən tagaktaga, agha Bitrus nǝnga, agha band akur kwa ndǝra nǝ uudan kǝ hǝngah tǝ vakaiya, ǝn da ɓaatlǝr dǝ kǝgh nai kǝ fǝtǝrna ndzǝɗ kǝ yaa dadda gata kaiya, kwa da maay nǝ ǝmtsǝg dǝ ndzǝɗa tǝghǝr kǝ iitǝr biya.
MAT 16:19 Ən da vǝlakvǝlǝg kǝ dǝga wura tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla, dlaɓa badǝm nǝ dǝgiti agha ngwuɗǝgant nǝng ma duniya, da ngwuɗav ma ghǝrazhigǝla, baɗǝm dǝgiti agha pǝlnanǝng ma duniya, da pǝlav ma ghǝrazhigǝla.”
MAT 16:20 Ɓǝlatǝraaɓǝlǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ magyi kǝ mbǝrzahaan ba vaivai aa tagarar bi aanji ndǝwar taakiya kai nǝ Kǝristi biya.
MAT 16:21 Ciigǝt ma kwahiin kǝ sart wa tagatǝr nǝ Yesu kǝ mbǝrzahaan taakiya, barari dagal damma Wurshalima, da hǝɓuu kǝ dlaɗa shahshaha, ma dǝv kǝ maalaha ard maala zhiila kǝssufah ard lii tsaga adzahadzaha, da tsǝvana, tǝ hǝng hǝkǝrɗa da ciivant dǝ shifǝga.
MAT 16:22 Ngal tǝɗant nǝ Bitrus damma dlǝmmbaava, cagaraa kǝ gyiya, amaa, “Aa tsanttsǝg nǝ Daadamazhigǝla, Yaazhigǝla, da dzǝgaar bi nǝ wan dǝ kǝgh ba dǝm biya.”
MAT 16:23 Kaa gwiyav nǝ Yesu da vak Bitrus, amaa, “Yagh vakar Shatanaha, agha akura mbǝɗa uud tǝ ɗuul nǝng vakara, agha dzamaghǝr band uuda dǝg shiga ndǝ Daadamazhigǝl biya.”
MAT 16:24 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Baɗǝm dadda kwa na gata kaiya, bamma ɗugharsɗuug kǝ ghǝraana, kǝsant kǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝgaana, gatǝkwagatǝga.
MAT 16:25 Aɗaba baɗǝm dadda kwa na kata shifǝgaana, da ɓǝgaan dagala, Badǝm nǝ daddakwa ɓǝlda shifǝgaan mbakyarvad kaiya da tlǝknatlǝga.
MAT 16:26 Au peɗaan kǝ uud akwama tlakǝnatlǝg kǝ duni baɗǝmma, tǝhalakwaha ɓǝldan kǝ shifǝgaani? Nii auwa da vǝlǝda nǝ uudan dlakulva shifǝgaani?
MAT 16:27 Zǝra Uuda da sii dǝ zǝrɓǝlgahaan ma ndangǝra Daddaana, da vǝlgarvǝlg kǝ dǝg shigaan aanji war kalkala dǝgiti ɓagaa nǝ iina.
MAT 16:28 Ən takurtaga, mǝng nǝ kyalma uudahi ghaciga vakwanǝnna ar da maay ǝmtsǝg biya bamma nǝghǝgharanghǝg kǝ saay Zǝra Uuda ma tlǝkǝsǝraana.”
MAT 17:1 Tǝhala hǝngah ǝngkwaha kaa langtǝrdǝtlang nǝ Yesu kǝ Bitrus, ard Yakubu, ard zǝrababba Yakub, kwa iin nǝ Yuhwan, dagat damma ghǝra aghwa ba kyakw ba daghuvaatǝra.
MAT 17:2 Kaa gwivǝtgwiig nǝ ndzǝganan tǝvuukwatǝra, baz huɗǝvǝgaan ndakwi mbiig band faciya, sǝdavaan ndakwi kaa nǝg kǝ maɗǝkw ba tǝlla.
MAT 17:3 Batwatsǝra kaa tsǝgwatsugw kǝ tlayang Musa ard tlayang Iliya. Kaa taa ghai kǝ iitǝr dǝ Yesu.
MAT 17:4 Aiyam Bitrus taa kǝ Yesu, “Yaazhigǝla, marawa nǝ ndzǝgana miyam vaakwana. Akwama haighanthaiga ǝn tafǝgan kǝ tsakwamah hǝkǝrɗa, pal kǝskǝgha, pal kǝ Musa, pal kiyava Iliya.”
MAT 17:5 Ma sartǝn ba ndzǝgaan taa ghai nǝ Bitrusa, kaa hǝɗtǝrduhǝɗǝg nǝ akummba, kaa cinngvacinng nǝ ghai sagal ma akumb taakiya, “Kwana iin zǝrara, kwan waig naiya, ǝn cinngaan kǝ ǝmtakǝraan ba vaivaiya. Cinngamarnucinnga.”
MAT 17:6 Cinngara ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan ǝndkwaha, kaa gǝdzǝgǝtgǝdzǝg kǝ iitǝr ba vaivaiya, baz mbǝɗa damma haay kǝ iitǝra.
