MAT 17:7 Kaa sagau kǝ Yesu taptǝrnana amaa, “Ciyamciiga, gǝdzam biya.”
MAT 17:8 Kaparant ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ ghǝra, nǝghara bi aanji ndǝwar biya, nǝghara ba Yesu daghuvaana.
MAT 17:9 Ar tǝghǝrdǝga saay nǝ iitǝr ma aghwa, am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Tagamarbi aanji kǝ war kǝ dǝgiti amaa nǝghǝga nǝ uuram biya, bamma ciyavantciig Zǝra Uud ma gǝtlah dǝ shifǝga.”
MAT 17:10 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg nǝ mbǝrzahaan taakiya, “Aujibǝg kǝ lii tsaga adzahadzaha Muus ar taakiya, barari bamma tlayang Iliya wada saay ba zǝnngwi?”
MAT 17:11 Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ba pakatta da saay nǝ Iliya, da ɓadlǝna kǝ dǝgitah ba ɗǝmma.
MAT 17:12 Ən tagkurtag ciya, sahi ba wur nǝ iliya, nǝgharaaka bi kǝ iin biya, baz ɓagar dǝgitahi naaghant nǝ ghǝraatǝra. Bandkwah dlaɓa Zǝra Uud da hǝɓgaan kǝ dlaɗ mizha dǝvaatǝra.”
MAT 17:13 Ngal nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg kǝ mbǝrzahaan taakiya, tagtǝr tǝghǝr kǝ Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝga.
MAT 17:14 Daral ba nǝ iitǝr da vaka dzahava dlamaa kǝlaawa, kaa sagau kǝ uuda nǝ iin da vak Yesu kǝla kǝ iin kǝ ghunnj tǝvuukwana,
MAT 17:15 amaa, “Yaazhigǝla, zhuwardaalazhuug yagh kǝ zǝrara, tsagwara nǝ shiɗkwa shatanaha, hǝɓgaan dlaɓ kǝ dlaɗ ba vaivaiya. Shiga ngwɛn wan ba ɓalgaan damma kaara ard yuwa.
MAT 17:16 Langandalang davak mbǝrzahagha, pǝletǝrvaapileg nǝ mbǝgaana.”
MAT 17:17 Kaa ngugarangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Kuram uudaha zamanna, am maay dǝ fadghǝr biya, am ɓa kǝlaadǝra, ǝn da zǝlma ǝmkyangar nai dǝ kurami? Ən da zǝlma ǝmkyangar nai ɓǝshkur kwanahaani? Ayakam kǝ zǝriin sa vaakwana.”
MAT 17:18 Kaa cagaraacag nǝ Yesu kǝ gyi kǝ shiɗkwa Shatanhna, kaa ɗugarsɗuug kǝ shiɗkwa shatanah kǝ zǝriina, batwatsǝra ngal mbǝg kǝ iina.
MAT 17:19 Kaa sagau kǝ mbǝrzah sa vak Yesu ma sartǝn maay aanji ndǝwar vakaan biya, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Aujilbǝg kǝskǝmnd pǝlekǝmndvaa lagwa shiɗkwa Shatanahiini?”
MAT 17:20 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kwakyarvad hǝtsalhǝtsǝg nǝ fadghǝraruwa, ǝn tagkurtag kǝ jiira, akwamaa mǝng nǝ fadghǝraru ba hǝɗikǝn band zǝra mastada, mammaa tagardatag kǝ aghwǝn taakiya, ‘Ciig vaakwana, dǝg da vaakwaha,’ maa ciiga. Maa maay nǝ dǝgiti pilkurvaapilǝg biya.
MAT 17:21 Lagwguvda bi nǝ hulfa kwanahaan biya, bamma tǝdvad dzǝgwazhigǝla ard kǝsa andǝla.”
MAT 17:22 Dzaharvǝt ba nǝ mbǝrzahǝn ma Galili, kaa tagtǝrtag nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Da vǝlav Zǝra Uud damma dǝv kǝ uudaha,
MAT 17:23 ar da tsǝgaana. Tǝ hǝnga hǝkǝrɗ ta ciivant dǝ shifǝga.” Kaa tsǝtǝratsǝg kǝ vǝgh ba vaivai kǝ mbǝrzahaana.
MAT 17:24 Daragha ba nǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan damma Kafarnahum, kaa tlǝgaraatlǝg nǝ lii cauwa hadam kwakyarvad vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl kǝ Bitrusa, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Maay nǝ dadda kwa tsagkur dǝgit ɗiya hadam kwakyarvad vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl biya?”
MAT 17:25 Aiyam nǝ Bitrusa, “Ɗigaana.” Dagha ba nǝ Bitrus da hǝnyaha, kaa fǝgarzhafǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ tagar ghaiy taakiya, “Au wagha nǝghǝga nǝng tǝghǝr kǝ ndavǝgni? Ar caug vak war nǝ tlǝksaha duni kǝ hadam, ar caug vak zarhaatǝr nii, ar caug vak uudahi tlǝrǝn hi?”
MAT 17:26 Ngwa ba nǝ Bitrus taakiya, “Vak uudahi tlǝrna.” Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Mbats maay nǝ zarhaatǝr ɗigaan biya.
MAT 17:27 Bakǝvakwaha, haik badza ǝrviɗmahuɗ kǝ iitǝr dǝ kǝmya, dǝg damma yuwa haiya ɓǝlǝg kǝ kwanjara, agha wurant kǝ ghaiya kilfi agha fǝgarzha nǝng kǝ vigaana, agha da tlǝknatlǝg kǝ kwaɓi da tlǝgaltlǝg kǝ pǝlgaana, agha kǝsant kǝ kwaɓiina, agha ɗiya kǝ hadamagh ard dǝgara.”
MAT 18:1 Ma kwahiin kǝ sarta, kaa sagau kǝ mbǝrzah da ndavgaru kǝ Yesu taakiya, “War kaci wa juujig baɗǝm kǝ ɗyakǝr ma tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝli?”
MAT 18:2 Kaa ɗahant kǝ iin kǝ zǝrzǝriin sa vakaana, ghacnan ma taatakaatǝra.
MAT 18:3 Aiyama, “Bak jiira wan tagkurtaga, akwama namal bi band zǝrzarhǝn biya, am tapna bi kǝ daa damma tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝl biya.
MAT 18:4 Mbakyarvad kwaha, baɗǝm daddakwa fǝsauna ghǝraan band zǝrzǝrǝna, iin wa ɗyak ma tlǝkǝsǝra ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 18:5 Baɗǝm dadda kwa dlǝghaadlǝghǝg kǝ zǝrzǝr ndǝ kwanǝn ma ɗaagara, dlǝghakwidlǝghǝg kǝskaiya.
MAT 18:6 “Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa fǝgara pal ma zarhahaan kwar fadghǝr tǝ kai kǝ ɓa haipa, da ngulǝm ba nguɗvardǝm nǝ akura vaar ɗyak ma kuungy ɓǝlvdǝm damma yuwa haiya kiyava ndǝgaana.
MAT 18:7 Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ duniya kwakyarvad dǝgitahi fǝgaraa uudah kǝ ɓa haipa, barari sagau nǝ dǝgitahi da fǝgaraa uudah kǝ ɓa haipa, dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ dadda kwa sagau tǝdvad iina.
MAT 18:8 “Akwama fǝkaa kǝ ɓa haip nǝ dǝvagh bi shigagha, ghuddaghudǝg agha ɓǝldana. Da ngulǝm agha tlǝkkǝna kǝ shifǝga damma zǝrazǝr dǝ dǝv palla bi shig palla, tǝghǝr kwa da ɓǝlvdǝm nǝ uud damma kaara fai dǝ dǝvahagh buwa ard shigahagh buwa.
MAT 18:9 Akwama gyiyagh wa fǝkaa ɓa haipa, tǝɗdatǝɗǝg agha ɓǝldana. Da ngulǝm agha tlǝkǝna kǝ shifǝga damma zǝrazǝr dǝ gyi palla, tǝghǝr kwada bǝlkadǝm nǝ uud damma kaara faiya dǝ gyiyahagh ba bǝrkuɗa.
MAT 18:10 “Famfǝg kǝ hyimiya, nɛnnɛmbi aanji kwar pal ma zarhahaan biya. Ən tagkurtaga, zǝrɓǝlgahaatǝr ba kǝlaa hǝnng ma ghǝraazhigǝla ar nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ huɗvǝga Daadar ma ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 18:11 Aɗaba sahi ba kǝrkangyakw nǝ Zǝra Uud da kata lii zaraazǝga.
MAT 18:12 “Mam tlǝg nǝ uuram, akwama dǝ tuughah dǝrmǝk nǝ uudana, kaa zaazǝg pallaatǝra, abi ɗuugaan kǝ kul vaslaambaɗ tar vaslaambaɗǝn vaka piig kaa dagal da gata pallǝn aa zaazǝgǝn?
MAT 18:13 Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, akwama tlakǝnatlǝg kǝ tuugh na zǝgazǝgna, hwaɗagaana juujig kǝ kul vaslambaɗ tar vaslambaɗǝn kwa zahara bi na.
MAT 18:14 Band kwah dlaɓa nǝ Daadaru ma ghǝrazhigǝla naabi zaan aanji pall ma zǝrzarhahaan biya.
MAT 18:15 “Akwama ɓagakaɓag nǝ zǝraabagh kǝ haipa, tagarnaatag kǝ haipaana, aandz ba kǝghar dǝ iina. Akwama cinngakanaacinnga gwighǝdaagwiig kǝ ndzǝganaru dǝ zǝraabagha.
MAT 18:16 Akwama cinngakanaa biya, agha gwiya dagal dǝ uud pal bi uudah buwa, kiyava cinngva nǝ ǝlbǝg tǝdvad shida uudah buwa bi hǝkǝrɗa.
MAT 18:17 Akwama lawalǝg nǝ zǝraabagh kǝ cinngtǝrcinnga, agha tagtǝr kǝ yaa dadda gata Yesu, akwama lawalǝg kǝ cinngtǝrcinnga, nǝdalnǝg band kǝrdiya bi band dadda dza hadama.
MAT 18:18 “Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, badǝm nǝ dǝgiti am nguɗǝgant nǝ uuram ma duniya, nguɗanguɗa ma ghǝrazhigǝla, dǝgiti am pǝlna nǝ uuram ma duniya, da pǝlav ma ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 18:19 “Ən gwiya tagkurtaga, akwama haiyaranthaig nǝ uudah bu ma kuram kǝ ghala dǝgit ma duniya, da ɓagtǝrɓag nǝ Daadar kwama ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 18:20 Baɗǝm vakavaki dzahvǝt nǝ uudah buwa bi hǝkǝrɗa ma ɗaagara, ǝn ba ǝmtaɗ dǝ iitǝra.”
MAT 18:21 Kaa sagau kǝ Bitrus da vak Yesu, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Yaazhigǝla, da ɓagwi shig ngwɛɛn nǝ zǝraabar kǝ haip lakuti ǝn ɓǝsharnaani? Ɓagaɓag damma shig uuɗiffa?”
MAT 18:22 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Shig uuɗif kalti biya, shig uuɗif damma kul uuɗifa.
MAT 18:23 Mbakyarvad kwaha, da gǝrav nǝ tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl dǝ tlǝksa kwa naa kǝdla dǝgahaan kwama dǝv kǝ kwanahahaana.
MAT 18:24 Fǝgharzha ba nǝ tlǝks kǝ kǝdlǝgaana, kaa sǝvardǝvsǝg nǝ uudi gatǝg nǝ iin tǝ ambǝla adawan alfu kǝlaawa.
MAT 18:25 Pilgharvaa ba nǝ pǝlgaana, kaa tagaan kǝ tlǝkǝsǝn taakiya, aa vǝlvǝtvǝlǝg baz iina baz uusaana baz zarhaana baz dǝgitahi dǝ vakai nǝ iin baɗǝmma kiyava pǝlgaana.
MAT 18:26 Kaa ghalgaan kǝ kwatnahaanǝn kǝla kǝ ghunnj tǝvuukwana, aiyama, ‘Fǝwifǝg kǝ huɗa ǝn da pǝlakpǝlǝg baɗǝmma.’
MAT 18:27 “Kaa zhugardaalazhuug nǝ dadda hǝnyahaan kǝ kwatnahǝn ɓǝsharna kǝ gǝmauwaan ba ɗǝmma ɗuwars dagalaana.
MAT 18:28 “Bad sagala kwatnahǝn waha, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ tsaghwa tlǝraan kwa gatǝg nǝ iin tǝ gǝmauwa sǝll kǝlaawa, ngal viyit kǝ iin hǝkyarna kǝ mbakulera, amaa, ‘Pǝlwipǝlǝg kǝ gǝmauwi ǝn gatak naiya.’
MAT 18:29 Ngal kǝlgakǝlǝg nǝ tsaghwa tlǝraanǝn kǝ ghunnj tǝvuukwan ghalgaana, amaa, ‘Fǝwifǝg kǝ huɗa ǝn da pǝlakpǝlga.’
MAT 18:30 Lawalǝg nǝ kwatnahǝn kǝ cinngaana, ngal ɓǝldǝm kǝ iin damma guda bǝrfina, bamma pǝlaapǝlǝg kǝ gǝmauwaana.
MAT 18:31 Cinngara ba nǝ tsaghwaha tlǝraan kǝ dǝgiti dzǝghaardzǝgna, cinngaru bi kǝ ǝmtakǝraan biya, kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr ar tagar kǝ dadda hǝnyahaatǝr kǝ dǝgiti dzǝghaardzǝg baɗǝmma.
MAT 18:32 Kaa ɗahgantɗahǝg nǝ dadda hǝnyahǝn kǝ kwatnahǝna, amaa taa kǝ iina, ‘Agha kǝlaada kwatnah nǝnnga, ɓǝshankanaaɓǝshig nai kǝ gǝmauwǝn baɗǝm mbakyarvad ghalgagha.
MAT 18:33 Mbats kalkalaan bi kǝskǝgh agha zhuwardaala kǝ tsaghwa tlǝragh band kwana zhuukadaala naiyin biya?’
MAT 18:34 Tsaatsǝg nǝ ǝrviɗmahuuɗ kǝ tlǝks ba vaivaiya, vǝlda kiyava vǝlgar dlaɗa, bamma pǝlaapǝlǝg kǝ gǝmauwiin baɗǝmma.
MAT 18:35 “Da ɓagtǝr bandkwan nǝ Daadar kwa ma ghǝrazhigǝl kǝ lii larwalǝg kǝ ɓǝshtǝrna kǝ zǝraabahaatǝr bad ǝrviɗmahuɗ palla.”
MAT 19:1 Ghyǝnnga ba nǝ Yesu kǝ taa kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, kaa ɗugarsɗuug kǝ iin kǝ larda Galili damma larda Yahuda, kwa tǝ gyaba kwah kǝ Zaagha Judan.
MAT 19:2 Kaa gatǝgaan kǝ uudah baɗyaka, dlaɓa mbahghanambahǝg kǝ lii dǝ kuzah vaakwaha.
MAT 19:3 Kaa sagau kǝ kyalma Farisiyah da fishgaana, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Tǝdvad tsagaana Muusa, kalkalaan kǝ uudan tagwavǝgha dǝ uusaan aanji tǝghǝr kǝ hulfa kwar kǝ dǝgiti ɓaga nǝ iina?”
MAT 19:4 Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu amaa, “Mbats, karantama bi taakiya, bamma daa zǝnngwa, Dadda Virɗiga, ‘ndǝraandǝrǝg kǝ ghwalva ard uus biya?’
MAT 19:5 Amaa dlaɓa, ‘Mbakyarvad kwaha, ɗuugaan nǝ uud kǝ daddaana ard babbaan ǝmtsǝvǝt tǝ uusaana, ba bǝrkuɗ ar da nǝg kǝ vǝgh palla.’
MAT 19:6 Ar madlai vǝgh buwa biya, naralnǝg kǝ vǝgha palla, dǝgiti aa matlǝgant nǝ Daadamazhigǝla, aa tagw bi nǝ uud biya.”
MAT 19:7 Aiyam nǝ iitǝra kǝ iina, “Ma ba ǝndǝkwah tsauwa, aujilbǝg kǝ Musa taga taakiya, barari ghudvara nǝ kakaɗa tagwavǝgh kǝ uusa, dlaɓa lagwvarsi?”
MAT 19:8 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Mbakyarvad dǝkdǝka ghǝraruwa wa haiyakurant musa taakiya, aa ghudvarghudǝg nǝ kakkaɗa tagwavǝgh kǝ uusa, ndza ǝndkwah bi ma daa zǝnngw biya.
MAT 19:9 Ən tagkurtaga, baɗǝm daddakwa tagwvǝgha dǝ uusaana, ma maay kwakyarvad gwaragwar biya, ma kǝsuukǝsǝg kǝ kwatlǝrn kǝ uusa, ɓaa ba gwaragwar dǝ iina.”
MAT 19:10 Aiyam nǝ mbǝrzah taa kǝ iina, “Akwama bandkwan nǝ ndzagana zhiila ard uusa, mbats ndzǝga kwal kǝsa uusa wa marawa.”
MAT 19:11 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ɗǝm bi nǝ uudahi haiganthaig kǝ ǝlbǝgǝn biya, bamma lii haitǝrant nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 19:12 Mǝng nǝ lii yavvǝtǝra kǝɓkya, ar da kǝsguu bi kǝ uus biya, mǝng nǝ lii datlatǝrǝt nǝ uudaha, mǝng dlaɓ nǝ lii hayarant nǝ iitǝr bad ghǝraatǝr taakiya, ar maay da kǝsa uus mbakyarvad gata tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl biya. Baɗǝm daddakwa haiganthaig kǝ ǝlbǝgna aa haiyanthaiga.”
MAT 19:13 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa sǝgardǝvsǝg nǝ uudah kǝ zarhaha kǝ Yesu kiyava fǝtǝra dǝva, dlaɓa dzǝgwtǝra kǝ zhigǝla. Nǝghara ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan ǝndkwaha, kaa cagtǝraacag kǝ iitǝr kǝ gyi kǝ lii sarardǝvsǝgna.
MAT 19:14 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ɗuwamtǝrɗuug kǝ zarha sa vakara, tsamtǝrǝva biya, aɗaba tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla dǝga hulfa kwan kǝ zarha.”
MAT 19:15 Fatǝrnaa ba nǝ iin kǝ dǝva, ngal mǝla dagalaana.
MAT 19:16 Mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iina sǝghǝv sa vak Yesu amaa “Dadda tsaga dǝgita, awan nǝ dǝgit maraw ǝn da ɓag nai ǝn tlǝkna kǝ shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝri?”
MAT 19:17 Aiyama nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Aujilbǝg agha ndavakai tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgiti marauwi? Ba Daadamazhigǝla pal wa marauwa. Akwama agha naagaan agha tlǝkna kǝ shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝra, tsufanttsufǝg kǝ kwanahaan kǝ adzahadzahaha.”
MAT 19:18 Aiyama taa kǝ Yesu, “Kwar kǝ adzahadzahahi?” Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “‘Tsǝbi kǝ shifǝga biya, ɓag bi kǝ gwaragwar biya, ɓag bi kǝ gǝl biya, ghudars bi dlaɓ kǝ fiid kǝ uud biya,
MAT 19:19 faarafǝg kǝ daadagha ard baabagha,’ dlaɓa ‘agha wayant kǝ tlǝgharaawakyaghagh band ghǝragha.’ ”
MAT 19:20 Am nǝ daala zǝrǝn taa kǝ Yesu, “Tsufananttsufǝg baɗǝm kǝ kwanahaana, au dlaɓ wa tǝmgwani?”
MAT 19:21 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Akwama agha naagaan agha nal kǝ uuda jiijiira, valǝtvalǝg kǝ dǝgahagh baɗǝmma, agha tagwarda kǝ talagaha, agha da tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ dǝgshigah ma ghǝrazhigǝla, kaa gatkwagatǝg kǝskǝgha.”
MAT 19:22 Cinngha ba nǝ daala zǝrǝn kǝ ǝlbǝgna, kaa badzǝdabadzǝg kǝ iin kǝ ǝrviɗmahuɗa, aɗaba dadda hyah nǝ iin ba vaivaiya, kaa ba mǝla dagalaana.
MAT 19:23 Aiyam nǝ Yesu kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Ən takurtaga, da dǝgaa ba dlah nǝ dadda hyah damma tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 19:24 Ən gwiya tagkurtaga, da tsaftsaf kǝ adlǝgwam dagal tǝ ɗuula liipǝr tǝghǝr kǝ dadda hyah daa damma tlǝksǝra Daadamazhigǝla.”
MAT 19:25 Cinnghara ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan ǝndkwaha, kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ iitǝra, ba vaivaiya aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Ma ba ǝndkwan tsaa, war kaci wada tlǝkǝna katǝgi?”
MAT 19:26 Ngal zhartǝrzharǝg kǝ Yesu, amaa taa kǝ iitǝr, “Kwan kǝ dǝgita ɓaga bi vak uud biya, vak Daadamazhigǝla ɓagaɓag nǝ wanahaan baɗǝmma.”
MAT 19:27 Aiyam Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Wai ci, ɗuwamndarɗug kǝ dǝgahamnd baɗǝmma kwakyarvad gata kǝgha. Au ci wa kǝmnda tlǝkna nǝmndi?”
MAT 19:28 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitra, “Jiir wan tagkur naiya, ma zamanǝn kwa da sagauna, Zǝra Uuda da cihurga tǝ avǝda kwargaan ma tlǝksǝraan kwa ndanga, kuramǝn gatamkwagatǝgna, kuram wam da cihurga tǝ avǝdah kǝlaawa tar buwa, kiyava kwara kuɗigaha yaa Izraila kǝlaawa tar buwa.
MAT 19:29 Baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa ɗugars vǝgyaha, bi zǝraabahaana, bi dughaha babbaana, bi daddaana bi babaana bi uusaana, bi zarhaana ard guhah kwakyarvad kaiya, da tlǝkǝnatlǝg juujig kwah shig dǝrmǝkka, da tlǝkna dlaɓa kǝ shifǝg tangw damma zǝrazǝra.
MAT 19:30 Da baɗyaka nǝ uudaha zǝnngwa ar da nǝg kǝ dǝga hala, dǝga hala dlaɓa ar da nǝg kǝ dǝga zǝnngwa.
MAT 20:1 “Tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla da band dadda hǝnyhiin kwa dal ba wurkǝs da gata bariyamah kiyava ɓa tlǝr ma guha inabiyaana.
MAT 20:2 Kaa tagvatag kǝ iitǝr kǝ gana kwab kwa ɗivar kǝ baryam ma vannga, ngal lanngtǝrdan damma guhaana.
MAT 20:3 “Tamaha karfi vaslambaɗa dlakadura, kaa gwiya dagal kǝ iin dlaɓa, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ uudahiin ar ghacga ba gyagyaan tǝ ɓalla kasukwa.
MAT 20:4 Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, ‘Kuram ndakwani damdǝg damma guhara, ǝn da ɗiikurɗiig ba marauwa.’
MAT 20:5 Kaa dagal kǝ iitǝra. “Kaa gwiya dagal kǝ iin dǝ vaci tǝghǝra, dlaɓa ard kalkala karfi hǝkǝrɗa hwaasa, ɓagtǝra bandkwa ɓagatǝra nǝ iin kǝ uudahaatsa.
MAT 20:6 Damma karfi dlǝɓa hwaasa, kaa gwiya dagal tlǝtǝraa kǝ uudahiin ar ghacga ba gyagyaana, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, ‘Aujilbǝg bǝrnif vanng am ndzǝga ba gyagyaani?’
MAT 20:7 “Aiyam nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, ‘Aɗaba maay dadda kwa vǝlkǝmnd tlǝra ɓag biya.’ “Amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, ‘Kuram ndakwani damdǝg da ɓatlǝr ma guhara.’
MAT 20:8 “Ɓǝlaa ba nǝ hwaasa, kaa ba tagartag nǝ dadda guhǝn kǝ daddakwa mǝlgaru kǝ fa hyimmi tǝ guhna, ‘Ɗahtǝrantɗahǝg kǝ lii ɓa tlǝrǝn agha ɗiitǝra kǝ kwaɓa tlǝraatǝra, farzhafǝg dǝ dǝga hala dat dǝga zǝnngwa.’
MAT 20:9 “Lii dalar tamaha damma karfi dlǝɓa hwaasana, ma waratǝr dlǝgha dǝgiti diivar kǝ baryam ma vannga.
MAT 20:10 Lii fararzha dagal ba zǝnngwna, tlatlar taakiya da jiguujig nǝ kwaɓatǝr kǝ dǝga kyalma uudaha, ghǝravaatǝr ndakwani ma waraatǝr dlǝgha ba dǝgiti diivar kǝ baryam ma vannga.
MAT 20:11 Cauwara ba nǝ iitǝra, kaa zavgarǝv ghaiy kǝ iitǝr kǝ dadda guha.
MAT 20:12 Ar taakiya, ‘Lii araa sǝgal tǝhalǝna, araa ɓaga ba tlǝra aawa palla, agha ɗiikǝmnda ba kalkal dǝ iitǝra, kǝmǝndi kǝma vannga ba ɓa tlǝra, aɗuug ci kǝ dlaɗa faciyi kǝmnda hǝɓguu nǝmnda.’
MAT 20:13 “Kaa ngwarangug kǝ iin kǝ pall ma taatakaatǝra, amaa, ‘Tsaghwara zangku biya, tagikǝvai kǝ gan taakiya, ǝn da ɗiyak kwaɓi ɗiivar kǝ baryam ma vanga biya?
MAT 20:14 Cauwacaug kǝ dlayagha dǝg daasagha, na naagant ba nai kǝ diitǝr kǝ lii aa sǝgal tǝhala kalkal dǝgiti na vǝlak naiya.
MAT 20:15 Mbats ǝn maay dǝ ndzǝɗa ɓa dǝgiti na naagant nǝ ghǝrar dǝ kwaɓar biya? Nii agha shilg kwakyarvad ǝn ɓa hɛrǝr ba vaivaihi?’
MAT 20:16 “Ar da nǝg band kwan nǝ dǝga hal kǝ dǝga zǝnngwa, dǝga zǝnngwa ar da nǝg kǝ dǝga hala.”
MAT 20:17 Tǝ ɗuula dagat damma Wurshalim nǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaana, kaa ɗahtǝrǝtɗahǝg damma gyaba, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra,
MAT 20:18 “Kiyam dagat damma Wurshalima vakavaki da vǝlav nǝ Zǝra Uuda damma dǝv kǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsuufah ard lii tsaga adzahadzaha, ar da ghudara kǝ sharia ǝmtsǝga.
MAT 20:19 Tǝhalakwaha ar da vǝltǝr damma dǝv kǝ lii Yahudah biya, ar da nengaana ar da kalaakana, da hǝrtǝvǝta, tǝ hǝnga hǝkǝrɗ da civanta.”
MAT 20:20 Kaa sagau nǝ babba zarha Zabadi dǝ zarhaan da ghalǝg vak Yesu, kǝla kǝ iin kǝ ghunj tǝvuukwaana ngal ghala dǝgit vakaana.
MAT 20:21 Aiyama taa kǝ iina, “Au wa nag nǝngi?” Am nǝ uusiin taa kǝ Yesu, “Haiyanthaig yaan kǝ zarharǝn buna ma pal cǝhura tǝ dǝva kafagha, pal tǝ dǝva ghyaɓagh ma tlǝksǝragha.”
MAT 20:22 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ zarhahina, “Am sǝrgai kǝ dǝgiti am ghalǝg nǝ uuram biya. Am hǝɓgahǝɓǝg kǝ dlaɗǝn ǝn da hǝɓǝg naina?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Kǝm hǝɓgahǝɓǝga.”
MAT 20:23 Amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ba pakat am da hǝɓǝgahǝɓǝg kǝ dlaɗara, ndzǝgan tǝ dǝvaa kafara ma dǝva ghyaɓara kai bi wa dǝ ndzǝɗa vǝlgaan biya, kwanahaan kǝ vakavakaha, ɓadlavtǝrna kǝ lii dzǝratǝraaka nǝ Daadar kwa ma ghǝrazhigǝla.”
MAT 20:24 Cinnghara ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝlaawǝn ǝndkwaha, kaa badzǝdabadzǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ ǝrviɗmahuɗ dǝ zarhabaabahǝn buwna.
MAT 20:25 Kaa ɗahtǝrǝtɗahǝg nǝ Yesu baɗǝmmaatǝra, amaa, “Am sǝrgasǝrg taakiya tlǝksahi kwar Yahudah biya ar fǝtǝra ngǝɗǝp kǝ uudahatǝra, maalahatǝr ndakwani ar martǝr ndzǝɗa kǝ uudahatǝra.
MAT 20:26 Da ǝndkwah bi ma taatakaru biya. Dlakulvakwaha, badǝm daddakwa naa nǝg kǝ maal ma kurama, barari nal kǝ kwatnaharuwa.
MAT 20:27 Dlaɓa baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa naa nǝg kǝ maal ma kurama, barari naal kǝ ɛɛvaruwa.
MAT 20:28 Bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ Zǝra Uuda sahi bi mbakyarvad ɓagvarnǝs kwatnahǝr biya, sahi mbakyarvad ɓa kwatnahǝra, vǝlda dlaɓ kǝ shifǝgaan kiyava vara uudah baɗyaka.”
MAT 20:29 Ar tǝ ɗuula ɗuwa Yariku nǝ Yesu ard mbǝzahaana, kaa gatǝgaan kǝ uudah baɗyak dagala.
MAT 20:30 Mǝng nǝ gulfah bu ar cihurga tǝ ghyaba ɗuula, cinngara ba nǝ iitǝr taakiya Yesu wa ghuda dagala, kaa dzǝgantdzǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ ghaiya, am nǝ iitǝra, “Yaazhigǝla, Zǝra Dauda! Zhukǝmdaalazhuuga!”
MAT 20:31 Kaa cagtǝraacag nǝ uudah kǝ gyiya, ar tagtǝr taaki aa ndzarandzǝg ba ɗǝwa. Ar gwiya dzǝgant kǝ ghai bad halavuwa ndzǝɗahatǝr ar taakiya, “Yaazhigǝla, Zǝra Dauda! Zhukǝmndaalazhuuga!”
MAT 20:32 Kaa ghacgaghacig kǝ Yesu, ɗahtǝrǝt amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Auwam nag nǝ uuram ǝn ɓagkurani?”
MAT 20:33 Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Yaazhigǝla, kǝm naa magha wurkǝmndant kǝ gyiyahamnda.”
MAT 20:34 Ngal zhutǝrdaalazhuug kǝ Yesu, tapnan kǝ gyiyahaatǝra, batwatsǝra kaa wurgǝtwurǝg kǝ gyiyahaatǝra, ngal gata Yesu kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 21:1 Hǝrzarǝt ba nǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan damma Bǝtafaji gǝdzǝrkǝsa kwa hǝrz dǝ Wurshalima vaka Aghwa Uufaha Zaitun, kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ iin kǝ mbǝrzah buwa.
MAT 21:2 Amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Damdǝg daadamma kǝsǝn tǝvuukwaruna. Bad daasaruwa am da nǝghǝganǝghǝg ka aghyunngw nguɗgan dǝ zǝraan tǝvǝgha, pǝlamtǝrdaapǝlǝg am sǝtǝrdaa sa vaakara.
MAT 21:3 Akwama ndavakurundavǝg nǝ uudana, tagamartag taakiya, Yaazhigǝl wa naatǝrnaaga, da gwiya saas dǝ iitǝr ba ndakwana.”
MAT 21:4 Dzaghaar kiyava righa dǝgiti tagada nǝ tlayanng taakiya,
MAT 21:5 “Tagamtǝrtag kǝ uudaha Wurshalima, ‘Wayam nǝ tlǝksaru da vakaaruwa, kalaaliya uuda nǝ iina, dagal tǝ aghyunngwa, zǝra aghyunngw wa dagal nǝ iin tǝ vakaiya.’ ”
MAT 21:6 Kaa dagal kǝ mbǝrzahaana ar ɓagnan bandkwa tagatǝr nǝ Yesu.
MAT 21:7 Ar sardǝv kǝ aghyunngwiin baz zǝraana, ar ɓala kǝ sǝɗavahaatǝr tǝ iitǝra, kaa ba ɗalgaan kǝ Yesu cihura tǝ vakaiya.
MAT 21:8 Kaa ɓala sǝɗavahaatǝr nǝ uudah ba ɗyak tǝ ɗuula, kyalmah dlaɓa ar kala kǝ aabayah tǝ uuf ar ɓala kǝ iitǝr tǝ ɗuula.
MAT 21:9 Uudahi mǝlara dagal tǝvuukaana ard lii gatǝg mahala ar dzǝgant kǝ ghai ar taakiya, “Galyamgalǝg kǝ Zǝra Dauda. Barǝk kǝ dadda kwa sagau ma ɗaaga Yaazhigǝla! Galyamgalǝg kǝ Daadamazhigǝla!”
MAT 21:10 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu damma Wurshalima, kaa cigǝtciig kǝ hǝnkala uudah baɗǝm ma kǝsiin ar taakiya, “War wa nǝ iin kǝ uudi?”
MAT 21:11 Aiyam nǝ uudahǝn dagal gata Yesuwǝn taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kwan iin nǝ tlayang Yesu, kwa sǝghal ma Nazarat ma Galili.”
MAT 21:12 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu damma gaagazaiya vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, lagwatǝrda kǝ lii vǝla dǝgitah ard lii sagwa dǝgitah ma vakai baɗǝmma, tlagars kǝ iin kǝ tibǝra lii mɓǝɗa kwaɓa ard avǝdaha lii vǝla takalamasara.
MAT 21:13 Amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Vindavavindǝga taakiya, “ ‘Vǝgyar da ɗahav dǝ Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla,’ namdalnǝg nǝ uuram kǝ ‘zazza shiɓa gǝlaha.’ ”
MAT 21:14 Kaa sagau kǝ gulfah ard ghurɗikaha da vakaan ma Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, mbǝttǝrana.
MAT 21:15 Nǝghara ba nǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsuufah ard lii tsaga adzahadzah kǝ dǝga japǝrǝn ɓǝgaa nǝ Yesu na, ard ɗiya cauwa zarh ma gaagazaiya Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, ar taakiya, “Galiyamgalǝg kǝ Zǝra Dauda.” Kaa badza ǝrviɗmahuɗ kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 21:16 Aiyam nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ Yesu, “Agha cinngacinng kǝ dǝgiti ar tag nǝ zarhahaan kwana?” Kaa ngwangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Mbats tapamnai kǝ karantǝgaan ma kaɗkaɗa ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl vindavindan taakiya, “ ‘Yaazhigǝla, kǝgh wa tagh taaki agha ɗaag tǝdvad ghaiya zarhaha ard vuunjah nǝng kǝ galgagh sagal biya’?”
MAT 21:17 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa ɗuutǝrsɗuug kǝ iin ma kǝsiina, kaa ba mǝla dagal damma Betani, ngal hǝnng kǝ iin vaakwaha.
MAT 21:18 Wurraa ba nǝ kǝsa, kaa gwiyaghǝra saas kǝ Yesu damma Wurshalima ngal njǝkǝnnjiig kǝ wai tǝ ghǝrdǝga.
MAT 21:19 Nǝghgha ba nǝ Yesu kǝ uufa ghǝgyiv tǝ ghaiya ɗuula, kaa dagau kǝ iin da tǝvǝgh kǝ uufina, tlakǝna bi aanji dau tǝvakai biya, ba hyǝmiya. Amaa taa kǝ uufiina, “Ba dǝm agha maadlai gwiya ya zǝr biya.” Tǝhala kwaha kaa ghulǝg kǝ uufiina.
MAT 21:20 Nǝghara ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan ǝndkwana, kaa ɓaa jappǝr kǝ iitǝr ba vaivaya. Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Aujilbǝg kǝ uufǝn aa ghulgal ba watswatsi?”
MAT 21:21 Kaa ngutǝrang kǝ Yesu, amaa, “Bak jiir wan tagkurtaga, akwamamma mǝng dǝ fadghǝra, dlaɓa am maay ɓaa ndaundau biya, mammaa ɓagaɓag kwa juujigg kǝ dǝgiti na ɓagara nai kǝ uuffa ghǝgyivna, am tagardatag dlaɓ kǝ aghwǝn taakiya, ‘Ciig vaakwana dǝg damma yuwa haiya,’ maa ciiga.
MAT 21:22 Akwama famdǝghǝrǝtfǝga, baɗǝm nǝ dǝgiti am ghalga nǝ uurama vak Daadamazhigǝla ma dzǝgwazhigǝla, am tlǝkǝnatlǝga.”
MAT 21:23 Dagha ba nǝ Yesu damma gaagazaiya Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, kaa tsagtǝr dǝgit kǝ uudah, ngal sagau kǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsuufah ard maalah tǝghǝr kǝ dlamaa kǝlaaw da vakaana, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Agha ɓag dǝ kwar kǝ ndzǝɗ nǝng kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitahi? Dlaɓa vǝlakak war kǝ ndzǝɗi?”
MAT 21:24 Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ən ndavkurundavǝg ghǝravar kǝ ndavǝg palla. Akwama tagamwitaga, ghǝravar ndakwani ǝn tagkurtag kǝ ndzǝɗi ǝn ɓag nai kǝ tlǝr dǝ vakaiya.
MAT 21:25 Ndzǝɗǝn ndza dǝ vakai Yuhwan dadda tsuufǝgǝn tsaa, vǝlghar nǝ Daadamazhigǝl nii uudhi?” Kaa tagkǝvatag kǝ iitǝr mataatakatǝra, taakiya, “Akwama tagiyamatag taakiya, ‘Sahi vak Daadamazhigǝla,’ da tagaan taakiya, ‘Aujilbǝg ci famdǝghǝrǝt bi tǝ iin biyi?’
MAT 21:26 Akwama tagiyamatag taakiya, ‘Vak uuda,’ kiyam gǝdza dǝgǝti ar da ɓagkiyam nǝ uudaha, aɗaba baɗǝm nǝ uudah haiyaranthaig taakiya ndza tlayanga nǝ Yuhwana.”
MAT 21:27 Kaa ngugarangug kǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Sǝramdai kǝ vakavaki sal dǝ ndzǝɗiin biya.” Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ghǝravar ndakwani ǝn maay tagkurtag, kǝ ndzǝɗi ǝn ɓag nai kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitah biya.
MAT 21:28 “Au wamaa tlǝg uurami? Mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin dǝ zaraa ghwalvah buwa, kaa dagau da vak kǝ dǝga zǝnngwa, amaa taa kǝ iina, ‘Zǝrara, dǝg da ɓa ɓatlǝr ma guha inabi hinana.’
MAT 21:29 “Aiyam nǝ zǝrǝn taa kǝ iina, ‘Ən maay dagal biya,’ tǝhalakwaha, kaa ɗayaghǝr kǝ iin kaa ba dagala.
MAT 21:30 “Ngal dagau kǝ daadiin da vak kǝ dǝga buwa, tagar kǝ iin kǝ dǝgiti taghar nǝ iin kǝ zǝngwna, kaa ngwangug kǝ zǝriin taakiya, ‘Iiya, ǝn dagau, daada,’ tǝhalakwaha lǝwa kǝ dagala.
MAT 21:31 “Ma iitǝr buna tsaa, warwa ɓagaa dǝgiti naag daddaatǝri?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Dǝga zǝnngwa.” Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝr dlaɓa, “Bak jiira ǝn tagkurtaga, lii cauwa hadahama ard tandaha ar da dǝgaa nǝ iitǝr damma tlǝksǝra Daadamazhigǝl tǝghǝr kǝskurama.
MAT 21:32 Aɗaba sahisǝg nǝ Yuhwan da markurd ɗuula jiirjiira, famdǝghǝrǝt bi nǝ uuram tǝ iin biya. Lii cauwa hadama ard tandaha fardghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ iina. Bakǝvakwaha, ndzaa tǝhala nǝghǝganǝghǝgaru kwana, lamwalǝg kǝ pǝlaghǝr am fǝdghǝrǝt tǝ iina.
MAT 21:33 “Kaa tagtǝrtag kǝ Yesu kǝ garava. Mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin kwa ɓagaa guha inabi, ɓǝlaraa kǝ ghǝrgha, tǝfa kǝ vaka pǝrtsa zǝra inabi, dlaɓa ndǝrǝt kǝ gud ba tlaɗ kiyava dadda uufakyauwa. Vǝltǝr kǝ mbuucaan kǝ yaa dadda uusǝga, kaa dagal kǝ iin damma lardi tlǝrna.
MAT 21:34 Ɓagaa ba sarta caa zǝra inabi, kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ iin kwatǝnahahaan davak lii cauwar mbuuca guhǝna, kiyava sǝgarda zarha inabi ma guha.
MAT 21:35 “Ngal viigǝtviig nǝ lii cauwar mbuucin kǝ kwatnahahaana, ar kalaaka kǝ palla, ar tsa kǝ palla, ar ɗawala kǝ kwah dǝ akura.
MAT 21:36 Gwiya ɓǝlant kǝ kwatlǝrn kǝ kwatanahah baɗyaka kwa jarujig kǝ lii ndza zǝnngwa, ngal ɓagaan kǝ lii cauwar mbuucin band kwa ɓagartǝra nǝ iitǝra kǝ lii ndza zǝnngwa.
MAT 21:37 Tǝhalakwah baɗǝmma, kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg nǝ dadda guhǝn kǝ zǝraan da vak lii cauwara mbuucna, amaa, ‘Mbatak ar da fǝgaarafǝg kǝ zǝrarna.’
MAT 21:38 “Nǝghara ban lii cauwara mbuuca guhǝn kǝ zǝrna, kaa tagkǝvatag kǝ iitǝr mataatakatǝr taakiya, ‘Wan ci dadda kwada gwigaana, na tsiyamatsǝga, kiyava nǝg guhiin kǝ dǝga miyamma.’
MAT 21:39 Ar viyǝt, ar ɗuuldan da gyilga ghǝrgha, ar tsana.
MAT 21:40 “Aitsaa, akwama saghaasǝg nǝ dadda guhǝna, au kaci wa da ɓagtǝr nǝ iin kǝ lii cauwara mbuuca guhni?”
MAT 21:41 Am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Da ciɓan kǝ kǝlaadahaan vǝlatǝr nǝ iin kǝ mbuuca guhna, da vǝltǝr kǝ guhiin kǝ uudahitlǝrn kwar da vǝlgar dlaiyaan ma kadlannga guhiina.”
MAT 21:42 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Mbats tapamnai karantǝgaan ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl biya? “ ‘Akuri ɗuwarars nǝ yaa dadda ndǝrga, iin wa nal kǝ akura nɗǝrǝg marawa. Kwana tlǝra Yaazhigǝla, dǝga jappǝr dlaɓ ma gyiyahaamnda.’
MAT 21:43 “Mbakyarvad kwaha, ǝn tagkurtaga, da cauwav nǝ tlǝksǝra Daadamazhigǝl vakaruwa, da vǝlǝvtǝr kǝ uudahi tlǝrǝn kwar da ɓa dǝgitahi naag nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 21:44 Baɗǝm daddakwa mbǝɗǝga da tuuk kwanǝn kǝ akurna, kalǝg ba hwɛɓhwɛɓa, dlaɓa uudani ɓǝlhi na akurǝn da tǝghǝr kǝ iina, ɗǝgaan ba tukwtukwa.”
MAT 21:45 Cinngara ba nǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsuufah ard Farisiyah kǝ garavahaan tagada nǝ iina, kaa nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr taakiya tag tǝghǝr kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 21:46 Kaa gata ɗuula viigaan kǝ iitǝra, gǝdzar gyiya uudaha, aɗaba kǝsarantkǝsǝg nǝ uudah kǝ iin taakiya tlayannga.
MAT 22:1 Gwiya tagatǝrtag nǝ Yesu kǝ kwatlǝrǝn kǝ garava, amaa,
MAT 22:2 “Tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl band tlǝks kwa ɓagghara hwaɗaga kǝsa uus kǝ zǝraana.
MAT 22:3 Kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ iin kwatnahahaan da tagtǝr kǝ lii ɗahavtǝrɗahǝgǝn da vaka hwaɗaga kǝsa uusna, larwalǝg nǝ uudahiin kǝ sagauwa.
MAT 22:4 “Ngal gwiya ɓǝltǝrǝtɓǝlǝg kwatlǝrǝn kǝ kwatnahah amaa, ‘Tagamtǝrtag kǝ uudahaan ɗahavtǝrɗahgǝn taakiya, “Wa ɓadlannaɓadlǝg nǝ dǝgzǝga, haravahǝrǝg nǝ kauwaha ard tlah ngatlangatlana, wa gyǝnngavagyǝnng ɓadla dǝgitah baɗǝmma. Aa sarasǝg sa vaka hwaɗagiina.” ’
MAT 22:5 “Far bi nǝ iitǝr kǝ hyǝmi biya, kaa mǝla dagalaatǝra. Kwana dal damma guhaana, kwatlǝrǝn dal da ɓa kasukwana.
MAT 22:6 Kyalǝmah dlaɓa ar vaitǝrǝt kǝ kwatnahahaana, ar kaltǝraakana, ar ciɓtǝrana.
MAT 22:7 Kaa badza ǝrviɗmahuuɗ kǝ tlǝksǝn ba vaivaiya. Ngal ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ iin kǝ tlaujahaana, ar vaitǝrǝta, ar ciɓtǝra kǝ lii ciɓara shifǝgna, ar haar kǝ kaar kǝ kǝsaatǝra.
MAT 22:8 “Tǝhalakwaha, amaa taa kǝ kwatnahahaana, ‘Ghyǝnngavaghyǝng nǝ ɓadla vaka hwaɗga kǝssa uusna, lii ɗahantǝr nai da vaka hwaɗaga kǝsa uusna, maa dlaitǝr bi kǝ sagau biya.
MAT 22:9 Mbakyarvad kwaha, tamtǝg kǝ baabura, ɗahamatǝrɗahǝg kǝ uudahi am tlǝgara nǝ uuram baɗǝmma, aa sarsǝg da vaka hwaɗaga kǝsa uusa.’
MAT 22:10 Kaa ba dagal kǝ kwatnahaanǝn tǝ baabur baabur ar ɗahant kǝ uudahi tlararaa nǝ iitǝra baɗǝmma, lii kǝlaadaha ard lii ɓa dǝga jiijiira, righǝtrighǝg nǝ vaka hwaɗag dǝ ghulabaha.
MAT 22:11 “Daghan ba nǝ tlǝksǝn da vaza ghulabaha vaka hwaɗaga, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ uuda nǝ iin kwa tsǝguv bi kǝ sǝɗava hwaɗag biya.
MAT 22:12 Aiyama taa kǝ uuda nǝ iina, ‘Tsaghwa, aghaa sǝgaa ndar nǝng da vaka hwaɗagǝn ba kwal tsǝguv sǝɗava hwaɗaga kǝsa uusi?’ Pilgharvaapilǝg nǝ dǝga tag kǝ uuda nǝ iina.
MAT 22:13 “Am tlǝksǝn taa kǝ kwatnahahaana, ‘Ngwaɗamnanguɗǝg kǝ dǝvaahaan ard shigahaana, ɓǝlamdaɓǝlǝg da gyimala, damma gurtla, vaakwaha da tuug ǝmtaɗ dǝ ghwada dǝv dǝ tlǝrɗa.’
MAT 22:14 “Baɗyak nǝ uudahi ɗahavtǝrantɗahǝga, ba hǝɗiikǝn nǝ lii dzǝravtǝraakadzǝga.”
MAT 22:15 Kaa ɗiya sawari kǝ Farisiyaha tǝghǝr kǝ ɗuuli ar da ngar nǝ iitǝr kǝ dlǝgǝd kǝ Yesu tǝdvaɗ ǝlbǝgahi da tag nǝ iina.
MAT 22:16 Kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ mbǝrzahaatǝr ard kyalma uudaha Hirudus da vak Yesu, am nǝ iitǝra, “Dadda tsaga dǝgit, kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya agha uuda jiirjiira, agha tsaga ɗuula Daadamazhigǝl ba jiirjiira, agha maay dlaɓ fa dagar ma uudah biya, kǝsghankǝsǝg kǝ uudah ba kalkala.
MAT 22:17 Tagkǝmndtag kǝ jiira, kalkalaan nii kǝskǝmnd ɗiigar hadam kǝ Kaisara kalkalaaan bi hii?”
MAT 22:18 Nǝghaakanǝghǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ kǝlaadǝraatǝra, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kuram muniyahaana, aujilbǝg am fǝsha kaiyi?
MAT 22:19 Maramwadamarǝg ndan kǝ kwaɓiin ɗiyav dǝ hadamna.” Ngal ar sardǝv kǝ kwaɓiina.
MAT 22:20 Aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Dzakǝva wara ard ɗaaga war wa nǝ iin tǝvakaini?”
MAT 22:21 Kaa ngug kǝ iitǝra, “Dǝga Kaisara.” Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Vǝlamarvǝlǝg kǝ Kaisar kǝ dǝga Kaisar, am vǝlar kǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ dǝga Daadamazhigǝla.”
MAT 22:22 Cinngara ba nǝ iitǝr ǝndkwaha, kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ iitǝra, ar ɗuwarsa. Kaa mǝla dagalaatǝr kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 22:23 Ba daghuvala kwahiina, mǝng nǝ kyalma Sadukiyaha, iitǝr wa fardghǝrǝt bi taaki mǝng ciig ma gǝtlah biya, sarǝv sa vak Yesu dǝ ndavǝga,
MAT 22:24 am nǝ iitǝra, “Dadda tsaga dǝgita, vindakǝmndavindǝg Musa taakiya, akwama ǝmtsaaǝmtsǝg nǝ uudan kwal yiga kǝ zǝr dǝ uusaana, kǝsgaan nǝ zǝrababbaan kǝ uusiin kiyav yaagar zarh kǝ zǝra babbaana.
MAT 22:25 Ndza mǝng nǝ zarha baabah uudif ma taatakamnda, kǝsuu nǝ yag kǝ uussa, ǝmtsan ba kwal yiga kǝ zǝra, kaa kǝsguukǝsǝg kǝ zǝra babbaan kǝ uusaana.
MAT 22:26 Dzǝghaar bandkwah dǝ zǝra buwa, baz zǝra hǝkǝrɗa, tanngw dat zǝra uuɗiifa.
MAT 22:27 Tǝhalakwaha kaa ǝmtsǝgaǝmtsǝg nǝ uusiina.
MAT 22:28 Aici tsaa, da nǝg kǝ uusa warkaci nǝ iin pal ma iitǝr daghuvala ciig ma ghǝtlah? Aɗaba uuɗiffa ǝmtaɗaatǝr kǝsarukǝsǝga.”
MAT 22:29 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Dzamaghǝraru kalkal biya, aɗaba am sǝrgai kǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl vinndavinndan biya, dlaɓa am sǝrgai kǝ ndzǝɗa Daadamazhigǝl biya.
MAT 22:30 Daghuvala ciig ma gǝtlaha, da maay nǝ ghwalvah kǝsa uuss biya, da maay dlaɓ pǝghwav nǝ dǝghwah da vǝgya zhiil biya. Ar da nǝg band zarha ɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 22:31 Dlaɓa tǝghǝr kǝ ciig ma gǝtlaha, karantama bi kǝ dǝgiti tagakur nǝ Daadamazhigǝl taakiya,
MAT 22:32 ‘Kai nǝ Daadamazhigǝla Ibrahim, Daadamazhigǝla Ishaku, ard Daadamazhigǝla Yakub biya’? Daadamazhigǝla lii dǝ shifǝg nǝ iina, dǝga lii ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝg biya.”
MAT 22:33 Cinngara ba nǝ uudah ǝndkwana, kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ iitǝr tǝdvad tsagaanaana.
MAT 22:34 Cinngara ba nǝ Farisiyah taakiya piletǝvaatag nǝ dǝga tag kǝ Sadukiyah vak Yesu, kaa dzahav kǝ iitǝr.
MAT 22:35 Mǝng nǝ dadda tsaga adzahadzaha Mus ma taatakatǝr kwa fǝsha Yesu dǝ ndavǝga.
MAT 22:36 Amaa, “Dadda tsaga dǝgit, kwar ka adzahadzah wa juujig ma adzahadzah baɗǝmmi?”
MAT 22:37 Ngugharangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “ ‘Wayantwaig kǝ Yaazhigǝl Daadamazhigǝlagh bad ǝrviɗmahuɗagh baɗǝmma, baz shifǝgagh baɗǝmma, baz hǝnkalagh baɗǝmma.’
MAT 22:38 Kwana iin nǝ adzahadzaha zǝnngwa, dlaɓ iin wa juujig baɗǝmma.
MAT 22:39 Dǝga bu ndakwi band dǝga zǝnngwa, ‘Waiyantwaig kǝ tlǝgharaawakyaghagh band ghǝragha.’
MAT 22:40 Baɗǝm nǝ adzahadzaha Musa ard tlayangngaha araa haciga bat kwanahaan ka adzahadzah buna.”
MAT 22:41 Dzaharvǝt ba nǝ Farisihyah vak palla, kaa ndavtǝruundavǝg nǝ Yesu,
MAT 22:42 amaa, “Auwa tlatlǝg nǝ ghǝraru tǝghǝr kǝ Kǝristi? Zǝra war ni nii?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Zǝra Dauda.”
MAT 22:43 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ɓagaa ndar ci nǝ Daud tǝdvad ndzǝɗa Shiɗǝkw Daadamazhigǝl ɗaha dǝ, ‘Yaazhigǝli’? Am nǝ Dauda,
MAT 22:44 “‘Am nǝ Yaazhigǝl taa kǝ Yaazhigǝlara, “Cihuracihurǝg tǝ dǝvaa kafara bamma nandalnǝg kǝ tlǝghumahagh da mizhangyil kǝ shigahagha.” ’
MAT 22:45 “Akwama ɗaag dǝ Kǝristi nǝ Daud kǝ ‘Yaazhigǝl tsaa,’ Nǝgal ndar kaci nǝ Kǝristi kǝ zǝraani?”
MAT 22:46 Maay wa ngugharangug biya. Ciigǝt daghuvala kwahiina maay wa gwiya shughana gyiya ndavgharundavǝg biya.
MAT 23:1 Am Yesu taa kǝ dzaha dlamaa kǝlaawa ard mbǝrzahaana,
MAT 23:2 “Vǝlavtǝr kǝ lii tsaga adzahadzaha ard Farisiyah nǝ ndzǝɗa tsaga adzahadzaha Musa.
MAT 23:3 Mbakyarvad kwaha, famfǝg kǝ hǝnkal kǝ ɓa dǝgitahi ar tsagkur nǝ iitǝra, ɓagam bi kǝ dǝgiti ar ɓag nǝ iitǝr biya. Aɗaba ar maay ɓa dǝgiti ar tsag nǝ iitǝr biya.
MAT 23:4 Ar ngwaɗant kǝ kadlanngah kwa ɗǝmɗǝma, ar faatǝra kǝ uudah ma ghǝra, ghǝravaatǝr ndakwani ar maay mǝltǝrumǝlǝg aanji dǝ zǝra dǝv pal biya.
MAT 23:5 “Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgitahi ar ɓag nǝ iitǝra, ar ɓag ba kiyava nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ uudaha, ar mbaghant kǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl ba maandala, ar ngwaɗǝt tǝ ghaiya uuvǝgaatǝra, dlaɓa ar kutǝr kǝ sǝɗav kwada apatsapats ba tlaɗ tlaɗ tuuk ghaiyaana.
MAT 23:6 Ar naa ba vǝlvǝtǝr vaka ndzǝgan marawa vaka ɓa hwaɗaga, ard dǝga ndzǝgan ndannga ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝla.
MAT 23:7 Ar naa ba fǝvtǝraaran dǝ taa uus ma kasukwa, dlaɓa ar naa ba ɗahvǝtǝr dǝ ‘Dadda Tsaga Dǝgita’.
MAT 23:8 Aiciya, aa ɗaakur bi nǝ uud dǝ ‘Dadda Tsaga Dǝgiti’ biya, aɗaba Dadda Tsagkur Dǝgit ba palla, am ba zaraabah baɗǝmma.
MAT 23:9 Ɗahambi aanji war dǝ ‘Daada,’ ma duni biya, aɗaba ba pal nǝ Daada kǝskurama, kwama ghǝrazhigǝla.
MAT 23:10 Aa ɗahkur bi dlaɓ nǝ uud dǝ ‘Tlǝvuukw’ biya, aɗaba ba pal nǝ Tlǝvuukw kǝskurama, iin nǝ Kǝristi.
MAT 23:11 Baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa ɗyak ma kuurama, aa nǝdalnǝg kǝ ghǝraan kǝ kwatnahaaruwa.
MAT 23:12 Baɗǝm dadda kwa fǝgaara ghǝrana da nenneva, dadda kwa nenna ghǝraana, da fǝvaarafǝga.
MAT 23:13 “Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝsǝkuram lii tsaga adzahadzaha Musa ard Farisaha, muniyaha! Hǝɗamarduhǝɗǝg nǝ uuram kǝ ɗuula daa damma tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝla. Kuram dǝ ghǝravaru ndakwi damagha biya, dlaɓa ɓǝlamtǝrnaa bi kǝ lii naa daas biya.
MAT 23:14 Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ sǝkuram lii tsaga adzahadzaha Musa ard Farisiyaha, muuniyaha! Am naa ba zaa kadlanga ǝngwasahi ruuwa zaalahatǝra, am naa ba dzǝgwazhigǝl ba tlaɗa kiyava nǝghǝkurnǝghǝg kǝ uuda, mbakyarvad kwaha, da vǝlkurvǝlǝg nǝ uud kǝ dlaɗ ba vaivaya.
MAT 23:15 “Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ sǝkurama lii tsaga adzahadzaha ard Farisiyaha, muuniyaha! Am dahadagal damma kǝsah shahshah dlaɓa am dzava yuwa haiya kiyava tlǝkna dadda pǝlaghǝr aanji ba palla, akwama tlamkǝnatlǝga, am nǝdal kǝ zǝra kaara fai juujig kǝskurama.
MAT 23:16 Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝskuram gulfaha lii martǝr ɗuul kǝ uudaha! Am taakiya, ‘Baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa zaazǝg kǝ ngwaɗǝg dǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla maay nǝ dǝgit tǝ vakai biya, baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa zaazǝg kǝ ngwaɗǝg dǝ adawan kwa ma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, barari viigaan nǝ ngwaɗǝga.’
MAT 23:17 Kuram dlagah gulfaha, kwar wa juujig dǝ ɗyaka, adawan nii, vǝgya Daadamazhigǝli kwa ɗǝfghaaka adawanhi?
MAT 23:18 Am taagaan taakiya, ‘Baɗǝm dadda kwa zǝgga ngwaɗǝg dǝ bagadiya, maay dǝgit tǝ vakai biya, aɗaba baɗǝm dadda kwa zǝgga ngwaɗǝg dǝ vǝlga gyagyaan kwa ɗiyav tǝ bagadiya, barari viigaan nǝ ngwaɗǝga.’
MAT 23:19 Kuram gulfahaana, kwar wa juujig kǝ ɗyakǝra! Vǝlga gyagyaan nii bagadi kwa pǝsha vǝlga gyagyaan hi?
MAT 23:20 Mbakyarvad kwaha, baɗǝm dadda kwa zǝgga ngwaɗǝg dǝ bagadiya kyulǝga, zaazǝg kǝ ngwaɗǝg dǝ vakaiya ard dǝgitahi tǝ vakai baɗǝmma.
MAT 23:21 Baɗǝm dadda kwa zǝgga ngwaɗǝg dǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, zaazǝg kǝ ngwaɗǝg dǝ vakaiya ard Daadamazhigǝl kwa ndzǝga ma vakaiya.
MAT 23:22 Baɗǝm daddakwa zǝgga ngwaɗǝg dǝ ghǝrazhigǝla, zaazǝg kǝ ngwaɗǝg dǝ avǝda kwarga Daadamazhigǝla ard dadda kwa cihurga tǝ vakaiya.
MAT 23:23 “Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ sǝkuram lii tsaga adzahadzaha ard Farisiyaha, muuniyahaana! Am sagal dǝ pal ma kǝlaaw ma kadlangaha caccakuram ǝnd kyimba, araariya ard mbakila, lamwalǝg kǝ ɓaa dǝgitah kwa juujig kǝ maraw ma adzahadzaha, ǝnd jiira, zhuwadaala ard fadghǝra, kwanahaan wa maa dlaiyaan kǝskuram kǝ ɓagaan ba kwal ɗugars kǝskuram kǝ ɓaa kyalmahaana.
MAT 23:24 Kuuram gulfaha lii martǝr ɗuul kǝ uudaha, am rahgarzharahǝg kǝ dǝgiti ǝngykwah ǝnd dǝg pǝghyiga, bakǝvakwaha, am ndǝgaan kǝ adlǝgwama.
MAT 23:25 “Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝskuram lii tsaga adzahadzaha ard Farisiyaha, muuniyaha! Am bar ba ilgaan kǝ kuwa ard dafa, aɗaba mahuɗmahaɗa righarighan dǝ dlǝrmǝg ard naaghǝra.
MAT 23:26 Kǝgh gulfa zhiila Farisiya, farzhafǝg kǝ bara huɗa kuwa ard huɗa dafa, aɗaba ilgaan ndakwani nal ba cuwaɗaɗɗa.
MAT 23:27 “Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝskuram lii tsaga adzahadzah ard Farisiyaha, muuniyaha! Am band gǝtlah kwa masavǝt nǝ dǝgit tǝll tǝ vakaiya, kwa maraw kǝ vazǝg tǝ ɓalaɓala, mahuɗmahuɗa righarighan dǝ tlatla uudahi ǝmtsaharaǝmtshǝga ard dǝgitahi ghwaɗghwaɗa.
MAT 23:28 Am band kwah ghǝravaruwa, mar zharkurzharǝg nǝ uudah tǝ ɓalaɓala, am band uudaha jirjira, mbats mahuɗmahuɗa, am righarighan dǝ muuniyira ard kǝlaadǝra.
MAT 23:29 “Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝskurama, lii tsaga adzahadzaha ard Farisiyah, muuniyaha! Aɗaba am ndara gǝtlaha tlayanngaha, dlaɓa am caɗa gǝtlaha uudaha jiirjiira.
MAT 23:30 Am tagaan dlaɓ taakiya, ‘Akwama kǝmnda ndza mǝng nǝmnd ma zamana daadijahamnda, maa mǝlamntǝrubi kǝ ɗiya avǝza tlayanngah biya.’
MAT 23:31 Tǝdvad kwah wa maramda nǝ uuram taakiya, kuram zarha lii ciɓara tlayanngha.
MAT 23:32 Bam zavukw dǝ ghyǝnnga tlǝraha kǝlaadǝrǝn kwa fǝgharzha nǝ daadijaru kǝ ɓagaana.
MAT 23:33 Kuram ghavalahaana, kuram faɗǝga ghavalahaan dǝ gurna! Am da ngǝdlgarwa ndandar nǝ uuram kǝ kaara faiyi?
MAT 23:34 Mbakyarvad kwah wan ɓǝlkur nai kǝ tlaiyangaha ard lii ɗyamɗyamǝr ard lii tsaga adzahadzaha Musa, am da ciɓgaan kǝ kyalmaha, am da hǝrtǝt kǝ kyalmaha, dlaɓa am da ɓaltǝra kǝ tsǝg kǝ kyalmah ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝlaruwa, baz gatǝrgatǝg kǝskuram damma kǝssaha, am vǝltǝr dlaɗa.
MAT 23:35 Aɗabad kwaha, da gwiya daa damma kunngyaru nǝ avǝza uudaha jiijiir kwa ciɓava ma duniya, ciigǝt tǝ avǝza Habil uuda jiirjiir tangw da tǝ avǝza Zakariya zǝra Berekiya, kwa tsama nǝ uuram ma taataka bagadi ard vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 23:36 Bak jiirjiir wan tagkur naiya, baɗǝm nǝ wanahaan da dzǝgaardzǝg dǝ uudaha zamana.
MAT 23:37 “Au wan Wurshalima, Wurshalima! Lii ciɓa tlaiyannga Daadamazhigǝla, lii ɗawala lii ɓǝlavant da vakaruwa, shig ngwan kǝskai na dzaha kuram band kwa dzahǝg nǝ ghwacik kǝ zarhaan damma dlambakaana, lamwalǝg nǝ uurama.
MAT 23:38 Waici, ɗuwakurna ɗuug nǝ uud kǝ vǝgyaru nalnǝg kǝ kwazaha.
MAT 23:39 Wan tagkurtag ciya, am da maadlai nǝghkwanǝghǝg biya, da ba daghuvala kwam da taag nǝ uuram taakiya, ‘Dǝ bark nǝ dadda kwa sagau ma ɗaaga Yaazhigǝla.’ ”
MAT 24:1 Sǝghal ba nǝ Yesu ma Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, kaa mǝla dagalaana, kaa margardamarǝg nǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl ndǝrandǝrana.
MAT 24:2 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Am nǝghǝganǝghǝg ba ɗǝmma nǝ wanahaan ndǝrandǝranna? Bak jir wan tagkur naiya, maay na akur aanji pal da Ɗuuvars tǝghǝr kǝ zǝrabaan biya. Da tlagav saaya baɗǝmma.”
MAT 24:3 Cihurgan nǝ Yesu ta Aghwa Zaituna, kaa dagau kǝ mbǝrzahaan da vakaana ba daghuvaatǝra, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Takǝmndtaga da dzǝgaar hǝr nǝ wanǝn kǝ dǝgiti? Au nǝ dǝgiti kǝm da sǝrgaaka nǝmnd taakiya agha hǝrzh saaya ard ghyinnga zamani?”
MAT 24:4 Ngwatǝrangug nǝ Yesu, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Famfǝg kǝ hyǝmiya, aa valkurdai nǝ uud biya.
MAT 24:5 Aɗaba uudah ba ɗyaka ar da sagau ma ɗaagara ar taakiya, iitǝr nǝ Kǝristiya, ar da valgaan kǝ uudah ba ɗyaka.
MAT 24:6 Am da cinngacinng kǝ ǝlbǝga ghwaava ard dlahalǝg ghwaava, gǝdzam biya, aɗaba kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitaha barari bamma dzǝghardzǝga, halavuwaana sǝghǝvbi ndan biya.
MAT 24:7 Larda da dǝgaradǝg kǝ kwatlǝrn kǝ Larda dǝ ghwaava. Tlǝksǝra da dǝgara kǝ kwatlǝrn kǝ tlǝksǝr dǝ ghwaava. Da sagau nǝ waiya, haay ndakwani da gajagav vakavak shahshaha.
MAT 24:8 Baɗǝmma wanahaan ba fǝgarzhan ndana.
MAT 24:9 Tǝhala kwaha ar da vaikurvaiga, ar da vǝlkur kǝ dlaɗa, ar da ciɓkurana, ar da naakur bi nǝ uudah mbakyarvad ɗaagar biya.
MAT 24:10 Ma kwahiin kǝ sarta da ba dyak nǝ uudahi da ɗuwa fadghǝraatǝra, ar da zuu kǝ langyiya zǝraabaahatǝra, dlaɓa ar da naabi kǝ zarabahaatǝr biya.
MAT 24:11 Tlayannga fiidfiidah ar da sagau badyaka, ar da valda kǝ uudah baɗyaka.
MAT 24:12 Mbakyarvad ɗyakǝra kǝlaadǝra, wayakǝva uudah baɗyak da maadlaiya.
MAT 24:13 Baɗǝm daddakwa ɓǝshgaan tanngw dat halavuwana da tlǝkǝnatlǝg katǝga
MAT 24:14 Kwan kǝ ǝlbǝg marawa tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝlna da tagav aanji takwar ma duniya, kwakyarvad nal kǝ shiid kǝ uudah baɗǝmma, tǝhalakwaha kaa da sagau nǝ halavuwana.
MAT 24:15 “Akwama nǝghamanaghǝg kǝ dǝgit dzah kwada sa dǝ ǝmtsǝg ghaciga ma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, bandkwa tagada nǝ tlayang Daniyela, dadda karantǝgaana aa nǝghaakanǝghǝga,
MAT 24:16 lii ndzǝga ma Yahudiya, aa mdǝrarǝmdǝrǝg damma aghwaha.
MAT 24:17 Dadda kwa tǝghǝra guda, aa sabi saay sa kǝssa dǝgit hǝnnyah biya.
MAT 24:18 Dadda kwa ma guuh dlaɓa, aa gwi bi saas sa kǝssa sǝdavaan biya.
MAT 24:19 Da dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ ǝngwasahi ǝnhuɗa ard lii dǝ zar ma dlaaga ma kwanǝn kǝ sarta.
MAT 24:20 Dzǝgwamdzǝgw kǝ zhigǝla aa sabi nǝ ǝmdǝrgǝn ma sarta akuhya ard sarta faciya ngiig biya.
MAT 24:21 Aɗaba ma kwahiin kǝ sarta da hǝɓav nǝ dlaɗ ba vaivaiy kwa tapavnai hǝɓgaan gwil fazha duni tangw samma haniina, da maadlabi hǝɓav hulfaan biya.
MAT 24:22 “Maa maay mbakyarvad gulavnagulǝg hǝnngahǝn biya, maa maay nǝ uuda dǝgshig tǝmǝg dǝ shifǝg biya, mbakyarvad uudahaan dzǝravtǝraakaanǝna, da gulav nǝ hǝngaha.
MAT 24:23 Ma sarta kwahiina, akwama tagakuratag nǝ uud taakiya, ‘Wanam Kǝristi vaakwana!’ bi ‘Wai vaakwaha!’ haiyamant biya!
MAT 24:24 Aɗaba da sagau nǝ Kǝristiya fiidfiida ard tlayanngaha fiidfiida, ar da ɓagaan kǝ dǝgaha sǝrga ard dǝgaha jappǝr baɗyak kiyava vala uudaha, akwama ɓagaaɓaga baz lii dzǝravtǝraakana.
MAT 24:25 Aiciya, wa tagankurtag bamma sarta.
MAT 24:26 “Mbakyarvad kwaha, akwama tagakurtag nǝ uud taakiya, ‘Wai nǝ iin ma tǝghala,’ dambi dagal biya. Akwma tagakuratag nǝ uud taakiya, ‘Wai nǝ iin ma huɗa guda,’ haiyamant biya.
MAT 24:27 Bandkwa wukyiɗǝg nǝ zhigǝl sagatsǝg ba parakrak tanngw dagata. Da band kwah nǝ saaya Zǝra Uuda.
MAT 24:28 Vakavaki dǝ dǝgiti ǝmtsaǝmtsana, ar dzahav vaakwah guumbaha.
MAT 24:29 “Tǝhala hǝɓa dlaɗa nǝghǝgaraa gyina, “ ‘Da ba niknik nǝ faciya, kyil dlaɓa da maay mara parakaan biya, da ɓala saay nǝ kwadladlah tǝ zhigǝla, da gajagav nǝ dǝgitah ɗyak ɗyak tǝ zhigǝla.’
MAT 24:30 “Tǝhala kwaha, da nǝghvanǝghǝg nǝ dǝga sǝrga Zǝra Uud tǝ zhigǝla. Baɗǝm nǝ uudaha duniya ar da tuug mbakyarvad dladlawa. Ar da nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ Zǝra Uud sii ma akumba dǝ ndzǝɗa ard dǝ ndanngǝr ba vaivaiya.
MAT 24:31 Da ɓǝlgaan kǝ zarha ɓǝlgaan da fǝrta dǝraw kwa tuug ba vaivaiya, ar da dzahant kǝ lii dzǝravtǝraaka sagatsǝga, dii dǝ dǝga, saa dǝ sǝga, dagal dǝ dǝga ciigǝt ma ngyila zhigǝl dat ghaalaana.
MAT 24:32 “Tsagamtsag kǝ ndzǝgana uufa ghǝgiva. Akwama fǝgharzgafǝg nǝ dǝvahaan kǝ ɗa daala ndaɗa, dlaɓa farzha kǝ daala hyǝmiya, sǝramasǝrǝg taakiya hǝrz nǝ madara.
MAT 24:33 Bandkwah dlaɓ akwama nǝghamanǝghǝg kǝ dǝgitahaan tagankur nai baɗǝmma, sǝramasǝrǝg taaki hǝrzǝthǝrzǝg nǝ sart ba mbɛv dǝ ghaiya guda.
MAT 24:34 Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, uudaha zamanǝnna ar da maay ǝmtsǝg biya, bamma dzǝghardzǝg nǝ wanahaan kǝ dǝgit baɗǝmma.
MAT 24:35 Zhigǝla ard haaya ar da ghyinnga, ǝlbǝgara da maay ghyinng biya.
MAT 24:36 “Maay wa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ sart ma faciyi da dzǝgaar wanǝn kǝ dǝgit biya, aanji Zarha ɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝli ma zhigǝla ma zǝraana, ba Daadiin kaltiya.
MAT 24:37 Bandkwa ɓagava ma zamana Nuhu, da dzǝgaar bandkwah daghuvala saaya Zǝra Uuda.
MAT 24:38 Band ma kwah kǝ sart lakwti kǝ sagaw kǝ yu kǝlg ɗyaka, ar zǝgaan nǝ uudaha, ar hǝɓgaana, ar gaan nǝ ghwalvah kǝ uusa, pǝghwav dlaɓ nǝ dǝghwaha da vǝgya zhiila, tanngw damma sarti dagha nǝ Nuhu damma pɛrayuwa.
MAT 24:39 Lakuti ar nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg kǝ dǝgiti dagala, nǝghar bak tlǝtǝraatlǝg nǝ ghavala yu kǝlg ɗyak hutstru ba ɗǝmma. Da band kwah dlaɓ nǝ saaya Zǝra Uuda.
MAT 24:40 Ma kwahiin kǝ sarta, da nǝghvanǝghǝg nǝ uudah bu ɓatlǝr ma guha, da kǝsvant palla, da Ɗuuvars wa palla.
MAT 24:41 Da nǝghvanǝghǝg nǝ ǝnghwasah bu ar haiya vaar ǝmtaɗa, da kǝsvant palla, da Ɗuuvars wa palla.
MAT 24:42 “Mbakyarvad kwaha ndzamandzǝg ba ɓadlaɓadlana, aɗaba am sǝrgai kǝ sarti da saay nǝ Yaazhigǝlaru biya.
MAT 24:43 Sǝramasǝrǝg taakiya, akwamaa sǝrgasǝrǝg nǝ dadda hǝnyah kǝ sart da sagau nǝ gǝl da vǝgyaan kavǝɗa, maa maay hǝna haar biya, dlaɓa maa ɗugarnaai kǝ gǝlǝn da vǝgyaan biya.
MAT 24:44 Mbakyarvad kwaha, kuram ndakwani ɓadlamvǝghaɓadlǝga, aɗaba am sǝrgai kǝ sarti da sii nǝ Zǝra Uud biya.
MAT 24:45 “War kaci kwatnahǝn kwa fǝvdǝghǝrǝtfǝgǝna, kwad dabari, kwa fǝghardǝm nǝ dadda hǝnnyahaan kǝ vǝgyaan ma dǝvaan kiya fa hyimi kǝ iin tǝ vakaiyana, dlaɓ vǝltǝr kǝ kaf kǝ kyalma kwatnah bamma sarti?
MAT 24:46 Dǝ bark nǝ kwatnahǝn kwada tlǝgara nǝ dadda hǝnyahaan ɓa tlǝr ma sǝghaasǝga.
MAT 24:47 Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, da fǝgardǝmfǝg kǝ kadlanngahaan baɗǝm damma dǝvaan kǝ kiyava fa hyimmi tǝ vakaiya.
MAT 24:48 Mbatak dadda nguɗi kwatanahǝna, dlaɓa tagaratag kǝ ghǝraan taakiya, ‘Da maay dadda hǝnnyahar saas wats biya,’
MAT 24:49 da farzha kǝ iin kǝ kala tsaghwaha tlǝraana, dlaɓa zǝgaan kaa hǝɓgaan dǝ lii hǝɓa kya.
MAT 24:50 Akwama ɓagaaɓag ǝndkwaha, da saas dadda hǝnnyahaan daghuvali maay ma taɗaan biya dlaɓa ma sarti sǝrgabi nǝ iin biya.
MAT 24:51 Da tlǝkǝntlǝgg nǝ dadda hǝnyahaan dǝ tsǝg ba vaivaiya, dlaɓa da vǝlar kǝ dlaɗ ǝmtaɗ dǝ muuniyaha, vaakwaha da tuug nǝ uuda ǝmtaɗ dǝ ghwada dǝv dǝ tlǝrɗa.
MAT 25:1 “Ma kwahiin kǝ sarta, da gǝrav nǝ tlǝksǝra ghǝrazhigǝl dǝ dǝghwah kǝlaawa kwa kǝsarant kaaraha jahuramb da vaka dlǝgha zhiila ghuula.
MAT 25:2 Dlǝɓ ma iitǝra ar dlagaha, dlǝɓ dlaɓa ar ɗyamɗyama.
MAT 25:3 Ma sarta kwa kǝsarant nǝ dlagahaan kǝ kaaraha jahurambatǝra, kǝsarantbi kǝ wal vakaatǝr biya.
MAT 25:4 Lii ɗyamɗyamna kǝsarantkǝsǝg kǝ kaaraha jahuramb baz wal ma mǝrt vakaatǝra.
MAT 25:5 Zǝlamazǝlmǝg nǝ zhiila ghuulǝn lakwti sagauwa, kaa njitǝrnjiig kǝ haara, ngal ba tsǝtǝratsǝg kǝ haara.
MAT 25:6 “Ma kyakyaka avǝɗa, ngal cinngvacinng nǝ ɗaag taakiya, ‘Wanam zhiila ghuula! Asama sa dlǝghgaana.’
MAT 25:7 Kaa ba ciig kǝ dǝghwahaan kǝlaaw ǝmtaɗaatǝra, ar ɓadlǝna kǝ kaaraha jahurammbatǝra.
MAT 25:8 Am nǝ dlagahaan taa kǝ lii ɗyamɗyamna, ‘Gamkǝmndugǝg yaru kǝ wal ba hǝɗiikǝna, aɗaba naa ǝmtsǝg nǝ kaaraha jahurambamnda.’
MAT 25:9 Aiyam nǝ lii ɗyamɗyamǝn taa kǝ iitǝra, ‘Maaya, da tlǝkiyamaara biya. Ngulǝm dam da vak lii vǝlgaan am sǝgwa kǝ dǝgaruwa.’
MAT 25:10 Daral ba nǝ iitǝr da sǝgwa walna, lakwti saas kǝ iitǝra, sǝghaasǝg nǝ zhiila ghuula, kaa daas kǝ lii ɓadlarvǝghaɓadlǝg ǝmtaɗ dǝ iina da vaka hwaɗaga, kaa hǝɗvarduhǝɗǝg nǝ wakyagha.
MAT 25:11 “Tǝhalakwaha, kaa sǝgaasǝg kǝ dlaga dǝghwahaan dlǝɓna, am nǝ iitǝra, ‘Dadda ndannga, Dadda ndannga, wurkǝmndantwurg kǝ wakyagha!’
MAT 25:12 Kaa ngutǝrangug nǝ zhiilaghuulǝn taakiya, ‘Bak jiira wan tagkur naiya, Ən sǝrkur biya.’
MAT 25:13 “Mbakyarvad kwaha ndzamandzǝg ba ɓadlaɓadlana, aɗaba am sǝrgai kǝ faciya ma sart biya.
MAT 25:14 “Tlǝksǝra Daadamazhigǝla band garava uudi kwada dagal dǝ dǝga, kaa ɗahtǝrǝt kǝ kwatnahaan fǝtǝrdǝm kǝ dǝgahaan da mizha dǝvaatǝra.
MAT 25:15 Vǝlar kǝ pall kǝ adawan alfu dlǝɓa, pall dlaɓ vǝlar kǝ adawan alfu buwa, vǝlar dlaɓ kwatlǝrǝn kǝ adawan alfu palla, makwaraatǝr vǝlghar ba kalkala ndzǝɗaana, Kaa dagalaana.
MAT 25:16 Kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ dadda kwa cauwa adawan alfu dlǝɓǝn kǝ mbǝɗa dǝv bat watsǝra, kaa ba tlǝnatlǝg kǝ iin kǝ yu alfu dlǝɓ tuuk vakaiya.
MAT 25:17 Bandkwah dlaɓ dadda kwa cauwa adawan alfu buna, tlakǝna kǝ yu alfu bu tuuk vakaiya.
MAT 25:18 Kiyava dadda kwa cauwa adawan alfu pallǝna, nǝghǝghar bak kwaɗǝgakwaɗǝg kǝ affǝk hǝɗnan kǝ kwaɓa dadda hǝnyahaanǝna.
MAT 25:19 “Tǝhala zǝlmazǝlmǝga, kaa gwiyaghǝra saas kǝ dadda hǝnyaha kwatnahahaan kiyava sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgiti ɓagara nǝ iitǝr dǝ kwaɓiina.
MAT 25:20 Kaa sagau kǝ dadda kwa cauwa adawan alfu dlǝɓǝn dǝ kwatlǝrǝn kǝ alfu dlǝɓa amaa, ‘Dadda hǝnyaha, adawan alfu dlǝɓ wa vǝlghwa nǝnnga. Wan nǝ yu alfu dlǝɓ naa tlǝkǝna nai tuuk vakaiya.’
MAT 25:21 Am nǝ dadda hǝnyahaan taa kǝ iina, ‘Uusa, kwatnaha jiijiira, kwa fǝvdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ vakaiya. Fǝvdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tsau dǝ kǝgh tǝghǝr kǝ zǝr dǝgit hǝdikǝna, ǝn da vǝlakvǝlǝg kǝ tlǝri juujig kwana. Asǝg sa dlaig ǝmtaɗ dǝ kaiya.’
MAT 25:22 “Kaa sagau kǝ dadda kwa cauwa alfu buwa adawana, amaa, ‘Dadda hǝnyaha, alfu buwa adawan wa vǝlghwa nǝnnga. Wan nǝ yu alfu bu naa tlǝkǝna nai tuuk vakaiya.’
MAT 25:23 Am nǝ dadda hǝnyahaan taa kǝ iina, ‘Uus, kwatnaha jiijiira, kwa fǝvdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ vakaiya. Fǝvdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tsau dǝ kǝgh tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgit hǝdikǝna, ǝn da vǝlakvǝlǝg kǝ tlǝri juujig kwana. Asǝg sa dlaig ǝmtaɗ dǝ kaiya.’
MAT 25:24 “Kaa sagau kǝ dadda kwa cauwa alfu adawan pallna, amaa, ‘Dadda hǝnyaha, ǝn sǝrgasǝrg mbǝlɛmbǝlɛn ɓagakǝv dǝ kǝgha, agha ghuda hii vakavaki riigha biya. Agha vai ba dzaha dǝgit vakavaki kutgha biya.
MAT 25:25 Iin wa gǝdzakut kaiya, ǝn kwaɗa kǝ afka ǝn hǝɗnanna. Na kǝ dǝgagha.’
MAT 25:26 “Am nǝ dadda hǝnyahaan taa kǝ iina, ‘Kǝgh, kwatnahǝn kǝlaadna, mandǝlghna! Mbats agha sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya ǝn ghuda hii vakavaki riyana biya, dlaɓa ǝn vai ba dzaha dǝgit vakavaki kutana biya.
MAT 25:27 Maa fǝghwifǝg kǝ kwaɓar ma banka, maa bad saasar ǝn tlǝkǝna kǝ yu tuuk vakaiya!
MAT 25:28 Mbakyarvad kwaha, cauwamarvacaug kǝ alfuwa adawan pallna am vǝlar kǝ dadda kwad alfu kǝlaawna.
MAT 25:29 Aɗaba baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa dǝ dǝgita, da fǝvarnaafǝga tlǝkna baɗyaka. Kwa maay dǝ vakai biya, aanji hǝɗikǝni dǝ vakai nǝ iina, da cauwav vakaana.
MAT 25:30 Ɓǝlamdǝmɓǝlǝg kǝ kǝlaada kwatnahǝn damma gurtla. Vaakwaha da tuug ǝmtaɗ dǝ ghwada dǝv dǝ tlǝrɗa.’
MAT 25:31 “Ma Sarti da saay nǝ Zǝra Uud ma ndanngǝraan ǝmtaɗ dǝ zarha ɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝl baɗǝmma, ngal da cihura tǝ avǝd ndanng ma tlǝkǝsǝraana.
MAT 25:32 Da dzahvant nǝ uudaha duni badǝm da tǝvuukwana, da wahtǝrzha kǝ uudah hutsǝg buwa, bandkwa wahgarzh nǝ dadda piya alman kǝ tughah ard aagwaha guja.
MAT 25:33 Da dzant kǝ tughah damma dǝvaa kafaana, aagwah da tǝ dǝvaa ghyaɓaana.
MAT 25:34 “Tǝkalakwah da tagtǝrtag nǝ tlǝkǝs kǝ lii tǝ dǝvaa kafaanǝn taakiya, ‘Asamasǝg nǝ uuramǝn fakura nǝ Daadar kǝ barkna! Na dlǝghamadlǝghǝg kǝ tlǝksǝrǝn ɓadlakurna Daadamazhigǝl bamma fazha duniya.
MAT 25:35 Aɗaba sarta kwandza njǝkwa nǝ waiya, vǝlamwavǝlǝg nǝ kǝ dǝga zǝga. Sarta kwandza njǝkwa nǝ andǝla, gamwadgǝg kǝ yuwa hǝɓǝga. Ndzan ghulaba, dlǝghamkwidlǝghǝga.
MAT 25:36 Ndzan maay dǝ sǝɗav biya, vǝlamwavǝlǝg kǝ sǝɗava. Ndzan yang biya, famwufǝg kǝ hyimiya. Ndzan ma guda bǝrfina, nǝghamwanǝghǝga.’
MAT 25:37 “Tǝhalakwaha, kaa da ngugarngug nǝ uudaha jiijiir taakiya, ‘Yaazhigǝl, nǝghamnd kak hǝr nǝmnd njak wai kǝm vǝlak kǝ dǝga zǝgi? Bii njak nǝ andǝl kǝm gǝgku kǝ yuwa hǝɓǝgi?
MAT 25:38 Nǝghamnd kak hǝr nǝmnd agha ghulab kǝm dlǝghkani? Bii agha maay dǝ sǝɗav kǝm vǝlak kǝ saɗavi?
MAT 25:39 Nǝghamnd kak hǝr nǝmnd agha yangbiya, bii agha ma guda bǝrfin kǝm nǝghkaani?’
MAT 25:40 “Kaa da ngutǝrangug nǝ tlǝsksǝn taakiya, ‘Ba jiir wan tagkur naiya, ɓagamaraɓag tsau kǝ daddakwa hǝɗiikǝn pall ma kwanahaan kǝ zaraabaharna, bakalkal amaa ɓagwi ba kǝskaiya.’
MAT 25:41 “Tǝhakwah da tagtǝrtaag kǝ lii tǝ dǝvaa ghyaɓaan taakiya, ‘Yagham vakar lii tlafatlafanǝnna, damdǝg damma kaara fai kwa maay ghyinng ba dǝm biya, kwa ɓadlavarna kǝ Shatanah ard zarha ɓǝlgaana.
MAT 25:42 Aɗaba ndza njǝkwa nǝ waiya, vǝlamwa bi kǝ dǝga zǝg biya. Ndza njikwa nǝ andǝla, gamwad bi kǝ yu biya.
MAT 25:43 Ndzan ghulaba, dlǝghamkwi biya, ndzan maay dǝ sǝɗav biya, vǝlamwabi kǝ sǝɗav biya, ndzan yang biya, dlaɓa ndzan ma guda bǝrfina nǝghamwa biya.’
MAT 25:44 “Ghǝravaatǝr ndakwani ar da ngug taakiya, ‘Yaazhigǝla, nǝghamnd kak hǝr nǝmnd agha ɓǝsha wai, bi njak nǝ andǝl, bi agha ghulaba, bi agha maay dǝ sǝɗav, bi agha yang biya, bi agha ma guda bǝrfina kǝm lǝwa kǝ fǝku hyǝmiyi?’
MAT 25:45 “Kaa da ngutǝrngug taakiya, ‘Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, ɓagamara bi tsau kǝ dadda kwa hǝɗiikǝn pall ma uudahaanǝn biya, ɓagamwi bi kǝskai biya.’
MAT 25:46 “Kwanahaan kǝ uudaha, ar da hǝɓa dlaɗ tangw damma zǝrazǝra, uudaha jiikiira ar damma shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝra.”
MAT 26:1 Ghyǝnnga ba Yesu kǝ tagtǝr kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitah baɗǝmma, aiyama taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana,
MAT 26:2 “Am sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya tǝmaa ba hǝnng bu kǝ Hwaɗaga Haarakǝsa Dzava Hǝnyaha, da vǝlǝvda dlaɓ nǝ Zǝra Uuda da hǝrtǝvǝta.”
MAT 26:3 Kaa dzahav kǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsauufah ard tlǝvuukwah tǝghǝr kǝ uudaha ma vǝgya maal ba tingting ma zhiila kǝsauufah, kwa ɗahav dǝ Kayafa.
MAT 26:4 Kaa ba ɗiya sawariya viya Yesu kǝ iitǝr da gǝlagǝl kiyava tsǝgaan kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 26:5 Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Ɓag yam bi sarta hwaɗag biya, haik kǝ ciya hǝnkal kǝ uudaha.”
MAT 26:6 Ma sartǝn ndza ma Bitani nǝ Yesu ma vǝgya Siman kwandza njakǝn vǝcca.
MAT 26:7 Kaa sagau nǝ uusiin da vak Yesu dǝ mǝrta kwa ɓagava dǝ akura onis, righarighan dǝ tǝrshǝn bǝtbǝt kwa ba pir ganan ɗiyarǝt dat ghǝr ma sartǝn ndza zaa dǝga zǝg nǝ iina.
MAT 26:8 Nǝghǝghara ba nǝ mbǝrzahǝn ǝndkwaha, kaa badzǝg kǝ ǝrviɗmahuɗatǝra, aiyam nǝ iitǝra ma taatakatǝra, “Badza ba dǝgiti nǝ wanna.
MAT 26:9 Maa vǝlavu nǝ tǝrshinna, maa tlavkǝnatlǝg nǝ kwaɓ ba ɗyaka maa vǝlavtǝrvǝlǝg kǝ talagaha.”
MAT 26:10 Sǝrghaakasǝrǝg tsau nǝ Yesu kǝ dǝgiti ar tag nǝ iitǝra aiyama taa kǝ iitǝra, “Aujilbǝg am gaghya uusǝn ǝndkwani? Abi dǝgit maraw wa ɓagwi nǝ iina.
MAT 26:11 Ba kǝlaa hǝnga am ba ǝmtaɗ dǝ talagaha, ǝn maay nai ǝmtaɗ dǝ kuram kǝlaa hǝnng biya.
MAT 26:12 Kwan kǝ tǝrshinǝn aa ɗaigǝt nǝ iin tǝ vǝgharna, aa ɓag kwakyarvad ɓadla hǝɗa kaiya.
MAT 26:13 Bak jiijiir wan tagkur naiya, baɗǝm nǝ vakavaki da tagav nǝ ǝlbǝg maraw ma duni baɗǝmma, da ba tagav nǝ dǝgiti ɓagaa nǝ uusǝn kiyava dzamgaana.”
MAT 26:14 Kaa ba dagal kǝ pal ma mbǝrzah kǝlaawa tar buwna, kwa ɗahav dǝ Yahuda Iskariyuti, da vak maalah ma zhiila kǝsauufaha.
MAT 26:15 Aiyama, “Awam da vǝlgwa nǝ uuram, akwama vǝlankurvǝlǝgi?” Ar vǝlar kǝ sǝl kul hǝkǝrɗa.
MAT 26:16 Ciigǝt tǝ kwahiin kǝ sarta wa fǝgharzha nǝ iin kǝ gata ɗuul vǝltǝr Yesu.
MAT 26:17 Daghuvala zǝngwa Hwaɗaga Haara kǝssa bǝruudi kwal yista, kaa sagau nǝ mbǝrzahaan da vak Yesu, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Vaakwar wagha naag nǝng ma kǝmǝnda ɓadlkana kǝ dǝgazǝg Hwaɗaga Haara kǝssa dzava hǝnyah kiyava zǝgaan kǝskǝghi?”
MAT 26:18 Aiyama, “Damdǝg damma huɗa kǝsa da vak uuda nǝ iina, tagamartaga, ‘Daada tsaga dǝgiti, waa taakiya, ɓagaaɓag nǝ sart kwan da zǝg nai kǝ dǝga zǝga Hwaɗaga Haarakǝsa Dzava Hǝnyah ma vǝgyagh ǝmtaɗ dǝ mbǝrzahaara.’ ”
MAT 26:19 Kaa ɓagaan kǝ mbǝrzahaan bandkwa tagatǝr nǝ Yesu kǝ ɓagaana, kaa ɓadlnaɓadlǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ dǝga zǝga Hwaɗaga Haarakǝsa Dzava Hǝnyaha.
MAT 26:20 Ɓǝlaa ba hwaasa, ngal cihuran da za dǝga zǝga ǝmtaɗ dǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝlaawa tar buwa.
MAT 26:21 Ar tǝghǝrdǝga za dǝga zǝga, am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Bak jiijiir wan tagkur naiya, palla ma kurama da vǝla kaiya.”
MAT 26:22 Kaa njitǝrnjiig ba vaivaiya, ar farzha kǝ ndavgarundavǝg ba da palla palla ar taakiya, “Kai ni, Yaazhigǝla?”
MAT 26:23 Kaa ngutǝranguga amaa, “Daddakwa za dǝga zǝg ǝmtaɗ dǝ kaiya ma kuwa, iin wa da vǝla kaiya.
MAT 26:24 Zǝra Uuda da ǝmtsǝg bandkwa vindava ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl tǝghǝr kǝ iina. Dǝga zhuwadaal kǝ daddakwa da vǝla Zǝra Uuda! Ngulǝn maa yava bi nǝ uuda nǝ iin biya.”
MAT 26:25 Aiyam nǝ Yahud kwa vǝlǝt Yesu na, “Kai ni, dadda tsaga dǝgita?” Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Kǝgh ndakwani taghǝdataga.”
MAT 26:26 Ar tǝghǝrdǝga za dǝga zǝga, kaa kǝsgantkǝsǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ bǝruudiya, tagar kǝ uus kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, lahnan vǝltǝr kǝ mbǝrzahaana, amaa, “Namamma zamzǝga, kwana iin nǝ vǝghara.”
MAT 26:27 Kaa kǝsgantkǝsǝg kǝ iin kǝ kuwa yuwa inabiya, tagar kǝ uus kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, vǝltǝra amaa, “Hǝɓamhǝɓǝg baɗǝmaruwa.
MAT 26:28 Kwana iin nǝ avǝzara dǝga righa lanngiya kwa ɗiyavda mbakyarvad uudah baɗyaka, kiyava ɓǝsha haipahaatǝra.
MAT 26:29 Ən tagkurtaga, ǝn madlai da gwiya hǝɓa yuwa inabiyin biya, bamma daghuvali ǝn da hubǝg nai kǝ daalaan ǝmtaɗ dǝ kuram ma tlǝksǝra Daadara.”
MAT 26:30 Ɓǝlara ba Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan kǝ ǝngsa, kaa sagal kǝ iitǝra, ngal ba dagat kǝ iitǝr damma Aghwa kwa dǝ Uufaha Zaitun.
MAT 26:31 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Bamma huɗa avǝɗna, baɗǝmaru am da mbǝɗǝg ma fadghǝraru am da ɗukusa, mbakyarvad dǝgiti da dzǝgaar dǝ kaiya, aɗaba ba vindavindan taakiya, “ ‘Ənda tsǝgaan kǝ dadda piiya almana, da kwazǝg nǝ agyaragyara tughwaha.’
MAT 26:32 “Tǝhala kwama da ciyakutciig nǝ uud dǝ shiifǝga, ǝn da dǝgaa nai tǝghǝr kǝskuram damma Galili.”
MAT 26:33 Am nǝ Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Aanji ar mbǝɗan ma fadghǝraatǝr baɗǝm mbakyarvad dǝgiti da dzǝgaar dǝ kǝgha, ǝn da maay nai biya.”
MAT 26:34 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Bak jiir wan tagak naiya, bamma huɗa avǝɗna, lakuti wiig kǝ ghwatkala, agha da ɓagaan kǝ agajawa sǝrkwai shig hǝkǝrda.”
MAT 26:35 Aiyam nǝ Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Aanji ǝn da ǝmtsǝg ǝmtaɗ dǝ kǝgha, ǝn da maay ɓagaan kǝ agajawa sǝra kǝgh biya.” Tagarar bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ mbǝrzah baɗǝmma.
MAT 26:36 Kaa dagal kǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan damma Getsamani, aiymaa taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Ndzamandzǝg vaakwana, ǝn dagal da dzǝgwazhigǝl vaakwaha.”
MAT 26:37 Kaa ba dagal kǝ iin dǝ Bitrus ard zarha Zabadi buwa, ngal mbǝkǝnmbǝga dlaɓa kaa badza ǝrviɗmahuud kǝ iina.
MAT 26:38 Amaa dlaɓ taa kǝ iitǝra, “Badzǝga ǝrvidmahuɗǝn ǝn dǝvakai naina, anǝgha ba tsakwitsǝga. Ndzamandzǝg vaakwana, uufamuufǝg ǝmtaɗ dǝ kaiya.”
MAT 26:39 Gavǝt ba nǝ iin dagal da tǝvuukw hǝɗiikǝna, ngal tsǝɗi kǝ iin kǝ ghǝraan damma haay dzǝgwa kǝ zhigǝla, amaa, “Daadara, akwama ɓagaaɓaga, kǝswaarakǝssǝg kǝ kwanǝn kuwa dlaɗa, bakǝvakwaha, gat bi kǝ dǝgiti ǝn naag nai biya, bamma dǝgiti agha naag nǝnnga.”
MAT 26:40 Sagha ba nǝ iin savak mbǝrzahaana, tlatǝra hǝna haara, amaa taa kǝ Bitrusa, “Mbats am uufǝgabi kǝ dǝga aau pal ǝmtaɗ dǝ kai biya.
MAT 26:41 Uufamuufǝga am dzǝgwaan dlaɓ kǝ zhigǝl haik dagau kǝskuram damma fǝshiga, shiɗǝkw naagaana, vǝgh wa ɗǝmɗǝma.”
MAT 26:42 Kaa gwiya dagal kǝ iin kǝ dǝga buwa, dzǝgwa kǝ zhigǝl amaa, “Daadara akwama da ghudkwaarabi nǝ wan kǝ dlaɗ bamma hǝɓanuuhǝɓǝga, aandzandzǝg bat naagagha.”
MAT 26:43 Gwiyaghǝra ba nǝ iin saasa, tlatǝra ba hǝna haara, Aɗaba haar wa ma gyiyaatǝra.
MAT 26:44 Kaa gwiya ɗutǝrǝsɗuug kǝ Yesu, ngal ba gwiya dagal da dzǝgwazhigǝl kǝ dǝga hǝkǝrɗa, kaa gwiya tagaan kǝ iin kǝ ǝlbǝgi tagada nǝ iin wura.
MAT 26:45 Kaa saas kǝ iin da vak mbǝrzahaan amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gwaastǝn am badlaɓ ba hǝnahaar am ɗiya kuɗga? Wa ɓagaaɓag ci nǝ sart kwada vǝlav nǝ Zǝra Uuda damma dǝv kǝ yaa dadda haipa.
MAT 26:46 Ciyamciiga, jiyam dagala. Wa sǝghaasǝg nǝ dadda vǝla kaiya.”
MAT 26:47 Ba ndzǝgaan Yesu ba taa ghaiya, ka sagau kǝ Yahuda pall ma kǝlaawa tar buwna, ǝmtaɗ dǝ dzahava dlamaa kǝlaaw baɗyak dǝ katsakarah ard dǝ zadaha, ɓǝlartǝr nǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsauuf ard dǝ tlǝvuukwaha.
MAT 26:48 Aɗaba tagatǝrdatag daddakwa da vǝlgaanǝn kǝ dǝga sǝrgi da marg nǝ iin taakiya, “Dadda kwanda ɓǝrhug nai na, iin nǝ uuda nǝ iin viyamviiga.”
MAT 26:49 Bad saasaana, kaa dagau kǝ iin da tǝvǝgh kǝ Yesu amaa taa kǝ iina, “Uus, dadda tsaga dǝgita!” Kaa bǝrhugaan kǝ Yahuda.
MAT 26:50 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Tsaghwa, ɓag kǝ dǝgiti aa sǝkadsǝga.” Kaa sagau kǝ uudahiin, ar viyit kǝ Yesu ar hǝkynana.
MAT 26:51 Nǝghǝgha ba nǝ pal ma lii ǝmtaɗ dǝ Yesu ǝntkwaha, ngal tǝɗda kǝ katsakaraan ghudarda kǝ hyimmi kǝ kwatnaha maal ba tingting ma zhiila kǝsauufaha.
MAT 26:52 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Gwidǝmgwiig kǝ katsakaragh damma kumbǝghaana, aɗaba baɗǝm daddakwa tǝɗda katsakara, da tsǝg ba katsakara.
MAT 26:53 Mam tlǝg nǝ uuram ǝn ɗahgant bi kǝ Daadar, tlǝgwadi ba watswats kǝ zarha ɓǝlg kwa juujig kǝ dakwala tlaujah kǝlaawa tar bu biya?
MAT 26:54 Ai ci tsaa, da righav ndandar wa tagada nǝ Əlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl vindavindan taaki ba pakat wanǝn kǝ dǝgit dzǝgardzǝgi?”
MAT 26:55 Ma kwahiin kǝ sarta amaa taa kǝ uudahiina, “Amaa sagau dǝ katsakarah ard dǝ zadah da viya kai bandgi ǝn dadda zaa ɗuula? Ba kǝla hǝnnga ǝn bamma gaagazaiya Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl ǝn tsaga dǝgita, viyamkwa biya.
MAT 26:56 Baɗǝm wanahaan dzǝghaar ba kiyava righa dǝgiti vindara nǝ tlayanngah ma Əlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl vindavindana.” Cinngaraba nǝ mbǝzahaan kwanǝnna, kaa ta dagalaatǝr kǝ iitǝr baɗǝm ar ɗuwarsa.
MAT 26:57 Kaa lanngaan kǝ lii viyarǝt Yesu dagal da vak Kayafa, zhiila kǝsauuf maamaala, vakavaki dzaharvǝt nǝ maalaha lii tsaga adzahadzah ard tlǝvuukwaha.
MAT 26:58 Kaa gatǝrgatǝg kǝ Bitrus mahal mahal ba bitky tangw dat ghaiya wakyagha zhiila kǝsauuf maamaala, kaa daas kǝ iin damma gaagazayan cihura ǝmtaɗ dǝ lii uufa wakyagh kiyava vaza dǝgiti da dzǝgardzǝga
MAT 26:59 Kaa ba gata shiidaha fiid kwada tagav tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu nǝ zhiila kǝsauufah maamaal ard lii ma gyiɗ baɗǝmma, kiyava tsǝgaan kǝ iitǝra.
MAT 26:60 Tlarkǝna biya, bakǝvakwaha mǝng nǝ kyalma uudah ba ɗyak sarǝv sa ɓa shiida fiida. Tǝhalakwaha kaa sagau kǝ uudah buwa
MAT 26:61 aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Kwan kǝ uuda wa taga taaki, ‘Ən dlagnadlag kǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, ǝn gwiya ndǝrǝt bamma hǝng hǝkǝrɗa.’ ”
MAT 26:62 Kaa ciig kǝ maal ba tingting ma zhiila kǝsauufaha, amaa taa kǝ Yesu, “Agha maay dǝ ǝlbǝg biya? Shiidǝn tag nǝ uudahaan tǝghǝr kǝskǝghǝnmi?”
MAT 26:63 Mbǝɗabi Yesu kǝ ghaiyaan biya. Aiyam maal ba tingting ma zhiila kǝssauufah taa kǝ iina, “Aɗabad Daadamazhigǝl kwad shifǝga, tagkǝmndtag akwama kǝgh Kǝristi, Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla.”
MAT 26:64 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Band kwagha tagda nǝnnga. Ən tagkurtag baɗǝmma, ciigǝt ndakwana am da nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ Zǝra Uuda cihurgan tǝ dǝvaa kafa Dadda Ndzǝɗa, sii ma akumba zhigǝla.”
MAT 26:65 Kaa tahdatahǝg kǝ maal ba tingting ma zhiila kǝsauufah kǝ sǝɗavaan mbakyarvad badzǝga ǝrviɗmahuuɗ amaa, “Badzadabadzǝg kǝ ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝla! Kwar kaci kǝ shiid wa kiyam gwiya naag nǝmyami? Amaa cinngacinng aa badza ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 26:66 Au wamaa nǝghǝga nǝ uurami?” Kaa ngugangug kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Tlaltlǝg maa tsǝvana!”
MAT 26:67 Kaa tafgarvatafǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ ashaghwvai ma huɗvǝga, ar dlaghara kǝ tsǝga, ar ɓalara kǝ mahupennga,
MAT 26:68 ar taakiya, “Tagkǝmndtag kǝ tlayanngǝra, akwama ba kǝgh nǝ Kǝristiya, tag kǝ dadda kwa tsaktsǝga!”
MAT 26:69 Ma kwaniin kǝ sarta, ndza cihurgan ma gaagazaya hǝnnyahiina Bitrusa, kaa sagau nǝ dǝghwiin ɓatlǝr hǝnyahiin da vakaan amaa taa kǝ iina, “Abi ghǝravagh ndakwi agha ǝmtaɗ dǝ Yesu uuda Galilin!”
MAT 26:70 Kaa ɓala gajau kǝ Bitrus tǝvuukwatǝr baɗǝmma, amaa, “Ən sǝrgabi nai kǝ dǝgiti agha tag nǝng tǝghǝr biya.”
MAT 26:71 Saal ba nǝ iin samma bǝrcama, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg nǝ dughwi tlǝrǝn kwa ɓa tlǝr ma hǝnyahiina, amaa taa kǝ lii ghacga vaakwahiina, “Kwanǝn kǝ uud araa ndzaa ǝmtaɗ dǝ Yesu uuda Nazarat!”
MAT 26:72 Kaa gwiya ɓala agajau kǝ Bitrus baz zaha ngwaɗǝg taakiya, “Ən sǝrga bi var kǝ uudanǝn biya.”
MAT 26:73 Tǝhala zǝlam ba hǝɗikǝna, kaa sagau kǝ lii ghacga vaakwahiin davak Bitrusa, am nǝ iitǝra, “Ba pakat kǝgh ndakwani agha pal nǝng ma iitǝr yaana. Ghayi agha tag nǝng wa markadamarǝga.”
MAT 26:74 Ngal farzha kǝ tlafa ghǝraana, ndaha ngwaɗǝga, taakiya, “Ən sǝrgai var kǝ uudanǝn biya.” Tǝhala kwaha kaa wiig kǝ ghwatkala.
MAT 26:75 Kaa dzamnadzamǝg Bitrus kǝ ǝlbǝgi tagghar Yesu taakiya, “Lakuti wiig nǝ ghwatkal hinana, agha da ɓagaan kǝ agajawa sǝrkwai shig hǝkǝrɗa.” Kaa dagal kǝ Bitrus da gyimal ngal tuug kǝ iin ba vaivaiya.
MAT 27:1 Wura ba kǝssa, kaa ɗǝya sawariya tsa Yesu kǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsauufa ard tlǝvuukwaha dlamaa kǝlaawa badǝmma.
MAT 27:2 Ar ngwaɗarna kǝ dǝva, kaa langan kǝ iitǝr dagala, ar vǝlar kǝ gumna Bilatus.
MAT 27:3 Nǝghǝgha ban Yahud kwa vǝlǝt Yesu taakiya, ghudavardaghudǝg shariya ǝmtsǝg kǝ Yesu, kaa mbǝkǝnmbǝg ma ǝrviɗya, ngal daas kǝ iin davak lii maamal ma zhiila kǝsauufah ard tlǝvuukwaha, gwitǝrdan kǝ sǝl kul hǝkǝrɗa adawanǝn cauwa nǝ iinna.
MAT 27:4 Amaa, “Ɓaganaɓag kǝ haipa kwa vǝlanǝt nai kǝ dadda kwa maay dǝ haipǝn kiyava tsǝgga.” Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Au lambamǝndi? Waigagh kǝskǝgha.”
MAT 27:5 Ɗiida kǝ iin kǝ kwaɓa adawanǝn ma Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, ngal dagal hǝrtǝt kǝ ghǝraana.
MAT 27:6 Ar cagant maalaha zhiila kǝsauufahǝn kǝ kwaɓǝna, amaa nǝ iitǝra, “Dzah laɓa kwaɓiin dǝ kwaɓ Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, aɗaba kwaɓa avǝza.”
MAT 27:7 Kaa ɗiya sawari kǝ iitǝr tǝghǝr kwaɓiina, ar sǝgwa kǝ vakavak vak lii ndǝra shakka, aɗaba nal kǝ vaka hǝɗa zǝr ndzǝgaha.
MAT 27:8 Kwakyarvad kwan wa ɗahav nǝ iin gwastaan dǝ vaka avǝzna.
MAT 27:9 Tǝdvad kwan wa righavant nǝ dǝgiti tagada nǝ tlaiyanng Irmi taakiya, “Kǝsavantkǝsǝg nǝ sǝl kwul hǝkǝrɗa adawana, kwaɓi haiyarant nǝ uudaha Israil kǝ ɗiigaan tǝ iina.
MAT 27:10 Ar sǝgwa kǝ vakavaka vak lii ndǝra shak dǝ vakaiya, bandkwa tagghwa Yaazhigǝla.”
MAT 27:11 Ma sartǝn ghacgan nǝ Yesu tǝvuukwa gumna, kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ gumǝn taakiya, “Kǝgh nǝ tlǝkessa Yahudaha?” Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Bandkwa agha tagda nǝnnga.”
MAT 27:12 Kaa ghwadgarnǝs ǝlbǝg kǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsauufah ard tlǝvuukwaha, tagatǝr bi nǝ Yesu aanji ndau biya.
MAT 27:13 Aiyam nǝ Bilatus taa kǝ iina, “Agha cinnga bi kǝ ǝlbǝgahaan ar tag nǝ iitǝr tǝghǝr kǝskǝghǝn biya?”
MAT 27:14 Ngughara bi Yesu kǝ ndavǝg aanji pal biya, kaa ba ɓa jappǝr kǝ gumǝn ba vaivaiya.
MAT 27:15 Ma kwar kǝ sarta Hwaɗaga Haarakǝsa Dzava Hǝnyaha, nǝtnǝg gumǝn kǝ ɓǝla uud pal sagal ma guda bǝrfin kwa naag nǝ uudaha.
MAT 27:16 Ma kwahiin kǝ sart ndza mǝng nǝ ɛɛvya kwa sǝrvasǝrg ba vaivai ma guda bǝrfin ɗaagaan Barabbas.
MAT 27:17 Dzaharvǝt ba dlamaa kǝlaawa, kaa ba ndavtǝrundavǝg kǝ Bilatus taakiya, “War wam naag nǝ uuram ǝn ɓǝlkurǝsi? Barabbas nii Yesu kwa ɗahav dǝ Kristiyinhi?”
MAT 27:18 Aɗaba sǝrghaakasǝrǝg Bilatus taakiya kwakyarvad shilǝg wa vǝlarda nǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu.
MAT 27:19 Cihurgan tǝ avǝda ta shari Bilatusa, kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg nǝ uusaan kǝ ghaiya amaa, “Aa tap bi kǝ uuda jiijiirǝn biya, aɗaɓa mbakwambǝg nǝ dlaɗ ma sǝng haniin tǝghǝr kǝ iina.”
MAT 27:20 Kaa shahtǝrshahǝg kǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsuufah kǝ dlamakǝlaaw aa tagartag taakiya aa ɓǝlvarsɓǝlǝg nǝ Barabbas, aa tsǝvatsǝg nǝ Yesu.
MAT 27:21 Kaa gwiya tagtǝrtag kǝ gumnǝn taakiya, “Kwar ma uudahaan buna wam naag nǝ uuram ǝn ɓǝlkurnǝsi?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝra “Barabbas.”
MAT 27:22 Aiyam nǝ Bilatus taa kǝ iitǝra, “Auci wanda ɓag nai dǝ Yesu kwa ɗahav dǝ Kǝristini?” Kaa ngugangug kǝ iitǝr baɗǝm taakiya, “Aa hǝrtǝvǝthǝrtǝga!”
MAT 27:23 Am nǝ Bilatusa, “Kwakyarvad auwi? Au nǝ haipi aa ɓaga nǝ iini?” Bakǝvakwaha, gwiya fararaa bad fǝg nǝ uudah kǝ ɗiya cauwa, ar taakiya, “Aa hǝrtǝvǝthǝrtǝga!”
MAT 27:24 Nǝghǝgha ba nǝ Bilatus taakiya maay nǝ dǝgiti da ɓagaɓag nǝ iin biya, dlaɓa uudaha ar naa ciya jaaga, kaa gǝt kǝ iin kǝ yu barda kǝ dǝvahaan tǝvuukwa uudaha, amaa, “Zhigǝlaa dǝvar ma kunngya, tlǝkwibi nǝ avǝza uuda jiijiirǝn biya. Ba kwa vakaruci waha.”
MAT 27:25 Kaa ngugangug kǝ uudah baɗǝmma, am nǝ iitǝra, “Dǝgshiga avǝzaana aa dǝg damma kungyamnda ard zarhamnda!”
MAT 27:26 Kaa ɓǝltǝrnǝsɓǝlǝg kǝ iin kǝ Barabbas. Tǝhalakwa dlaghavaru kiiɓ kǝ Yesu, vǝlda kǝ iin kiyava hǝrtǝvǝta.
MAT 27:27 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa langaan kǝ tlaujaha gumǝn damma gaagazaiya vǝgya gumna, ar dzaharaa kǝ dakwala tlaujah baɗǝm da tǝghǝr kǝ iina,
MAT 27:28 ar sǝɗardan kǝ sǝɗava, ar tsugɗǝm ma sǝɗav kyang hulfa dǝga tlǝksaha.
MAT 27:29 Ar ɓagara kǝ dzakwa kwarǝg dǝ dǝga taka, ar farǝm maghǝra, ar faraa kǝ hǝkya zad ma dǝvaa kafaana, tǝhalakwaha ar kǝla kǝ ghunj tǝvuukwan ar nenigaan ar taakiya, “Kǝm ma barkagh tlǝksa Yahudaha!”
MAT 27:30 Ar tafarva kǝ ashaghwvaiya, ar cauwarva kǝ zadiina, kaa kalgaan kǝ iitǝr dǝ zad maghǝra.
MAT 27:31 Ghyǝngara ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ nenigaana, ar sǝɗardan kǝ sǝɗavǝn kyangna, ar tsugwardǝm kǝ sǝɗavahaana. Kaa langaan kǝ iitǝr kiyava hǝrtǝga.
MAT 27:32 Ar tǝghǝrdǝga dagala, kaa fadzaghǝr kǝ iitǝr dǝ zhiila Sayirin, ɗaagaan Siman, kaa fǝraafǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝsa tlaɓa hǝrta Yesu bad ndzǝɗa.
MAT 27:33 Daral ba nǝ iitǝr da vakavaki ɗahav dǝ Golgota, dǝgiti tuukvakai nǝ Golgota, iin kuwa ghǝra.
MAT 27:34 Kaa vǝlgarvǝlǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ yuwa inabi laɓalaɓan dǝ dǝgit ɗyahɗyaha kiyava hǝɓgaana, tapghana ba nǝ iina, lǝwa kǝ hǝɓgaana.
MAT 27:35 Hǝtaret ba nǝ iitǝra, kaa ba tagwnatagw kǝ iitǝr kǝ sǝɗavahaan tǝdvad tsa tsatsa.
MAT 27:36 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa cahwarga cahwarǝg kǝ iitǝr vaakwahiin ar uufǝgaana.
MAT 27:37 Kaa bǝgǝtbǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ haipaan vindavindan tǝvaghǝraan taakiya, “KWANA IIN NƏ YESU TLƏKSA YAHUDAHA.”
MAT 27:38 Kaa hǝtǝvǝthǝrtǝg dlaɓ nǝ gǝlah bu ǝmtaɗ dǝ iina, pal tǝ dǝvaa kafaana, pal tǝ dǝvaa ghyaɓaana.
MAT 27:39 Uudahi ar tǝ ɗuula dagala ar nenigaana, ar gajaga ghǝra,
MAT 27:40 ar taakiya, “Kǝghi tagh taakiya agha dlagnadlag kǝ Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl agha gwiya ndǝrǝt bamma hǝng hǝkǝrɗa, katǝgci kǝ ghǝragha, akwamma agha ba zǝra Daadamazhigǝla, asǝgci saay tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝgǝn ndana!”
MAT 27:41 Nenner bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsauufaha ard lii tsaga adzahadzaha Muusa ard tlǝvuukwaha, ar taakiya,
MAT 27:42 “Katghantkatǝg kǝ uudahi tlǝrna, pilgharvaapilǝg kata ghǝraana. Akwama ba iin nǝ tlǝksa yaa Israˈila, aa sasǝgci saay ndan tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝgna, lakwti kǝmnda fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg dǝ iina
MAT 27:43 Tsaghǝr tǝ Daadamazhigǝl tsauwa, aa katǝgci nǝ Daadamazhigǝl ndakwana, akwama ba naagaana, aɗaba tagadatag taakiya, ‘Ən Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla.’ ”
MAT 27:44 Bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ gǝlah buna kwa hǝrtavtǝrǝt ǝmtaɗ dǝ iina, ghǝravatǝr ndakwani nenǝrnenga.
MAT 27:45 Ciigǝt dǝ vaci tǝghǝra, tangw damma karfe hǝkǝrɗa hwaasa, hǝɗgharduhǝɗǝg nǝ gurtl kǝ lard baɗǝmma.
MAT 27:46 Tamaha karfe hǝkǝrɗa faciya hwaasa kaa dzǝghantdzǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ ghaiya, amaa, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” Iin taakiya, “Daadamazhigǝlara, Daadamazhigǝlara, fiighkwada kwakyarvadawi?”
MAT 27:47 Cinngaraba nǝ kyalma uudahi ghaciga vaakwahiin ǝndkwaha, am nǝ iitǝra, “Iliya wa ɗaag nǝ uudanǝnna.”
MAT 27:48 Bat watswatsǝra kaa ǝmndǝrg kǝ pallǝraatǝra sǝdaa kǝ abarabara, rǝmndaa kǝ iin ma yuwa zǝra inabi kwarekreka, fǝt tǝ zad vǝlar kiyava hǝɓga.
MAT 27:49 Am kyalma, “Ɗuwamarsɗuug ndana, vaziyamvazǝg mbatak da sii nǝ Iliya da katǝgaana.”
MAT 27:50 Kaa gwiya dzǝgantdzǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ ghai bad halavuuwa ndzǝɗaana, tǝhalakwaha vǝlda kǝ shifǝgaana.
MAT 27:51 Bamma kwahiin kǝ sart wa tǝhǝm ɓǝlɛɓǝlɛ kwama Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl hutsǝg buwa, ciigǝt maghǝr damma suuha. Kaa gajagav kǝ haaya, akurah dlaɓa caɓaracaɓǝga.
MAT 27:52 Kaa wargǝtwarǝg kǝ gǝtlaha, baɗyak nǝ uudaha jiijiiri ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝga, ciyarǝtciig dǝ shifǝga,
MAT 27:53 saharalsahǝg ma gǝtlahaatǝra. Tǝhala ciiga Yesu ma gǝtlaha kaa daas kǝ iitǝr damma gǝdǝrkǝs caccuwanacaccuwana, nǝghartǝrnǝghǝg nǝ uudah baɗyaka.
MAT 27:54 Ma sartǝn nǝghǝgha nǝ tlauja Roma maamaalǝn ard lii uufa Yesu kǝ gajagava haaya ard dǝgiti dzǝghaardzǝg baɗǝmma, kaa gǝdzǝg kǝ iitǝr ba vaivaiya, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Ba pakata, ndza Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla!”
MAT 27:55 Mǝng dlaɓ nǝ kyalǝma ǝngwasah baɗyak kwa gatar Yesu kǝsantaan ma Galili ar ba mǝlgarumǝlga. Kaa ghacigaghacig kǝ iitǝr ba ndzaɗɗa, ar vaza dǝgiti dzǝgaardzǝga
MAT 27:56 Ma iitǝra mǝng nǝ Maryam Magadala, ard Maryam babba Yakuba ard Isuvu, dlaɓa ard babba zarha Zabadi.
MAT 27:57 Ɓǝlaa ba hwaasa, kaa sagau kǝ dadda hyahiina, zhiil Arimatiya, ɗaagaana Isuvu, gharavaan ndakwani mbǝrza Yesu.
MAT 27:58 Kaa dagau kǝ iin davak Bilatus da ghala tluuwa vǝgha Yesu. Ngal ba vǝlgavǝlǝg nǝ Bilatus kǝ ɗuula kǝsgaana.
MAT 27:59 Kaa kǝsgantkǝsǝg nǝ Isuvu kǝ tlǝwa vǝgha Yesu, faɗant ma kǝlpakan kwal laliya.
MAT 27:60 Fǝdǝm kǝ iin ma daala gǝtlaana, kwa hurghana nǝ iin ma kura. Hǝɗardu kǝ iin kǝ ghaiya gǝtliin dǝ maandala akura, kaa ba dagalaana.
MAT 27:61 Maryam Magadala, ard kwa pal kǝ Maryam ar cuhurgan ba gyakaɗ dǝ gǝtliina.
MAT 27:62 Wurga kǝsaana, tǝhala Faciya Ɓadlavǝgha kaa dzahvǝtdzahǝg nǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsauufah ard Farisah tǝvuukwa Bilatus,
MAT 27:63 Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Kǝm ma barkagha. Dzamamndnadzamǝg kǝ dǝgiti taga dadda vala uudǝn sarta kwan ndza dǝ shifǝg nǝ iin amaa, ‘Ən da ciig dǝ shiifǝg tǝhala hǝng hǝkǝrɗa.’
MAT 27:64 Mbakyarvad kwaha, fǝtǝraafǝg kǝ uudah da uufa gǝtlǝn ba vaivaiya tangw dat hǝng hǝkǝrɗa, haik kǝ dagal kǝ mbǝrzahaan da ghǝla tluuwa vǝghaana, aɗaba ar da tagtǝrtag kǝ uudah taaki ciyitciig ma gǝtlaha. Valga hala da jǝguujig kǝ valga zǝngw ba vaivaiya.”
MAT 27:65 Aiyam Bilatus taa kǝ iitǝra, “Dzǝgamǝtdzǝg kǝ tlaujaha, damdǝg da uufǝgaana, ɓagamɓag kǝlaa ndzǝɗaruwa.”
MAT 27:66 Kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr da uufa gǝtliina, ar tsǝt kǝ dǝga sǝrga tlǝkǝs tǝ akura gǝtliina, dlaɓa ar fǝtǝraa kǝ tlaujah kǝ uufǝgaana.
MAT 28:1 Dal ba faciya ngiiga Yahudaha, daghuvala laad ba wur kǝsa, kaa dagal kǝ Maryam Magdaliya ard kwa pallǝn kǝ Maryam da zhara gǝtla.
MAT 28:2 Kaa gajagvǝtgajag haay baɗyakɗyaka, aɗaba zǝr ɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝl wa sahi ma zhigǝl da tlǝgarwa akurǝn kwa hǝɗavardu dǝ gǝtlna, cihura tǝvakaiya.
MAT 28:3 Ndzǝganan mbiig band wukyiɗǝga. Sǝɗavaan maɗǝkw ba tǝll band tluuzha.
MAT 28:4 Nǝghǝghara ba lii uufǝgaana, kaa gǝdzgǝtgǝdzǝg kǝ iitǝr ba vaivaiya, tǝg nǝ vǝghaatǝra, ar mbǝɗa damma haay bandgi ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝga.
MAT 28:5 Am Zǝr ɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝlǝn taa kǝ ǝnghwasahaana, “Gǝdzam biya, ǝn sǝrgasǝrǝg am gata Yesu kwa hǝrtavǝtta.
MAT 28:6 Maay vaakwan biya, ciyitciiga band kwa tagada nǝ iina, wan vakavaki hǝnngavna nǝ iina.
MAT 28:7 Damdǝg ba watswatsa tagamtǝrtag kǝ mbǝrzahaan taakiya, ‘Ciyitciig ma gǝtlaha, wada dǝgaa nǝ iin tǝghǝr kǝskuram damma Galili, am da nǝghǝga vaakwaha.’ Əna sǝgga bak tagkur kwanǝnna.”
MAT 28:8 Kaa hadzala dagal kǝ ǝngwasahiin vaka gǝtliina, gǝdzarǝtgǝdzǝga bakǝvakwaha ar dlaig ba vaivaiya, kaa ǝmdǝra daas kǝ iitǝr ar tagtǝr kǝ mbǝrzaha Yesu.
MAT 28:9 Kaa tlǝtǝraatlǝg kǝ Yesu bad ghǝraana, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gabǝr tǝghǝr kǝskurama!” Kaa gavva daas kǝ iitǝr ba mbɛɛv da tǝvǝgh kǝ iina, ngal bǝrhwa shigahaan kǝ iitǝr ar ɓagarnǝs kwatnaha.
MAT 28:10 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gǝdzam biya. Damdǝg tagamtǝrtag kǝ zaraabahar aa dardǝg damma Galili, ar da nǝghǝkwa vaakwaha.”
MAT 28:11 Ar tǝghǝrdǝga daas nǝ ǝnghwasahiina, kaa daas kǝ kyalǝma lii uufa gǝtlahǝn damma kǝssa, kaa tagtǝrtag kǝ iitǝr kǝ dǝgiti dzǝghaardzǝg baɗǝm kǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsauufaha.
MAT 28:12 Dzahavǝt ba nǝ maalah ma zhiila kǝsauufah ard tlǝvuukwaha dlamaa kǝlaawa, kaa ɗǝya sawari kǝ iitǝr ar vǝltǝr kǝ kwaɓ baɗyak kǝ tlaujaha.
MAT 28:13 Aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Tagamtǝrtag kǝ uudah taaki, ‘Mbǝrzahaan wa ghǝlarda kavǝɗ ma sarta kwa tsakǝmnda haara.’
MAT 28:14 Aanji dǝm nǝ ǝlbǝgǝn damma hyǝmmi kǝ gumna, kǝm da tagartag nǝmnd kǝ ǝlbǝga, am da maay hǝɓa dlaɗ biya.”
MAT 28:15 Kaa caugacaug kǝ tlaujah kǝ kwaɓiina, ar tagda band kwaa tagavtǝra. Kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, gwastaan ar ba kutgaan Yahudaha.
MAT 28:16 Kaa dagal kǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝlaawa tǝmkikǝn damma Galili, damma aghwǝn tagatǝr nǝ Yesu taaki aa dzarghǝradzǝga.
MAT 28:17 Nǝghara ba nǝ iitǝra, kaa ɓagar kwatnahǝr kǝ iitǝra, bakǝvakwaha, kyalmatǝr ɓagar ndaundauwa.
MAT 28:18 Kaa saas kǝ Yesu sa tǝvǝgh kǝ iitǝr amaa, “Vǝlghwavǝlǝg nǝ uud kǝ ndzǝɗ baɗǝm ma ghǝrazhigǝla ard duniya.
MAT 28:19 Mbakyarvad kwaha, damdǝg namtǝrdanǝg kǝ uudaha duni kǝ mbǝzahar baɗǝmma, am ɓagtǝra kǝ tsuufǝg ma ɗaaga Daada, ma ɗaaga Zǝra, ard Shiɗkw Daadamazhigǝla.
MAT 28:20 Tsagamtǝrtsag kǝ dǝgitahi tagankur nai baɗǝm aa faraarafǝga. Ba pakata ǝn ba ǝmtaɗ dǝ kuram ba kǝlaa hǝnnga tangwa damma ghyinnga zamana.”
MAR 1:1 Kwanǝnna iin nǝ ǝlbǝg maraw tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu Kǝristi, Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla.
MAR 1:2 Bandkwa fǝgharzha nǝ tlayang Ishay kǝ vindǝgaan ma kakkaɗaan taakiya, “Am Daadamazhigǝla, ‘Ənda ɓǝlgaan kǝ zǝr ɓǝlgar kiyava ɓadlak ɗuul lakuti aghada saaya.’
MAR 1:3 Uudana ɓǝla tlǝhǝg ma tǝghala taakiya, ‘Ɓadlamarnaɓadlǝg kǝ ɗuulaan kǝ Yaazhigǝl ba ndǝɗɗa.’ ”
MAR 1:4 Tsugwa ba nǝ Yuhwan dadda tsufǝg ma tǝghala, kaa tagtǝr ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl kǝ uudaha. Amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, pǝlampǝlǝg kǝ ghǝra ɓag kura nǝ uud kǝ tsuufǝga, dlaɓa ɓǝshkurna Daadamazhigǝl kǝ haipaharuwa.
MAR 1:5 Kaa ba sagau kǝ uudah baɗyak ma haiya Yahudiya, ard uudah ma kǝssa Wurshalim da vak Yuhwana. Ar tagaan kǝ haipahatǝra, ɓagtǝra kǝ iin kǝ tsuufǝg ma zaagha Judan.
MAR 1:6 Sǝɗavi tsuguv Yuhwan ɓagava dǝ guja adlǝgwama. Dǝga ndzǝɗa huɗaana ɓagava dǝ hǝluwa, dlaɓa dǝga zǝgaana, ndzaba ayayuwa ard yuwa mamma.
MAR 1:7 Kaa tagtǝrtag kǝ iin kǝ uudah taakiya, “Daddakwa da sagau tǝ halara jakwaraajig dǝ ndangǝra, kwa tlanalbi nai kǝ ngǝghrangǝg da pǝla aanji zawwa kimbakaan biya.
MAR 1:8 Kai ǝn ɓagkur dǝ yu kǝ tsuffǝga, iina da ɓagkur dǝ Shǝɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl kǝ tsuffǝga.”
MAR 1:9 Makwahiin kǝ sarta, sǝghaasǝg nǝ Yesu saama kǝssa Nazarat ma haaya Galili. Kaa ɓagaraɓag kǝ Yuhwan kǝ tsuffǝg ma zaagha Judan.
MAR 1:10 Bad sagal Yesu ma yuwa, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ ghǝrazhigǝl wurga, dlaɓa kaa tsugwatsugw Shiɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl saay da tǝghǝr kǝ iin band garava kakura.
MAR 1:11 Kaa cinngalcinng nǝ kungy sii ma ghǝrazhigǝl taakiya, “Kǝgh zǝrara, ǝn wayakwaig ba vaivaiya.”
MAR 1:12 Zǝlamai tǝhala kwah biya, kaa langaan kǝ Shǝɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl kǝ Yesu damma tǝghala,
MAR 1:13 hǝngaan kwul uufaɗ ba vaakwaha, fǝshgaan Shatanaha. Yesu ndzar ǝmtaɗ dǝ dǝg tǝghalaha, dlaɓa zarha ɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝla sarǝvsǝg da mǝlgarumǝlga.
MAR 1:14 Tǝhalakwa ɓǝlavdǝm Yuhwan ma guda bǝrfina, kaa dagal kǝ Yesu damma Galili taa ǝlbǝg maraw tǝghǝr kǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
MAR 1:15 Amaa, “Ɓagaaɓag sarta. Tlǝkǝsǝra Daadamazhigǝl hǝrzǝthǝrzǝg saaya. Pǝlampǝlǝg kǝ ghǝra, am fǝdghǝrǝt tǝ ǝlbǝg marawǝna.”
MAR 1:16 Ghuda dagal nǝ Yesu tǝvǝgh kǝ yuwahaiya Galili, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ Siman ard zǝrababbaan Andrawus, ar bǝla amshiyaha vaiya kilf ma yuwahaiya aɗaba ar ya dadda vaiya kilf nǝ iitǝra.
MAR 1:17 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gatamkwagatǝga, ǝn da nǝkurdalnǝg kǝ lii ɗaha uudah sa vakara.”
MAR 1:18 Bat watswatsǝra, kaa ɗugarsɗuug kǝ iitǝr kǝ amshiyaha vaiya kilfatǝra, kaa gatǝgaan kǝ iitǝra.
MAR 1:19 Gavǝt ba nǝ iin da tǝvukw hǝɗikǝnana, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ zarha Zabadi, Yakuba ard Yuhwana. Ar ma pɛrayuwa, ar ɓadla amshiyaha vaiya kilfaatǝra.
MAR 1:20 Bat watswatsǝra kaa ɗahtǝrǝt kǝ iina, kaa ɗugarsɗuug kǝ iitǝr kǝ daddaatǝr Zabadi ma pɛrayu ǝmtaɗ dǝ lii hutsarant nǝ iitǝr kǝ ɓa tlǝra, kaa gataa Yesu kǝ iitǝra.
MAR 1:21 Yesu ard lii gatǝgaan daragha damma kǝssa Kafarnahuma. Ɓagaa ba Faciya Ngiiga, kaa daas kǝ iin damma guda dzahava Yahudaha, kaa farzha tsagtǝr dǝgit kǝ uudaha.
MAR 1:22 Kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ iitǝr dǝ tsagaanana, aɗaba tsagatǝr dǝgit ba kalkala, gǝrgǝr dǝ ɗuuli tsag nǝ lii tsaga adzahadzaha Musa.
MAR 1:23 Maay ma taaɗatǝr biya, kaa dǝgaadǝg kǝ uuda nǝ iin kwa dǝ shǝɗǝkw ghwaɗ damma guda dzahava, huulǝg taakiya,
MAR 1:24 “Au lambagh dǝ kǝmnd Yesu Uuda Nazaret? Agha sagau da ghyǝhha kǝmnda? Ən sǝrgasǝrga magha war nǝngnga. Kǝgh daddakwa Caccuwanacaccuwanan sahi vak Daadamazhigǝla.”
MAR 1:25 Kaa cagaraacag nǝ Yesu kǝ gyi kǝ shǝɗǝkw ghwaɗǝna, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Ɗǝw amǝnga. Assagal ma uudanǝna.”
MAR 1:26 Kaa gajagantgajag ba dladlaɗ nǝ shǝɗǝkw ghwaɗǝn kǝ uudanǝna. Kaa huulǝg kǝ iin dlaɓa kaa tsugwa dagalaana.
MAR 1:27 Baɗǝm nǝ uudahi ndzar vaakwahiin ar ɓa jappǝr ba vaivaiya, baz ndava ghǝrahaatǝr kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Au wa nǝ iini? Kwar kǝ daala tsaga dǝgit wanii? Tsaga dǝgit ba kalkala. Baz fǝtǝraafǝg kǝ iin kǝ shǝɗǝkw ghwaɗah kǝ ɓa dǝgiti naag nǝ iina.”
MAR 1:28 Caaricaari nǝghar bak cinngalcinng nǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ iin aanji taakwar mahuɗa haaya Galili.
MAR 1:29 Ba dǝ Sagala Yesu ǝmtaɗ Yakub ar dǝ Yuhwana ma guda dzahava, kaa daas kǝ iitǝr da vǝgyaz Bitrus ar dǝ Andrawus.
MAR 1:30 Babba uusa Bitrus hǝngan njǝkǝn fǝɗa. Bat watswatsǝra, kaa tagartag kǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝra.
MAR 1:31 Kaa dagau kǝ iin da vakaana, hakyǝnan kǝ dǝvaan ciyanta. Kaa ɗugarsɗuug fǝɗiina, tǝhalakwaha bagtǝra nǝ uusǝn kǝ dǝgzǝga.
MAR 1:32 Dǝghwaasa, tǝhala daaya faciya, kaa sǝdǝvsǝg kǝ uudah kǝ lii yangbi baɗǝm ard lii dǝ shǝɗkw ghwaɗ ma vǝghahaatra.
MAR 1:33 Kaa dzahav kǝ lii ma kǝsiin baɗǝm tǝghaiya hǝnyahiina,
MAR 1:34 kaa mbahnambahǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ lii dǝ kuzah shahshaha. Lagudan baz shǝɗǝkw ghwaɗ mavǝgh kǝ uudaha ba ɗyaka. Ɗuwatǝrnai kǝ shǝɗkw ghwaɗah kǝ taaghai biya, aɗaba ar sǝrgasǝrg ghǝravaatǝr taaki ma war nǝ iina.
MAR 1:35 Dlakadur ba wurra, lakuti cag nǝ kǝsa, ciyitciig nǝ Yesu ɗugharsɗuug kǝ hǝnyaha, kaa dagal kǝ iin da vakavaki maay band war biya. Dzugwa kǝ iin kǝ zhigǝl vaakwaha.
MAR 1:36 Kaa dagal kǝ Siman ǝmtaɗ dǝ tsaghwaha dagalaan da gatǝgaana.
MAR 1:37 Tlararaa ba nǝ iitǝra, kaa tagaratag kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Baɗǝm nǝ uudah ar gatakǝgha.”
MAR 1:38 Ngwangwug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Jiyam dagal damma gǝdzǝr kǝssahi kwa hɛffa, kiyava da taa ǝlbǝg maraw kǝskai vaakwah dlaɓa. Aɗaba sanhi mbakyarvad kwah naiya.”
MAR 1:39 Tǝhala kwaha kaa gwaivagwaig kǝ iin baɗǝm ma haaya Galili, taa ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝla ma guda dzahavaatǝra. Lagwdaan dlaɓ kǝ shǝɗkw ghwaɗah ma vǝgha uudaha.
MAR 1:40 Mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin njǝkǝn vǝca sǝv sa vak Yesu, kǝla kǝ iin kǝ ghunja kaa ghalgaan taakiya, “Ma haighanthaiga, agha mbǝkwimbǝgga.”
MAR 1:41 Kaa zhugardaalazhug kǝ Yesu, ɓǝlaraa kǝ dǝva, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Haiyanant haiga, mbambǝgga.”
MAR 1:42 Bat watswatsǝra kaa ɗugarsɗuug kǝ kuza vǝciina, kaa mbǝgambǝg kǝ iina.
MAR 1:43 Kaa ɓǝlgaraɓǝlǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ magiya ba vaivaiya, ɓǝlars kǝ iin dagala.
MAR 1:44 “Tagarbi aanji ndǝwar kǝ dǝgiti aa dzǝgardzǝg biya. Dǝga agha marda kǝ ghǝragh vak zhiil kǝsuufa, agha ɓaga kǝ kyulǝg bandkwa tagada Musa taakiya aa ɓagavɓag mbakyarvad caccuwagha. Ɓagnaɓag kwana kiyava fadghǝr kǝ uudah taakiya mbǝghambǝga.”
