MAR 14:54 Kaa gatǝgaan kǝ Bitrus kǝ Yesu tǝhal tǝhala, ba bǝtky tagwavaatǝra. Gatǝgharsgatǝg ba tangw damma huɗa gaagazaiya vǝgya zhillakǝsuuf ba tingtinga. Cǝhura kǝ iin ǝmtaɗ dǝ lii uuffa hǝnyaha, ɗiira kaara.
MAR 14:55 Gatargatǝg nǝ maalaha ma zhillakǝsuufaha ard gyiɗa maalah badǝm kǝ dǝgiti maraa da tlǝkǝna nǝ iitǝr kǝ shiid tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu taakiya, ɓagaɓag kǝ haipa kiyava tsǝgaan kǝ iitǝra, bakǝvakwaha, viiyarǝti dǝ haip biya.
MAR 14:56 Ghwadararsghwadǝg nǝ uudah ba ɗyak kǝ fiid kǝ Yesu, bakǝvakwaha ndzaabi ghaiyatǝr tǝ dǝgit pal biya.
MAR 14:57 Tǝhalakwaha kaa gwiya ciig kǝ kyǝlǝm uudaha, ar ghwudars kǝ fiid kǝ Yesu taakiya,
MAR 14:58 “Cinngamndacinng tagadatag taakiya, ‘Ən dlagnadlag kǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝlǝn kwa ndǝraran nǝ uudaha, ǝn ndǝrant kwatlǝrǝn bamma hǝng hǝkǝrɗa, kwa ndǝrg uud biya.’ ”
MAR 14:59 Bakǝvakwah ǝlbǝgahaatǝr ndzaabi tǝ dǝgit pal biya.
MAR 14:60 Kaa ciig kǝ maal batinting ma zhillakǝsuufah ghacan mataatakaatǝra, kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg kǝ iin kǝ Yesu, amaa, “Agha maay dǝ ǝlbǝg biya? Əlbǝgahaan aa tagav tǝghǝr kǝskǝgh nǝm?”
MAR 14:61 Bakǝvakwaha mbǝɗabi nǝ Yesu kǝ ghaiyan biya, ndza kǝ iin ba ɗǝwa. Kaa gwiya ndavgarundavǝg kǝ maal batingting ma zhillakǝsuuf taakiya, “Kǝgh haa nǝ Kǝristi, Zǝra Daddakwa dǝ barkna?”
MAR 14:62 Ngwangw nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Aana ba kaiya. Am da nǝghanǝghǝg kǝ Zǝra Uuda ndzǝgan tǝ dǝvaa kaffa Daadamazhigǝl ǝmkyaɗaka, dlaɓa da saay ma akumba zhigǝla.”
MAR 14:63 Kaa tahnatahǝg kǝ maal batingting ma zhillakǝsuuf kǝ sǝɗavahaana, amaa, “Kwar kǝ shiid dlaɓ wa kiyam naag nǝ miyami?
MAR 14:64 Cinngamacing dlaɓa ghǝravaru kǝ badza ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝl aa tag nǝ iina! Auwam nǝ urami?” Kaa ghudgardaghud nǝ uudahi ndzar vaakwahiin baɗǝm kǝ shariya taakiya aa tsǝvatsǝgga.
MAR 14:65 Kaa fǝgarzhafǝg nǝ kyalǝmah kǝ tafgarǝv ashavaiya, ar mbuusaaraka kǝ gyiya, dlaɓa ar dlagharaa kǝ tsǝgga, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Tagga kǝ daddakwa tsakǝgha!” Lii uuffa wakyagh dlaɓa ndakwani kaa kalgaan kǝ iitǝra.
MAR 14:66 Ndza mangyila gaagazaiya hǝnyaha nǝ Bitrusa, kaa sagau kǝ dǝghwiin pal ma kwatnaha maal batingting ma zhiilakǝsuuf da vaakwahiina.
MAR 14:67 Nǝgha ba nǝ iin kǝ Bitrus ɗiira kaara, kaa vazǝgaan kǝ iin ba marawa, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Kǝgh ndakwi agha ǝmtaɗ dǝ Yesu zhilla Nazareta!”
MAR 14:68 Kaa ɓalla gajau kǝ Bitrusa, amaa, “Ən sǝrgabi var kǝ dǝgiti agha tag nǝng biya. Nǝghanaakabi ba lingiling biya!” Tagada ba nǝ iin kǝ kwaha, Kaa ciya dagal kǝ iin damma bǝrcama hǝnyahiina, kaa wiig kǝ ghwatkala tǝhala kwaha.
MAR 14:69 Gwiiya nǝgha ba nǝ dǝghwǝn kǝ Bitrus vaakwaha, kaa tagatǝrtag kǝ iin kǝ lii ghacǝga vaakwahiina, “Kwan ndakwani pal ghǝravaan ma iitǝra.”
MAR 14:70 Kaa gwiiya ɓalla gajau kǝ Bitrus dlaɓa. Tǝhala zǝlam hǝɗiikǝnana, aiyam lii ghacǝga tǝvǝgh kǝ Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Bak jiijiira agha pal nǝng yan miitǝra. Aɗaba agha zhiil Galili nǝ ghǝravagha.”
MAR 14:71 Kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ Bitrus ɗaava ghǝraana, dlaɓa kaa tlafa ghǝran baz ndaha waɗǝg tǝvukwatǝr taakiya. “Ən sǝrgai var kǝ uudanǝn am tag nǝ uuram kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝrǝn biya.”
MAR 14:72 Batwatswatsǝra kaa wiig kǝ ghwatǝkala kǝ dǝga buwa. Kaa dzamnadzamǝg nǝ Bitrus kǝ ǝlbǝgi taghar nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Lakwti wiig nǝ ghwatǝkala shig buwa, agha da ɓallǝgaan kǝ agajauwa sǝrkwabi shig hǝkǝrd biya.” Dzamghana ba nǝ iin kwan kǝ ǝlbǝga. Kaa ɓǝlaru kǝ iin kǝ tuuga.
MAR 15:1 Dlakadur bawura, kaa ɗiya sawari kǝ maalaha zhiil kǝsauufaha, ard tlǝvuukwah ard lii tsaga adzahadzaha Musa, ard dzahava lii ma gyiɗ baɗǝmma. Kaa ngwaɗǝnangwaɗǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu, ar langda da tǝvuukwa Bilatusa, ar fardǝm ma dǝva.
MAR 15:2 Kaa ndavgaruundavǝg nǝ Bilatus kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Kǝgh tlǝkǝssa Yahudaha?” Ngwugharangug Yesu amaa, “Aana, bandkwa tagǝda nǝnga.”
MAR 15:3 Kaa ghwadgarǝva ǝlbǝgah ba ɗyak nǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsauufaha.
MAR 15:4 Kaa gwiya ndavgarundavǝg nǝ Bilatus taakiya, “Agha maay mbǝɗa ghai biya? Cinng kǝ dǝgitahi ar tag nǝ iitǝr tǝghǝr kǝskǝgh ba ɗyaka.”
MAR 15:5 Gwastǝna, mbǝɗabi Yesu kǝ ghaiyan biya, kwana vǝlgharvǝlǝg kǝ Bilatus kǝ dǝga jappǝr.
MAR 15:6 Dǝgiti nǝt tlǝkǝs kǝ ɓagaan sarta hwaɗaga iin taakiya, ɓǝlars kǝ uud palla kwa ghalga nǝ uudah sagal ma guda bǝrfina.
MAR 15:7 Mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin ɗaagaan Barabbas kwa ɓǝlaavdǝm ma guda bǝrfina, ǝmtaɗ dǝ lii dzagwara dlagwam kwa tsara uuda ma sartǝn ciyit nǝ dlagwamǝna.
MAR 15:8 Kaa sagau kǝ dzahava dlamakǝlaaw da ghala Bilatus maa ɓagtǝra kǝ dǝgiti nǝt nǝ iina kǝ ɓagaana.
MAR 15:9 Ngwatǝrangug nǝ Bilatus amaa, “Am naagaan ǝn ɓǝlkurnǝs kǝ tlǝkǝssa Yahudaha?”
MAR 15:10 Aɗaba nǝghaakanǝghǝg nǝ Bilatus taakiya, ba shilǝg wa fatǝra maalah zhiilakǝsauufah kǝ vǝlla Yesu damma dǝvaana
MAR 15:11 Maalaha zhiilakǝsauufah wa shaharant uudah kǝ taakiya aa ɓǝlkǝmndarsɓǝlǝg nǝ uud kǝ Barabaas tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu.
MAR 15:12 Kaa ndavtǝrundavǝg nǝ Bilatus taakiya, “Au kaci wanda ɓag nai dǝ kwam ɗaag nǝ uuram dǝ tlǝkǝssa Yahudahni?”
MAR 15:13 Ar ɗǝyaru kǝ iitǝr kǝ cau ar taakiya, “Aa hǝrtǝvǝthǝrtǝgga!”
MAR 15:14 Aiyam nǝ Bilatus taa kǝ iitǝra, “Mbakyauwi? Au nǝ haipaani?” Ar gwiya dzǝgant kǝ kungy ar taakiya, “Aa hǝrtǝvǝthǝrtǝgga!”
MAR 15:15 Naagaan tsau nǝ Bilatus hǝngtǝrna kǝ ǝrviɗmahuɗaatǝra, ɓǝltǝrnǝs kǝ Barabaas. Tǝhalakwa fǝgharaa nǝ iin kǝ uudah kǝ dlaghgaru kiiɓ kǝ Yesu, kaa vǝltǝr kǝ iin kiyava hǝrtǝgga.
MAR 15:16 Kaa dadǝg nǝ tlaujah kǝ Yesu damma gaagazaiya vǝgya gumna. Ar dzahant kǝ tlaujah baɗǝmma.
MAR 15:17 Ar tsǝgwardǝm kǝ sǝdav kyang hulfa dǝga tlǝkǝssaha, dlaɓa ar ɓagara kǝ dzakwa takka, ar fardǝm ma ghǝra.
MAR 15:18 Ar farzha kǝ tagar uus taakiya, “Kǝm ma barkagh tlǝkǝssa Yahudaha!”
MAR 15:19 Kaa kalgaan kǝ iitǝr dǝ zad ma ghǝra, ar tafarǝva kǝ ashavaiya. Tǝhalakwaha ar kǝlla kǝ ghunj tǝvuukwana am nǝ iitǝra ar fǝgaaradfǝga.
MAR 15:20 Ghyǝngara ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ nenegaana, ar sǝɗarda kǝ sǝɗava tlǝksǝna, ar tsagwɗǝm ma sǝɗavahaana. Tǝhalakwaha ar langda dagal da gyǝmal kiyava hǝrtǝgaana.
MAR 15:21 Ar tǝghǝrdǝga dagala, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ uuda nǝ iin ghwudadagal, kwa ɗahav dǝ Siman, zhiila Sayirina, daddaatǝr kǝ Alekzanda ard Rufus, saas ma gǝdzǝr kǝssa, ar faraa baɗ ndzǝɗ kǝ kǝssa tlaɓa hǝrta Yesu.
MAR 15:22 Ar langda kǝ Yesu da vakavakiin kwa ɗahav dǝ Golgata, (dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ iina “Vakka kuwa ghǝra”).
MAR 15:23 Vǝlarar vaakwahiin nǝ iitǝr kǝ yuwa innabi laɓalaɓan dǝ mur, luwa kǝ hǝɓgaana.
MAR 15:24 Ar hǝrtǝtta. Ar tagwna dlaɓ kǝ sǝɗavahaan ma taatakaatǝra, kaa tsa tsats kǝ iitǝr tǝghǝr kiyava vaza dǝgiti aa tlǝkǝna aanji waratǝra.
MAR 15:25 Hǝrtarǝt ma sarta vaslambaɗa dlakadura.
MAR 15:26 Ar vinda tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝg kǝ ǝlbǝgi ghwudararva nǝ iitǝr taakiya, “TLƏKƏSSA YAHUDAHA.”
MAR 15:27 Ar hǝrtǝt kǝ gǝlah buwa ǝmtaɗ dǝ iina, pal tǝ dǝvaa kaffaana, pal dlaɓ tǝ dǝvaa ghyaɓɓaana. [
MAR 15:28 Kwan iin nǝ righǝgga tlayangǝr kwa tagaa taakiya, “Kǝdlavǝna ma lii haipaha.”]
MAR 15:29 Uudahi ghudadagal ar tagar ǝlbǝga nenega, ar gajaga ghǝr ar taakiya, “Caa! Kǝghi agha dlagǝnadlag kǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, dlaɓa agha da gwiya ndǝrant bamma hǝng hǝkǝrɗa,
MAR 15:30 katǝg ci kǝ ghǝragha, agha sii bi dlaɓ tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝg biya!”
MAR 15:31 Bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ maalah ma zhiilakǝsauufah ard lii tsaga adzahadzaha Musa, kaa nenegaan kǝ iitǝr ma taatakaatǝr ar taakiya, “Katǝghankatǝg kǝ kyalǝma, pilgharvaapilǝg kata ghǝraana!
MAR 15:32 Aa sasii ci ndan Kǝristi tlǝkǝssa Israˈilǝn ndakwan tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝgǝna, kiyava nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝskǝmnd kǝm fǝdghǝrǝta!” Baz gǝlahǝn hǝrtavǝt ǝmtaɗ dǝ iinǝn ndakwani kaa taa ǝlbǝgahi ghwaɗghwaɗ kǝ iitǝr tǝ iina.
MAR 15:33 Bad vacci tǝghǝra, kaa hǝɗgarduhǝɗǝg nǝ gurtl kǝ lard baɗǝma, tangw damma hǝkǝrɗa hwassa.
MAR 15:34 Tǝhalakwaha, sarta hǝkǝrɗa hwaasa, kaa dzagantdzǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ kuungy bad halavuwa ndzǝɗaan, amaa, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” Iin taakiya, “Daadamazhigǝl Daadamazhigǝla, agha fiikwada daɓawi?”
MAR 15:35 Cinngara ba nǝ lii ghaciga vaakwahiin kwaha, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Wai nǝ iin ɗaa tlaiyang Iliya.”
MAR 15:36 Kaa ǝmdǝrǝg kǝ pallǝraatǝra, rǝmda kǝ abarabar dǝ yuwa inabi kwarekreka tǝ zadda, vǝlar kǝ Yesu kiyava hǝɓɓǝga, aiyama, “Vazyamvazǝg ndana! Mbatak da sagau nǝ tlayang Iliya da sii dǝ vakaiya.”
MAR 15:37 Kaa dzǝgantdzǝg Yesu kǝ kungy bad halavuuwa ndzǝɗaana, tǝhalakwaha, kaa ɗiya shifǝgga halavuuwana, ǝmtsana.
MAR 15:38 Kaa tǝhgǝmtǝhǝg kǝ ɓǝlyaɓǝlya Vǝgya Daadamaazhigǝl hutsǝg buwa ciigǝt ma ghǝraan tangw damma suhwaana.
MAR 15:39 Nǝgha ban nǝ tlaujin ndza ghaciga tǝvuukwa Yesu kǝ ɗuuli ǝmtsa nǝ iina, aiyama, “Ba pakat uudanǝn Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla!”
MAR 15:40 Kyalma ǝnghwasaha, ghaccara ba ndzaɗɗa ar vazǝggaana. Ma iitǝra mǝng Maryam Magadala, ard Maryam babba Yakub kudǝrkudǝra ard Isuvuwa, ard Salomi.
MAR 15:41 Gatarars ciigǝt sagat ma Galili nǝ ǝnghwasahaan ar ba mǝlgarumǝlga. Dlaɓa baɗyak nǝ kyalǝma ǝnghwasah kwa darǝt ǝmtaɗ dǝ iin ma Wurshalim ndakwi ndzar ba vaakwaha.
MAR 15:42 Ɗǝm ba faciya hwaasa, kaa ɓadlav kǝ uudaha, aɗaba dlakaduraan Faciya Ngiiga.
MAR 15:43 Kaa sagal kǝ uuda nǝ iin ma Arimatiya ɗaagaan Isuvuwa. Pall ma gyiɗya lii maalmala nǝ iina, dlaɓa fǝvaarafǝga, kwa pakka saaya tlǝkkǝssǝra Daadamazhigǝla. Shughanashug kǝ gyi da vak Bilatus, da ghala ma vǝlvar nǝ tlǝwa vǝgha Yesu.
MAR 15:44 Cinngha ba nǝ Bilatus taakiya ǝmtsaǝmtsǝg nǝ Yesu, vǝlgharvǝlǝg kǝ dǝga ajappǝra. Ɗahant kǝ iin kǝ maala tlaujiin ndavaru taakiya bak jiirjiira ha ǝmtsaǝmtsǝg nǝ Yesu.
MAR 15:45 Cinngha ba nǝ iin vak maala tlaujin taakiya band kwaha, kaa vǝlar kǝ iin kǝ Isuvu kǝ tlǝwa vǝgha Yesu.
MAR 15:46 Kaa sǝgwdaasǝgw nǝ Isuvu kǝ kǝlpakana, sǝddi kǝ iin kǝ tlǝwa Yesu tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝgga, faɗant ma kǝlpakana, fǝdǝm kǝ iin ma gǝtl kwa kwaɗava ma kura. Tǝhala kwaha, hutambardi kǝ akura hǝɗardu kǝ iin kǝ ghaiyan dǝ vakaiya.
MAR 15:47 Nǝghǝranǝghǝg nǝ Maryamu Magadala ard Maryamu babba Isuvu kǝ vakavaki fava dǝ tlǝwa vǝgha Yesu.
MAR 16:1 Dal ba faciya ngiigga, kaa sǝgwasǝgw kǝ Maryam Magadala, ard Maryam babba Yakub, ard Salomi kǝ tǝrshan kiyava dzuupǝg tǝ tlǝwa Yesu.
MAR 16:2 Davala faciya zǝngw ma maaka, kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr damma gǝtlah ba dlakaduur wur kǝssa.
MAR 16:3 Tǝghǝrdǝgga dagala, am nǝ iitǝr mataatakaatǝra, “War wada tlǝkkiyamarwatlǝg kǝ akuriin tuuk kǝ ghaiya gǝtli?”
MAR 16:4 Daragha ba nǝ iitǝr da vaakwahiina, dzǝgarant ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ ghǝraatǝra, kaa nǝghǝganǝgh kǝ iitǝr mbats tlǝgavarwatlǝg nǝ akuriin dagala. Akuriin ndza maanda.
MAR 16:5 Daragha ba nǝ iitǝr damma gǝtliina, kaa nǝghǝgaanǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ daala zǝr tsagwatsagwan ma sǝɗav maɗǝkwa cǝhurga tǝ ghyaɓa dǝvaakaffa, kaa gǝdzǝgǝtgǝdzǝg kǝ iitǝra.
MAR 16:6 Am daala zǝrǝn taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ɓagambi kǝ ajappǝr biya. Am gata Yesu uuda nazare kwa hǝrtavǝtǝna? Abi, ciyitciiga. Maay vaakwan biya. Wan vakavaki hǝngavna nǝ iina.
MAR 16:7 Damdǝga, am tagar kǝ mbǝrzahaana, ard Bitrus, taakiya da dǝga nǝ iin tǝghǝr kǝ iitǝr damma Galili, ar da nǝghǝga vaakwah nǝ iitǝr bandkwa tagatǝr nǝ iina.”
MAR 16:8 Kaa ǝmndǝra saggal kǝ ǝnghwasahahaana, ar ɓa jappǝr dlaɓa tǝg nǝ vǝghatǝra. Tagararbi aanji ndǝwar kǝ ǝlbǝg biya, aɗaba gǝdzarǝtgǝdzǝgga. [
MAR 16:9 Ciyit ba nǝ Yesu ma gǝtlah dlakadur ba wur davala faciya zǝngw ma maaka, marda kǝ ghǝraan ba zǝngw vak Maryamu Magadala, kwa lagwgharda nǝ iin kǝ shatanah uuɗiif ma vǝghaana.
MAR 16:10 Kaa daas kǝ iin tagtǝr kǝ uudahi ndzar ǝmtaɗ ba bawur dǝ iina, lii taa dzǝgwagha ar tuuga.
MAR 16:11 Cinngaraba nǝ iitǝr taakiya dǝ shifǝg nǝ Yesu, dlaɓa nǝghghanǝghǝg nǝ Maryama kǝ iina, fardghǝrǝt biya.
MAR 16:12 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa mbǝɗvǝghambǝɗǝg nǝ ndzǝgana vǝgha Yesu, kaa mardamarǝg kǝ ghǝraan vak mbǝrzah buwa masarta kwa ndzar tǝ ɗuula dagal damma gǝdzǝrkǝsa.
MAR 16:13 Kaa gwiyadaas kǝ lii buna ar tagar kǝ kyalmaha, bakǝvakwaha larwalǝg kǝ fadǝghǝr tǝ ǝlbǝgiina.
MAR 16:14 Tǝhalakwaha, kaa mardamarǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ ghǝran vak kǝlawa tǝmkikǝn ma sarta kwa ndzar za kaffa. Kaa cagtǝraacag kǝ iin kǝ gyi tǝghǝr kǝ maira fadghǝraatǝra ard dǝkdǝka ghǝraatǝra, aɗaba fadghǝrǝtbi dǝ lii nǝgharanǝghǝg tǝhala ciigaan biya.
MAR 16:15 Amaa taa kǝ iitǝr dlaɓa, “Damdǝg damma duni baɗǝmma, tagamtǝrtag kǝ ǝlbǝg maraw kǝ uudah dǝshiga.
MAR 16:16 Baɗǝm daddakwa fadghǝrǝtfǝga, dlaɓa ɓagvara nǝ tsuufǝgga, da tlǝkkǝnatlǝg kǝ katǝgga. Baɗǝm daddakwa fadghǝrǝt biya da vǝlǝvtǝr dlaɗa.
MAR 16:17 Wan nǝ dǝgiti da ɓag lii gata kaiya kiyava marra fadǝghǝratǝra. Ar da lagwan kǝ shatanah ma ɗaagara, ar da tagaan dlaɓa kǝ ǝlbǝg dǝ daala ghaiyaha.
MAR 16:18 Ar da kǝssǝggaan kǝ ghavalah dǝ dǝvahaatǝra. Ma hǝɓaruhǝɓǝg kǝ gurra, maay nǝ dǝgiti da ɓagtǝr nǝ iin biya. Ar da fǝgaan dlaɓa kǝ dǝvahaatǝr tǝ lii yangbiya, ar da mbǝgga.”
MAR 16:19 Tǝhala kwa tagatǝra nǝ Yaazhigǝl Yesu kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, kaa kǝsvantkǝsǝg dǝvdǝt damma ghǝrazhigǝla, ndza kǝ iin tǝ dǝvaa kaffa Daadamazhigǝla.
MAR 16:20 Kaa dagal kǝ mbǝrzahaana, kaa taa ǝlbǝg maraw kǝ iitǝr aanji takwara. Ɓagaɓag nǝ Yaazhigǝl kǝ tlǝr ǝmtaɗ dǝ iitǝra, dlaɓa mara jiira ǝlbǝgahatǝr tǝdvad dǝgaha sǝrgah kwa vǝlla jappǝr fatǝraa nǝ iin kǝ ɓaggaan ǝmtaɗ dǝ ǝlbǝgahiina.]
JOH 1:1 Bamma zunngwura ndza mǝng nǝ ǝlbǝga, ǝlbǝgna ndza ǝmtaɗ dǝ Daadamazhigǝla, ǝlbǝgna Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 1:2 Iin wandza ǝmtaɗ dǝ Daadamazhigǝl bamma zǝnngwura.
JOH 1:3 Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgitah ɓaggava ba tǝdvad iina. Maay nǝ dǝgitahi ɓagavnan kwal tǝdvad iin biya.
JOH 1:4 Əlbǝgǝn iin gyigyiya shifǝga, shifǝgna iin wa vǝlgar parakrakǝr kǝ uudah baɗǝmma.
JOH 1:5 Kwanǝn kǝ parakka ba parakrak ma gurtla, gurtlǝn tsǝgarva bi kǝ parak kǝ ɓa parakrakǝr biya.
JOH 1:6 Ndza mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin ɗahav dǝ Yuhwana kwa ɓǝladi Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 1:7 Sahi sa taggar ǝlbǝg jiir kǝ uudah tǝghǝr kǝ parakna, aɗaba maraa fǝdghǝrǝt nǝ uudah baɗǝmma tǝdvad iina.
JOH 1:8 Yuhwan bi nǝ parakǝn biya, sahi kwakyarvad tagtǝr kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ parakǝn kǝ uudaha.
JOH 1:9 Tagatǝrdagag nǝ Yuhwan taakiya, Parak jiijiira da sii sa ma duniya da vǝltǝr kǝ parak kǝ uudah baɗǝma.
JOH 1:10 Kwanǝn kǝ uuda iin parakka ndza bamma duniya, virɗyava tǝdvad iin nǝ duniya, bakǝvakwaha sǝraraaka bi nǝ-uudah biya.
JOH 1:11 Sǝghǝv ba nǝ iin savak uudahaana, larwalǝg nǝ uudahaan kǝ dlǝghǝggaana.
JOH 1:12 Aiciya, baɗǝm nǝ uudahi dlǝgharadlǝghǝg kǝ iina, dlaɓa ar fǝdghǝrǝt tǝ iina, vǝlatǝrvǝlǝg kǝ ndzǝɗɗa nǝg kǝ zarha Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 1:13 Naral bi kǝ zarha Daadamazhigǝl tǝdvad uuda dǝgshig biya, bi tǝdvad camarakǝv biya, bi tǝdvad dzamaghǝra uud biya, bamma yavva tǝdvad naaga Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 1:14 Kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga nalnǝg kǝ uuda, ndzaandzǝg mataatakamiyama. Nǝghamndanǝghǝg kǝ ndanngǝraana, Ndangǝra Zǝraan pal ba nǝ iin kwa sahi vak Daada, righarighan dǝ hɛrrǝr ǝmtaɗ dǝ jiira.
JOH 1:15 Tagadatag nǝ Yuhwan kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ iin vak kǝ uudah bad halavuwa ndzǝɗaan taakiya, “Kwanǝn kǝ uud wa tagaan nai kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr taakiya, ‘Kwada sagau tǝhalara jakwaarajig dǝ ɗyakǝr ba vaivaiya, aɗaba lakuti kǝskaiya ba mǝng nǝ iina.’ ”
JOH 1:16 Tǝdvad ɗyakǝra hɛrǝraan wa tlǝyamkǝna nǝmyam kǝ hɛrǝr tǝghǝr kǝ hɛrǝra.
JOH 1:17 Vǝlada tǝdvad Muus nǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ adzahadzaha, dlaɓa vǝlada hɛrǝr ard jiir tǝdvad Yesu Kristi.
JOH 1:18 Maay nǝ uudi tapghanitapǝg kǝ nǝghǝgga Daadamazhigǝl dǝ gyi biya, bamma Zǝriin palla, kwa ghǝravaan ndakwi Daadamazhigǝla. Kwa cǝhurga ǝmtaɗ dǝ Daadamazhigǝla iinwa marakiyamnda iina, dlaɓa kaa fǝkiyamafǝg kǝ sǝrgasǝrg kǝskǝmyam kǝ iina.
JOH 1:19 Wan nǝ ǝlbǝgi tagada nǝ Yuhwan masarta kwa bǝlartǝrǝt nǝ maalah Yahudah kǝ zhiila kǝssa-uufah ard lii fa hyimi tǝ vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl kwa saral ma Wurshalima sa ndavgaru taakiya, “Agha war nǝngi?”
JOH 1:20 Ɓalla bi nǝ Yuhwan kǝ agajau biya, tagadatag bat ɓalaɓal taakiya, “Kai bi nǝ Kristi biya”.
JOH 1:21 Kaa ba ndavgarundavǝg kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Agha war nǝngi? Kǝgh nǝ Iliya?” Ngal ba ngutǝrangug kǝ iin taakiya, “Kai biya.” “Kǝgh tlayangǝn kǝm pakǝg nǝmndna?” “Kai bi, awarama.”
JOH 1:22 Tǝhala kwaha, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Agha war kaci nǝnngi? Tagkǝmndtag magha war nǝnnga aɗaba kǝm sǝra kǝ dǝgiti kǝmnda tagtǝr nǝmnd kǝ liiya ɓǝla kǝmnda. Agha ɗaag dǝ war kaci nǝnng kǝ ghǝraghi?”
JOH 1:23 Ngwatǝrangwug nǝ Yuhwan tǝdvad ǝlbǝgaha tlayang Ishaya taakiya, “Kai nǝ ghai kwa ɓǝla tlǝhǝg ma tǝghala, ‘Ɓadlamarnaɓadlǝg kǝ ɗuulan kǝ Yaazhǝgǝla!’ ”
JOH 1:24 Kyalma lii ɓǝlavtǝrǝtɓǝlgna ndzar Farisiyaha.
JOH 1:25 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ Yuhwan taakiya, “Akwama kǝgh bi nǝ Kǝristi biya, kǝgh bi nǝ Ili biya, dlaɓa kǝgh bi tsau nǝ Tlayangǝn biya, Kwar kǝ ndzǝɗ kaci wagha dǝ vakai nǝng agha ɓagtǝr tsuufǝg kǝ-uudahi?”
JOH 1:26 Ngal ngutǝrangug Yuhwan taakiya, “Ən ɓagtǝr dǝ yu nai kǝ tsuufǝg kǝ uudaha, bandakwan bamma taatakaruwa mǝng nǝ daddakwam sǝrga bi nǝ uuram biya.
JOH 1:27 Iin wa taggan nai taakiya da sagau tǝhalara, kwa tlanal bi nai kǝ pǝla zauwa kimmbakaan biya.”
JOH 1:28 Baɗǝm wanahaan dzǝghaar ma Betani, kilga zaagha Yudan, vakavaki ɓagatǝr nǝ Yuhwan kǝ tsuufǝg kǝ uudaha.
JOH 1:29 Dlakaduraana, kaa nǝghganǝghǝg Yuhwan kǝ Yesu da vakaan amaa, “Wayam, nǝ Zǝr tuugha Daadamazhigǝl kwada kǝsa haipa uudaha duniya
JOH 1:30 Kwanǝn wa taggan nai kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr taakiya, ‘Mǝng wa da saggau tǝhalara kwa jakwarajig kǝskaiya, aɗaba mǝng nǝ iin lakwti yikwayig nǝ uuda.’
JOH 1:31 Dzan sǝrgabi ghǝravar kǝ iin wur biya. Tsuufǝgǝn ɓagan nai dǝ yu na, ɓaggan mbakyarvad marǝvtǝrda nǝ iin kǝ uudaha yaa Israˈal bat ɓalaɓala.”
JOH 1:32 Kaa tagdatag kǝ Yuhwan kǝ shiid tǝghǝr kǝ iin taakiya, “Nǝghananǝghǝg kǝ Shǝɗǝkw Daadamazhigǝl band garava kakur sii ma ghǝrazhigǝl, ngal tsǝgwatsǝgw tǝghǝr kǝ iina.
JOH 1:33 Ndzan sǝrgai nai kǝ iin wur biya, bamma Daadamazhigǝli ɓǝllakut kai da ɓa tsuufǝg dǝ yu, iinwa taghwatag taakiya, ‘Uudi agha nǝghǝgga nǝng kǝ shǝɗǝkw sii sa tǝghǝr kǝ-iin dlaɓa ndzan tǝghǝr kǝ iina, iin dadda ɓa tsuufǝg dǝ Shǝɗǝkw Daadamazhigǝla.’
JOH 1:34 Ba kai dǝ ghǝrara nǝghananǝghǝg kwana, ǝn tagkurtaga, kwanǝn kǝ uuda zǝra Daadamazhigǝla.”
JOH 1:35 Wurga kǝsaana, Yuhwan ghacǝgan vaaakwahiina ǝmtaɗ dǝ mbǝrzahaan buwa.
JOH 1:36 Kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ Yesu ghuda dagala, amaa, “Vazamvazǝga, wayam nǝ Zǝr mbaklaka Daadamazhigǝla!”
JOH 1:37 Cinngara ba nǝ mbǝrzahaan buna kǝ Yuhwan taa ghaiya, kaa gata Yesu kǝ iitǝr dagala.
JOH 1:38 Ɓǝlaa ba nǝ Yesu kǝ gyi dat hala, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr ar gatǝgaana, kaa ndavtǝrundaavǝg taakiya, “Awam gatǝg nǝ uurami?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Rabbi” iin taaki dadda tsaga dǝgita, “Agha ndzǝga mǝri?”
JOH 1:39 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Asamasǝga am da nǝghǝganǝghǝga.” Kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr ar vazzǝna kǝ vakavaki ndzǝga nǝ iina, ar cahwaran ǝmtaɗ dǝ-iin vaakwahiina. Kwan kǝ dǝgita dzǝghaar kalkala karfi uufaɗa hwasa.
JOH 1:40 Pal nǝ Andrawus zǝra babba Siman Bitrus ma uudahaan buwǝn gatar Yesu tǝhala kwa cinngara nǝ iitǝr kǝ ǝlbǝga vak Yuhwan tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu.
JOH 1:41 Dǝgiti ɓagaa nǝ Andrawus ba zǝnngwa fǝgharzh gata zǝra babbaan Siman, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Tlamndkǝnatlǝg kǝ Tlǝkatǝgna,” Iin nǝ Kristi.
JOH 1:42 Sǝdǝv kǝ-iin kǝ Siman da vak Yesu. Kaa vazǝggaan nǝ Yesu kǝ Siman amaa taa kǝ-iina, “Kǝgh nǝ Siman zǝra Yuhwana? Da ɗahak dǝ Kefas nǝ-uuda.” (Dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ Kefas ard Bitrusa ba dǝgit palla, iin na akura).
JOH 1:43 Dlakaduraana fadǝmfǝg nǝ Yesu ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaan dagal damma Galili. Kaa tlǝgaratlǝg kǝ iin kǝ Filigus taakiya, “Gatkwagatǝga.”
JOH 1:44 Filigus uuda kǝsa Betsaid nǝ iina, vakavaki saral nǝ Andrawus ard Bitrusa.
JOH 1:45 Tlǝghara ba nǝ Filigus kǝ Nataniyela, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Tlamndkǝnatlǝg kǝ uudanǝn kwa vinda nǝ Muus ma kakaɗa adzahadzah taakiya da saaya. Dlaɓa vindaravindǝg nǝ tlayangngah kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr band kwaha. Iin nǝ Yesu Uuda Nazarat, Zǝra Isuvu.”
JOH 1:46 Kaa tagaan kǝ Nataniyel taakiya, “Nazarata? Sǝgalsǝg dǝgit maraw ma Nazarata?” Aiyam nǝ Filgus taa kǝ-iina, “Saw na vaznavazǝgga.”
JOH 1:47 Nǝgha ba nǝ Yesu kǝ Nataniyel sagau sa vakaana, aiyama, “Wayam nǝ uuda jiijira yaa Israila, kwa maay nǝ fiid ma ghaiyan biya.”
JOH 1:48 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg nǝ Nataniyel kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Sǝrghkwa ndari?” Ngal ngugara-nggug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Nǝghankak bamma sartǝn ndza agha miizhangyil kǝ uufa ghǝgyivvǝna, lakwti ɗahakɗahǝg kǝ Filigusa.”
JOH 1:49 Am Nataniyel taa kǝ Yesu, “Dadda tsagga dǝgita, kǝgh Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla! Kǝgh nǝ Tlǝksa Israila!”
JOH 1:50 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ Nataniyel taakiya, fǝghdǝghǝrǝt mbakyarvad tagankak taakiya nǝghankak miizha ghǝgyivva? Agha da nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ dǝgiti juujig kǝ kwaha.
JOH 1:51 Kaa gwiya tagtǝrtag kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ən tagkurtag kǝ jiira, am da nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ ghǝrazhigǝl wurawurana, Zarha ɓǝlga Daadamazhigǝla ar dagat ar saay tǝ Zǝra uuda.”
JOH 2:1 Daghuvala hǝnnga hǝkǝrɗa, ndza mǝnng nǝ hwaɗaga kǝsa uus ma Kana kwama Galili. Babba Yesu ndakwi ndza ba vaakwahiina.
JOH 2:2 Baz Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan ndakwi ɗahavtǝrǝɗahǝg da vaka hwaɗaga kǝsa uusiina.
JOH 2:3 Ghyǝnnga ba nǝ yuwa inabiya, kaa tagartag nǝ babbaan kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Maadlabi nǝ yuwa inabiyaatǝr biya.”
JOH 2:4 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ babbaana, “Baaba, aujilbǝg agha taggǝwa kwan kǝskayi? Bagaa bi nǝ sartar ndan biya.”
JOH 2:5 Am nǝ babba Yesu taa kǝ lii ɓa tlǝra, “Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgiti tagkur nǝ iina, ɓagamɓaga.”
JOH 2:6 Vaakwahiina mǝnng nǝ ndǝghwah ǝngkwah kwa ndǝrava dǝ akura hulfa kwa ɗiyav nǝ yu mavakaiya, ar bara vǝghatǝr nǝ Yahudah dǝ yuwiin kwakyarvad dǝga daadijahaatǝra. Makwar kǝ ndǝghwa hǝɓa dǝfuu ǝnkwaha.
JOH 2:7 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ lii ɓa tlǝrna, “Reghamantreghǝg kǝ ndǝghwahaana dǝ yuwa.” Kaa reghǝgantreghǝg kǝ iitǝr ba pɛkapɛkan.
JOH 2:8 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gahamgahǝg ci ndakwana, gamǝtgǝga damardadǝg kǝ zhiilghuu.” Kaa gǝtgǝg kǝ iitǝr ar dardana.
JOH 2:9 Tapghana ba zhilghuu kǝ yuwǝn kwa gwiyavǝt damma yuwa inabi, sǝrghabi kǝ vakavaki tlavkǝna nǝ iin biya lii ɓa tlǝra ar sǝrgasǝrga. Ɗahant kǝ iin kǝ zhiila ghuul damma dlǝmmbaava.
JOH 2:10 Amaa taa kǝ iina, “Abi, aanji ba war saggal dǝ yuwa inabi marawǝn ba zǝngwa, akwama tlatǝrtlǝg kǝ uudaha, kaa saggal kǝ uud dǝ dlǝmndalaana. Agha shǝɓna nǝng kǝ yuwa inabi marawǝn agha da sagal tǝhal nǝng dǝ vakaiya!”
JOH 2:11 Kwan nǝ dǝga jappǝri ɓagaa nǝ Yesu ba zǝnngwa ma Kǝsa kana kwama haaya Galili. Marada ndkwan kǝ ndangǝrana, kaa fadghǝr kǝ mbǝrzahaan tǝ vakaiya.
JOH 2:12 Tǝhala kwaha kaa di damma kǝssa Kafarnahum kǝ Yesu dǝ babbaana ard zarha babbaana ǝmtaɗ dǝ mbǝrzahaana. Ar gahha kǝ hǝnngah hǝɗiikǝn vaakwaha.
JOH 2:13 Hǝrzǝt ba nǝ sarta haarakǝsa dzava hǝnnyaha Yahudaha, kaa dagat kǝ Yesu damma Wurshalima.
JOH 2:14 Kaa daas kǝ-iin damma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, tlǝtǝra kǝ uudah vǝlla tlaha, aagwaha, takalamasaraha. Dlaɓa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ kyalma uudah ar cihurgan tǝvǝgh kǝ tebǝrahaatǝr ar mbǝɗǝgar kwaɓ kǝ uudaha.
JOH 2:15 Kaa ndǝrgandǝrǝg kǝ iin kǝ zauwa kiiɓa, lagwtǝrda dagal baɗǝm ma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, baz tuughwaha baz tlaha. Tlagars kǝ teburaha lii mbǝɗa kwaɓa, kwaztǝrda kǝ kwaɓatǝr da tǝhaaya.
JOH 2:16 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ-lii vǝla takalamasarna, “Hutsamndahutsǝg kwanahaan dagal vaakwana! Lamdal bi kǝ vǝgya daadar kǝ kasukwa biya.”
JOH 2:17 Dzǝghaar ba nǝ wanǝnna, kaa dzamnadzamǝg kǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ dǝgiti vindava ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, “Waigǝn ǝn waig nai kǝ vǝgyaghna zǝkwazǝg tǝ ǝrviɗmahud band kaara”.
JOH 2:18 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ tlǝvuukwaha Yahudah kǝ Yesu, taakiya, “Kwar kǝ dǝga jappǝr wagha da markǝmndada nǝng kwada mara taakiya agha dǝ ndzǝɗa ɓa kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitah baɗǝmmi?”
JOH 2:19 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ-iitǝra, “Dlagamnadlag kǝ Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝlna, ǝn ndǝrgaan nai bamma hǝngah hǝkǝrɗa.”
JOH 2:20 Am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ Yesu, “Viig kul uufaɗ tar ǝnkwah kǝ uud ndǝra vǝgya Daadamazhigǝlna, aitsǝm ǝn ndǝrgandǝrǝg bamma hǝngngah hǝkǝrd amǝngnga?”
JOH 2:21 Vǝgyǝn tag nǝ iin kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝrǝna, vǝghaana.
JOH 2:22 Tǝhalakwa ciyavant nǝ Yesu ma gǝtlaha, kaa dzamnadzamǝg kǝ mbǝrzahaan kǝ dǝgiti tagga nǝ Yesu, kaa fadghǝr kǝ iitǝr tǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl vindavindana, ard ǝlbǝgahi taggada Yesu.
JOH 2:23 Sarta kwandza ma Wurshalim nǝ Yesu mbakyarvad haarakǝssa dzava hǝnnyaha, uudaha baɗyaka fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ iin mbakyarvad garava dǝgaha jappǝri nǝghara nǝ iitǝr kwa ɓag nǝ-iina.
JOH 2:24 Hayatǝrǝt bi nǝ Yesu dǝ iitǝr biya, aɗaba sǝrgasǝrg kǝ dǝgitahi ma ǝrviɗmahuɗa uudah baɗǝmma.
JOH 2:25 Maay wa tagardatag kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ uuda dǝshig kǝ iin biya, aɗaba sǝrǝgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgit ma ǝrivǝɗ uuda.
JOH 3:1 Ndza mǝng nǝ zhiila Farisiyin ɗaagaan Nikodimus, pal ma tlǝvuukwa Yahudaha.
JOH 3:2 Kwanǝn kǝ uuda sǝvsa vak Yesu kavǝɗɗa, amaa, “Dadda tsagga dǝgita, kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya agha dadda tsagga dǝgit kwa ɓǝladi nǝ Daadamazhigǝla, aɗaba maay wa ɓagnaɓag kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgit biya bamma daddakwa ǝmtaɗ nǝ Daadamazhigǝl dǝvakaiya.”
JOH 3:3 Kaa ngugarangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Bak jiira wan tagaktaga, maay wa dǝgaadǝg damma tlǝkǝssǝra Daadamazhigǝl biya, bamma gwiya yavayiga.”
JOH 3:4 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg nǝ Nikodimus kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Da gwiya yaav ndar nǝ uud ma nalnǝg kǝ malahi? Gwiya daadamma huɗɗa babbaan da yiva kǝ dǝga bunii?”
JOH 3:5 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Bak jiira, ǝn tagaktagga, maay wada dǝggaadǝg damma tlǝkǝssǝra Daadamazhǝggǝl biya, bamma gwiya yavayig tǝdvad yuwa ard shǝdkwa Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 3:6 Uuda dǝgshiga yaba uud nǝ-iin kalti, akwama yaayig nǝ shǝɗkwa Daadamazhigǝl kǝ uuda, kwah kǝ-uuda daba ǝmtaɗ dǝ shǝɗkwa.
JOH 3:7 Aa nali kǝ dǝga jappǝr vakagh wanaa taggak nai taakiya, ‘Barari bamma gwiya yakurayig nǝ-uud biya.’
JOH 3:8 Fǝɗa dagal da vavaki naag nǝ iina, agha cingaciing kǝ tlaavaana, bakǝvakwaha agha tagdai kǝ vakavaki aa sǝgga dǝ iin biya bi vavaki dagal nǝ-iin biya. Bandkwah dlaɓa agha tagdai kǝ ɗuuli yav nǝ uud tǝdvad shǝɗkwa Daadamazhigǝl biya.”
JOH 3:9 Kaa ndavgaru ndavǝg nǝ Nikodimus kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Da dzǝggaar ndar wan kǝ dǝgitahi?”
JOH 3:10 Ngal nguggarangug kǝ Yesu amaa, “Kǝgh agha dadda tsagga dǝgit maamaala ma Israˈala, gwaastǝn nǝghaakai kǝ dǝgitahaan biya?
JOH 3:11 Bak jiira ǝn tagaktagga, dǝgiti kǝm sǝrga nǝmnd wa kǝm tagkur nǝmnda, ard dǝ dǝgiti nǝghamnda nǝmnda, bakǝvakwaha lamwalǝg kǝ haigant dǝgiti tagamndkur nǝmnda.
JOH 3:12 Tagankurtag kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgaha duniya, famdǝghǝrǝt biya, am da fǝdghǝrǝt ndar kaci akwama taggankurtag kǝ dǝggit tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgaha ghǝrazhǝggǝli?
JOH 3:13 Maay wa tapghani dagat dama ghǝrazhǝggǝl biya ba Zǝra Uud pal wa sahi ma ghǝrazhǝggǝla.”
JOH 3:14 Band kwa dzǝgghant nǝ Muus kǝ ghavala vǝrzhagan ma tǝghala, Zǝra-uud ndakwi barari dzǝgvanta.
JOH 3:15 Baɗǝm dadda kwa fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ-iina, tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ shifǝgga damma zǝrazǝra.
JOH 3:16 “Waighantwaig Daadamazhigǝl kǝ duni ba vaivaiya vǝlda kǝ zǝraan pal ba nǝ iina, baɗǝm dadda kwa fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ iina da maay ǝmtsǝg biya, da tlǝknatlǝg kǝ shifǝgga tangw damma zǝrazǝra.
JOH 3:17 Ɓǝladi bi nǝ Daadamazhǝggǝl kǝ zǝraan damma duni kwakyarvad ghazǝna kǝ duni biya, ɓǝladi kwakyarvad tlǝkkǝna nǝ duni kǝ katǝg tǝdvad iina.
JOH 3:18 Baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla, maay da ghazav biya. Dlaɓa baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa lawalǝg kǝ fadghǝr tǝ iina, ghazaghazana, aɗaba fadghǝrǝt bi nǝ-iin tǝ ɗaaga Zǝra Daadamazhigǝl pal ba nǝ-iinǝn biya.
JOH 3:19 Kwakyarvad kwan wa tǝghara nǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ shari kǝ uudaha. Paraka sǝghawisǝg saama duniya, bakǝvakwaha uudaha ar waiya gurtl dlakulǝva paraka, aɗaba tlǝra kǝlaadǝr war ɓag nǝ-iitǝra.
JOH 3:20 Baɗǝm nǝ dadda ɓa kǝlaadǝra naabi kǝ parakǝn biya, maay vaan sagau sa tǝvǝgh kǝ parakiin biya, haik kǝ marazha saggal kǝ tlǝrahaana.
JOH 3:21 Dadda kwa ɓa dǝga jiira sagau savak kǝ parak, kiyava nǝghǝva-nǝghǝg bat ɓalaɓal taakiya dǝgiti ɓag nǝ-iina ɓag bad mǝlgarumǝlga Daadamazhigǝl.”
JOH 3:22 Tǝhala kwaha, kaa ba dagal kǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan damma larda Yahudiya. Zǝlarmazǝlg ar ba ǝmtaɗ vaakwah ɓagtǝr tsuufǝg kǝ uudaha.
JOH 3:23 Yuhwan dlaɓa ndza tsuufǝg ma Ainun hǝrǝz dǝ Salim aɗaba mǝng nǝ yu ba ɗyak vaakwaha. Uudaha ar sahasagawa sa vakaana kaa ɓagtǝrɓag kǝ iin kǝ tsuufǝga.
JOH 3:24 Dzǝghaardzǝg nǝ wan lakuti ɓǝlav nǝ Yuhwan ma guda bǝrfina.
JOH 3:25 Kaa ciigǝtciig ka gajau ma taataka mbǝrzaha Yuhwan ard zhiila Yahudaha tǝghǝr kǝ bara vǝgha lakwti kǝ ɓa kwatǝnahǝra.
JOH 3:26 Kaa dagau kǝ mbǝrzahǝn da vak Yuhwan am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Dadda tsagga dǝgita, uudanǝn ndzam ǝmtaɗ nǝ uuram kilga zaagha Yudana, kwa ba kǝgh dǝ ghǝragh ndakwani vǝlghǝdavǝlǝg kǝ shiid tǝghǝr kǝ-iin taakiya iin Kǝristi, wai nǝ-iin ɓagar tsuufǝg kǝ uudaha, aanji ba war daggau da vakaana.”
JOH 3:27 Kaa ngwanggug nǝ Yuhwana taakiya, “Maay wa tlǝknatlǝg aanji ndau biya, bamma vǝlgardi nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 3:28 Ghǝravaru ndakwani am shidahara aɗaba taganatag taakiya, ‘Kai bi nǝ Kǝristi biya, ɓǝlakutɓǝlǝg nǝ uud lakuti saay nǝ iina.’
JOH 3:29 Daddakwa kǝsguu ghuula, iin nǝ zhiila ghuula. Tsaghwa zhiila ghuula paka ba taakiya maa cinnga kǝ kungya zhiila ghuula. Dlaig ba vaivai akwama cingngacing kǝ ghaiya zhiila ghuula. Mbakyarvad kwana reghǝt-reghǝg nǝ dlaigara aɗaba sahisǝg nǝ zhiila ghuula.”
JOH 3:30 Mbakyarvad kwaha barari kǝ uudanǝn fǝgara ba ndangǝra, kai dlaɓ ǝn gulǝg dǝ gulǝga.
JOH 3:31 “Uudi sahi ma ghǝrazhigǝla juujig kǝ uudah baɗǝmma. Uudi sal ma duniya ba dǝga duniya, dlaɓa tag band uudi aasǝgal ma duni kǝ ǝlbǝga. Uudi sahi ma ghǝrazhigǝla juujig kǝ uudah baɗǝm.
JOH 3:32 Taa dǝgitahi cinngha nǝ iin ard dǝgiti nǝgha nǝ iina, bakǝvakwaha maay wa haighanthaig dǝ ǝlbǝgaan biya.
JOH 3:33 Baɗǝm daddakwa haighanthaig kǝ ǝlbǝgaana, haighanthaig taakiya dadda jiir nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 3:34 Aɗaba kwa ɓaladi nǝ Daadamazhigǝlna, ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl wa tagga nǝ-iina, aɗaba vǝlgharvǝlǝg nǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ shǝɗkwaan kwa maay nǝ ghalaan biya.
JOH 3:35 Waigaan nǝ Daad kǝ Zǝraana, vǝlgharvǝlǝg kǝ dǝgitah badǝm damma dǝvaana.
JOH 3:36 Baɗǝm dadda kwa fadghǝrǝfǝg tǝ Zǝriina, dǝ shifǝga damma zǝrazǝra. Baɗǝm daddakwa naay kǝ zǝriin biya, tlǝkna bi kǝ shifǝg biya. Da ɗiigaan Daadamazhigǝl kǝ ǝrviɗmahudaan tǝ iina.
JOH 4:1 Sǝrghaakasǝrǝg nǝ Yesu taakiya cinngaracinng nǝ Farisiyah taakiya ɓagtǝr tsuufǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ-uudaha, dlaɓa tlǝkkǝnatlǝg kǝ mbǝrzah juujig dǝga Yuhwana.
JOH 4:2 (Bakǝvakwaha, Yesu kataghǝraan bi wan ndza ɓagatǝr tsuufǝg kǝ uudah biya, ndza mbǝrzahaana.)
JOH 4:3 Aɗabadkwaha, kaa ɗugarsɗuug nǝ Yesu kǝ haaya Yahudi, kaa gwiya damma haaya Galili kǝ-iina.
JOH 4:4 Nalnǝg kǝ barari kǝ Yesu ta haaya Samariya.
JOH 4:5 Kaa daas kǝ-iin damma kǝsiin ma Samariya kwa ɗahav dǝ Saikar. Kwanǝn kǝ kǝsa ba hǝrz dǝ guhǝn vǝlghar nǝ Yakub kǝ zǝraan Isuvu ba wura.
JOH 4:6 Uuva Yakuba ndza vaakwaha, dlaba kuɗɗalkuɗǝg nǝ Yesu mbakyarvad dǝ dagala, cǝhura kǝ iin tǝ ghaiya uuviina. Kwanǝnna dzǝghaar dǝ vaci tǝghǝra.
JOH 4:7 Kaa sagau kǝ uusiina, dǝghwa Samariyah sa ga yuwa. Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ uusiina, “Kwats yagh kǝ yuwa hǝɓǝga.”
JOH 4:8 Makwahiin kǝ sarta, mbǝrzaha Yesu daral bawur da sǝgwa dǝgzǝg ma huɗa kǝsa.
JOH 4:9 Aiyam nǝ uusa Samariyahǝn taa kǝ Yesu, “Kǝgha agha zhiil Yahuda, kai kwana ǝn uusa Samariyah agha ghallǝg ndar kaci kǝ yuwa hǝɓɓǝg vakari?” Aɗaba Yahudah ard Samariyaha ar nahakǝv biya.
JOH 4:10 Ngugharangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Akwamaghaa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ gyagyaana na Daadamazhǝggǝla, ard daddakwa ghala yuwa hǝɓǝg vakaghǝna, maa ghalǝghaghallǝg kǝ iina, da vǝlakakvǝlǝg kǝ yu kwa da vǝlak shifǝga.”
JOH 4:11 Aiyam nǝ uusǝn taa kǝ Yesu, “Dadda ndannga, tiidl ndakwi maay vakagh biya, uuvǝn ndakwi ba tlaɗɗa, agha da tlǝkkǝna mǝr kaci nǝng kǝ yuwǝn kwa vǝla shifǝg ni?
JOH 4:12 Jighaarajig nǝng kǝ daadamnd Yakuba, kwa ɗuwakǝmndars uuviina? Ba iin dǝ ghǝraana, ard zarhaan, baz almanahaan hǝɓaruhǝɓɓǝg kǝ yu ma vakaiya?”
JOH 4:13 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Baɗǝm dadda kwa hǝɓǝguu kwanǝn kǝ yuwa, gwiya tsǝgaan nǝ andǝla
JOH 4:14 Aɗaba baɗǝm dadda kwa hǝɓǝguu yuwi ǝn da vǝlgar naiya, maadlai gwiya tsǝgaan nǝ andǝl ba dǝm biya. Yuwǝn ǝn da vǝlgar naina da ndzǝga bamma vǝghaan band njamar kwada za vukw dǝ kǝlga, nal kǝ shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝr kǝ-iina.”
JOH 4:15 Aiyam nǝ uusǝn taa kǝ iina, “Dadda ndannga, kwats kǝ yuwiina, haik gwiya njikwanjiig andǝl kǝskaiya, dlaɓa haik gwiya saggau kǝskai da gayu vaakwana.”
JOH 4:16 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Dǝg ɗahantɗahǝg kǝ zhiilagh sa vaakwana.”
JOH 4:17 Kaa ngwangug kǝ uusiin aiyama, “Maay nǝ zhiilar biya.” Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Bak jiira agha maay dǝ zhiil biya,
JOH 4:18 dǝgiti agha tagda nǝnngna ba jiira, aɗaba zaalah dlǝɓ wa kǝsghu nǝnnga, kwam ǝmtaɗ nǝ uuram ndakwana zhiilagha biya.”
JOH 4:19 Aiyama taa kǝ Yesu, “Dadda ndannga, man tlǝg nai agha tlayannga.
JOH 4:20 Daadijahamnd ɓagararnǝsɓag kǝ kwatnahǝr kǝ Daadamazhigǝl tǝ kwanǝn kǝ aghwna. Kuram Yahudaha am taakiya bamma ɓagvar ma Wurshalim kwatnahǝr kǝ Daadamazhigǝla awaram nǝ uurama.”
JOH 4:21 Kaa ngwarangug nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Uusǝn, fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ dǝginǝn ǝn tagak naina, aɗaba da sagau nǝ sart kwada maadlai ɓagvar nǝ kwatnahǝr kǝ Daada tǝ kwanǝn kǝ aghwǝn aanji ma Wurshalim biya.
JOH 4:22 Kuram uudaha Samariya am ɓagar kwatnahǝr kǝ dǝgiti am sǝrga bi nǝ-uuram biya, kǝmnd Yahudaha, kǝm ɓagar kǝ Daadamazhigǝli kǝm sǝrga nǝmnd kǝ kwatnahǝra, aɗaba katǝg sǝghal tǝdvad Yahudaha.
JOH 4:23 Mǝng sart da sagauwa, bandakwan ndakwani ɓagaaɓaga, lii ɓa kwatnahǝra jiira arda ɓaggar kwatnahǝr kǝ Daad ma Shiɗǝkw Daadamazhigǝla ard jiira, aɗaba, hwulfaatǝr wa gatǝg nǝ Daad kǝ ɓagarnǝs kwatnahǝra.
JOH 4:24 Daadamazhigǝl Shiɗǝkw nǝ-iina, lii ɓagar kwatnahǝr dlaɓa barari ar ɓagar ma Shiɗǝkwa ard jiira.”
JOH 4:25 Am nǝ uusiin taa kǝ Yesuwa, “Ən sǝrgasǝsǝrg taaki da saay nǝ Tlǝkatǝg kwa ɗahav dǝ Kǝristi. Akwama da sahisǝga da tagkǝmndtag kǝ dǝgitah baɗǝmma.”
JOH 4:26 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ uusǝna, “Kaiyin ǝn taaghai dǝ kǝghna, ba kai nǝ iina.”
JOH 4:27 Bad ghyǝngaghyǝngaan kǝ taa ghaiya, kaa sǝgaasǝg kǝ mbǝrzahaan, kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ-iitǝr aɗaba tlarara taaghai dǝ uusa. Maay wa ndavgharu kǝ uusiin taakiya, “Auwagha naag nǝng biya?” Bii kwa ndavgharu kǝ-iin taakiya, “Aujilbǝg kǝskǝgh taaghai dǝ uusǝn biya?”
JOH 4:28 Tǝhala kwah kaa ɗuugarsɗuug nǝ uusǝn kǝ tǝfuwa yuwan vaakwaha, kaa daas kǝ iin damma huɗɗa kǝssa da tagtǝr kǝ uudah taakiya,
JOH 4:29 “Sawam na vazamvazǝg kǝ uudi aa taguwa dǝgitahi ɓagana naiya baɗǝmma. Mbatak ɓagaɓag iin nǝ Kǝristina?”
JOH 4:30 Kaa ba sahasagal kǝ uudah ma huɗɗa kǝss da vakavaki dǝ Yesuwa.
JOH 4:31 Tǝghǝrdǝga ɓa kwan nǝ uuda, kaa ghalla Yesu kǝ mbǝrzahaan taakiya, “Dadda tsagadǝgita, zǝg kaffa.”
JOH 4:32 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ-iitǝra, “Mǝng nǝ dǝg zǝg vakar kwam sǝrgai nǝ uuram kǝ dǝgit tǝghǝr biya.”
JOH 4:33 Kaa ndavǝg kǝ mbǝrzahaan ma taatakaatǝr taakiya, “Mǝng nǝ daddakwa sǝgardǝv dǝga zǝg nii?”
JOH 4:34 Aiyam nǝ Yesu, “Kaffar iin taakiya ǝn ɓagna kǝ dǝgiti naag daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya, dlaɓa ǝn ghyǝngna kǝ tlǝraana.
JOH 4:35 Abi am tagaan taakiya, tǝmma kyil uufaɗ lakuti kǝ saa dǝ dǝgwai? Wan tagkurtag ciya, vazamvazǝg kǝ dǝgwai tǝhaltǝhǝga, dlaɓa tlaral tlǝg kǝ ghudǝga.
JOH 4:36 Dadda ghudǝgaana tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ dǝg shǝgaana, dzahgaan dlaɓ kǝ dǝgwai kiyava shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝr, kiyava hwaɗag kǝ dadda riig ǝmtaɗ dǝ dadda ghudǝggaana.
JOH 4:37 Kwakyarvad kwaha, bak jiir nǝ ǝlbǝg dǝghurǝn kwa taga taakiya, ‘Shah dadda kwan riiyaariiga, shah nǝ dadda ghudgaana.’
JOH 4:38 Ɓǝlankurǝt da ghuda dǝgiti hǝɓamuubi nǝ uuram kǝ dlaɗa riigaan biya. Uudahi tlǝrǝn wa hǝɓaru dlaɗa, kuram wa za dlaiva dlaɗaatǝra.”
JOH 4:39 Baɗyak nǝ uudaha yaa Samariya ma kwahiin kǝ kǝsa, fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Yesu mbakyarvad ǝlbǝgǝn kwa tagga nǝ uusǝn taakiya, “Taghwatag kǝ dǝgitahi ɓagana nai baɗǝmma.”
JOH 4:40 Saral ba nǝ uudaha Samariyah da vak Yesu, kaa ghalgaan kǝ iitǝr maa ndzan vakaatǝra. Kaa ndzanganzǝg kǝ hǝng buwa.
JOH 4:41 Uudah baɗyak fardghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Yesu mbakyarvad ǝlbǝgahaana.
JOH 4:42 Tǝhala kwaha kaa tagartag kǝ uudaha Samari kǝ uusǝn taakiya, “Ndakwana famdǝghǝrǝtfǝga, aanji mbakyarvd dǝgiti taghǝda nǝngǝn biya, kǝmnd ndakwi cinngamndacinng bad hyǝmiyamnda, dlaɓa kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg ba pakat taakiya kwanǝn kǝ uuda, iin wada kata uudaha duniya.”
JOH 4:43 Tǝhala hǝnng buwa, kaa ciya dagal damma haaya Galili kǝ Yesu.
JOH 4:44 Aɗaba ndza tagadatag nǝ Yesu bad ghǝraan taakiya, “Tlayangnga maay dǝ ndang ma kǝssaan biya.”
JOH 4:45 Dagha ba nǝ iin damma haaya Galili, kaa ba dlǝghga-dlǝghǝg kǝ lii ma Galili bad dǝva buwa aɗaba ghǝravaatǝr ndakwani daral da vakka hwaɗaga haara kǝssa dzava hǝnnyah ma Wurshalima, nǝghara nǝghǝg kǝ dǝgitahi ɓagaa nǝ Yesu baɗǝmma.
JOH 4:46 Kaa gwiya daas kǝ Yesu damma Kana ma Galili, vakavaki gwighant nǝ iin kǝ yu damma yuwa inabi. Vakwahiina ndza mǝng nǝ uudaniina kwa ɓagar tlǝr kǝ tlǝkǝsa ma Kafarnahum yang bi nǝ zǝraan biya.
JOH 4:47 Cinngha ba nǝ uudanǝn taakiya gwiya saghasǝg nǝ Yesu saama Yahudiya damma Galili, kaa dagau kǝ iin da vak Yesu da ghalgaan taakiya maa dagau maa mbǝna kǝ zǝraan kwa tǝ ghǝrdǝgga ǝmtsǝga.
JOH 4:48 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Akwama nǝghamabi kǝ dǝga sǝrǝg ard tlǝraha jappǝr biya, am maay fadghǝr aanji hǝɗikǝn biya.”
JOH 4:49 Am nǝ daddakwa ɓagar tlǝr kǝ tlǝkǝsǝn taa kǝ Yesu, “Asǝg naji dagal lakuti ǝmtsǝg kǝ zǝrraa.”
JOH 4:50 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Dǝgaa, da mbǝg nǝ zǝriina.” Fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg nǝ uudanǝn dǝ dǝginǝn taghar nǝ Yesuna, kaa ba daasan kǝ-iina.
JOH 4:51 Tǝghǝrdǝga daas nǝ iin da hǝnnyaha, kaa fadzaghǝr kǝ iin dǝ kyalǝma kwatnahaana, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Mbaambǝg nǝ zǝriina.”
JOH 4:52 Kaa ndavgaan kǝ iin kǝ kalkala sarti fǝgharzha nǝ iin kǝ ngulmǝga. Kaa tagartag kǝ iitǝr taaki, “Dahukwa kalkala karfi palla faciya wa ɗughars fǝɗiina.”
JOH 4:53 Kaa nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg kǝ dadda zǝriin taakiya ba kalkala kwahiin kǝ sart wa tagghar nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Da mbǝg nǝ zǝragha.” Ngal fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg nǝ ghwalvǝn ard yahaan baɗǝmma tǝ Yesu.
JOH 4:54 Kwana iin nǝ tlǝra jappǝra buwa kwa ɓagaa nǝ Yesu tǝhala kwa ɗughars nǝ-iin kǝ Yahudi kǝ dagal damma Galili.
JOH 5:1 Tǝhala kwaha, kaa dagat kǝ Yesu damma Wurshalima davaka hwaɗaga haarakǝsa Yahudaha.
JOH 5:2 Ma Wurshalima, tǝvǝgh kǝ ghaiya guda tughwaha, mǝng nǝ dǝlva kwa ɗahav dǝ Betasda ma ghaiya Yahudaha, tsavarvaara dǝ tsakwamah dlǝɓa.
JOH 5:3 Ma tsakwamahaan mǝng nǝ lii yang biya narǝtnǝg kǝ hǝnnga mavakaiya ndǝ gulfaha, ard ghurɗikaha ard lii ǝmtsaǝmtsan nǝ vǝgha. Ar paka uushvant nǝ yuwa,
JOH 5:4 aɗaba kǝ sart kǝ sart sahasagau nǝ zǝr ɓǝlga Yaazhigǝl da uusha yuwiina. Baɗǝm nǝ dadda kwa dǝhi zǝngw damma yuwǝn tǝhala uushgaana, da mbǝg aanji tuuk kwar kǝ kuzahi njǝkǝnjiig baɗɗǝmma.
JOH 5:5 Mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin ndza vaakwaha, viigaan kulhǝkǝrɗ tar tǝhǝs ba yang biya.
JOH 5:6 Nǝgha ba nǝ Yesu hǝnngan vaakwahiina, nǝghaakanǝghǝg taaki zǝlamazǝmǝg tuuk kǝ kwanǝn kǝ kuza, aiyama taa kǝ iina, “Agha naagaan kǝ mbǝga?”
JOH 5:7 Am nǝ dadda kuzzǝn taa kǝ iina, “Dadda ndannga, ǝn maay dǝ daddakwa da mǝlgwadmǝlǝg kǝ di damma dǝlvǝn ma sartǝn uushivant nǝ yuwǝn biya. Ma sartǝn ǝn ɓag nai kǝ kǝlla ndzǝɗar kǝ daay damma vakaiya, ba jǝkwaara nǝ uuda.”
JOH 5:8 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Ciiga, kǝssant kǝssǝg kǝ kǝjagh, dǝg dagalagha.”
JOH 5:9 Bat vakaitǝvakai, kaa mbǝgambǝg kǝ uudanǝn, kaa kǝsgantkǝsǝg kǝ iin kǝ kǝjaana kaa farzha kǝ dagala. Kwanǝn kǝ dǝgita dzǝghaar davala faciya ngiiga Yahudaha.
JOH 5:10 Mbakyarvad kwaha am nǝ maalaha Yahudah taa kǝ daddakwa mbavnambǝgna, “Hinana faciya ngiiga kalkalbi kǝskǝgh ɓa tlǝr biya, haiyakant bi nǝ adzahadzah kǝsa kǝjagh biya.”
JOH 5:11 Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ uudanǝn taakiya, “Daddakwa mbǝkwii kai wa taggwa taaki kǝssǝg kǝ kǝjagha dǝgdagala.”
JOH 5:12 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ-iitǝr taakiya, “Kwar kǝ-uud wa tagak taaki kǝsǝg kǝ kǝjagh dǝgdagalni?”
JOH 5:13 Uudanǝn mbavnanǝn sǝrgabi kǝ daddakwa mbǝghani-mbǝg biya, aɗaba mǝng nǝ uudah baɗǝyaka vaakwahiina, zǝgharaazǝg nǝ Yesu ma taataka uudaha.
JOH 5:14 Tǝhala zǝlam hǝɗiikǝna, kaa tlǝgaratlǝg nǝ Yesu ma vǝgya Daada ma zhigǝla, amaa taa kǝ-iina, “Agha, yagh mbǝghambǝga. Gwiyarzharabi kǝ ɓa haip biya, aɗaba aa gwiya tlǝka bi nǝ dǝgiti ghwaɗ kwa juujig kwanǝn biya.”
JOH 5:15 Kaa dagal kǝ uudanǝn tagtǝr kǝ maalaha Yahudah taakiya, “Yesu wa mbaghanimbǝga.”
JOH 5:16 Mbakyarvad ɓag daghuvala faciya ngiig nǝ Yesu kǝ kwanahaana, kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ maalaha yaa Yahudah kǝ pǝcca ghaiyaana.
JOH 5:17 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Daadar ba kǝlaa hǝng ɓa tlǝra, ghǝravar ndakwi ǝn ɓag band kwaha.”
JOH 5:18 Kwakyarvad kwanǝn wa fatǝra kǝ maalaha yaa Yahudah kǝ zavukw dǝ gata ɗuula tsa Yesu. Am nǝ iitǝra, “Aɗuug yagh kǝ adzahadzaha ngiigǝn kǝlada nǝ iinǝn biyin ndakwani, ɗa Daadamazhigǝla dǝ daddaana, aɗabad kwaha gǝrra ghǝraan kalkal dǝ Daadamazhigǝla.”
JOH 5:19 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Bak jiira wan tagkurtaga, maay nǝ dǝgiti ɓagnaɓag nǝ zǝriin dǝ ndzǝɗa ghǝraan biya, bamma dǝgiti nǝghǝga nǝ iin kǝ daddaan ɓagaan kalti. Aɗaba baɗǝm nǝ dǝgiti ɓag nǝ daadiin, iin wa ɓag nǝ zǝriina.
JOH 5:20 Aɗaba waigaan nǝ daadiin kǝ zǝrana, dlaɓa marghardamarg kǝ dǝgitahi ɓag nǝ iin baɗǝmma. Dlaɓa, da margarmarg baz tlǝrahi juujiig kwanahaan kiyava ɓa jappǝr kǝskurama.
JOH 5:21 Bandkwa ciig nǝ daad kǝ uudah ma gǝtlaha vǝltǝr kǝ shifǝga, band kwah dlaɓ nǝ zǝriin vǝlgarvǝlǝg kǝ shifǝg kǝ daddakwa waig nǝ iina.
JOH 5:22 Daad dǝ ghǝraan maay tǝgar shari kǝ uud biya. Vǝlgharvǝlǝg kǝ ndzǝɗa ta shari baɗǝmma damma dǝva zǝraana.
JOH 5:23 Kiyava fǝgaarafǝg kǝ uudah baɗǝm kǝ zǝriina, bandkwar fǝgaara nǝ iitǝr kǝ Daadiina. Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa fǝghaarabi kǝ Zǝriin biya, fǝghaarabi kǝ Daadi ɓǝladi iin biya.
JOH 5:24 “Bak jiira, wan tagkurtaga, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa cinnga ǝlbǝgara, fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg dlaɓ dǝ daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya, dǝ shifǝga damma zǝrazǝra. Maay da tǝvar shari biya, dzǝvaadzǝvǝg kǝ ǝmtsǝg damma shifǝgga.
JOH 5:25 Bak jiir wan tagkurtaga, mǝng sart da sagauwa, bandakwan ndakwi ɓagaaɓaga, lii ǝmtsaharaǝmtsahǝg arda cinnngacinnng kǝ ghaiya Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla, lii cinngaracinnga arda tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ shifǝga.
JOH 5:26 Bandkwa gyigyiya shifǝg nǝ Daadna nǝdal dlaɓ kǝ gyigyiya shifǝg kǝ zǝraana,
JOH 5:27 Vǝlgharvǝlǝg dlaɓ kǝ ndzǝɗa ta shari aɗaba Zǝra Uud nǝ iina.
JOH 5:28 Ɓagambi kǝ ajappǝra kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝg biya, aɗaba da sagau nǝ sarta, baɗǝm nǝ lii ma gǝtlaha ar da cinngacinng kǝ ghaiyaana,
JOH 5:29 ar da sagal ma gǝtlaha. Lii ɓagaraɓag kǝ dǝgitah marawa ar da ciiga ar tlǝkǝna kǝ shifǝg damma zǝrazǝra. Lii ɓagara dǝgitahi ghwaɗa, da ghudǝvtǝrda nǝ shariya.
JOH 5:30 Ən maay ɓa dǝgit tǝdvad ghǝrar biya, ǝn taa shari kǝ uudah bandkwa tagghwa nǝ Daadamazhigǝl taaki ɓaga. Mbakyarvad kwaha shariyara ba kalkala, aɗaba naaga ghǝrarbi wan ɓag nai biya, naaga daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya.
JOH 5:31 “Akwama kai wan taa ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ ghǝrara, ǝlbǝgara da haivant biya.
JOH 5:32 Mǝng nǝ daddakwa taa dǝgit tǝghǝr kǝskaiya, ǝn sǝrgasǝrǝg dlaɓ taakiya dǝgiti tag nǝ iin ba jiira.
JOH 5:33 Am ɓǝlant kǝ uudah davak Yuhwana, iin dlaɓa tagakurtag kǝ jiira.
JOH 5:34 Bakǝvakwaha, ǝn maay nai fadghǝr dǝ shiida uuda dǝgshig biya. Ən tagkur mbakyarvad am tlǝkna kǝ katǝga.
JOH 5:35 Yuhwana ndza kaara jahuramb kwa mbiig ba parakaraka, haiyamanthaig nǝ uuram kǝ cinnga ǝmtakǝra parakaan kǝ dǝga sart hǝɗiikǝna.
JOH 5:36 Ən mǝng nai dǝ shiid kwa juujig kǝ dǝgiti tagaa Yuhwan tǝghǝr kǝskaiya. Tlǝrahi vǝlghwa nǝ Daadar mana mbasnana, iin wan ɓag naiya. Iitǝr shiidar taakiya Daada wa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya.
JOH 5:37 Dlaɓa Daadi ɓǝlakwadi kaiya ba iin dǝ ghǝraan shidara. Tapamnabi kǝ cinnga ghaiyaan biya, dlaɓa tapamnabi kǝ nǝghǝga ndzǝgana huɗvǝgaan biya.
JOH 5:38 Əlbǝgaan dlaɓ ndzaabi ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaharu biya, aɗaba famdghǝrǝtbi tǝ dadda kwa ɓǝladi nǝ iin biya.
JOH 5:39 Am hǝgaan kǝ shiga ǝlbǝgaha Daadamazhigǝl vindavindana, mam tlǝg nǝ uuram am da tlǝkkǝnatlǝg kǝ shifǝg damma zǝrazǝr ma iitǝra. Kwan kǝ ǝlbǝgaha iin shiid tǝghǝr kǝskaiya.
JOH 5:40 Bakǝvakwaha lamwalǝg kǝ sa vakar am tlǝkkǝna kǝ shifǝga.
JOH 5:41 “Maay nǝ lambar dǝ galga uudah biya.
JOH 5:42 Ən sǝrkursǝrga, am maay nǝ uuram waiya Daadamazhigǝl ma ǝrviɗyaharu biya.
JOH 5:43 Sanhi ma ɗaaga Daadara dlǝghamkwi biya, akwama sǝgǝv ma ɗaaga ghǝraan nǝ uudanna, am dlǝghgaan ba dǝ ǝrviɗmahuɗ pala.
JOH 5:44 Am da fǝdghǝrǝt ndarndar kaci tǝ kaiyi am haigara ba dlǝbǝg mataatakaruwa. Am naay kǝ dlǝbgǝn kwa sagal vak Daadamazhigǝl kwa pal ba nǝ iinǝn biya?
JOH 5:45 Tlatlam bi taaki ǝn da kǝla ghunnjaru vak Daad biya. Mǝng wada kǝla ghunnjaruwa, iin nǝ Muusa, kwam tlǝg nǝ uuram da mǝlkurumǝlga.
JOH 5:46 Akwama famdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Muusa, maa famdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ kaiya, aɗaba vindavindǝg Muus tǝghǝr kǝskaiya.
JOH 5:47 Haiyamant bi tsau kǝ dǝgiti vinda nǝ iin biya, am da haigant ndar kaci kǝ ǝlbǝgari?”
JOH 6:1 Tǝhala kwanahaana, kaa dzǝva yuwa haiya Galili kǝ Yesu, kwa ɗahav dǝ Tibariya.
JOH 6:2 Kaa gatǝgaan kǝ uudah baɗyaka, aɗaba ar nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ dǝgaha jappǝri ɓagtǝr nǝ-iin kǝ lii yang biya.
JOH 6:3 Kaa dagat kǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan damma aghwa ar cahwarana dǝ mbǝrzahaana.
JOH 6:4 Hǝrzǝt ba nǝ sarta haarakǝssa dzava hǝnyaha yaa Yahuda.
JOH 6:5 Dzǝghant ba nǝ Yesu kǝ ghǝra kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ dzahava uudah sagau sa vakaana, kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ iin kǝ Filigusa, “Kiyam da sǝgwdaa mǝr kǝ bruudi kwada tlǝtǝrara kǝ uudahaani?”
JOH 6:6 Ndava kiyava fǝsha Filigus nǝ Yesu, aɗaba sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgiti da ɓag nǝ iina.
JOH 6:7 Ngugharangug nǝ Filigus taakiya, “Aanji bruudiya kwaɓa hǝngah tlǝra bariyam dǝrmǝk buwa, tlǝgǝti bi tǝ iitǝr aanji ba hǝɗikǝn hǝɗikǝn biya.”
JOH 6:8 Aiyam pal ma mbǝrzahaan kwa ɗahav dǝ Andrawus, zǝra babba Siman Bitrus taa kǝ Yesu,
JOH 6:9 “Mǝng nǝ zǝriin vaakwan dǝ ɗummba bruudi dlǝɓa kwa ɓagava dǝ ahupiya bale ard kilf buwa. Da tlǝtǝraara mǝr kaci kǝ uudah ɗyak ǝndkwani?”
JOH 6:10 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Tagamtǝrtag kǝ uudah taaki aa cahwararacahwarga.” Mǝng nǝ kazhakwa ba ɗyak vaakwahiina. Kaa cahwargacahwarǝg kǝ uudaha, ghwalvahi ndzar vaakwaha ar mǝng damma alfu dlǝɓa.
JOH 6:11 Kaa kǝsgantkǝsǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ ɗuumbaha bruudiina, tǝhala tagar uus kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, vǝlatǝrvǝlǝg kǝ digiti da tlǝtǝraaratlǝga. Ɓagaa band kwah dlaɓ dǝ kilfa.
JOH 6:12 Tǝhalakwa zaru nǝ uudah dlaɓa tlatǝrtlǝga, amaa taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Dzahamantdzahǝg kǝ ghwadgahaan kwa tǝmgatǝmgani aada badzalbi bagya biya.”
JOH 6:13 Kaa dzahghantdzahǝg kǝ mbǝrzah kǝ tǝmga ghwadgahaa bruudi dlǝɓǝn kwa jatruu kǝ zǝga kwa ɓagava dǝ ahupiya bale, kaa righantrighǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ alǝghw kǝlawa tar buwa.
JOH 6:14 Nǝghara ba nǝ-uudah kǝ dǝga jappǝra sǝrgǝn ɓagaa nǝ Yesu na, aiyam nǝ iitǝra, “Ba pakat iin nǝ tlayangǝn kwa kiyam pakkǝg nǝmyam kǝ saayan sama duniya.”
JOH 6:15 Nǝghaaka ba nǝ Yesu taaki ar na ɓa dabariya nǝdal kǝ tlǝkǝs bad ndzǝɗa, kaa ghǝlvalghǝlǝg kǝ iin ba daghuvaan damma aghwa.
JOH 6:16 Ɓagaa ba nǝ hwaasa, kaa sii samma dǝlva kǝ mbǝrzaha Yesu.
JOH 6:17 Ma kwahiina kǝ Sarta dǝmdǝg nǝ gurtla, Yesu dlaɓa sǝvbi sa vakaatǝr ndan biya. Kaa dǝgǝmdǝg kǝ mbǝrzah damma pɛra yuwa kiyava dzǝva dagal damma Kafarnahum.
JOH 6:18 Kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ fǝɗ ɓǝlǝg bad ndzǝɗa, kaa ghubǝɗǝg kǝ yuwa.
JOH 6:19 Tǝhalakwa darant nǝ iitǝr kǝ dǝga mil hǝkǝrɗa bi uufaɗa, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu dagal tǝ yuwa sagau sa tǝvǝgh kǝ pɛra yuwiina, Kaa gǝdzǝgǝtgǝdzǝg kǝ iitǝra
JOH 6:20 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Gǝdzam biya, ba kaiya.”
JOH 6:21 Kaa haiganthaig kǝ iitǝr ar ɓǝlarna kǝ damma pɛrayuwa caaricaari kaa tsugwatsugw kǝ pɛrayuwǝn vakavaki ar dagal nǝ iitǝra.
JOH 6:22 Cagaa ba nǝ kǝsa kaa nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg nǝ kyalǝma uudahaanǝn ndzar faɗǝga tǝghaiya gardza dǝlva taakiya mbats ndza ba pal nǝ pɛrayu ndza vaakwaha, dlaɓa nǝgharaakanǝghǝg taakiya dagha bi nǝ Yesu damma pɛrayu ǝmtaɗ dǝ mbǝrzahaan biya, daral ba daghuvaatǝr nǝ mbǝzahaana.
JOH 6:23 Ndza mǝng nǝ pɛrayuwah kwa saragha ma Tibariya ar ghacan hǝrǝz dǝ vakavaki zar nǝ uudah kǝ bruudi tǝhala kwa taghar nǝ Yesu kǝ uus kǝ Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 6:24 Nǝgharaaka ba nǝ uudah taakiya Yesu ard mbǝrzahaan ar maay vaakwah biya, ka dǝgǝmdǝg kǝ iitǝr damma pɛrayuwah kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr damma Kafarnahum da gata Yesu.
JOH 6:25 Tlararaa ba nǝ iitǝr tǝ ghyaba kwah kǝ ghaiya dǝlva, am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Dadda tsaga dǝgita, agha sǝgaa hǝr sa vaakwani?”
JOH 6:26 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Bak jiira wan tagkurtaga, am gatǝkwa mbakyarvad dǝga sǝrgi ajappǝri nǝghama nǝ uuram biya, am gatǝkwa mbakyarvad zaamuzǝg kǝ bruudi tlakurtlǝga.
JOH 6:27 Hǝɓam bi kǝ dlaɗ tǝghǝr kǝ gata kaf kwa badzǝg biya, hǝɓamhǝɓǝg kǝ dlaɗ tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgazǝg kwa zǝlmazǝlǝg tangw damma zǝrazǝra. Kwan kǝ dǝgazǝg wada vǝlkur nǝ Zǝra Uuda. Aɗaba Zǝra Uud wa vǝlghar nǝ Daad Daadamazhigǝl kǝ ndzǝɗa ɓa kwanahaana.”
JOH 6:28 Kaa ndavgaru-ndavǝg nǝ uudah kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Auwa kǝmnda ɓag nǝmd kiyava ɓa tlǝrahi naag nǝ Daadamazhigǝli?”
JOH 6:29 Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Wan nǝ tlǝri naag nǝ Daadamazhigǝla, famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ daddakwa ɓǝladi nǝ-iina.”
JOH 6:30 Kaa ndavgaru-ndavǝg nǝ uudahiin kǝ Yesu am nǝ-iitǝra, “Kwarci kǝ garava dǝgasǝrg wagha da ɓag nǝng kiyava fadghǝr kǝskǝmnd tǝ kǝghi? Au wagha da ɓag nǝngi?
JOH 6:31 Daadijahamiyam zaruuzǝg kǝ manna ma tǝghala, band kwa vinndava ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, ‘Vǝlatǝrvǝlǝg kǝ dǝgazǝg siima ghǝra zhigǝl kiyava zǝgga.’ ”
JOH 6:32 Tǝhala kwaha, kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu amaa, “Bak jiir wan tagkurtaga, Muus bi wa vǝlakurdi bruudi sii ma ghǝrazhigǝl biya, Daadar wa vǝlakurdi bruudiya jiir sii ma ghǝrazhigǝla.
JOH 6:33 Aɗaba bruudiya Daadamazhigǝl iin bruudi kwa saay ma ghǝrazhigǝla vǝlgar shifǝg kǝ duniya.”
JOH 6:34 Kaa am nǝ-iitǝr taa kǝ-iina, “Dadda ndangnga, ndzaa ba vǝlkǝmnd-vǝlǝg kǝ bruudiyin bakǝlaa hǝngnga.”
JOH 6:35 Kaa ngutǝraangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Kai nǝ bruudiya shifǝga, dadda kwa sǝgǝv sa vakar maadlai wai da njǝkǝn-njiig biya. Dadda kwa fadghǝr tǝ kaiya maadlai nǝ andǝl da njǝkǝn-njiig biya.
JOH 6:36 Bandkwa tagankur naiya, nǝghamkwanǝghǝga, bakǝvakwaha am lǝwa kǝ fadghǝr tǝ kaiya.
JOH 6:37 Baɗǝm lii vǝlgwa nǝ daada, ar da sagau sa vakara, daddakwa sǝgǝv sa vakara dlaɓa, ǝn maay lagwan biya.
JOH 6:38 Sanhi sa ɓa dǝgiti naag ghǝrar bi nai mazhigǝl biya, sanhi mbakyarva ɓa dǝgiti naag daddkwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya.
JOH 6:39 Naaga daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kai iin takiya, aa zannai aanji pal mali vǝlghwa nǝ-iin biya, ǝn ciitǝrǝt davala ghyǝngnga duniya.
JOH 6:40 Aɗaba kwan nǝ naaga Daadar taakiya, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa vazza dat Zǝrna, dlaɓa fadghǝr tǝ iina, da tlǝkkǝnatlǝg kǝ shifǝga damma zǝrarǝra, kai dlaɓa ǝn da ciigaan davala ghyǝngnga duniya.”
JOH 6:41 Kaa zavaghai kǝ Yahudah tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu aɗaba tagada taakiya, “Kai nǝ bruudiyin sahi ma ghǝrazhigǝlna.”
JOH 6:42 Am nǝ-iitǝra, “Abi Yesu, zǝra Isuvu, bakwa kǝm sǝrga nǝmnd kǝ daddaana ard babbaanǝn ɗang? Tag ndar kaci taaki, ‘Sanhi ma ghǝrazhigǝli?”
JOH 6:43 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iintǝra, “Ɗuwamarsɗuug kǝ zavaghai ma taatatakaruwa.
JOH 6:44 Maay wa dzǝgwantdzǝgw sa vakar biya, bamma sǝdda nǝ Daad kwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya, ǝn da ciyant nai kǝ uudanǝn davala ghyǝgnga duniya.
JOH 6:45 Vinndava-vinndǝg ma kakkaɗa tlaiyangngah taakiya, ‘Baɗǝmaatǝr da tsagtǝr ba nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.’ Baɗǝm daddakwa cingngharnu-cingng kǝ Daadiina dlaɓa tsagaan vakaana, da sagau sa vakara.
JOH 6:46 Maay wa ɗǝyit gi tǝ Daad biya bamma daddakwa sahi vak Daadamazhigǝla, ba iin pal wa nǝghgha Daadiina.
JOH 6:47 Bak jiir wan tagkurtagga, baɗǝm daddakwa fadghǝrǝt-fǝga, mǝng dǝ shifǝga damma zǝrazǝra.
JOH 6:48 Kai nǝ bruudiya shifǝga.
JOH 6:49 Dadijaha dadijaharu zaruzǝg kǝ mana ma tǝghal, bakǝvakwaha ruwararuuga.
JOH 6:50 Wan nǝ bruudi kwa sii ma zhigǝla, baɗǝm dadda kwa zǝguu bruudina, maay ǝmtsǝg biya.
JOH 6:51 Kai nǝ bruudiya shifǝg kwa sahi ma ghǝrazhigǝla. Baɗǝm dadda kwa zǝguu bruudina, tlǝknatlǝg kǝ shifǝga damma zǝrazǝra. Kwan kǝ bruudiya vǝghara, kwan da vǝlda nai kiyava tlǝkkǝna shifǝg kǝ uudaha duniya.”
JOH 6:52 Kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ Yahudah kǝ ɓala agajau ma taatakaatǝr ba dladlaɗa, taakiya, “Vǝlkiyam ndar nǝ uudanǝn kǝ tluwa vǝghaan kiyava zǝggi?”
JOH 6:53 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ-iitera, “Bak jiijiira ǝn tagkurtaga bamma zamuzǝg kǝ tluw Zǝra Uuda, dlaɓa am hǝɓɓu kǝ avǝzaana, am maay dǝ shifǝg ma kuram biya.
JOH 6:54 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa zǝguu tluwa vǝghara, hǝɓɓu dlaɓ kǝ avǝzara, mǝng dǝ shifǝgga damma zǝrazǝra, ǝnda ciigaan davala ghyǝngnga duniya.
JOH 6:55 Aɗaba tluwa vǝghara iin nǝ dǝgazǝga jiirjiira. Avǝzar ndakwi iin nǝ dǝga hǝɓɓǝga jiirjiira.
JOH 6:56 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa za tluwa vǝghara, dlaɓa hǝɓɓǝgaan kǝ avǝzara, ndzǝga ma kaiya, kai dlaɓ ma vǝghaana.
JOH 6:57 Bandkwan ndzǝgan nai mbakyarvad Daada dadda shifǝg kwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya, bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ daddakwa zǝg tǝ kaiya, da ndzǝga mbakyarvad kaiya.
JOH 6:58 Kai nǝ bruudiyin sahi ma ghǝrazhigǝlna. Daadijaha daadijaharu zaruzǝg kǝ mana, bakǝvakwaha ruwararuuga, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa zǝguu kwanǝn kǝ bruudiya da ndzǝga bad shifǝga damma zǝrazǝra.”
JOH 6:59 Tagada ma Kafarnahum nǝ Yesu kwan kǝ ǝlbǝg ma sarta kwandza tsaga dǝgit ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝl Yahudaha.
JOH 6:60 Cinngara ba nǝ-iitǝr ndǝkwana, kaa ba taggaan kǝ kyalǝma mbǝrzahaan taakiya, “Kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga mblemlen kǝ nǝghǝgaakanǝhǝga, warwa haiganthaigi?”
JOH 6:61 Nǝghǝghaaka ba nǝ Yesu taakiya zavaghai nǝ mbǝrzahaan tǝghǝr kǝ ǝlbǝgna, kaa amaa taa kǝ-iitǝra, “Badzakurda-badzǝg kǝ ǝrviɗy nǝ wanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga?
JOH 6:62 Da ndzǝga ndar kaci nǝ ǝrivǝɗmahuɗaru akwama nǝghamanǝghǝg kǝ Zǝra uuda dagat da vakavaki sahi nǝ-iini?
JOH 6:63 Shiɗǝkw iin wa vǝla shifǝga. Maay nǝ vǝgh dǝ ndzǝɗa ɓa aanji ndau biya. Əlbǝgahaan tagankur naina sǝghal vak Shiɗǝkwa dlaɓa vǝla shifǝga.
JOH 6:64 Mǝng nǝ kyalmaruwi fardghǝrǝt biya.” Bamma facta sǝrgasǝrg nǝ Yesu kǝ lii fardghǝrǝt bi tǝ-iin biya, sǝrghasǝrǝg dlaɓ kǝ daddakwa da vǝlgaana.
JOH 6:65 Kaa gwiya tagaan kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Iin wa tagankur naiya, ‘Maay wa dzǝgwantdzǝgw sa vakar biya, bamma vǝlgharvǝlǝg nǝ Daad kǝ ndzǝɗa.’ ”
JOH 6:66 Tǝhala ǝlbǝgahaan taga Yesu na, kaa gwiya dat hal kǝ mbǝrzahaan ba ɗyak ar ɗuwars dlaɓa ar lǝwa kǝ gwaiyav ǝmtaɗ dǝ-iina.
JOH 6:67 Kaa ndavtǝrundavǝg nǝ Yesu kǝ kǝlawa tar buna taakiya, “Baz kuram ndakwani amnaa dagalaruwa?”
JOH 6:68 Kaa ngwangug nǝ Siman Bitrus taakiya, “Yaazhigǝla, kǝmnda vak wari? Kǝgh wagha taa ǝlbǝga vǝla shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝra.
JOH 6:69 Famdghǝrǝtfǝg nǝmnd dlaɓa kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya, kǝgh Caccuwanacaccuwananǝn kwa sahi vak Daadamazhigǝla.”
JOH 6:70 Kaa ngngwagug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Dzǝrankuraakadzǝrga baɗǝmaru kǝlawa tar buna, bakǝvakwaha pal ma kuram shatanaha uuda.”
JOH 6:71 Tag tǝghǝr kǝ Yahuda, zǝra Siman Iskariyoti, aɗaba iin wada vǝla Yesu, bakǝvakwaha pal nǝ-iin ma lii kǝlawa tar buna.
JOH 7:1 Tǝhalakwaha kaa gwaivagwaig kǝ Yesu ma haaya Galili, naha bi kǝ damma haaya Yahud biya, aɗaba ar gata ɗuula tsǝgaan nǝ maalaha Yahudah vaakwaha.
JOH 7:2 Hǝrzǝt ba nǝ sarta haarakǝssa taha babramaha yaa Yahuda,
JOH 7:3 kaa tagartag kǝ zaraabahaan kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Marawuraana magha dagal damma Yahudiya, kiyava nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ mbǝrzahaghi vaakwah kǝ dǝgaha jappǝri agha ɓag nǝnga.
JOH 7:4 Abi lii naa sǝrvtǝr ar maay shǝɓa dǝgiti ar ɓag nǝ-iitǝr biya. Nalnǝg tsau taaki agha ɓagaan kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, agha margaan kǝ ghǝragh kiyava sǝraksǝrg kǝ duniya.”
JOH 7:5 Aɗaba aanji zarha babbaan kǝ Yesu ndakwi fardghǝrit bi tǝ iin biya.
JOH 7:6 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ɓagaa bi sartar ndan biya, vakaruwa aanji kwar kǝ sarta, ba kalkala.
JOH 7:7 Da ɗuukurǝs bi nǝ duni kǝskuram biya, kai wa ɗuukus nǝ iina. Aɗaba ǝn tagar tlǝraha kǝladǝri ɓag nǝ iina.
JOH 7:8 Damdǝg nǝ uuram dagal da vaka haarakǝssiina, ǝn maay nai dagal biya, aɗaba ɓagaa bi nǝ sartar ndan biya.”
JOH 7:9 Tǝhalakwa tagatǝrda nǝ Yesu kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, kaa ndzǝgandzǝg kǝ iin ndan ma Galili.
JOH 7:10 Daral ba nǝ zarha babba Yesu da vaka hwaɗaga haara kǝsna, kaa ba dagal kǝ Yesu tǝhalaatǝr kwal sǝrgasǝrgaatǝra, kwal nǝghǝga kǝ uudaha.
JOH 7:11 Kaa gatǝgaan kǝ maalaha Yahudah vaka haara kǝssǝna, ar ndava taaki, “Mǝr nǝ uuda nǝ iini?”
JOH 7:12 Kaa ba ɗung kǝ uudah mataatakaatǝr vaka dzahavǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu. Kyalǝm ar taakiya, “Uuda jiijiir nǝ iina.” Kyalǝm dlaɓ ar taakiya, “Maaya, abi vala ba uudaha.”
JOH 7:13 Maay wa shughana gyi kǝ taaghai tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu tǝ ɓalaɓal biya, aɗaba ar gǝdza maalaha Yahudaha.
JOH 7:14 Davǝm ba damma ghadghada haara kǝsna, Kaa daas kǝ Yesu damma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl kaa farzha kǝ tsagtǝr dǝgit kǝ uudaha.
JOH 7:15 Kaa ɓa jappǝr kǝ Yahudahi ndzar vaakwah ar ndava taakiya, “Tsaguu ndar nǝ uudanǝn kǝ dǝgit ǝndkwan bakwal dǝgal damma makaranti?”
JOH 7:16 Kaa ngwangug kǝ Yesu amaa, “Dǝginahaan ǝn tsag naina, dǝgar biya dǝga daddakwa ɓǝlakwaadi kaiya.
JOH 7:17 Baɗǝm daddakwa kǝsghaakakǝsǝg kǝ ɓa dǝgiti naag Daadamazhigǝla, da nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg taakiya tsagaanara sǝghawi vak Daadamazhigǝla, vakar biya.
JOH 7:18 Daddakwa tsaga dǝga ghǝraana, tsag mbakyarvad faara kǝ ghǝraana. Daddakwa naa fǝgaara kǝ daddakwa ɓǝladi iina, taa ba jiira, maay nǝ fiid ma ghaiyan biya.
JOH 7:19 Abi Muus wa vǝlakur adzahadzah? Bakǝvakwaha maay ma kuram wa tsuufǝghant adzahadzahiin biya. Aujilbǝg ci kǝskuram am naa tsakayi?”
JOH 7:20 Kaa ngwangug kǝ uudah taakiya, “Mǝng nǝ shatanah ma vǝghagha. Yaar dlaɓ wanaa tsakǝghi?”
JOH 7:21 Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ba dǝga jappǝr pal wa ɓagana nai davala ngiiga, baɗǝmmaru ɓagamaɓag kǝ ajappa.
JOH 7:22 Vǝlakurvǝlǝg nǝ Muus kǝ adzahadzaha ɓa guvaca, bakǝvakwaha iin bi wa fǝgharzhafǝg biya, fararzha daadijaha daadijaharuwa. Am ɓagaan kǝ aguvac aanji daghuvala ngiiga.
JOH 7:23 Akwama ɓagvaraɓag nǝ aguvac kǝ zǝr daghuvala faciya ngiigga kiyava tsuufa tsagaana Muusa, aujilbǝg ci kǝskuram am nguɗa ǝrivǝɗ dǝ kai mbakyarvad uudi mbanna nai daghuvala ngiigi?
JOH 7:24 Ɓagam bi kǝ shari nǝgha gyi biya, ɓagamɓag kǝ shariy tǝdvad jiirjiira.”
JOH 7:25 Makwahiin kǝ sarta, kaa ndavǝg kǝ kyalǝma uudahi kwar ndzǝga ma Wurshalima taakiya, “Abi, kwan kǝ-uud war naa tsǝg nǝ-iitǝr?
JOH 7:26 Iin ɗang wan taaghai bat ɓalaɓalǝn? Tagarar bi aanji ndau biya. Nii mbatak hayaranthaig maalah taakiya iin Kǝristiyin hii?
JOH 7:27 Ghwalvǝn kiyam sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ vakavaki sǝghsal dǝ iina, akwama da sǝghawisǝg nǝ Kǝristi jiirjiira, maay wada sǝrgasǝrg kǝ vakavaki sǝghal dǝ-iin biya.”
JOH 7:28 Ba ndzǝgaan ba tsagtǝr dǝgit nǝ Yesu kǝ uudah ma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, kaa dzǝgantdzǝg kǝ iin kǝ kunngy amaa, “Aana am sǝrkwasǝrga, am sǝrgasǝrǝg dlaɓ kǝ vakavaki sanal naiya. Sanhi dǝ ndzǝɗa ghǝrar biya, aɗaba Daadamazhigǝli ɓǝlakwadi kaiya dadda jiir nǝ iina, kuram am sǝrgabi nǝ uuram kǝ-iin biya.
JOH 7:29 Ən sǝrgasǝrǝg nai kǝ-iina aɗaba sanhi vakkaana, iin dlaɓa wa ɓǝlakwadiɓǝlǝga.”
JOH 7:30 Tagada ba nǝ Yesu kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, kaa gata viigaan kǝ uudaha. Maay wa fǝt dǝv tǝ vakai biya aɗaba ɓagaa bi sartaan biya.
JOH 7:31 Bakǝvakwaha uudah ba baɗyaka ma dlammakǝlaw fardghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Yesu, ar taakiya, “Aitsaa, ma sartǝn da saay nǝ Kǝristiyin tsaa, da ɓagaan ni kǝ dǝga jappǝrah kwa juujig kwa ɓagaa nǝ ghwalvǝna?”
JOH 7:32 Cinngaraba nǝ Farisiyah kǝ uudah taa ghaiy tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu ma haay ma haaya, Kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ maalaha Zhilla kǝsuufah ard Farisiyah kǝ lii uufa vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl da viigaana.
JOH 7:33 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Tǝmma ba hǝɗiikǝn sarta ndzǝganar vakaru, tǝhala kwaha ǝn da gwiya daas da vak dadda kwa ɓǝlakwadiɓǝlga.
JOH 7:34 Am da gatkwagatǝgga am da tlǝkwi biya. Vakavaki dǝ kai am da sǝgǝv biya.”
JOH 7:35 Aiyam nǝ Yahudah ma taatakaatǝra, “Naa da dagal da vaakwar nǝ uudanǝn kwada tlǝvaraa bi ni? Mbatak da dagal da vak Yahudahǝn kwazaral ar ndzǝgan dǝ Helenahǝn kiyava tsagtǝr kǝ Helenah vaakwah hi?
JOH 7:36 Auwa tlatlǝg nǝ-iin dǝ taakiya, ‘Am da gatkwagatǝg, am da tlǝkwi bi ni’? Au dlaɓ wa tlatlǝg nǝ-iin taakiya, ‘Vakavaki dǝ kai am da sǝgǝv bi nii’?”
JOH 7:37 Daghuvala ghyǝngnga haara kǝssa, iin faci kwa juujig baɗǝmma, kaa ghacigaghacig kǝ Yesu dzǝgant kǝ ghaiyaan amaa, “Baɗǝm daddakwa njikǝn nǝ andǝla aa sasǝg sa vakar da hǝɓuwa.
JOH 7:38 Baɗǝm daddakwa fadghǝr tǝ kaiya, bandkwa taga nǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl vinda-vinndana taakiya, njamara yuwa kwa vǝla shifǝga da kǝla sagal ma ǝrviɗyana.”
JOH 7:39 Tag tǝghǝr kǝ Shiɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl nǝ Yesu, kwada dlǝghǝg lii fadghǝr tǝ iina, aɗaba ma kwanǝn kǝ sarta vǝlavda bi nǝ Shiɗǝkw Daadamazhigǝl ndan biya, aɗaba favvaara bi nǝ Yesu ndan biya.
JOH 7:40 Cinngara ba nǝ kyalǝma uudah kǝ ǝlbǝgǝn tagaa nǝ Yesu na, kaa am nǝ-iitǝra, “Ba pakat kwanǝn kǝ uuda Tlayanga.”
JOH 7:41 Am nǝ kyalma, “Iin nǝ Kǝristi.” Gwastǝna kyalǝm ar ndava taakiya, “Ɓaga ndar nǝ Kǝristi sagal ma Galili?
JOH 7:42 Abi tagatag nǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl vindavindan taakiya Kǝristi da sagal ma kuɗiga Dauda? Dlaɓa ma Bitalahami kǝssǝn kwa ndzaa nǝ Daudǝn biya?”
JOH 7:43 Aɗabad kwaha, kaa tagwvǝmtagw nǝ araja uudah tǝghǝr kǝ Yesu.
JOH 7:44 Kyalǝm nahar viyarviiga, bakǝvakwaha, maay wa fǝt dǝv tǝ-iin biya.
JOH 7:45 Gwiyara ba nǝ lii uufa vǝgya Daadamazhigǝlǝn daada vak maalaha zhiila kǝssauufah ard maalaha Farisiyaha, kaa ndavtǝruundavǝg nǝ maalahaan taakiya, “Aujilbǝg samdaabi?”
JOH 7:46 Am nǝ-lii uufǝgǝna, “Maay nǝ uudi tapghana taaghai ndǝ ghwalvǝn biya.”
JOH 7:47 Am nǝ Farisah taa kǝ-lii uufǝgǝna, “Caa, baz kuram ndakwani valakurda valǝga?
JOH 7:48 Nii mǝng ha nǝ uud maamal ma uudah bi ma Farisiyah kwa fadǝghǝrǝt tǝ-iin hii?
JOH 7:49 Maaya, bamma uudahaan kwar sǝrgai kǝ dǝgit tǝghǝr kǝ tsaga Muus biya. Tlafatǝratlafǝg nǝ Daadamazhigǝla.”
JOH 7:50 Nikodimus kwandza dal da vak Yesu wura, dlaɓa palma dakwalaatǝra, kaa ndavǝg kǝ-iin taakiya.
JOH 7:51 “Tagadai kwan nǝ adzahadzaha miyam taakiya, kimya maay tǝgar shari kǝ uud, bamma cingngavacing nǝ dǝgit ɓaga nǝ iin ma ghaiyaan biya?”
JOH 7:52 Kaa ngugarangug kǝ-iitǝr taakiya, “Kǝgh ndakwi agha uuda Galiliya? Hahǝg dan kǝ shigaan ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl vinnda-vinndana, aghada nǝghǝgaaka-nǝghǝg taakiya maay nǝ tlayangngi sǝghal ma Galili biya.”
JOH 7:53 Kaa daas kǝ uudah da vǝgyahaatǝra.
JOH 8:1 Kaa dagal dat gavala uufaha zaitun.
JOH 8:2 Dlakadur bawura kaa daas kǝ Yesu damma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla. Kaa dzahvǝtdzahǝg kǝ uudah vakaana, cǝhuran kaa tsagtǝrtsagga.
JOH 8:3 Kaa sǝdǝvsǝg kǝ lii tsaga adzahadzaha muus ard Farisah kǝ uusiin kwa viyavǝt ɓaa gwaragwara, ar ghacinan mataatakatǝra.
JOH 8:4 Kaa tagartag kǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Dadda tsaga dǝgit, uusǝn aa vivǝt ɓa gwaragwara.
JOH 8:5 Tagakǝmndatag nǝ adzahadzaha Muus taakiya aa ɗawalav-ɗawalǝg nǝ hulfa kwan kǝ uudah da akura bamma ǝmtsara-ǝmtsǝgga. Auci amǝng?”
JOH 8:6 Ɓagar kwakyarvad ar ngarant kǝ dlǝgǝd nǝ-iitǝr kǝ ndavǝgna, dlaɓa maraa tlǝkǝna kǝ haipani ar da ɗiig nǝ-iitǝr kǝ ghunnjana. Kaa ngǝghǝrangǝg kǝ Yesu farzha kǝ vindǝg tǝ haay dǝ zǝra dǝva.
JOH 8:7 Mbǝraras ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ Yesu dǝ ndavǝgaha, kaa cigǝtciig kǝ iin ghacan amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa maay dǝ haip ma kuram biya aa farzhafǝg kǝ ɗuulǝgaan da akura.”
JOH 8:8 Kaa gwiya ngǝghrangǝg kǝ Yesu, ngal vindǝg tǝ haaya.
JOH 8:9 Cinngara ba nǝ iitǝr ǝndkwaha, kaa fǝgarzhafǝg kǝ iitǝr ciyadagal vaakwahiin ba da palapala, ciggǝt tǝ maalatǝr dat lii ngyikwah ngyikwaha, tǝmma ba nǝ Yesu ard uusǝn ghaciga tǝvuukwana.
JOH 8:10 Kaa cigǝtciig kǝ Yesu ghacan, ndavaru kǝ uusǝn amaa, “Uusǝn ar mǝr nǝ iitǝri? Maay wa ghaza kǝgh biya?”
JOH 8:11 Kaa ngwangug kǝ uusǝn taakiya, “Daada ndangnga, maay aanji ndǝwar biya.” Kai ndakwani ghazanka biya, “Dǝga gwiyarzhara bi kǝ ɓa haip biya.”
JOH 8:12 Tǝhala kwaha kaa gwiya tagtǝrtag nǝ Yesu kǝ ǝlbǝg kǝ uudaha amaa, “Kai nǝ paraka duniya. Baɗǝm daddakwa gata kaiya tapnai kǝ dagal ma gurtl biya, da tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ paraka shifǝga.”
JOH 8:13 Am nǝ Farisiyah taa kǝ Yesu, “Agha ɓagar shiid kǝ ghǝragha, shidaghǝn maay wa haiganthaig biya.”
JOH 8:14 Ngwatǝrangug nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Aanji ǝn ɓaga kǝ shiid tǝghǝr kǝ ghǝrara, shidar ba jiira, ǝn sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ vakavaki sanal naaya ard vakavaki ǝnda gwiya daas naiya, aɗaba am sǝrgai nǝ uuram kǝ vakavaki sanal nai ard vakavaki ǝnda gwiya daas nai biya.
JOH 8:15 Am taa shariya nǝgha gyiya nǝ uurama. Ən maay nai tǝgar shari aanji kǝ war biya.
JOH 8:16 Aanji mana da tǝgaan kǝ shariya, shariyara ba jiijiira, aɗaba kai pal biya, kǝm ǝmtaɗ dǝ Daadar kwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya.
JOH 8:17 Ma dzahadzaharuwa vindavavindǝg taakiya akwama tagaratag shidah bu kǝ dǝgit palla, barari dlǝghav nǝ shidaatǝra.
JOH 8:18 Kaiya ǝn shiida ghǝrara, dǝga buwa iin nǝ Daadari bǝlakwadi ɓǝlga.”
JOH 8:19 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ itǝr taakiya, “Vaakwar nǝ Daadaghini?” Kaa ngutǝrngug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Am sǝrkwa bi kǝskai biya, Daadar ndakwi am sǝrga biya. Akwamammaa sǝrkwasǝrga, mammaa sǝrgasǝrg kǝ Daadara.”
JOH 8:20 Tagada ma sarta kwandza tsag nǝ iin kǝ dǝgit tǝvǝgh kǝ vakavaki ɗiyav nǝ kwaɓa baiko ma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla. Bakǝvakwaha maay wa viyitviig biya, aɗaba ɓagaa bi nǝ sartaan ndan biya.
JOH 8:21 Kaa gwiya tagtǝrtag Yesu kǝ uudahaan dzaharvǝtǝn taakiya, “Ən da dagalara, am da gatkwagatǝga, am da ǝmtsǝg ma haipaharuwa. Vakavaki ǝn da dagal naiya, am da dǝgal biya.
JOH 8:22 Mbakyarvad kwan wa tagar nǝ maalaha Yahudah taakiya, “Da tsa ghǝran ni kwa taga nǝ iin taakiya, ‘Vakavaki ǝn da dagal naiya, am da dǝgal bina’?”
JOH 8:23 Ka zavukw kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Kurama am dǝga duni nǝ uurama, kai sanhi maghǝrazhigǝla. Kuram am dǝga duunina, kaiya ǝn dǝga duuniyin biya.
JOH 8:24 Iinwa tagankur nai taaki am da ǝmtsǝg ma haipaharuna. Aɗaba akwama famdǝghǝrǝt bi taakiya, kai wa tagankur nai taaki kaiyin nǝ iin biya, bak jiirjiir am da ǝmtsǝg ma haipaharuwa.”
JOH 8:25 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ-iitǝr kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Agha war nǝngngi?” Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Ba kai wandza tagankur nai bawur taakiya, bakaiya.
JOH 8:26 Mǝng nǝ dǝgitah baɗyak kwan tagdatag nai tǝghǝr kǝskurama, dlaɓa ǝn tǝkura kǝ shari tǝghǝra. Daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya, ǝlbǝgaana tlaltlǝg fǝvdǝghǝrǝta. Dǝgiti cingananai vakaana, iin wan tagtǝr nai kǝ uudaha duniya.”
JOH 8:27 Nǝgharaakai nǝ uudah taakiya tag tǝghǝr kǝ Daddaan kǝ ǝlbǝg biya.
JOH 8:28 Iin wa nǝ iin tagatǝr nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Sartǝn am da kapgant nǝ uuram kǝ Zǝra Uuda, am da nǝghǝgaaka sartaan taakiya kai nǝ-iina, dlaɓa maay nǝ dǝgiti ǝn ɓag nai kataghǝrar biya, ǝn taa ba dǝgiti tsagghwad nǝ Daadar kaltiya.
JOH 8:29 Daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya ǝmtaɗ dǝ kaiya, ɗuwakus bi nǝ-iin daghuvar biya. Ən ɓa ba dǝgiti naag nǝ-iin ba kǝla hǝnnga.”
JOH 8:30 Ma sarta taa kwanahaan kǝ Yesu uudah ba ɗyak fardghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ iina.
JOH 8:31 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ Yahudahǝn fardǝghǝrt tǝ-iinna, “Mam ba zǝgaan kǝ vukw dǝ hǝkya dǝgiti ǝn tsagkur naiya, am mbǝrzahara ba jiijiira.
JOH 8:32 Am da sǝrgasǝrg kǝ jiira, kwanǝn kǝ jiira iin wada vǝlkur kwarga ghǝraruwa.”
JOH 8:33 Kaa ngwangug kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Kǝm zhigha Ibrahim nǝmnda, tapamndnai kǝ nǝg kǝ ɛɛva aanji war biya. Aujilbǝg ci kǝskǝgh taaki kǝmnda tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ kwarga ghǝramndi?”
JOH 8:34 Kaa ngutǝrangug kǝ Yesu amaa, “Bak jiira wan tagkurtaga, baɗǝm daddakwa fadǝmfǝg kǝ ghǝraan ma ɓa haipa ɛɛva haip nǝ-iina.
JOH 8:35 Maay nǝ ɛɛvǝ ndzǝga hǝnnyah tangw damma zǝrazǝr biya, zǝran kǝ dadda hǝnyaha, ǝndzǝgan ba hǝnyah tangw damma zǝrazǝra.
JOH 8:36 Kwakyarvad kwaha, akwama tlamkǝnatlǝg kǝ kwargaghǝraru vak Zǝriina, am da tlǝkǝnatkǝg kǝ kwaraghǝra jiijiira.
JOH 8:37 Ən sǝrgasǝrg taaki samal am kuɗiga Ibrahima, bakǝvakwaha am naa tsakai nǝ-uurama, aɗaba dlǝghamabi kǝ ǝlbǝgar ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaharu biya.
JOH 8:38 Ən tagkur dǝgiti nǝghana nai vak Daadara, kuram am ɓa dǝgiti cingngama nǝ-uuram vak daadaruwa.”
JOH 8:39 Kaa ngwarangug kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Daadamnd nǝ Ibrahim.” Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝr, “Akwa mammaa zarha Ibrahim, maa ɓagamaɓag kǝ dǝgitahi ɓagaa nǝ Ibrahima.
JOH 8:40 Kaiya ǝn taa ba jiira dǝgiti cinngananai vak Daadamazhigǝla, kuram ghulamvaghulǝg kǝ naa tsa kaiya. Abi ɓagaabi nǝ Ibrahim kǝ hulfa kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitahaan biya.
JOH 8:41 Aɗaba am ɓa ba dǝgiti ɓag nǝ Daadaruwa.” Aiyam nǝ Yahudaha, “Kǝm masagwah bi nǝmnd biya. Daadamazhigǝl nǝ Daadamnda, ba iin dlaɓ pal nǝ Daadi kǝm dǝ vakai nǝmnda.”
JOH 8:42 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ-iitǝra, “Akwamaa Daadaru nǝ Daadamazhigǝla, mammaa waikwawaiga, aɗaba sanhi vak Daadamazhigǝl naiya. Kai wan kwan vaakwana, Daadamazhigǝl wa ɓǝlakwadiɓǝlga, sanhi dǝ ndzǝɗa ghǝrar biya.
JOH 8:43 Aujilbǝg ci nǝghamaaka bi kǝ ǝlbǝgari? Aɗaba am dzǝgwantbi kǝ cinnga ǝlbǝgar biya.
JOH 8:44 Am dǝga daadaru shatanaha, am naa ba ɓa ɗagiti naag daadaruwa. Dadda tsa shifǝg nǝ-iin bamma fakta, maay dlaɓ lammban dǝ jiir biya, aɗaba maay nǝ jiir ma ghaiyaan biya. Ba cukw sarti tag nǝ-iin kǝ fiida mara hǝnkalaana, aɗaba iin dadda taa fiid nǝ-iina, daada fiidah dlaɓa.
JOH 8:45 Kwakyarvad ǝn taa jiira, famdǝghǝrǝt bi tǝ kai biya.
JOH 8:46 Kwar ma kuram wa margwadamarǝg kǝ haipi tapannanai kǝ ɓaagaani? Akwama jiir wan tag naiya, aujilbǝg kaci famdǝghǝrǝt bi tǝ kai biyi?
JOH 8:47 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa dǝga Daadamazhigǝla, cinngaan kǝ dǝgit tag nǝ Daadamazhigǝla. Kuram haiyamant bi nǝ-uuram dǝ dǝgiti tag nǝ Daadamazhigǝl biya aɗaba am dǝga Daadamazhigǝl biya.”
JOH 8:48 Kaa ngugarangug nǝ Yahudah taakiya, “Mbats bak jiir wa tagamnd nǝmnd taakiya agha zhiil Samari dlaɓa shiɗǝkw ghwaɗ ma vǝghagh biya?”
JOH 8:49 Aiyam nǝ Yesu, “Ən maay nai dǝ shiɗǝkw ghwaɗ biya. Daadar wan fǝgaara naiya, kuram lamwalǝg kǝ fǝkwaarafǝga.
JOH 8:50 Kaibi wa gatgar ndangngǝr kǝ ghǝrar biya, mǝng wa gatgwagatǝga, iin dlaɓ nǝ dadda ta shariya.
JOH 8:51 Jiir wan tagkur naiya, daddakwa fǝghaarafǝg kǝ ǝlbǝgara maay ǝmtsǝg badǝm biya.”
JOH 8:52 Kaa am nǝ maalaha yaa Yahuda taa kǝ-iina, “Kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg ndakwanci taakiya bak jiir agha dǝ shiɗǝkw ghwaɗa. Abi ǝmtsaǝmtsǝg nǝ Ibrahim, bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ tlayangngah ǝmtsahara-ǝmtsahǝga. Bakǝvakwaha kǝgh agha taaki, ‘Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa fǝghaarafǝg kǝ ǝlbǝgagh da maay ǝmtsǝg badǝm biya.’
JOH 8:53 Magha tlǝg nǝng jighaarajig nǝng kǝ daadamnd Ibrahima? Ghǝravaan ndakwani ǝmtsaǝmǝga, tlayangngah ndakwi ǝmtsaharaǝmtsǝhǝga. Magha tlǝg nǝng agha war nǝngi?”
JOH 8:54 Ngwatǝrangug nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Akwama fanarafǝg kǝ ghǝrara, kwanǝn kǝ ndangngǝra maay tuuk ǝlbǝg biya. Daadari kwa kǝsamant nǝ-uuram taakiya iin nǝ Daadamazhigǝlaruwa iin wa fǝkwaraafǝga.
JOH 8:55 Am sǝrgai nǝ uuram kǝ-iin biya, kaiya ǝn sǝgasǝrǝg kǝ-iina. Maa tagankur nai taaki ǝn sǝrga biya, maa nanalnǝg kǝ dadda fiid band kurama. Ən sǝrgasǝrg nai kǝ-iina, ǝn cingngarnucing dlaɓ kǝ dǝgit tag nǝ-iina.
JOH 8:56 Daadaru Ibrahim dzamadzamǝg maa nǝghan kǝ zamanara, nǝghanǝghǝga dlaɓa dlaiyadlaiga.”
JOH 8:57 Am nǝ Yahudah taa kǝ Yesuwa, “Kǝgh kwana gwastǝn ɓaghabi kǝ viig kuldlǝb ndan biya, agha gwiya taaki nǝghanǝghǝg kǝ Ibrahima?”
JOH 8:58 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, yavva bi nǝ Ibrahim ndakwani ǝn ba mǝng naiya,”
JOH 8:59 Tagada ba nǝ Yesu kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga kaa cagantcag kǝ-iitǝr ka akur kiyava tsǝgaana. Shiɓvǝgha nǝ Yesu, kaa ba dagal kǝ-iin ma vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 9:1 Tǝghǝrdǝga dagal Yesu, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ-iin kǝ uuda nǝ-iin kwa yavva gulfa.
JOH 9:2 Ngal ndavgarundavǝg nǝ mbǝrzahaan taakiya, “Dadda tsaga dǝgit, haipa war wa nadal ghwalvǝn yavan gulfni? Haipaan nii, dǝga daddaan ard babbaanhi?”
JOH 9:3 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ-iitǝra, “Kwakyarvad haipa uudanǝn biya, bii haipa daddaana bii babbaan bi wa yavva nǝ-iin gulf biya, yavvayig nǝ-iin ǝndkwaha kwakyarvad marvda ndzǝɗa Daadamazhigǝl tǝ-iina.
JOH 9:4 Badlaɓ tsaw faciya, barari kiyam zǝgaan kǝ vukw dǝ ɓa tlǝra daddakwa ɓǝlkwadiɓǝlga, aɗaba sagaw nǝ avǝɗa maay wa da ɓagaɓag aanji kwar kǝ tlǝr biya.
JOH 9:5 Akwama ban ma duniya, ba kai paraka duniya.”
JOH 9:6 Tagada ba nǝ-iin kwaha, kaa tǝffa kǝ-iin kǝ ashavai dat haaya, kǝɗant kǝ haay dǝ vakaiya, kaa ghudǝt kǝ-iin kǝ haayǝn kǝtghant nǝ-iin da ashavayǝna, masara tǝ gyiya kǝ uudanǝna.
JOH 9:7 Amaa taa kǝ uudanǝna, “Dǝga, bardabarǝg kǝ gi ma dǝlva Siluwan.” Dǝgiti tuuk vakai nǝ Siluwana inn nǝ “Ɓǝlga”. Kaa dagau kǝ uudanǝn barda kǝ gyiyaana, sǝghaasǝg dǝ gyiyaan nǝghǝganǝghǝga.
JOH 9:8 Kaa ndavǝg kǝ tlǝgharawakyaghahaan ard lii narǝtnǝg kǝ nǝghǝganǝghǝg ghalǝg taakiya, “Abi ba ghwalvǝn wandza cǝhurga vaakwan ghalgǝn?”
JOH 9:9 Am nǝ kyalma “Iina.” Am nǝ kyalmaha, “Iin biya, dzakǝvaana.” Iina ǝmtsǝtǝmtsǝg taakiya, “Ba kaiyina.”
JOH 9:10 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ-iitǝr taakiya, “Mbaa ndar kaci giyaghi?”
JOH 9:11 Ngwaangwug amaa, ghwalvǝn kwa ɗahav dǝ Yesuwǝn wa kǝɗghant haay maswadǝm ma gyiya. Amaa taa kǝskaiya, dǝg bardabarǝg ma dǝlva Siluwam. Danal ba naya ǝn bardana, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝskaiya.
JOH 9:12 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ-iitǝra, “Mǝr nǝ uuda nǝ-iini?” Aiyama taa kǝ-iitǝra, “Ən sǝrga biya.”
JOH 9:13 Kaa langaan nǝ uudah kǝ ghwalviin kwandza gulf ba wurǝn davak Farisiyaha.
JOH 9:14 Aɗaba ndza daghuvala faciya ngiig wa kǝɗghant nǝ Yesu kǝ haay mbǝna kǝ gyiya uudanǝna.
JOH 9:15 Kaa ndavgarundavǝg nǝ Farisiyah kǝ ɗuuli mbaa gyiyaana. Aiyam nǝ uudanǝna, “Haay wa kǝɗghant nǝ-iin maswadǝm ma gyiya, kaa barda kǝskaiya, ndakwana ǝn nǝghǝganǝghǝga.”
JOH 9:16 Kaa tagaan kǝ kyalǝma Farisiyah taaki, “Sahi vak Daadamazhigǝl bi nǝ ghwalvǝn biya, aɗaba maay tsuufa faciya ngiig biya.” Ngal ndavǝg kǝ kyalǝmah taakiya, “Ɓagǝna dau nǝ dadda kwad haip kǝ hulfa kwanahaa kǝ dǝgaha jappǝrahi?” Buud taghwzhataghw kǝ dzamaghǝraatǝra.
JOH 9:17 Kaa gwiya ndavgaruundavǝg kǝ-iitǝr kǝ uudanǝn taakiya, “Au kaci nǝ wagha nǝghǝgaaka nǝng tǝghǝr kǝ uudanǝn, iin tsau wa wurakant gi?” Kaa ngutǝrangug nǝ uudanǝn amaa, “Tlayang nǝ-iina.”
JOH 9:18 Fardǝghǝrǝt bi nǝ maalaha Yahudah taakiya ndza gulf nǝ uudanǝn wura biya, ndakwana nǝghǝganǝghǝga. Aɗabad kwaha, kaa ɗahǝgantɗahǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ daddaana ard babbaana
JOH 9:19 Kaa ndavtǝru-ndavǝg kǝ-iitǝr taakiya, “Zǝraru wana? Ndza yavva gulf am nǝ uurama? Aaɓaga ndar kaci nǝghǝganǝghǝg ndakwani?”
JOH 9:20 “Kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg taaki zǝramnd nǝ zǝrna, dlaɓa yavva gulfa.
JOH 9:21 Kǝm sǝrgai kǝ ɗuuli nǝghǝga nǝ iin ndakwan biya, dlaɓa kǝm sǝrgai kǝ daddakwa mbǝghǝnimbǝg biya. Ndavamarundavǝga, zarh bi nǝ-iin biya, tagdatag nǝ iin bad ghaiyaana.”
JOH 9:22 Tagardatag nǝ daddaan ard babbaan ǝndkwana, mbakyarvad ar gǝdza maalaha Yahudaha. Nguɗarant ba wur nǝ maalaha Yahudah kǝ ǝlbǝgaatǝr taakiya, baɗǝm daddakwa tagadatag taaki Yesu iin nǝ Kǝristi, ar lagwaan dagal ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝla.
JOH 9:23 Iin wa tagar nǝ daddaana ar dǝ babbaan taakiya, “Zarh bi nǝ-iin biya, ndavamarundavǝga.”
JOH 9:24 Kaa gwiya ɗaha uudanǝn ndza gulf wurǝn kǝ Farisaha, am nǝ-iitǝr taa kǝ-iina, “Tag kǝ jiira aɗaba agha faara kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ uudanǝn dadda haipa.”
JOH 9:25 Aiyama, “Aanji dadda haip nǝ-iin ǝn sǝrga bi nai biya. Dǝgiti pal ǝn sǝrga naiya, wura ndzan gulfa, ndakwana ǝn nǝghǝganǝghǝga.”
JOH 9:26 Kaa gwiya ndavgarundavǝg kǝ-iitǝr taakiya, “Aukaci wa ɓagaka nǝ-iin? Wurakant ndarci kǝ gi?”
JOH 9:27 Ngwatǝrangug amaa, “Tagankurdataga lǝmwalǝg kǝ cingngaana. Aujilbǝg kǝskuram naa gwiya cingngaani? Nii am naa nǝg kǝ Mbǝrzahaanhi?”
JOH 9:28 Ngal ba ɗahgarv-ɗahǝg kǝ-iitǝr taakiya, “Kǝgh nǝ mbǝrzaana, kǝm Mbǝrzaha Muus nǝmnda.
JOH 9:29 Kǝm sǝrgasǝrg taakiya tagaatag nǝ Daadamazhigǝl kǝ ghai dǝ Muusa, kiyava kwan kǝ uuda, kǝm sǝrgai vavvaan kǝ vakavaki sal dǝ-iin biya.”
JOH 9:30 Kaa ngutǝrangug nǝ uudanǝn taakiya, “Wanam nǝ dǝga jappǝr haniina! Am sǝrgai kǝ vakavaki sal nǝ-iin biya, waici mbǝghwanimbǝg kǝ gyiyara,
JOH 9:31 Kiyam sǝrgasǝrǝg maay Dadamazghigǝl cingtǝrnucing kǝ yaa dadda haipah biya. Cingtǝrnuciing kǝ lii ɓagarnǝs kwatǝnahǝra baɗǝmma, dlaɓa ar ɓa dǝgit naag nǝ-iina.
JOH 9:32 Maay wa tapghanatapǝg ba dǝm kǝ cingaciing kǝ daddakwa wurgharant gyi uud yava gulf biya.
JOH 9:33 Akwamaa sahi vak Daadamazhigǝl bi nǝ uudanǝn biya, maa ɓagna bi bandau biya.”
JOH 9:34 Cinngaraba nǝ-iitǝr ǝndkwaha, aiyam nǝ-iitǝr taa kǝ-iina, “Dali kǝghii yakka bamma gyigyiya haip nǝ uud wagha naa tsagkǝmnd dǝgita?” Ngal lagwarslagw kǝ-iitǝra.
JOH 9:35 Cinngha ba nǝ Yesu taaki lagwararslagw kǝ uudanǝna, ngal tlǝgaratlǝg kǝ-iina, ndavaru taakiya, “Fǝghǝdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Zǝra Uuda?”
JOH 9:36 Kaa ngwangug kǝ uudanǝna, aiyama, “Dadda ndangnga, warwahiini? Tagwataga kiyava fadghǝr kǝskai tǝ-iina.”
JOH 9:37 Ngugharangug nǝ Yesu, taakiya, “Nǝghǝghanǝghǝg ghǝravagha, abi iin wa taaghai dǝ kǝghǝna.”
JOH 9:38 Aiyam nǝ uudanǝna, “Yaazhigǝla, fandǝghǝrǝtfǝga.” Kaa ɓagarnǝs kǝ-iin kǝ kwatnahǝra.
JOH 9:39 Aiyam nǝ Yesu, “Sanhi mbakyarvda taa shari nai sama duniya, aɗaba gulfaha ar nǝghana, dlaɓa lii nǝghǝganǝghǝga ar da nal kǝ gulfa.”
JOH 9:40 Cinngara ba nǝ Farisahǝn ndza tǝvǝgh kǝ-iinǝn ǝntkwana, aiyam am nǝ-iitǝr taa kǝ-iina, “Matlǝg-ghǝragh kǝmnd ndakwi, kǝm gulfaha?”
JOH 9:41 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ-iitǝra, “Akwa mammaa gulfa, mammaa maay dǝ haip biya, kǝm nǝghǝganǝghǝg tsau am nurama, haipaharuwa ndzǝga ba tǝghǝr kǝskurama.
JOH 10:1 “Bak jiir wan tagkurtag Farisiyaha, baɗǝm dadakwa dagha bi damma agɛɛragɛɛra dǝ ghaiy gud biya, bakǝvakwaha kaa tlǝlla ɗulla dass kǝ-iin tǝ kwatlǝrǝn kǝ ghyǝba, gǝlla dlaɓa gwarǝɗ nǝ-iina.
JOH 10:2 “Dadakwa dǝgaa dǝ ghaiya wakyagha, iin dadda piiya tuughwaha.
JOH 10:3 Dadda uufa ghaiya wakyagha wurgarwurǝgga kǝ-iina. Tuughwah dlaɓa ar cingarnucinga kǝ kungya dada piiga. Ɗahǝtǝrɗaga kǝ tuughwahaan dǝ ɗagahaatǝra, ngal langtǝrlang dagal da gyǝmǝlla.
JOH 10:4 Tǝhala kwama dadal kǝ tuughwahaan baɗǝm da gyǝmǝlla, kaa dal kǝ-iin tǝvukwatǝra, tuughahah dlaɓa ar gatǝgaan tǝhaltǝhala, aɗaba ar sǝrǝgasǝrǝg kǝ ghaiyaana.
JOH 10:5 Ar tapǝnaiy kǝ gata ghullab badǝm biya, ba kǝ jiirra ar hǝdla dagal vakaana, aɗaba ar dzǝgaakaiy kǝ ghaiya ghullab biya.”
JOH 10:6 Tagatǝrdatag nǝ Yesu kǝ uudaha kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝg dǝghura, bakǝvakwaha nǝghǝnǝgharaakai kǝ dǝgit tagtǝr nǝ-iin biya.
JOH 10:7 Aɗabadkwaha am Yesu kǝ-iitǝr gwiiyadalla, “Bak jiijiira, ǝn tagkurtaga, kaiy nǝ ghaiya gudlǝgha tuughwaha.
JOH 10:8 Baɗǝm lii sarǝva lakwti ǝn sagau naiya ar gǝllaha dlaɓa ar gwarǝɗɗaha, tuughwahahin ndakwi ar cingtǝrnu biya.
JOH 10:9 Kaiy nǝ ghaiya wakyagha, baɗǝm dadakwa dǝga tǝdǝvad kaiya da katava. Ar da saasa dlaɓa ar da dagala, ar da tlǝkǝnatlǝg vaka piig marawa.
JOH 10:10 Gǝla sagau kwakyarvad ɓa gǝl kaltiya ard tsa shifǝga dlaɓa ard ghyǝhǝga, kaiya sanǝv taakiya ar tlǝkǝna kǝ shifǝga, dlaɓa ar tlǝkǝnan bajar righǝrighaana.
JOH 10:11 “Kaiy nǝ dadda piig marawa. Dadda piig marawa iin wa vǝlla shifǝgaan kwakyarvad tuughwaha.
JOH 10:12 Suuniya iin bi nǝ dadda piig biya, dlaɓa tuughwaha dǝgaan biya. Aɗabadkwaha bamma sarti ma nǝghǝghanǝghǝg kǝ ghǝygya tǝghal sagauwa, kaa ɗuwaras kǝ-iin kǝ tuughwaha ngal hǝdla dagalaana. Ghǝgya tǝghal da dǝtraadǝg kǝ giɗya tuughwaha dlaɓa kwazǝtǝrdana.
JOH 10:13 Əmdǝradagala nǝ uuddanǝn aɗaba suuniya nǝ-iina ɓa tlǝra kwaɓa, maay lamban dǝ tuughwaha biya.
JOH 10:14 “Kaiy nǝ dadda piiga marawa. Ən sǝrǝgasǝrǝg kǝ tuughwahara, tuughwahara ar sǝrkwasǝrǝga.
JOH 10:15 Bandkwan sǝrkwa nǝ Daada, kai dlaɓ ǝn sǝrgasǝrǝga kǝ iina. Dlaɓa ǝn vǝlgaan kǝ shiifǝgara kwakyarvad tuughwahaha.
JOH 10:16 Ən mǝng nai dǝ kyǝlǝma tuughwaha kwar dǝga kwanǝn kǝ agɛɛragɛɛra biya. Iitǝr ndakwi barari ǝn sǝtǝrddana. Ghǝravaatǝr ndakwi ar da ciingaan kǝ kungyara, ar da nal kǝ agɛɛragɛɛra palla, dadda piig palla.
JOH 10:17 “Kwakyarvad kwah wa waikwa Daddara, aɗaba ǝn vǝldavǝlǝg kǝ shifǝgara, dlaɓa ǝn gwiidagwiiga.
JOH 10:18 Maay nǝ dadakwa kǝsǝgwavakǝsǝg kǝ shifǝg biya, aɗaba kaiy wan vǝlǝgaan dǝ naaga ghǝrara. Ən dǝ ndzǝɗa vǝldavǝlga, ǝn ndzǝɗa gwiidagwiga sǝddan dlaɓa. Kwan kǝ dǝgit wa taghwa nǝ Daddara kǝ ɓagaana.”
JOH 10:19 Kwakyarvad kwan kǝ ǝlbǝggǝn tagada nǝ Yesu, gwiya sadasǝg kǝ taagwavǝgh mataataka Yahudaha.
JOH 10:20 Baɗyak ma iitǝra, ar taakiya, “Shatanaha wa ma vǝghaana, iin wa ɓag nǝ-iin kǝ valaagǝrna. Aaujilǝbǝg am ciingarnuciingi?”
JOH 10:21 Bakǝvakwaha am kyǝlǝmaha, “Kwanahaan kǝ ǝlbǝga tagdai nǝ daddakwad shiɗǝkwa ghwaɗ mavǝghaan biya. Kats wurǝgarantwurǝg shiɗǝkwa ghwaɗ kǝ gyi kǝ gulǝfa?”
JOH 10:22 Masarta kwaha ndza akwhya vakka, ɓa hwaɗaga dzama hyaɗa vǝgya Dadamazhigǝl nǝ-uud ma wurushalima.
JOH 10:23 Yesu ndza gwayav ma gagaazaya Sulemanu ma vǝgya Dadamazhǝgǝla.
JOH 10:24 Kaa dzahvǝtdzahǝg kǝ Yahudaha tǝghǝr kǝ-iina, kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Agha ɗukǝmǝndars ndar ma dzamaghǝr tǝghǝr kǝskǝgh mbǝrdakwani? Maba kǝgh nǝ Kǝristi tagkǝmǝndtag bat ɓalaɓala.”
JOH 10:25 Ngwatǝrangug nǝ Yesu kǝ iitǝra, “Tagankurdatag bawura, famdǝghǝrǝt biya. Tlǝrahaan ǝn ɓag naay ma ɗaaga Daadarna, iitǝr shidahara.
JOH 10:26 Kurama famdǝghǝrǝt biya, aɗaba am tuughwahar bi nǝ-uuram biya.
JOH 10:27 Tuughwahara ar cinngacinng kǝ ǝlbǝgara ǝn sǝrǝtǝrsǝrǝga, dlaɓa ar gatkwagatǝga.
JOH 10:28 Ən vǝltǝr shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝra, ar da tapǝnay kǝ ǝmǝtsǝg biya, maay dlaɓa wa da hutsǝrvahutsǝg sagal miizha dǝvvar biya.
JOH 10:29 Daadara, kwa vǝlǝghwavǝlǝg kǝ tughwahaana jujig dǝ ndzǝd baɗǝma, maay wa da hutsǝtǝrdahutsǝg sagal miizha dǝva Daadar biya
JOH 10:30 Kaiya ard Daada kǝmba palla.”
JOH 10:31 Kaa gwiya cagantcag kǝ yaa Yahuda kǝ akurah kiyavva ɗawalǝgaana.
JOH 10:32 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ-iitǝra, ɓagankuraɓag kǝ tlǝrah maraw baɗyak vak Daada, am da ɗawalkwa kwakyarvad kwar kaci nǝ-uurami?”
JOH 10:33 Aiyam yaa Yahuda, kǝm ɗawalǝk kwakyarvad tlǝr marawǝn ɓagha nǝng biya, kwakyarvad badza ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝla. Kǝgha agha uud ba gyaagyaana a gǝra ghǝragh dǝ Dadamazhǝgǝla.
JOH 10:34 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Vindavai kwan ma adzahadzhaharu taakiya, ‘Amaiya am ghǝlaha biya’?
JOH 10:35 Am sǝrǝgasǝrǝg taakiya, ǝlbǝga Dadamazhǝgǝl vindavindana ndzǝga bat jiir ba kǝlaa hǝnga. Akwama ɗahavtǝr dǝ ‘Ghǝlaha’ nǝ lii cauwara ǝlbǝga Yaazhigǝla,
JOH 10:36 aujilbǝgci kǝskuram am taakiya ǝn badza ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝl mbakyarvad naa tagda taakiya Kaiy nǝ zǝra Daadamazhigǝli? Maay ba wah ndakwi kai wa fakwi nǝ Dadda ba kǝrkangyakwa, dlaɓa ɓǝlakwadiɓǝllǝg sama duniya.
JOH 10:37 Akwama tlǝra Daadar bi wan ɓag nai biya, famdǝghǝrǝt bi tǝ kaiy biya.
JOH 10:38 Akwama iitǝr wan ɓag naiya, aanji famdǝghǝrǝt bi tǝ kaiy biya, famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ tlǝrahara, aɗaba am sǝrana, dlaɓa am nǝghǝghaaka taakiya, Daada ma kaiya, kaiy dlaɓa ma iina.”
