JOH 10:39 Kaa gwiya ɓaa kǝla ndzǝɗatǝr kǝ viigaana, bakǝvakwaha ngǝdlatǝrvangǝdlǝg nǝ Yesu ma dǝvvatǝra.
JOH 10:40 Tǝhala kwaha kaa gwig kǝ Yesu damma hal dzǝva kǝ zaagha Urudun, da vavaki ɓaga nǝ Yuhwana kǝ tsuufǝg ba zǝngwa, ndza kǝ-iin vakwaha.
JOH 10:41 Uudaha baɗyaka sarǝvǝsǝg sa vakaana, kaa ba tagaan kǝ-iitǝr taakiya, “Tapǝghanaiy nǝ Yuhwana kǝ ɓa dǝga japǝr biya, bakǝvakwaha baɗǝm nǝ dǝgiti taga nǝ-iin tǝghǝr kǝ uudanǝna ba jirra.”
JOH 10:42 Lii ndzar vakwah dlaɓa baɗyaka fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Yesu.
JOH 11:1 Ndza mǝng nǝ uuda nǝ iin ɗaagaan Liyazaru kwa ndza yanng biya, ndzǝga ma Betani, gǝdzǝr kǝsaatǝr kǝ Maryam ard dǝghwa babbaan Marta.
JOH 11:2 Ba kwaniin kǝ Maryam wa yanng bi zǝra babbaan Lazarusa, iin wa ɗaighara wala tǝrshin bǝtbǝt tǝ shigahaha Yaazhigǝla, dlaɓa masardan dǝ guja ghǝraana.
JOH 11:3 Kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg kǝ dǝghwaha babbaan buna kǝ ghai davak Yesu taakiya, “Yaazhigǝla, dadda kwagha waig nǝngna, yanng biya.”
JOH 11:4 Cinngha ba nǝ Yesu ǝndkwaha, aiyama, “Kwan kǝ yanngbiyǝra da tsǝgabi kǝmtsǝg biya. Bakǝvakwaha, da saa dǝ ndanngǝr nǝ wan kǝ Dadamazhigǝla, dlaɓa fǝvvaara Zǝraana.”
JOH 11:5 Waigaan nǝ Yesu kǝ Martla ard dǝghwa babbaan Maryama ard Liyazaru.
JOH 11:6 Cinngha ba Yesu taakiya yanng bi nǝ Liyazaru biya, kaa gwiya gaha kǝ hǝngah bu vakavaki ndza dǝ iina.
JOH 11:7 Tǝhala kwaha, aiyama taa kǝ mbǝrzahaana, “Gwiya jiyam daadama haaya Yahudiya.”
JOH 11:8 Aiyam nǝ mbǝrzahaana taa kǝ iina, “Dadda tsaga dǝgita, bamma hǝnngahaan dalna, Yahudah ɓagarɓag kǝlaa ndzǝɗaatǝr kǝ ɗawala kǝgh da akur kiyava tsa kǝgha, aitsǝm agha naa gwiya daada vaakwaha?”
JOH 11:9 Kaa ngutǝrangug Yesu taakiya, “Abi au kǝlaawa tarbu ma vanng pal? Baɗǝm daddakwa dagal dǝ vaciya, maay tsǝgaan nǝ mɓǝdǝg biya, kwakyarvad nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ paraka duniya.
JOH 11:10 Daddakwa dagal kavǝɗa, tsǝgaan nǝ mbǝɗga, kwakyarvad maay nǝ parak vakaan biya.
JOH 11:11 Tǝhala kwa tagada nǝ iin kwaha, kaa gwiya tagtǝrtag kǝ iin taakiya, “Tsaghwa miyam Liyazaru tsaatsǝg haara, ǝn dagal da ciigaana.”
JOH 11:12 Aiyam mbǝrzahaan taa kǝ iina, “Yaazhigǝla, ma ba haara wa tsǝgatsǝga da mbǝga.”
JOH 11:13 Taga taakiya ǝmtsaaǝmtsǝg Liyazaru nǝ Yesu, mbǝrzahaan tlatlar ba taakiya ba haara jiijiir wa hǝnng nǝ iina.
JOH 11:14 Kaa ba tagtǝrdatag kǝ Yesu bat ɓalaɓal taakiya, “Əmǝtsaaǝmtsǝga Liyazaru.
JOH 11:15 Ən dlaiga nai kwakyarvad kurama aɗaba ndzan maay vakwah biya, kiyava fadǝghǝr kǝskurama. Ciyamciiga, jiyam dagal da vakaana.”
JOH 11:16 Am Toma, kwa ɗahav Didimus taa kǝ kyalǝma mbǝrzaha, “Jiyam dagal ghǝrava miyama, kiyam ǝmtsan ǝmtaɗ dǝ iina.”
JOH 11:17 Tsǝgwa ba Yesu vaakwahiina, cinnghacinng taakiya, ǝmtsaaǝmtsǝg Liyazaru, hǝngaan uufaɗ ma gǝtla.
JOH 11:18 Betani ndza ba hyɛf dǝ Wurshalima dǝt bi dat mil bu taatakatǝr biya.
JOH 11:19 Baɗyak Yahudahi sarǝv saa tagar dzǝgwagh ǝmtsǝga zǝra babbaatǝr kǝ Martla ard Maryama.
JOH 11:20 Cinngha ba Martla taakiya sagau Yesu, kaa dagal kǝ iin da tlǝgaraatlǝga. Maryam dlaɓa ndzǝga ma hǝnyaha.
JOH 11:21 Aiyam nǝ Martl taa kǝ Yesu, “Yaazhigǝla, magha ndza mǝng nǝng vaakwana, maa ǝmtsa bi zǝra baabar biya.
JOH 11:22 Aanji ba ndakwan ndakwi ǝn sǝrgasǝrga taakiya baɗǝm nǝ dǝgit agha ghalga nǝng vǝlakvǝlǝg Daadamazhigǝla.”
JOH 11:23 Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Da gwiya ciig zǝra baabagha.”
JOH 11:24 Kaa ngugarangug Martl taakiya, “Ən sǝrgasǝrga da ciig dǝ shiifǝg ma gǝtlah daghwvala ghyǝnga duniya.”
JOH 11:25 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Kai ciig ma gǝtlah ard shiifǝga. Daddakwa fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ kaiya, aanji ǝmtsana da ciig dǝ shiifǝga.
JOH 11:26 Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa ndzǝgan tǝdvad fadghǝr tǝ kaiya, da tapnai kǝ ǝmtsǝg biya. Fǝghǝdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ kwanna?”
JOH 11:27 Aiyam Martla taa kǝ iina, “Aana, Yaazhigǝla, fandǝghǝrǝtfǝg taakiya kǝgh nǝ Kǝristi, Zǝra Daadamazhigǝl kwa da sii samma duniya.”
JOH 11:28 Tagada ba Martl kwana, kaa daas kǝ iin ɗahant kǝ dǝghwa babbaan Maryam damma dlǝmmbaava, amaa, “Wa sǝghǝvsǝg dadda tsaga dǝgita, wai nǝ iin ndava kǝgha.”
JOH 11:29 Bad cinngacinnga Maryam waha, kaa ciya dagal kǝ iin ba watswats da vak Yesu.
JOH 11:30 Dagha bi nǝ Yesu damma gǝdzǝrkǝs ndan biya, ba ndzǝgaan vakavaki tlǝghara nǝ Martla.
JOH 11:31 Yahudahi kwa ndzar ǝmtaɗ dǝ Maryam ma hǝnyah ar tagar dzǝgwagha, nǝghara ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ ciya dagala Maryam ba watswatsa, kaa gatǝgaan kǝ iitǝr dagala, matlǝg ghǝraatǝr ndakwi dagal damma gǝtlaha da tuug vakwaha.
JOH 11:32 Dal ba nǝ Maryam da vakavaki dǝ Yesu, nǝghǝgha ba nǝ iina, kaa mbǝɗgambǝɗǝg kǝ iin tǝ vukwana, amaa taa kǝ iina, “Yaazhigǝla, magha mǝng nǝnga vaakwana, maa ǝmtsa bi nǝ zǝra baabaar biya.”
JOH 11:33 Nǝghǝgha ba Yesu kǝ Maryam tuuga, ard Yahudahi salar ǝmtaɗ dǝ iin ndakwi ar tuuga, kaa ngǝrɗkǝngǝrɗǝg kǝ Yesu ma ǝrviɗyana ba vaivaiya.
JOH 11:34 Kaa ndavtǝrundavǝg kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Hǝɗama vaakwari?” Am nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Yaazhigǝla, aasǝg saa vazgaana.”
JOH 11:35 Kaa tuug kǝ Yesu.
JOH 11:36 Kwakyarvad kwaha, kaa tagaan kǝ Yahudah taakiya, “Vazamvazǝg kǝ ɗuuli waiga nǝ iina.”
JOH 11:37 Aiyam kyalǝm ma iitǝr taa kǝ ghǝrahaatǝra, “Wurgharantwurǝg kǝ gyi kǝ gulfa. Maa tsǝgarvai dlaɓ kǝ uudanǝn kǝ ǝmtsǝg biya?”
JOH 11:38 Kaa gwiya mbǝkǝnmbǝg ma ǝrviɗan kǝ Yesu ba vaivaiya, ngal dagal kǝ iin damma gǝtliina. Gǝtliin huravna ma kura, kaa hǝɗvarduhǝɗǝg ghaiyan dǝ akura.
JOH 11:39 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Tlǝgamarwatlǝg kǝ akurna.” Aiyam Martla dǝghwa babba uudanǝn ǝmtsaaǝmtsǝgǝn taa kǝ Yesu, “Yaazhigǝla, abi shiig ndakwana, aɗaba hǝngaan uufaɗ hinanan ba vaakwaha.”
JOH 11:40 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Tagan kaki taakiya akwama fǝghǝdǝghǝrǝtfǝga, agha da nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ ndangǝra Daadamazhigǝl biya?”
JOH 11:41 Kaa tlǝgarwatlǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ akurǝna. Kaa dzǝgantdzǝg kǝ Yesu kǝ ghǝran damma ghǝrazhigǝla amaa, “Ən tagak uusa, Daada, kwakyarvad cinnghwanacinnga.
JOH 11:42 Ən sǝrgasǝrǝg agha cinngwanacinng ba kǝlaa hǝnga, na tagda kwakyarvad uudahaan ghacga vaakwanǝn ar fǝdghǝrǝt taakiya, kǝgh wa ɓǝlǝghkwadi kaiya.”
JOH 11:43 Tǝhala kwa tagada nǝ Yesu kǝ kwaha, kaa dzǝgantdzǝg kǝ iin kǝ ghaiya baɗyakɗyaka amaa, “Liyazaru, asǝg sagala!”
JOH 11:44 Kaa ba sagal kǝ uudanǝn ǝmtsaǝmtsanǝna, faɗafaɗan ma kǝlpakan baz dǝvvahaan ard shigahaana, huɗvǝgaan dlaɓa kutakutan ma kǝlpakanǝn hǝɗana dǝvakaina. Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Futamaarafutǝga, aa dǝg dagala.”
JOH 11:45 Aɗabad kwaha, baɗyak yaa Yahudah kwa salar sa nǝghǝgara kǝ Maryama, dlaɓa nǝghǝgharanǝghǝg kǝ dǝgit ɓagaa nǝ Yesu, kaa fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg kǝ iitǝr tǝ iina.
JOH 11:46 Bakǝvakwaha kaa dagal kǝ kyalmaatǝr davak Farisiha, ar tagtǝr kǝ dǝgit ɓagaa nǝ Yesu.
JOH 11:47 Aɗabad kwaha, kaa ɗahgantɗahǝg kǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsauufah ard Farisih kǝ dzahava gyiɗya. Ar ndavaru kǝ ghǝrahatǝra am nǝ iitǝra, “Auwa kiyam da ɓag nǝ miyammi? Vazǝg kǝ uudanǝn za ba vukw dǝ ɓa dǝgaha ajappǝr baɗyaka!
JOH 11:48 Akwama ɓǝlyamarnaaɓǝlg kǝ ɓa kwanahaana, baɗǝm nǝ uudaha ar da fadghǝr tǝ iina. Kaa da sagau kǝ Romah ar da kǝsuu kǝ Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla miyamma ard dlamaa kǝlaawa miyama.”
JOH 11:49 Pal ma iitǝra kwa ɗahav dǝ Kayafa, kwandza maal ba tingting ma zhiila kǝsauufah ma kwaha kǝ viiga, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kuram am sǝrgai ba ndau biya.
JOH 11:50 Nǝghamaaka biya, abi ngulǝm ǝmtsa nǝ uud pal kwakyarvad uudaha, tǝghǝr kwada ruuga nǝ dlamakǝlaaw baɗǝm?”
JOH 11:51 Tagada dǝ naaga ghǝran bi nǝ Kayaf kǝ kwah biya, aɗaba ndza iin maal ba tingting ma zhiila kǝsauufah makwaha kǝ viiga, tagadatag kǝ tlayangǝr taakiya, da ǝmtsǝg Yesu kwakyarvad dlamaa kǝlaawa Yahudaha,
JOH 11:52 mbakyarvad Yahudah kalti biya, dlaɓa kiyava dzaha zarha Daadamazhigǝl kwa kwazarakwazǝg aanji takwara, ar nal kǝ palla.
JOH 11:53 Ciigǝt daghuvala kwahiin kǝ sarta, kaa ɗiya sawariya tsa shifǝga Yesu kǝ iitǝra.
JOH 11:54 Kwakyarvad kwaha gwiya bi Yesu gwayav ma taataka dlamaa kǝlaawa Yahudah tǝ ɓalal biya, dlakulva kwaha kaa ɗuugharsɗug kǝ iin kǝ vakavakina, kaa ba dagal kǝ iin damma lard kwa hyɛf dǝ tǝghala, kaa daas damma gǝdzǝr kǝs kwa ɗahav dǝ Ifrayim, vakavaki ndza nǝ iin dǝ mbǝrzahaana.
JOH 11:55 Hǝrzǝt ba nǝ Haarakǝsa Dzǝva Hǝnyaha Yahudaha, kaa dagat kǝ lii ma gǝdzǝrkǝs baɗyak damma Wurushalima kiyava pǝsha ghǝraatǝr lakwti kǝ haarakǝs bandkwa tagaa nǝ dǝga daadijahaatǝra.
JOH 11:56 Tlatǝr ba gata Yesu, kaa daas kǝ iitǝr damma gaagazaiya Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl ar ghacan ar ndava zarabahaatǝr taakiya, “Au wam tlatlǝg nǝ uuram? Da ba sagau nǝ iin kwan damma haarakǝsa?”
JOH 11:57 Aɗaba ndza tagardatag nǝ maalaha zhiila kǝsauufah ard Farisiyah ba wur taakiya, baɗǝm daadakwa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ vakavaki dǝ Yesu, aa sasǝg sa tagaana, kiyava vigaan kǝ iitǝra.
JOH 12:1 Tǝmma ba hǝnng ǝngkwah kǝ haarakǝsa Dzava Hǝnnyaha, kaa ba dagal kǝ Yesu damma Betani vakavaki dǝ Liyazaru, kwa ciighant Yesu dǝ shiifǝga.
JOH 12:2 Kaa tǝvaratǝg kafa hwaas kǝ Yesu. Martl wa tagwa kafa, pal Liyazaru ma uudahi ndzar zaa kaf ǝmtaɗ dǝ Yesu.
JOH 12:3 Kaa ba kǝsgantkǝsǝg kǝ Maryam kǝ ghǝndǝka sǝmtala tǝrshǝna nardi, kwaba pir ganana, ɗayarǝt tǝ shigaha Yesu, dlaɓa masaradan kǝ shigahaan dǝ guja ghǝrana. Kaa ba gǝgagǝg kǝ shiiga tǝrshinǝn kǝ hǝnyah baɗǝmma.
JOH 12:4 Bakǝvakwaha, am Yahuda Iskariyoti, pal ma mbǝrzahaan kwa da vǝlǝgaana,
JOH 12:5 “Auwjilbǝg maa vǝlavǝt bi nǝ tǝrshinǝn tǝ kwaɓ kwa tlǝkǝna nǝ bariyam ma vannga dǝrmǝk hǝkǝrɗ, tǝhala kwaha vǝlvtǝr kǝ talagah biyi?”
JOH 12:6 Tagada kwakyarvad naa mǝltǝru kǝ talagah bi nǝ Yahud kǝ kwah biya, aɗaba gǝl nǝ iina. Dlaɓa iin dadda hǝkya kwaɓaatǝra, ɓaa gǝl sagal ma vakaiya.
JOH 12:7 Aiyam nǝ Yesu, “Aɗuuga, ndza fa kwakyarvad daghuvali kwada hǝɗkwa nǝ uuda.
JOH 12:8 Am ba kǝlaa hǝnng ǝmtaɗ dǝ talagaha, aɗaba am maay kǝlaa hǝnng ǝmtaɗ dǝ kai biya.”
JOH 12:9 Ciingara ba dzahava Yahudah baɗyak taakiya vakwan Yesu, kaa sagau kǝ iitǝra, sarǝv kwakyarvad Yesu kalti biya, aɗaba ar vaznan baz Liyazaru kwa cighant Yesu dǝ shiifǝga.
JOH 12:10 Kaa ɗiiya sawariya kǝ maalaha zhilla kǝsauufaha, kiyava tsǝgaan kǝ iitǝr baz Liyazaru,
JOH 12:11 aɗaba tǝdvad Liyazaru wa ɗuwarars Yahudah baɗyak kǝ zhilla kǝsauufahaatǝr ar fadghǝr tǝ Yesu.
JOH 12:12 Wurga kǝsaana, cinngaracinng nǝ uudah baɗyak kwa sarǝv sa vaka Hwaɗaga Haarakǝsa Dzava Hǝnnyah taakiya, tǝghǝrdǝga dagat damma Wurshalim Yesu.
JOH 12:13 Kaa cagantcag kǝ iitǝr kǝ apayapaya njuura, kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr da vakaana, ar dzǝgant kǝ ghai ar ɗiyaru kǝ cawa, ar taakiya, “Hosanna! Bark kǝ daddakwa sagauw ma ɗaaga Yaazhigǝla! Barka kǝ tlǝkǝsa yaa Israila!”
JOH 12:14 Tlǝghaara ba Yesu kǝ zǝra aghyungwa, kaa ɗalgaan kǝ iina, bandkwa vindava taakiya,
JOH 12:15 “Gǝdz bi Dǝghwa Sihiyon biya; vazǝg kǝ tlǝksagh saas cǝhurga tǝ zǝra aghyungwa”.
JOH 12:16 Ba zǝngwa nǝgharaaka bi mbǝrzahaan kǝ kwan kǝ dǝgit biya, da nǝgharaaka tǝhalakwa favaara Yesu, kaa dzamgaan kǝ iitǝr taakiya, vindavavindǝg nǝ wan kǝ dǝgitaha tǝghǝr kǝ iina, dlaɓa dǝginahaan dzǝghaardzǝg bakalkalla bandkwa viindavana.
JOH 12:17 Uudahi ndzar ǝmtaɗ dǝ iin masarta kwa ɗahghant nǝ iin kǝ Liyazaru sagal magǝtla, dlaɓa ciyan kǝ iin dǝ shiifǝga, kaa zavukw kǝ iitǝr dǝ tagtǝr dǝgitahi ɓagatǝra Yesu kǝ uudaha.
JOH 12:18 Daral nǝ uudah baɗyak da dlǝgha Yesu kwakyarvad cinngaracinng kǝ dǝga ajapǝri ɓagaa nǝ iina.
JOH 12:19 Aiyam Farisiyaha ma taatakatǝra, “Wayamciya, maay vakavaki langkiyam wan biya. Vazamzǝg kǝ ɗulli gatǝg duni kǝ iin baɗǝmma.”
JOH 12:20 Ndza mǝng kyalma Helenaha ma lii daral da ɓa kwatǝnahǝr ma sarta hwaɗaga haarakǝsa.
JOH 12:21 Kaa sagau kǝ iitǝr sa vak Filigus uuda Betsaida ma haaya Galili, kaa ndavgarundavǝg kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Dadda ndanga, ma kǝmnda naagaan ma kǝmnda nǝghǝgha kǝ Yesu.”
JOH 12:22 Kaa dagal kǝ Filigus da tagar kǝ Andrawus, kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr ba bǝrkuɗaatǝr ar tagar kǝ Yesu.
JOH 12:23 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iitǝr, “Ɓagaaɓag sart kwada fǝvaara Zǝra Uuda.
JOH 12:24 Bak jiijiira, ǝn tagkurtaga, ma riiyava bi zǝra hǝi damma haay ǝmtsan biya, ndzǝga ba njakǝɗinjaana. Akwama ǝmtsaaǝmtsǝga, yiigaan kǝ zǝrh baɗyaka.
JOH 12:25 Baɗǝm daddakwa waiya shifǝgaana da ɓǝlgaan dagala, baɗǝm daddakwa ɗuugant shifǝgaan ma duunina, da tlǝknatlǝg kǝ shifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝra.
JOH 12:26 Baɗǝm daddakwa da ɓaguwa tlǝra, barari gatkwagatǝga. Baɗǝm vakavaki dǝ kaiya, da ndzǝga ba ǝmtaɗ dǝ kai nǝ daddakwa ɓaguwa tlǝra. Da fǝgaarafǝg Daadar kǝ daddakwa ɓaguwa tlǝra.”
JOH 12:27 “Ndakwana mbakwambǝg ma ǝrviɗyara. Au ci wan da tag naiyi? Ən taakiya, ‘Daada, katkwakatǝg ma kwan kǝ sart nii?’ Maaya, sanhi ba kǝrkangyǝkw kwakyarvad kwan kǝ sarta.
JOH 12:28 Daada, faarafǝg kǝ ɗaagagha.” Kaa sii kǝ ghai sii ma ghǝrazhigǝla amaa, “Fanaarafǝga, dlaɓa ǝn da gwiya fǝgaarafǝga.”
JOH 12:29 Ciingara ba nǝ uudahaan ghacga vakwahǝn kǝ ghaiya, am nǝ iitǝra, “Karazhigǝl waa tlaava.” Am kyǝlǝm dlaɓa, “Zǝrɓǝlg waa tagar ghaiya.”
JOH 12:30 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kwan kǝ ghai sahi kwakyarvad mǝlkuruwa, kwakyarvad kai biya.
JOH 12:31 Da tǝvar ndakwan nǝ shari kǝ duniya, da lagwav ndakwan dlaɓ nǝ dadda kwara duunina.
JOH 12:32 Mada tsǝgwakuttsǝgw nǝ uud ma duniya, ǝn da tǝɗda kǝ uudah baɗǝm sa vakara.”
JOH 12:33 Tagada kwakyarvad marda nǝ Yesu kǝ hulfa ǝmtsǝgi da ǝmtsǝg nǝ iina.
JOH 12:34 Aiyam nǝ uudah taa kǝ Yesu, “Tagakǝmǝndatag nǝ adzahadzah taakiya, da ndzǝga bad shiifǝg nǝ Kǝristi ba ɗǝmma. Agha tag ndandar kaci taakiya barari nǝ zǝr uuda da tsǝgwavi? War nǝ Zǝr Uudiini?”
JOH 12:35 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Parakǝrǝn ǝmtaɗ dǝ kuramna, da zǝlma bi vaivai biya. Damdagal bamma sartǝn mǝng nǝ parak ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kurama, aa tlǝkuraa bi gurtl biya. Daddakwa dagal ma gurtla sǝrgai kǝ vakavaki dagal nǝ iin biya.
JOH 12:36 Famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ parakǝna, bamma sarti am ǝmtaɗ dǝ iina, aɗaba am nal kǝ zǝrha paraka.” Tǝhala tagdatag kǝ Yesu kǝ kwan kǝ ǝlbǝga, kaa dagal kǝ iin shǝɓvana.
JOH 12:37 Baaba dǝgaha jappǝrǝn ɓagaa Yesu tǝvukwatǝrna, bakǝvakwha larwalǝg kǝ fadǝghǝr tǝ iina.
JOH 12:38 Dzǝghaar kwakyarvad righǝvant nǝ dǝgit taga nǝ tlayang Ishaya wannǝn taakiya, “Yaazhigǝla, warwa fǝdghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ ǝlbǝgamndi, dlaɓa margharda kǝ war nǝ Yaazhigǝl kǝ dǝgiti ɓagaa nǝ dǝvaani?”
JOH 12:39 Kwakyarvd kwan nǝ iin wa fardghǝrǝt bi nǝ iitǝr biya, bandkwa tagada nǝ Ishaya vakavaki tlǝrǝn taakiya,
JOH 12:40 “Gulfǝghantgulfǝg kǝ gyiyahaatǝra, dlaɓa naatǝrdalnǝg kǝ ǝrviɗyatǝr ba dǝkdǝka, haik kǝ nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iitǝr dǝ gyiyahaatǝra, dlaɓa haik kǝ nǝghǝgaakanǝghǝg ma ǝrviɗyatǝra, haik gwiya sa vakar kǝ iitǝra, ǝn mbǝtǝranana.”
JOH 12:41 Tagada kwakyarvad nǝghanǝghǝg nǝ Ishaya kǝ ndangǝra Yesu, dlaɓa tagda kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ iina.
JOH 12:42 Bakǝvakwaha, uudah baɗyak fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Yesu, baz maalahatǝr baɗyak fardghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ iina. Kwakyarvad gǝdza Farisiyaha, tagarai taakiya fardghǝrǝtfǝg biya, haik lagwtǝrlagw sagal ma guda dzǝgwazhigǝla.
JOH 12:43 Aɗaba ar waiya ba galǝg vak uudaha tǝghǝr kǝ galǝg vak Dadamazhǝgǝla.
JOH 12:44 Kaa dzǝgantdzǝg Yesu kǝ ghaiya, amaa, “Baɗǝm daddakwa fadghǝr tǝ kaiya, fadghǝr tǝ kaiy kalti biya, fadghǝr tǝ dadakwa ɓalakwadi kaiya.
JOH 12:45 Baɗǝm daddakwa vaza dat kaiya, nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya.
JOH 12:46 Sanhi band parak nai samma duniya, aɗaba haik kǝ ndzǝgan kǝ daddakwa fadghǝr tǝ kai baɗǝm ma gurǝtla.
JOH 12:47 Baɗǝm dadakwa cinnghacinng kǝ ǝlbǝgahara, dlaɓa tsuufghant biya, kai bi dadda tǝgar shari biya. Sanhi kwakyarvad tǝgar shari kǝ duni nai biya, aɗaba ǝn katant kǝ duniya.
JOH 12:48 Daddakwa ɗuwakusɗuuga, dlaɓa haighant bi kǝ ǝlbǝgar biya, mǝng daddakwa tǝgar shariya, ǝlbǝgǝn taganda naina, iin wa da tǝgar shari daghuvala ghyǝnga duniya.
JOH 12:49 Dǝginahaan ǝn tag nai sagal vakar biya, Daada kwa ɓǝlakwadi kai iin wa taghwatag kǝ dǝgiti ǝn da tag naiya.
JOH 12:50 Ən sǝrgasǝrǝg dlaɓa shifǝga tangw dama zǝrazǝra tlǝvǝkǝna tǝdǝvad dǝgiti tag Daada. Kwakyarvad kwaha baɗǝm nǝ dǝgit naa tagda naiya, naa tagda ba kalkal bandkwa taghwa Daada taakiya aa tagantaga.”
JOH 13:1 Lakwti ɓag sarta Hwaɗaga Haarakǝsa Dzǝva Hǝnnyaha, sǝrghaakasǝrǝg Yesu taakiya ɓaagɓag sartaan kwada ɗuug nǝ iin kǝ duni kiyava gwiya daas da vak Daada. Waighantwaig tsau Yesu kǝ uudahaan ma duniya, dlaɓ maratǝrdamarǝg kǝ waiyakǝvaan tangw dat ghaalaana.
JOH 13:2 Lakwti za kafa hwaas kǝ Yesu ard mbǝrzahaana, fagharafǝg Shatanah kǝ Yahuda, zǝra Saminu Iskariyoti kǝ vǝla Yesu.
JOH 13:3 Sǝrgasǝrǝg Yesu taakiya, fadǝmfǝg Daad kǝ dǝgitah miizha dǝvaan baɗǝmma, dlaɓa sǝrgasǝrǝg sahi vak Daadamazhigǝla, da gwiiya daas da vak Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 13:4 Ma sartǝn ar za kafna, kaa ciigǝtciig Yesu, tsugda kǝ sǝɗavaani gyimala, kǝsant kǝ patkara sǝɗav nguɗǝs tǝ ngyilaana.
JOH 13:5 Tǝhala kwaha gǝt kǝ iin kǝ yu ma kuwa, farzha kǝ bara shigaha mbǝrzahaana, dǝrda kǝ shigahaatǝr dǝ patkara sǝɗav kwa nguɗǝs nǝ iin tǝ ngyilaanna.
JOH 13:6 Kaa sagauw kǝ Yesu da vak Bitrus. Am Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Yazhǝgǝla, kǝgh wa da bargwa shigahara?”
JOH 13:7 Kaa ngugangug Yesu taakiya, “Agha sǝrga bi kǝ dǝgit ǝn ɓag nai ndakwan biya, agha da nǝghǝgaaka tǝ hala.”
JOH 13:8 Aiyam Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Maaya! agha tapna bi kǝ bargwa shigahar biya.” Kaa ngugarangug kǝ Yesu, amaa, “Ai ciya, akwama barankada biya, agha maay ǝmtaɗ dǝ kai biya.”
JOH 13:9 Aiyam Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Yazhigǝla, aa ɗuug kǝ shigahar kalti biya, baz dǝvvahara ard ghǝrara.”
JOH 13:10 Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Akwama baraabarǝg nǝ uuda, baɗǝm nǝ vǝghaan ba cuwaɗaɗɗa. Madlai lambaan dǝ barg biya, bamma barda kǝ shigahaan kaltiya. Aɗaba am ba cuwaɗaɗɗa, bakǝvakwaha, ɗǝmaru biya.”
JOH 13:11 Aɗaba sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ daddakwa da za langyiyaana, iinwa tag nǝ iin taakiya, “Kuram ɗǝm bi wa cuwaɗaɗ biya.”
JOH 13:12 Ghyǝnnga ba nǝ iin bartǝr shiggahatǝra, kaa gwiya tsǝgwǝv kǝ sǝɗɗavaana, kaa gwiiya kǝ iin davak ndzǝggaanana. Kaa ndavǝtǝrndavǝg kǝ iina amaa, “Nǝghǝghamakanǝghǝg kǝ dǝgit ǝnna ɓagkur naiya?
JOH 13:13 Am ɗaa kai dǝ dadda tsaga dǝgita, dlaɓa Yazhǝgǝla. Ba kalkalla, aɗaɓa ǝn band kwaha naiya.
JOH 13:14 Ən Yazhǝgǝlaruwa ard Daddatsaga dǝgitaru tsauwa, barrankurdabarǝg kǝ shiga, kats kuram ndakwi barari am barrgarbarrǝg kǝ shig kǝ zaraabahaaruwa.
JOH 13:15 Marankurdamarǝg kǝ garav kǝyavva ɓagaan kǝskuram band kwana ɓakura naiya.
JOH 13:16 Bak jiijiira ǝn tagkurtaga, kwatnaha jigubi kǝ daddahǝnǝhya biya, zǝrɓǝllǝg dlaɓa jiguwi kǝ daddakwa ɓǝllǝgaan biya.
JOH 13:17 Ndakwanna am asǝrgasǝrg tsau kǝ kwannahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, akwaman ɓagaana am da dǝ barka.
JOH 13:18 Ən tag tǝghǝr kǝsskuram ɗǝm biya. Ən sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ uudahi dzǝrantǝraaka naiya. Kwannǝn dlaɓa kwakyarvad righǝvant nǝ dǝgit ma kakaɗa Dadamazhǝgǝla taakiya, ‘Daddakwa kǝm zaa kaf ǝmǝtaɗa nalnǝg kǝ tlǝghumara.’
JOH 13:19 Ən tagkurtag ndakwana lakuti dzǝgaadzǝga, aɗaba ma da dzǝghaardzǝga, famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg taakiya ba kaiyina.
JOH 13:20 Bak jiijiira ǝn tagkurtaga, daddakwa dlǝghadlǝg kǝ daddakwana ɓǝlgant nai bad rivǝɗmahuɗ palla, dlǝghaakwidlǝg kǝsskaiya. Dlaɓa daddakwa dlǝghaakwidlǝg kǝsskaiya dlǝghaadlǝg kǝ daddakwa ɓallakwadi kaiya.”
JOH 13:21 Tǝhala tagdataga Yesu kwanen kǝ ǝlbǝga, mbakǝnmbǝg ma ǝrivɗyana. Kaa tagaan kǝ iin bat ɓallaɓal taakiya, “Bak jiijiira, ǝn tagkurtaga, pallaruwa da vǝlkwavǝlǝga.”
JOH 13:22 Kaa vazakǝv kǝ mbǝrzahaan mataatakaatǝra, aɗaba ar sǝrgai kǝ mbǝrzi tag nǝ Yesu kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr biya.
JOH 13:23 Pal ma mbǝrzahaana, kwa waig nǝ iina, ndzǝgaan bahyǝf dǝ inna,
JOH 13:24 Wiika am nǝ Bitrus dǝ dǝv taa kǝ mbǝrzǝna, ndavarundavǝg kǝ Yesu tag tǝghǝr kǝ warra.
JOH 13:25 Kaa dǝngzharva kǝ mbǝrzǝn tǝvǝgh kǝ Yesu ndavaruwa amaa, “War wahiin, Yazhigǝli?”
JOH 13:26 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Ən da hǝgaan kǝ ghudǝga bruudi damma taasa. Dadakwan da vǝlga naiya, iin nǝ uuda nǝ iina.” Kǝssghant ba nǝ Yesu kǝ ghudǝga bruudin hǝdǝmma, kaa vǝlla kǝ iin kǝ Yahuda zǝra siman Iskariyoti.
JOH 13:27 Cauwa ba nǝ iin kǝ ghudǝga bruudi kaa dass kǝ shatanah dama vǝghaana bawatswatsa. Kaa am Yesu kǝ Yahuda, “Dǝginǝn aghanaa ɓag nǝngnaa ɓag bawatswatsa.”
JOH 13:28 Maay ma lii za kafǝn wa nǝghǝghakanǝghǝg kǝ dǝgit tuuk vakaiy wa taghar nǝ Yesu kǝ iin biya.
JOH 13:29 Yahuda tsau wa hǝkya ambǝlla kwaɓatǝra, kyǝlǝma mbǝrzaah tlatlar ba taakiya tagghar aa sǝgwasǝgw kǝ dǝgit naahaava kwakyarvad haarakǝssa nǝ Yesu, bi vǝllǝtǝr kǝ dǝgit kǝ talaggaha.
JOH 13:30 Cauwa ba nǝ iin kǝ ghudǝga bruudina, kaa dagalaana. Masarta kwaha ndza avǝɗ vakka.
JOH 13:31 Tǝhala kwa dagal Yahuda, am Yesu, “Aa fǝvvaara ndakwan nǝ Zǝr Uuda, dlaɓa faavaarafǝg nǝ Dadamazhǝgǝl tǝdǝvad iina.
JOH 13:32 Akwama fǝvaarafǝg nǝ Dadamazhǝgǝl tǝdǝvad iina, Dadamazhǝgǝl da fǝgaarafǝg kǝ zǝraan bad ghǝraana, dlaɓa da fǝgaarafǝga bawatswatsa.
JOH 13:33 “Kuram Zarhara, tǝmma bahǝɗiikǝn nǝ ndzǝgana ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kurama. Am da gatkwagatǝga, bandkwa tagantǝr nai kǝ yaa Yahud taakiya, ‘Ən tagkurtag bandakwanna, Vakavaki ǝn da dagal naiya am da sǝgǝv biya.’
JOH 13:34 “Dalla adzahadzah wan vǝllǝkur naiya, waiyamwaig kǝ uuda. Bandkwan waiyankurǝt naiya, kuram ndakwi waiyamwaig kǝ uudaha.
JOH 13:35 Tǝdǝvad kwamam waigaan kǝ uuda da sǝrǝggasǝrǝg aanji war taakiya am mbǝrzahaara.”
JOH 13:36 Ndavǝgharundavǝg Siman Bitrus kǝ Yesu amaa, “Yaazhigǝla, agha da dagal da vakwari?” Ngughaarangug nǝ Yesu amaa, “Ndakwana vakavaki ǝn da dagal naiya agha da gatkus biya, tǝhala agha da gatkusgatǝga.”
JOH 13:37 Aiyam Bitrus taa kǝ iina, “Yazhigǝla, aujilbǝg ǝn gatkǝsi ndakwan biyi? Ən da vǝlgaan kǝ shifǝgar kwakyarvad kǝgha.”
JOH 13:38 Aiyam nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Aaya, agha da vǝlgaan kǝ shifǝgagh kwakyarvad kaiya? Bak jiijiira, ǝn tagkataga, lakwti wiig ghwatkal agha da ɓalgaan kǝ agajauwa sǝrkwa bi shig hǝkǝrɗa.”
JOH 14:1 “Ndavǝm biya, famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Dadamazhǝgǝla, dlaɓa famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ kaiya.
JOH 14:2 Ma vǝgya Daadara mǝng nǝ vaka ndzǝgaan baɗyaka. Akwamaamaay ndkwaha biya manaa maay tagkurtag kwan biya. Ən dagal da vakwaha kwakyarvad ǝn ɓadlkurnan kǝ vakavaka.
JOH 14:3 Akwama danǝt ɓadlankurnaɓadlǝg kǝ vaka, ǝn da saaya ǝn dǝkurda da vakara, aɗaba kuram ndakwi am ndzan vavaki dǝ kaiya.
JOH 14:4 Ghǝravaru ndakwi am sǝrǝggasǝrǝg kǝ ɗuula daa da vakavaki ǝn dagal naiya.”
JOH 14:5 Am Toma taa kǝ Yesu, “Yaazhigǝla, kǝm sǝrǝgai kǝ vavaki agha dagal nǝng biya, kǝm da sǝrga ndandar kaci kǝ ɗuuli?”
JOH 14:6 Ngugharangug nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Kai ɗuula, kai jiira, kai dlaɓa ǝn shiifǝga. Maay wa dǝgaadǝg da vak Daada biya bamma tǝdǝvad kaiya.
JOH 14:7 Akwama maa sǝrkwasǝrga, mammaa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ Daadara. Ma ndakwanǝrna ndakwana am sǝrgasǝrǝga, dlaɓa nǝghǝghamakanǝghǝg kǝ iina.”
JOH 14:8 Aiyam Filigus taa kǝ iina, “Yazhigǝla, akwama marghǝkǝmdadamarǝg kǝ Daadiina, tsǝghatsǝg kǝ puutamnda.”
JOH 14:9 Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Zǝlanmazǝlmǝg ǝmtaɗ dǝ kurama, gwastǝn agha sǝrkwa bi Filibus biya? Baɗǝm daddakwa nǝghakwanǝghǝga, nǝghǝghanǝghǝg kǝ Daadiina. Agha tag ndarndar kaci, ‘Marwadamarǝg kǝ Daadiini’?
JOH 14:10 Fǝghǝdǝghǝrǝt bi taakiya kai ǝn ma Daada, dlaɓa Daada ma kaiy biya? Əlbǝgahahaan ǝn tagkur naina dǝ ndzǝɗa ghǝrar biya, Daadǝn ndzǝga ma kai na iin wa ɓa tlǝrahaaana.
JOH 14:11 Famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ kaiya masartǝn ǝn tag nai ǝn ma Daadna, Daadiin dlaɓ ma kaiya, aanji ba kwakyarvad tlǝraha japǝrǝn ǝn ɓag naiy na famdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ kaiya.
JOH 14:12 Bak jiijiir ǝn tagkurtaga, baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa fadǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ kaiya, da ɓagaan kǝ tlǝrahaan ǝn ɓag naiyna. Da ɓagaan baz kwa jujig kǝ kwannahaan kǝ tlǝraaha aɗaba ǝn daa da vak Daada.
JOH 14:13 Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgiti am ghalǝg nǝ uuram ma ɗagara ǝn ɓagkurɓaga, aɗaba Daadina fǝvaaran tǝdǝvad Zǝra.
JOH 14:14 Aanji aau wam ghallǝg nǝ uuram ma ɗagara, ǝn ɓagkurɓaga.
JOH 14:15 “Akwama mam waikwawaiga, gatamgatǝg kǝ adzahadzahara.
JOH 14:16 Ən da ghalgaan kǝ Daada, iin dlaɓa da vǝlkurvǝlǝg kǝ daddakwa da mǝlkurmǝlǝg ndzan ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kuram tangw damma zǝrazǝra.
JOH 14:17 Iin shǝɗkwa jiijiira, kwa lawa duni kǝ tlǝghǝgaana aɗaba nǝghǝghǝga biya bi sǝrǝga kǝ iin biya. Kurama am sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ iina, aɗaba ndzǝga ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kurama, dlaɓa da ndzǝga ma ǝrivɗyaruwa.
JOH 14:18 Ən ɗukurǝs bi ǝnd taaghah biya, ǝn da sagau sa vakaruwa.
JOH 14:19 Gǝɗya ba sart hǝɗikǝna da madlai duni nǝghǝkwanǝghǝg biya, amaa kurama am da nǝghkwanǝghǝga. Aɗaba ǝn dǝshiifǝga, kuram dlaɓa am da bad shiifǝga.
JOH 14:20 Daghuvala kwaniin kǝ faci wam da sǝrga nǝ uuram taakiya kaiya ǝn ma Daad, kuram dlaɓa am ma kaiya, kaiya dlaɓa ǝn ma kurama.
JOH 14:21 Baɗǝm nǝ dadakwa sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ adzahadzahara, dlaɓa gatǝgaana, iin wa waiya kaiya. Daddakwa waikwawaiga dlaɓa, Daadara da waiyǝgaan kǝ iina, kaiy dlaɓa ǝn da waigaan kǝ iina ǝn marda kǝ ghǝrar vakana.”
JOH 14:22 Am Yahud taa kǝ iina, kwa Yahuda Iskariyoti biya, “Yazhigǝla, aaujilǝbǝg da mara ghǝragh vakamǝnd, kwal margar kǝ duuniyi?”
JOH 14:23 Kaa ngugwarangug kǝ Yesu amaa taa kǝ iina, “Baɗǝm nǝ daddakwa waikwawaiga, da tsuufǝgaan kǝ ǝlbǝgara, Daada dlaɓa da waiyǝgaan kǝ iina, kǝm da sagau saa vakana kǝm ndzan ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ iina.
JOH 14:24 Daddakwa maay waiya kaiy biya, maay tsuufa ǝlbǝgar biya. Əlbǝgǝn am cinng nǝ uuramǝna dǝgar biya, dǝga Daddakwa ɓǝlakwadi kaiya.
JOH 14:25 Tagankurdatag kwanahaan kǝ digitah bama sartǝn ndzan ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kurama.
JOH 14:26 Dadda mǝlgaru kǝ uuda, Shǝɗkw Daadamazhigǝla, kwa da ɓǝllǝg nǝ Daada ma ɗagara, iin wa da tsakur dǝgit baɗǝma, dlaɓa da dzamkurǝs baɗǝm kǝ dǝgit tangaankurda naiya.
JOH 14:27 Gabǝrǝr wanaa ɗukurǝs naiya, vǝllankurvǝllǝg kǝ gabǝrara. Ənna vǝllǝkur ndǝkwa vǝllǝkur nǝ duni biya. Ndavambiya, dlaɓa gǝdzam biya.
JOH 14:28 Cinngamacinng nǝ uuram kǝskai taakiya ǝn dagata, ǝn da gwiiya saay da vakaru dlaɓa. Akwamamma waikwawaig mamma dlaig kwakyarvad ǝn daddavak Daada, aɗaba Daadara jakwarajiga.
JOH 14:29 Ndakwanna tagankurdataga lauti da dzǝgardzǝga, aɗaba mada dzǝghaardzǝga famdǝghǝrǝtfǝga.
JOH 14:30 Ən da madlai gwiiya taaghaiy ɗyak biya, aɗaba dadda kwara duunina sagauwa, maay dǝ ndzǝɗ tǝghǝr kǝskai biya.
JOH 14:31 Ən ɓa dǝgit ba kalkal kwa taghwa Daada ǝn ɓagaan aɗaba sǝran nǝ duni taakiya ǝn waigaan kǝ Daada. Ciiyamciiga ɗuyamantɗug kǝ vavakǝna.”
JOH 15:1 Kaiy nǝ gyigyiya uuffa inabi, Daadar dlaɓa iin dadda uusǝga.
JOH 15:2 Aanji kwar kǝ dǝv uuf tǝ kai kwa maay yaa zǝr biya, ghudarsa. Aanji kwar kǝ dǝva uuf kwa yaayig kǝ zǝra gwiya ɓadlav kiyavva gwiya yigaan kǝ zǝr baɗyaka.
JOH 15:3 Aanji bandakwan am ba cǝwaɗaɗa kwakyarvad ǝlbǝgǝn tagaankurda naina.
JOH 15:4 Ndzamandzǝg ma kaiya, kai dlaɓa ma kurama. Bandkwa yiga bi nǝ dǝva uufa inabi kǝ zǝr dǝ ghǝran biya, bamma ndzǝga tǝ uuffa inabi, ghǝravaru ndakwi bandkwah am yiga bi kǝ zǝr biya, ba mam ndzǝga tǝ kaiya.
JOH 15:5 Kai ǝn uuffa inabi, kuram nǝ dǝvvahana. Daddakwa ndzǝga ma kaiya, kai dlaɓa ma iina, iin wa da ya zǝr baɗyaka. Aɗaba mam maay ǝmtaɗ dǝ kai biya, am ɓaga bi aanji ndau biya.
JOH 15:6 Baɗǝm daddakwa ndza bi ma kaiy biya, band dǝva uuf kwa ɓǝlavdan ghulal, hulfakwah kǝ dǝva uufa dzaavanta ɗiivǝdǝm damma kaara, dlaɓa zuu.
JOH 15:7 Ma ndzamandzǝg ma kaiya, ǝlbǝgar dlaɓa ndzandzǝg ma kurama, am da ghalǝgaan baɗǝm kǝ dǝgit am naag nǝ uurama, am da tlǝkǝnatlǝga.
JOH 15:8 Ndzamandzǝg dǝ hǝnkala marawa kwada mardamarǝg taakiya kuram am mbǝrzahaara, band uuff kwa ya zarh marawa, aɗaba kwannahaan wa fǝgaara Daadara.
JOH 15:9 Bandkwa waiyakut nǝ Daada, ǝn waiykur band kwah dlaɓa naiya. Ndzamandzǝg ma waiyavǝr bandkwa marankur da naiya.
JOH 15:10 Kaiya fanaarafǝg kǝ adzahadzaha Daadara, dlaɓa ǝn ndzǝga ma waiyavaana. Bandkwah dlaɓa, akwamamam fǝgaarafǝg kǝ adzahadzara am ndzǝga ma waiyavara.
JOH 15:11 “Tagkurdatag kǝ kwanna kwakyarvad dlaig ǝrviɗmahuɗara aa ndzandzǝg ma kurama, dlaiga ǝrivɗmahuɗaru dlaɓa aandz ba righǝgharighana.
JOH 15:12 Kwanǝn iin na adzahadzahara, waiyamwaiyig kǝ zaraabahagh band kwa waiyankurǝt naiya.
JOH 15:13 Maay nǝ waiyavi jujig kǝ kwanǝn biya, taaki uuda vǝllada kǝ shiifǝgaan kwakyarvad tsaghwaana.
JOH 15:14 Am tsaghwahahara akwama ɓagaan kǝ dǝgit tag naiya taakiya ɓagamɓaga.
JOH 15:15 Ən madlaiy gwiiya ɗakurɗag dǝ kwatanah biya, aɗaba kwatǝnaha sǝrǝgai kǝ dǝgiti ɓag nǝ daada biya. Dlakulǝva kwaha ǝn ɗakur dǝ tsaghwahaha aɗaba tagaankurtag kǝ dǝgiti cinngana naiy baɗǝm vak Daadara.
JOH 15:16 Kurambi wa kǝssamkwakǝssǝg biya, kai wa kǝssankuraakǝsǝga ǝn fankura kǝ dagal da yaa zǝr maraw kwa da zǝlmazǝlmǝga. Tǝhala kwaha da vǝllǝkurvǝllǝg Daad kǝ dǝgiti am ghalga nǝ uuram ma ɗagaan baɗǝmma.
JOH 15:17 Kwanna iin nǝ adzhadzahara waiyamwaig kǝ zaraabaha.
JOH 15:18 “Akwama ɗuwakursɗuug duniya, sǝramasǝrǝg taakiya ɗuwakwi kaiya lauti ɗuwa kurama.
JOH 15:19 Akwamamma dǝga Duniya, duni ma waigaan kǝ dǝgaana, aɗaba am dǝga duni biya, dlaɓa kǝsankurakakǝsǝg ma duniya, iin wa nǝ iin ɗuuwakursɗug duniya.
JOH 15:20 Dzamamdzamǝg kǝ ǝlbǝgahi tangankur naiya, ‘Kwatǝnah jigu bi kǝ dadda hǝnnyahaan biya.’ Akwama mbarkwambǝga, kuram ndakwi arda mbkurmbǝga. Akwama faraarafǝg kǝ tsagaanara, ar da fǝgaarafǝg kǝ ǝlbǝgaru dlaɓa.
JOH 15:21 Ar da ɓagkurɓag kǝ kwanahaana kǝ dǝgit baɗǝmma kwakyarvad ɗaagara, aɗaba ar sǝrǝga bi kǝ dadakwa ɓǝlakwadiɓǝlǝg biya.
JOH 15:22 Akwama ndza sanhi bi ǝn tagtǝr kǝ ǝlbǝg biya, maraa ndzaa maay dǝ haip biya. Amaa ndakwanna, am maay dǝ ɗuula kyavaɗǝgv tǝghǝr kǝ haipahaatǝr biya.
JOH 15:23 Daddakwa ɗuwakwiɗuuga ɗuugharsɗug kǝ baz Daadara.
JOH 15:24 Bagannaɓag kǝ tlǝrah baɗyak ma iitǝra maay daddakwa tapghanitapǝg kǝ ɓagaan biya. Akwama ndza ɓaganna bi kǝ tlǝrahaan biya, maraa ndza maay dǝ haip biya. Ndakwanna nǝghǝghaaranǝghǝg kǝ dǝgit ǝn ɓaga naiya, bakǝva kwaha ɗuuwarkwiɗuga, dlaɓa ɗuuranɗug kǝ Daadara.
JOH 15:25 Dzǝghardzǝg wanǝn kwakyarvad righǝvant nǝ ǝlbǝgǝn viindavan ma adzahadzah taakiya, ɗuuwarkwiɗug bagyaana.
JOH 15:26 Mada sǝghawisǝg nǝ dadda mǝlkurmǝlǝga kwan da mǝllǝg naiya davakruwa vak daada, shǝɗkwa jiira, kwa sagal vak daada iin wa da ɓa shiid tǝghǝr kǝskaiya.
JOH 15:27 Kuram ndakwi am shiidaha, aɗaba bama daa zǝnngwa am ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kaiya.
JOH 16:1 “Tagaankurtag kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitah baɗǝma haik da mɓǝg kǝskuram ma fadghǝraruwa.
JOH 16:2 Ar da lagwkurlagw sagal ma guda dzahavaha. Bak jijirra sagau nǝ sarta baɗǝm daddakwa tsa kurama da tlatlǝgaan taakiya ǝn ɓa kwatǝnahǝr kǝ Dadamzhigǝla.
JOH 16:3 Ar da ɓagkurɓag nǝ nndah kǝ kwannahaan kǝ dǝgitah aɗaɓa ar sǝrǝgai kǝ Daada bi kaiya biya.
JOH 16:4 Tagankurdatag kǝ kwannahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, aɗaba mada ɓagaɓag nǝ sarta, am da dzamnan taakiya tagankurdataga. Tagaankurdai kwan ma daa zǝngw biya aɗaba ndzan ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kurama.
JOH 16:5 “Amaa ndakwanna ǝn dagat davak daddakwa ɓǝlakwadiɓǝlga. Bakǝvakwaha ma kurama maay nǝ daddakwa ndavghwadndavǝg taakiya, ‘Agha dagal da vakwar biya?’
JOH 16:6 Aɗaba naa tagankurdatag kǝ kwannahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, kaa badzaǝrivǝɗ kǝskurama.
JOH 16:7 Bak jiir wan tagkur naiya, daasar wa maraw kǝsskurama, aɗaba ma danagha biya, maay da saay nǝ dadda kwada mǝlkurumelgǝn biya. Akwama danaghana ǝn da ɓǝllǝgaan saavakaruwa.
JOH 16:8 Mada sǝghawisǝg nǝ dadda mǝlkurmǝlǝgna, da margarmarǝg kǝ duni taakiya kalkal bi nǝ dzamaghǝraatǝr tǝghǝr kǝ haip, jira, ard tǝghǝr sharriya.
JOH 16:9 Dzamaghǝraatǝr tǝghǝr kǝ haipa kalkal biya aɗaba larwalǝg kǝ fadǝghǝr tǝ kaiya.
JOH 16:10 Dzamaghǝraatǝra kalkal bi tǝghǝr kǝ jir biya, aɗaba ǝn daa da vak Daadara, dlaɓa am da madlai gwiiya nǝghǝghkwanǝghǝg biya.
JOH 16:11 Dzamaghǝraatǝr tǝghǝr kǝ sharriya, aɗaba ɓagavaraɓag nǝ sharri kǝ dada kwarra kwan kǝ duni bawurra.
JOH 16:12 Mǝng nǝ dǝgitah ǝn naa tagkur nai baɗyak ndana, am da dzǝgwanti ndakwan biya.
JOH 16:13 Mada sǝghawisǝg nǝ shiɗkwa jijiira, da mǝlkurumǝlǝg baɗǝm ma jiira, aɗaba da taa ǝlbǝga ghǝraan biya, da taa ba dǝgita aa ciingga nǝ iin kaltiya, dlaɓa da tagkurtag kǝ dǝgitah da dzǝgaaradzǝga.
JOH 16:14 Da fǝkwarafǝg kǝskaiya, aɗaba da dlǝghgaan kǝ ǝlbǝgara dlaɓa da tagkur kǝskurama.
JOH 16:15 Baɗǝm nǝ digiti dǝvakai nǝ Daada ba dǝgara, kwakyarvad kwah wanaa tag nai da dlǝghgaan nǝ shǝɗkw vakara da markurdana.
JOH 16:16 “Tǝhala sart hǝɗikǝna am da madlaiy nǝghkwanǝghǝg biya, tǝhala sart hǝɗikǝn dlaɓa am da nǝghkwanǝghǝga.”
JOH 16:17 Am kyǝlǝma mbǝrzah taa kǝ ghǝrahaatǝra, “Au nǝ dǝgiti tuuk vakai wa tag nǝ iin, ‘Tǝhala sart hǝɗikǝn am da madlai nǝghǝghkwanǝghǝg biya, tǝhala sart hǝɗikǝn dlaɓa am da gwiiya nǝghǝghkwanǝghǝgi?’ Dlaɓa au wa tlatlǝg nǝ iin dǝ taakiya, ‘Aɗaba ǝn daa da vak Daadarni’?”
JOH 16:18 Kaa zavukw kǝ iitǝr dǝ ndavǝg taakiya, “Aauw wa tlatlǝg nǝ iin dǝ taakiya, ‘tǝhala sart hǝɗikǝni’? Kiyam sǝrgai kǝ dǝgit tlatlǝg nǝ iin biya.”
JOH 16:19 Sǝrghaakasǝrǝg Yesu taakiya ar naa ndavagarundavǝg mbǝrzahaan tǝghǝr kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Am ndavǝgaru kǝ ghǝraharu kǝ dǝgiti ǝn tlatlǝg nai dǝ taakiya, ‘Tǝhala sart hǝɗikǝna am da nǝghǝghkwa biya, tǝhala sart hǝɗikǝn dlaɓa am da nǝghǝghkwanǝghǝga’?
JOH 16:20 Bak jiijiira ǝn tagkurtaga, sarti am da tuug dǝ badzǝga ǝrivǝɗmahuɗna, iin sarti da dlaig nǝ duniya, badzǝga ǝrivǝɗmahuɗaruwa da nǝg kǝ dlaiga.
JOH 16:21 Akwama tsugwgharaatsug kungula yiig kǝ uusa mbǝkǝnmbǝg nǝ dlaɗ ba vaivaiya, aɗaba sart yigaan ɓagaaɓaga. Ma yaayig kǝ zǝra, kaa vigaraaviig kǝ dlaɗan aa mbakǝnmbǝgǝna aɗaba dlaiga kwakyarvad yaayig kǝ zǝr sama duniya.
JOH 16:22 Bandkwaha vakaruwa. Ndakwana am badzǝga ǝrivǝɗa, amaa am da gwiya nǝghǝkwanǝghǝga dlaɓa tǝhala kwaha am da dlaiga, maay wa da kǝskurvakǝssǝg kǝ dlaigaru biya.
JOH 16:23 Ma kwahiin kǝ sarta kwahiina am da maay ghalgaan aanji ndau vakar biya. Bak jiir ǝn tagkurtaga, Daada da vǝllǝkurvǝllǝg baɗǝm kǝ dǝgit am ghallǝga nǝ uuram ma ɗagaara.
JOH 16:24 Gwasǝtaan ghalamai aanji ndauw ma ɗagara biya. Ghalamghalǝga, am da tlǝkǝnatlǝga, aɗaba dlaigaruwa aandz ba righǝgharighaana.”
JOH 16:25 “Aanji tagankur bad ǝlbǝg dǝghur kǝ ǝlbǝga. Da sagau nǝ sarta kwan da madlaiy batlǝr dǝ hulfa kǝ ghaiy biya. Dlakulǝva kwaha, ǝn da tagkurtag bat Ballaɓala tǝghǝr kǝ daadara.
JOH 16:26 Ma kwahiina kǝ am da ghalǝg ma ɗaagara. Kai bi wada ghallǝgaan kǝ Daada ma guufkaru biya.
JOH 16:27 Aɗaba Daadiin dǝ ghǝraana waiyakurwaiyga, kwakyarvad waiyamkutwaiyǝg kǝskaya, dlaɓa famdǝghǝrǝtfǝga taakiya sanhi vak Dadamazhǝgǝl naiya.
JOH 16:28 Sanhi vak Daadiin naiya, dlaɓa sanhisǝg sama duniya, ndakwan dlaɓa ǝn ɗuugaan kǝ duniya ǝn gwiiya daddavak Daddina.”
JOH 16:29 Aiyam mbǝrzahaana, ndakwan wagha tag nǝng kǝ tsalal ǝlbǝg bat ɓallaɓalla maay dǝ ǝlbǝg dǝghur biya.
JOH 16:30 Ndakwana nǝghamndakanǝghǝg taakiya agha sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgitah baɗǝma. Agha sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ ngugǝg ba kalkal lakwati ndavakndavǝg kǝ uuda. Kwanǝn waa fakǝmndafǝg kǝ fadǝghǝr taakiya sǝghi vak Daadamazhigǝla.”
JOH 16:31 Kaa Nguwatǝrangug nǝ Yesu taakiya, “Kats! famdghǝrǝtfǝg ndakwanna?
JOH 16:32 Sagau nǝ sarta, bak jirra ɓagaaɓaga kwamda kwazǝg nǝ uuram aanji kwararu da ǝmdrǝg daa da vǝgyaana am da ɗuukus kǝskai ba daavara. Bakǝvakwaha ǝn davar biya, aɗaba ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kai nǝ Daada.
JOH 16:33 Tagaankurdatag kǝ kwannahaan kǝ dǝgitah, aɗaba ma kaiya am tlǝkǝna kǝ gabǝrǝra. Mahuɗa duuninna hǝbamuhǝɓǝg kǝ dlaɗa, ndzamandzǝg dǝ fǝrivǝɗ mahuɗa aɗaba zaanuzǝg kǝ firr tǝghǝr kǝ duniya.”
JOH 17:1 Tǝhala kwa tagada Yesu kǝ kwannahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, kaa dzǝgant kǝ ghǝraan daa kǝ ghǝrazhigǝl dzǝgwa kǝ zhigǝla amaa, “Daada, ɓagaaɓag sarta. Faarafǝg kǝ Zǝragh kwakyarvad iin ndakwi fǝkaarana.
JOH 17:2 Kwakyarvad vǝlghavǝlǝg kǝ ndzǝɗ kǝ Zǝr tǝghǝr kǝ uudah baɗǝmma, aɗaba vǝlda kǝ shiifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝra kǝ lii vǝllǝgha nǝnga.
JOH 17:3 Shiifǝga tangw damma zǝrazǝra iin taakiya, sǝrak nǝ uudaha, kǝgh Daadamazhigǝla jiira palba nǝnnga, dlaɓa ar sǝran kǝ Yesu Tlǝkatǝga kwa ɓǝlghǝdi nǝnnga.
JOH 17:4 Fankaarafǝg ma duniya ghyinganaghyǝng tsau kǝ tlǝr vǝlghwa nǝnnga kǝ ɓagaana.
JOH 17:5 Ndakwan ciya, fǝkwaraafǝg Daada dǝ ndangǝri ndzan dǝ dǝvakaiy nai vakagh lakwti fǝvarzhafǝg nǝ duniya.
JOH 17:6 Marankadamarǝg vak lii vǝlghwa nǝng ma duniya. Ba gwil wur ndzar ba dǝgagha, vǝlghwavǝlǝg nǝnng kǝ iitǝra, dlaɓa fararfǝg kǝ ǝlbǝgagha.
JOH 17:7 Ndakwana ar sǝrǝggasǝrǝg taakiya baɗǝm nǝ dǝgit vǝlghwa nǝngga sǝghal vak agha.
JOH 17:8 Kwakyarvad ǝlbǝgahaan tagghwa nǝngǝna tagantǝrtaga, dlaɓa dlǝgharadlǝga. Sǝraraakasǝrǝg bak jiijiira sanhi vakagha, dlaɓa fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg bakǝgh pal wa ɓǝlghkwadiɓǝlǝga.
JOH 17:9 Ən dzǝgwazhǝgǝl kwakyarvad iitǝra. Kwakyarvad uudaha duni biya, amaa kwakyarvad uudahi vǝllǝghwa nǝnnga, aɗaba ar dǝgha.
JOH 17:10 Baɗǝm nǝ dǝgit ǝn dǝvakai naiya ba dǝgagha, dlaɓa baɗǝm nǝ dǝgit agha dǝvakai nǝnnga dǝgara. Dlaɓa maravdamarǝg nǝ ndangǝrara tǝdǝvad iitǝra.
JOH 17:11 Ndakwana ǝn da madlai ndzǝga ma duni biya, amma iitǝra ar bamma duniya, kai dlaɓa ǝn daas da vakagha. Daad Caccuwanacaccuwananna, katǝrkatǝg tǝdvad ndzǝɗa ɗaagagha, ɗaaga kwa vǝllǝghwa nǝngga, aɗaba ar nal kǝ palla, band kwa ki pal nǝmi dǝ kǝgha.
JOH 17:12 Ma sartǝn ndzan ǝmtaɗ dǝ iitǝra, katanrǝtkatǝg dǝ ndzǝɗa ɗaagagha, ɗaagǝn kwa vǝlghwa nǝngna. Katantrǝtkatǝga, maay wa zaazǝg aanji pal biya, ba kwapakǝna, aɗaba righǝvant nǝ ǝlbǝga Daadamazhigǝl viindaviinda.
JOH 17:13 Ndakwana ǝn daa da vakagha. Amaa ǝn ghala kwanǝn kǝ dǝgitah bamma sarti ǝn ba ndzǝgaan ma duniya kiyava righǝgh kǝ hwaɗagar ba vaivai ma ǝrivɗmahuɗaruwa.
JOH 17:14 Tagaantǝrdatag kǝ ǝlbǝgha. Gwiyatǝrdagwig duni kǝ ilga, aɗaba ar dǝga duni biya, bandkwa kwan ǝn dǝga duni bi nai biya.
JOH 17:15 Ghalgaara iin bi taakiya agha hutsǝtǝrda dagal ma duuniyin biya, amaa ǝn ghalgara iin taakiya magha katǝrǝt vak tlǝkǝlaadǝna.
JOH 17:16 Iitǝra ar dǝga duni biya, bandkwa kai ndakwi ǝn dǝga duni biya.
JOH 17:17 Pǝshtǝrapǝshig tǝdǝvad jiira, aɗaba ǝlbǝgaha iin jiira.
JOH 17:18 Bǝlantǝrǝtɓǝlǝg damma duniya, bandkwa ɓǝlghkwadi nǝng kǝskaiya.
JOH 17:19 Ən pǝshig kwakyarvad iitǝra kǝ ghǝrara, aɗaba iitǝr ndakwi pǝshivtǝra bak jiira.”
JOH 17:20 “Ghalgara kwakyarvad iitǝr kalti biya. Ən dzǝgwazhigǝl dlaɓa kwakyarvad lii fadǝghǝr tǝ kaiya tǝdǝvad ǝlbǝgaatǝra.
JOH 17:21 Aɗaba baɗǝmaatǝra maraa nal kǝ palla, bandkwa agha ma kai nǝnga, kai dlaɓa ǝn ma kǝgha, ǝn ghalga iitǝr ndakwi maraa ndza ma kǝmiya, kwakyarvad uudaha duniya ar fǝdǝghǝrǝta taakiya kǝgh wa ɓǝlghkwadibǝlga.
JOH 17:22 Kaiya vǝllantǝrvǝllǝg kǝ uudah kǝ ndangǝr kwa vǝllǝghwa nǝngga, aɗaba ar nal kǝ pal band kwakǝyi pal nǝmiya.
JOH 17:23 Kai ma iitǝra, kǝgh dlaɓa ma kaiya, aɗaba ar nal kǝ pal ba vaivaiya, aɗaba sǝran nǝ duni taakiya kǝgh wa ɓǝlghkwadiɓǝlga, dlaɓa ar sǝran waightǝrantwaiga bandkwa waighkut nǝnnga.
JOH 17:24 “Daada, manaa naagaan maraa ndza nǝ uudahaan vǝlghwa nǝnngǝn ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kai vakavaki dǝ kaiya, ǝn naagaan maraa nǝgha kǝ ndangǝragha, kwa vǝlghwa nǝnnga kwakyarvad agha waikwawaig lakwati virɗyav duniya.
JOH 17:25 Daada, dadda jirra, uudaha duniya ar sǝrak biya, kaiya ǝn sǝraksǝrǝga, kwanǝn kǝ uudah dlaɓa ar sǝrǝgasǝrǝg taakiya kǝgh wa ɓǝlkwadiɓǝlǝga.
JOH 17:26 Marantǝrdamarǝg kǝ ɗagagha, dlaɓa ǝn da zaavukw dǝ maratǝrmaraga, kwakyarvad waiyav kwa agha ɓagwa nǝng aa ndzan ma iitǝra, kai dlaɓa ǝn ndza ma iitǝra.”
JOH 18:1 Ghyǝnga ba Yesu dzǝgwazhigǝla, kaa dzǝva dlara Kidron kǝ iin ǝmtaɗ dǝ mbǝrazahaan da tǝ kwah ghyaba. Gyilga dlariina ndza mǝng ɗyaghaara guuha, kaa daas kǝ iin ǝmtaɗ dǝ mbǝrzahaan damma vakaiya.
JOH 18:2 Sǝrgasǝrǝg Yahud kwa vǝlǝt Yesu kwahiin kǝ vakavaka, aɗaba nǝtnǝg Yesu kǝ dzahav dǝ mbǝrzahaan vakwahiina.
JOH 18:3 Kaa sagau kǝ Yahud dǝ dakwala tlauja ard lii uufakyawa Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl kwa ɓǝlartǝrǝt mallaha zhiilakǝsuufah ard Farisiyaha, kaa dagal kǝ iitǝr damma ɗyaghaara guhiina, ar hakyahakya dǝ kaara jahuramba, ard zadah ard kadlanga ghwaava.
JOH 18:4 Sǝrgasǝrg tsau Yesu kǝ dǝgitahi da dzǝgaar dǝ iin baɗǝmma, kaa sagal kǝ iina, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “War wam gatǝg nǝ uurami?”
JOH 18:5 Kaa ngwangug kǝ iitǝr, taakiya, “Yesu zhiila Nazaret.” Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kai nǝ iina.” (Yahuda kwa vǝlǝt Yesu ndakwi ghacǝga ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ iitǝra.)
JOH 18:6 Tagatǝr ba Yesu taakiya, “Kai nǝ iina,” kaa hazha da tǝ hal kǝ iitǝra, ar mɓǝɗa da tǝ haaya.
JOH 18:7 Kaa gwiya ndavǝtǝrundavǝg Yesu, amaa, “Am gata wari?” Aiyam nǝ iitǝr taa kǝ iina, “Yesu zhiila Nazareta.”
JOH 18:8 Kaa ngugangug kǝ Yesu amaa, “Ən naa ndza tagkurtag taakiya, ba kai nǝ iina. Akwamam gata ba kaiya, ɗuwamtǝrǝsɗug kǝ uudahaan dagala.”
JOH 18:9 Dzǝghaar kwakyarvad righǝvant nǝ ǝlbǝgi tagada Yesu taakiya, “Ma uudahaan vǝlǝghwa nǝnngna, maay wa zaazǝg aanji pall biya.”
JOH 18:10 Siman Bitrus kwa ndza dǝ katsakara, tǝɗadatǝɗǝg kǝ katsakar ghudarda kǝ hyimiya dǝvakaf kǝ kwatǝnaha maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufaha. Ɗaaga kwanǝn kǝ kwatǝnaha Malkus.
JOH 18:11 Am Yesu taa kǝ Bitrusa, “Gwidaagwig kǝ katsakaragh damma kumbǝghaana. Ən maay da hǝɓǝgaan ma kuwǝn kwa vǝlǝghwa Daad ǝn hǝɓu biya?”
JOH 18:12 Kaa vigǝtviig dakwala tlauja ard tlǝvukwatǝra, ard lii uufakyawa Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla Yahudah kǝ Yesu, ar nguɗǝnana.
JOH 18:13 Kaa lanngaan kǝ iitǝr ba zunngw da vak Hannana, dadda uusa Kayafa. Kayafa wa ndza maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufah ma kwahiin kǝ viiga.
JOH 18:14 Kayafa wa ɗiyatǝra sawari kǝ Yahudah taakiya, ngulǝm ǝmǝtsa nǝ uud pall dlakulva kyalǝma uudaha.
JOH 18:15 Kaa gata Yesu kǝ Siman Bitrus ard kwatlǝrǝn kǝ mbǝrz tǝ halaa. Kwanǝn kǝ mbǝrza, sǝrǝgasǝrǝg maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufahǝn kǝ iina, kaa daas kǝ iin damma huɗa gaagazaiya vǝgya maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufahǝn ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ Yesu.
JOH 18:16 Kaa ghacǝgaghacǝg kǝ Bitrus tǝ ghaiya wakyagha. Kaa gwiya sagal kǝ mbǝrzǝn kwa sǝrǝgasǝrǝg maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufahǝn da taa ghai dǝ dǝghwa hǝnyaha zhiilakǝsuufǝn tǝ ghaiya wakyagha, tǝhala kwaha, sǝdaa kǝ Bitrusa.
JOH 18:17 Aiyam nǝ dǝghwǝn uufa wakyaghǝn kǝ Bitrusa, “Agha maay kwan nǝnng pall ma mbǝrzaha uudanǝn biya?” Ngwangug nǝ Bitrus amaa, “Ən maay ma iitǝr biya.”
JOH 18:18 Ndza akuhy vakka, kaa mbiigantmbiig kǝ kwatǝnahah ard lii uufakyawa kǝ kaara ghuvǝr ar ghacaraan ar cinnga hurfakaana, Bitrus ndakwi ndza ghacǝgan ǝmtaɗ dǝ iitǝra.
JOH 18:19 Kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufah kǝ Yesu tǝghǝr kǝ mbǝrzahaana ard tsagaanana.
JOH 18:20 Kaa ngughwarangug Yesu taakiya, “Tagandatag kǝ ǝlbǝg ba tǝ ɓalaɓal tǝvukwa uudah baɗǝmma, dlaɓa tlakwatlǝg tsagaan ma guda dzahavaha ard Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝla, vakavaki dzahavǝt Yahudah baɗǝmma. Tappana bi kǝ taa dǝgiti shǝɓashǝɓan biya.
JOH 18:21 Iyau, agha ndavǝgwa da ɓaw kaci kǝ ndavǝgahi? Ba agha ndavtǝru kǝ lii cinngaracinng kǝ dǝgiti tagantǝr nai kǝ ndavgahaana, aɗaba ar sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgiti taganda naiya.”
JOH 18:22 Tagada ba Yesu kǝ kwaha, kaa tsǝgaan kǝ pall ma lii uufakyau kwa ghacǝganǝn dǝ mahupeng kǝ Yesu, amaa, “Agha ngugugar ndkwan kǝ maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufaha?”
JOH 18:23 Kaa ngwangug kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Akwama mǝng dǝgiti kwa naa tagǝda nai ghwaɗa, marwadamarǝg kǝ ghwaɗǝraana. Akwama ba jiir nǝ dǝgiti naa tagda naiya, aujilbǝg kaci agha tsa kaiyi?”
JOH 18:24 Kaa ɓǝlgantɓǝlǝg Hannana kǝ uudah dagal dǝ Yesu nguɗanguɗan da vak Kayaf maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufaha.
JOH 18:25 Gwastaan ba ndzǝganaan Bitrus ba ghacǝga vakwah tǝghǝr kǝ kaara cinnga hurǝfaka. Kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg kǝ kyalmah taakiya, “Aayaa, agha maay nǝnng kwan pall ma mbǝrzahaan biya?” Kaa ɓala gajau kǝ Bitrus amaa, “Ən maay ma iiter biya.”
JOH 18:26 Am pall ma kwatǝnaha maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufaha. Yiiga kwa ghudǝgharda Bitrus kǝ hyimi na, amaa taa kǝ Bitrusa, “Mbats nǝghankak bi ǝmtaɗ dǝ iin ma guhiin kwan biya?”
JOH 18:27 Kaa gwiya ɓala gajau kǝ Bitrusa. Tǝhala kwaha, kaa wiig kǝ ghwatkala.
JOH 18:28 Kaa sǝdasǝg kǝ tlǝvuukwa Yahudah kǝ Yesu sagal ma vǝgya Kayafa da vǝgya gumǝna Roma. Ma sartǝn lanngar nǝ iitǝrna, cagaacag nǝ kǝsa. Kaa lǝwalǝg kǝ iitǝr daa damma huɗa gaagazaiya, hai kǝ ndzǝgana kwadlambǝr kǝ iitǝr tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl kwa da tsava iitǝr kǝ zaa kafa hwaɗaga haarakǝsa dzava hǝnnyaha.
JOH 18:29 Mbakyarvad kwaha, kaa sǝgalsǝg kǝ Bilatus saa vakaatǝr gyimala, amaa, “Hulfa kwar kǝ ɗiya ghunj wa maa sǝdǝv nǝ uuram tǝghǝr kǝ kwan kǝ uudi?”
JOH 18:30 Kaa ngugwangug kǝ iitǝr taakiya, “Akwama dadda haip bi nǝ iin biya, ma kǝmnda maay lanngaan saa vakagh biya.”
JOH 18:31 Am Bilatus taa kǝ iitǝra, “Lanngamlanng dagal ba dǝ ghǝraruwa, am ghudarda kǝ sharri kalkal dǝ adzahadzaharuwa.” Aiyam Yahudah taa kǝ iina, “Vǝlakǝmnd bi nǝ uud kǝ ndzǝɗa ghudǝgarda tsa shifǝg kǝ uud biya.”
JOH 18:32 Dzǝghaar kwakyarvad righǝvant nǝ ǝlbǝgi tagada Yesu tǝghǝr kǝ hulfa ǝmtsǝgi da ǝmtsǝg nǝ iina.)
JOH 18:33 Kaa gwiya daas kǝ Bilatus daa damma gaagazaiya tlǝkǝsa, tǝhala kwaha kaa ɗagantɗaag kǝ iin kǝ Yesu ndavaru amaa, “Kǝgh Tlǝkǝsa yaa Yahuda?”
JOH 18:34 Kaa ngugwarangug Yesu amaa, “Kwan kǝ ndavǝg aa sǝgal ma ghǝragh nii, uudahi tlǝrn ha wa tagakaktag kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝskaiyi?”
JOH 18:35 Kaa ngungangug Bilatus amaa, “Ən zhiila Yahudah naiya? Sarkadǝv zarabahagh Yahudah ard maal ba tingting ma zhiilakǝsuufah saa vakara. Au waghaa ɓaga nǝnngi?”
JOH 18:36 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Tlǝkǝsǝrara dǝga kwan kǝ duni biya. Akwama dǝga kwan kǝ duni tlǝkǝsǝrara, maraa ɓagaan kwatǝnahar kǝ ghwaav maa hai kǝ vikwaviig kǝ Yahudaha. Amma tlǝkǝsǝrar vakavaki tlǝrna.”
JOH 18:37 Aiyam Bilatus taa kǝ iina, “Kats agha tlǝkǝsa?” Kaa ngugwarangug kǝ Yesu amaa, “Kǝgh dǝ ghǝragh waa tagda taakiya ǝn tlǝkǝsa. Yaakwi kwakyarvad kwan nǝ uuda, dlaɓa sanhi kwakyarvad kwan sa ma duniya, aɗaba ǝn ɓaga kǝ shiida jiijiira. Dlaɓa baɗǝm daddakwa dǝga jiira, cinngaan kǝ ǝlbǝgara.”
JOH 18:38 Kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg kǝ Bilatus amaa, “Au jiiri?” Ndavǝgharu ba nǝ iin kwan kǝ ndavǝga, kaa gwiya sagal kǝ iin sa vak Yahudaha amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Viyanǝt bi nai dǝ haip biya.
JOH 18:39 Amma mǝnng nǝ dǝga daadijaharuwa, akwama ɓagaaɓag sarta hwaɗaga haarakǝsa dzǝva hǝnnyaha, ǝn ɓǝlkursɓǝlg kǝ uud pall ma guda bǝrfǝnga. Am naagaan ǝn ɓǝlkurnǝs kǝ tlǝkǝsa Yahudaha?”
JOH 18:40 Kaa gwiya ngugǝg kǝ iitǝra, ar ɗiyaru kǝ cauw ar taakiya, “Maaya kwan biya, Barabbas wa kǝm naag nǝmnda.” (Barabbas ndza dadda zaaɗuula.)
JOH 19:1 Kaa vǝldavǝlǝg Bilatus kǝ Yesu kiyava kalǝga.
JOH 19:2 Kaa faɗgafaɗǝg tlaujah kǝ dzakwa tlǝkǝs kwa ɓagava dǝ dǝva taka ar tsǝgwardǝm maghǝr kǝ Yesu, tǝhalakwah ar tsǝgwardǝm kǝ sǝɗav kyanng hulfa dǝga tlǝkǝssaha.
JOH 19:3 Ar gwayashig sa vakaana, ar ɓalgar mahupennga, ar taakiya, “Kǝm ma barkagha, tlǝkǝsa Yahudaha!”
JOH 19:4 Kaa gwiya sagal kǝ Bilatusa, amaa kǝ Yahudahi faɗǝga vakwahiina, “Waiyam ciya ǝn lanngkurlanng kǝ Yesu sagala, kwakyarvad ǝn naagaan am sǝra taakiya viyanǝti dǝ haip biya.”
JOH 19:5 Kaa sagal kǝ Yesu dǝ dzakwa tlǝkǝs dzakwa tak ma ghǝraan dlaɓa dǝ sǝɗav kyannga. Aiyam Bilatus taa kǝ iitǝra, “Waiyam nǝ uuda nǝ iina.”
JOH 19:6 Nǝghǝghaara ba maalah ma zhiilakǝsuufah ard lii uufakyawa Vǝgya Daadamazhigǝl kǝ Yesu, kaa ɗiya cau kǝ iitǝr ar taakiya, “Aa hǝrtǝvǝthǝrtǝga! Aa hǝrtǝvǝthǝrtǝga!” Am Bilatus taa kǝ iitǝra, “Damdagal am hǝrtǝt bad ghǝraruwa, aɗaba tlankǝna bi nai kǝ iin dǝ haip biya.”
JOH 19:7 Kaa ngugarangug kǝ Yahudah taakiya, “Kǝm da adzahadzaha, dlaɓa tǝdvad adzahadzahamnda, barari tsǝvana, aɗaba nadalnǝg kǝ ghǝraan kǝ Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla.”
JOH 19:8 Cinngha ba Bilatus kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, kaa gwiya gǝdzǝg kǝ iina.
JOH 19:9 Kaa gwiya daas kǝ iin damma huɗa vǝgyaana, ndavaru kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Agha sagal vakwari?” Amma lawalǝg Yesu kǝ ngugarngugga.
JOH 19:10 Aiyam Bilatus taa kǝ iina, “Lǝghwalǝg kǝ taa ghai dǝ kaiya? Agha sǝrǝgai taakiya ǝn dǝ ndzǝɗa ɓǝlǝkǝsɓǝlǝga ard ndzǝɗa hǝrtǝkǝthǝrtǝg biya?”
JOH 19:11 Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Agha maay dǝ ndzǝɗ tǝghǝr kǝskai akwama vǝllakaki nǝ uud sii ma ghǝrazhigǝl biya. Kwakyarvad kwaha daddakwa fakwadǝm ma dǝvvagha jakujig dǝ haipa.”
JOH 19:12 Tǝhala kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, kaa ba gata ɗuula ɓǝlgaars Yesu nǝ Bilatus, amma Yahudaha ar za ba vukw dǝ ɗiya cau ar taakiya, “Akwama ɓǝlgharǝsɓǝlǝg kǝ kwan kǝ uuda agha madlai tsaghwa Kaisar biya. Baɗǝm daddakwa nadalnǝg kǝ ghǝraan kǝ tlǝkǝsa, ciigar hǝnkal kǝ Kaisara.”
JOH 19:13 Cinngha ba Bilatus kǝ dǝgiti tagar nǝ iitǝra, kaa sagal kǝ iin dǝ Yesu, kaa cǝhurgacǝhurǝg Bilatus tǝ avǝda shari tǝ akur hahaana. Dǝ ghaiya Yahudaha ɗahav dǝ Gabbata.
JOH 19:14 Daghuvala kwahina, ndza faciya ɓadlava hwaɗaga haarakǝsa dzava hǝnnyaha, tamaha faci tǝghǝra. Aiyam Bilatus taa kǝ Yahudaha, “Waiyam Tlǝkǝsaruwa!”
JOH 19:15 Kaa ɗiya cau kǝ Yahudaha ar taakiya, “Aa tsǝvatsǝɡa! Aa tsǝvatsǝga! Aa hǝrtǝvǝthǝrtǝga!” Kaa ndavtǝrundavǝg kǝ Bilatus amaa, “Am naagaan ǝn hǝrtǝt kǝ Tlǝkǝsaruwa?” Kaa ngugangug kǝ maalah zhiilakǝsuufaha, am nǝ iitǝra “Kǝm maay dǝ kwatlǝrǝn kǝ tlǝkǝs biya, ba Kaisara.”
JOH 19:16 Tǝhala kwaha, kaa vǝldavǝlǝg Bilatus kǝ Yesu kiyava hǝrtǝga. Kaa daddǝg kǝ tlaujah kǝ Yesu.
JOH 19:17 Tǝghǝrdǝga sagal Yesu ma kǝsiin kǝsa tlaɓa hǝrtǝgaan ba dǝ ghǝraan da vakavakǝn kwa ɗahav dǝ kuwa ghǝra. (Dǝ ghaiya Yahudaha ɗahav dǝ Golgota nǝ wanǝn kǝ vakavaka.
JOH 19:18 Hǝrtavǝt vaakwahiin Yesu, ǝmtaɗ dǝ uudah buwa, pal tǝ dǝvva kafaana, pal dlaɓa tǝ dǝvva ghyaɓaana, iin ma taataka.
JOH 19:19 Vindavindǝg Bilatus kǝ ǝlbǝga, kwa favva tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝga. Dǝgiti vindavana, iin taakiya “YESU ZHIILA NAZARET, TLƏKƏSA YAHUDAHA.”
JOH 19:20 Karantarakarantǝg Yahudah ba ɗyak kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga aɗaba vakavakǝn hǝrtavǝt dǝ Yesu na, ba hyaf dǝ kǝs ɗyaka. Kwanǝn kǝ vindǝg dlaɓa vindava ma ghaiya Yahudaha, ard ghaiy Romaha, ard Heleniyaha.
JOH 19:21 Aiyam maalah ma zhiilakǝsuufaha Yahudah taa kǝ Bilatusa, “Vind bi taaki, ‘Tlǝkǝsa Yahudah,’ biya, vindavindǝg taakiya, ‘Am nǝ uudanǝnna, ǝn Tlǝkǝsa Yahudaha.’ ”
JOH 19:22 Kaa ngutǝranngug Bilatus taakiya, “Dǝgiti naa vinndǝga naiya, ndzandzǝga.”
JOH 19:23 Hǝrtarǝt ba tlaujah kǝ Yesu, ar hutsu kǝ sǝɗavahaana, ar tagwnan hutsǝg uufaɗa, aanji kwar kǝ tlauja kǝsuukǝsǝg kǝ hutsǝg palla. Ar kǝsuu baz sǝɗavaani tlaɗ kwama huɗmahuɗa, kwa havǝt dǝ hǝgga ciigǝt ma ghǝr ba dǝtl da tǝ haaya.
JOH 19:24 Aiyam nǝ iitǝr kǝ ghǝrahaatǝra, “Tahǝyamna bi kǝ sǝɗavǝn biya, tsǝyamtsǝg kǝ tsats tǝghǝra, kiyam vazǝgaan kǝ dadakwa da zǝgaana.” Dzǝghardzǝg wannǝn kwakyarvad righǝvant nǝ dǝgiti vindava ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝla taakiya, “Tagwarutagw kǝ sǝɗavahar ma taatakaatǝra, ar tsak kǝ tsats tǝghǝr kǝ sǝɗavahara.” Dǝgiti ɓagara tlaujah waha.
JOH 19:25 Lii ghacara tǝvǝgh kǝ tlaɓahǝrta Yesu, iitǝr naz Babbaana, batlǝrɗaana, ard Maryam uusa Kilobas, ard Maryamu Magadala.
JOH 19:26 Nǝghǝgha ba Yesu kǝ babbaana ard mbǝrzǝn kwa waig nǝ iin ghacǝga ba hyafa, aiyama taa kǝ babbaana, “Uusǝna, wan zǝragha!”
JOH 19:27 Aiyama kǝ mbǝrzǝn tǝ hala kwaha, “Nalnǝg nǝ uusǝn kǝ baabagha!” Ciigǝt ma kwahiin kǝ sarta, kaa lanngaan kǝ mbǝrzǝn kǝ babba Yesu da vǝgyaana.
JOH 19:28 Sǝrghasǝrǝg Yesu taakiya, ma kwahiin kǝ sarta ghyǝnnghanaghyǝnng kǝ ɓa dǝgitah baɗǝmma, kwakyarvad righǝvant nǝ dǝgiti vindava ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝla, aiyama, “Njakwanjiig nǝ andǝlla.”
JOH 19:29 Vakwahiin ndza mǝng nǝ ɗagw righarighaan dǝ yuwa inabi kwarekrekka fǝgana. Kaa rǝmnarǝmng kǝ iitǝr kǝ abarabar ma yuwa inabi kwarekrekka, ar fǝt tǝ zadda izob ar kapanta ar farǝt tǝ ghai kǝ Yesu.
JOH 19:30 Dlǝghaa ba Yesu kǝ yuwǝn kwarekerek na, amaa, “Ghyǝnngaghyǝnnga!” Tǝhala kwaha tsǝdi kǝ ghǝraana, vǝlda kǝ shifǝgaana.
JOH 19:31 Ndza daghuvala ɓadlav tsauwa, dlaɓa dlakadurana faciya ngiiga kwa shah dǝ kyalma faciya ngiiga. Aɗaba ar naay tlǝvuukwa Yahudah kǝ ɗuwa tluwa vǝghaha uudah tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝg daghuvala faciya ngiig biya, kaa ghalla Bilatus kǝ Yahudaha maa kalǝvana shigahaatǝra, dlaɓa maa sǝvdi tluwa vǝghahaatǝr tǝ tlaɓa hǝrtǝga.
JOH 19:32 Kaa sagau kǝ tlaujah ar kalna kǝ shigaha uuda zunngw kwa hǝrtavǝt ǝmtaɗ dǝ Yesu, ard shigaha daddakwa pallǝna.
JOH 19:33 Amma sarǝv ba nǝ iitǝr da vak Yesu, kalarna bi kǝ shǝgaan biya aɗaba tlarara ǝmtsaaǝmǝtsǝga.
JOH 19:34 Kaa ghwugaan kǝ pal ma tlaujah kǝ Yesu dǝ guup ma dlǝmbǝla, kaa sagal kǝ avǝz ard yu ba watswatsa.
JOH 19:35 Daddakwa nǝghǝghanǝghǝga kǝ dǝgitahi dzǝghaardzǝg wa vǝlada shiida, shiidi vǝlada nǝ iinaa ba jiira. Ba Iin dǝ ghǝraan ndakwi sǝrǝgasǝrǝg taakiya jiir wa tag nǝ iina, vǝlada kwakyarvad am fǝdghǝrǝta.
JOH 19:36 Dzǝghaar kwakyarvad rǝghǝvant nǝ dǝgitahi vindava ma Kakkaɗa Dadamazhǝgǝla, “Maay aanji pal ma tlatlaan wa da kǝlav biya.”
JOH 19:37 Band kwa vindava vakavaki tlǝrǝn ma Kakkaɗa Dadamazhigǝl taakiya, “Ar da vazǝgaan kǝ daddakwa ghwara nǝ iitǝra.”
JOH 19:38 Tǝhala kwaha, am nǝ Isuvu zhiil Arimatiya mbǝrza Yesu, amma shǝɓashǝɓan kwakyarvad gǝdza tlǝvuukwaha Yahudaha, kaa ghala Bilatus maa vǝlar kǝ tluwa vǝgha Yesu. Haigharanthaig Bilatusa, kaa dagal kǝ iin kǝssant kǝ tluwa vǝgha Yesu.
JOH 19:39 Nikodimus kwa tapghana sa vak Yesu kavǝɗa, daral ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ Isuvu, sadǝvsǝg kǝ tǝrshana mur ard alos uushauushana, tamaha kilo kulhǝkǝrɗa.
JOH 19:40 Kaa kǝsǝgantkǝsǝg kǝ uudahaan buwǝn kǝ tluwa vǝgha Yesu ar ngwaɗnan ma kǝlǝpakan ard kadlannga tǝrshǝn bǝtbǝta kwakyarvad dǝga daadijatǝr kǝ Yahudah akwa mar hǝɗa uuda.
JOH 19:41 Vakavakǝn hǝrtavǝt nǝ iinna, ndza mǝnng ɗyaghaara guuha, ma ɗyaghara guuhiina dlaɓa ndza mǝng nǝ daalla gǝtl kwa tapavnai hǝɗa uud ma vakaiy biya.
JOH 19:42 Ndza daghuvala faciya ɓadlava Yahudah tsauwa, dlaɓa ba hyaf gǝtl dǝ iitǝra, ar fǝdǝm kǝ tluwa vǝgha Yesu ma vakaiya.
JOH 20:1 Dlakadur ba wur daghuvala hǝnnga zunngw ma maaka, lakwti cag kǝsa, kaa ba dagal kǝ Maryamu magadala damma gǝtlaha, nǝghǝgha ba tlǝgavarwatlǝg nǝ akur tǝ ghaiya gǝtla Yesu.
JOH 20:2 Kaa ǝmndǝra saas kǝ iin da vak Siman Bitrus ard mbǝrz kwa waig Yesu, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Kǝsavdakǝsǝg Yazhigǝl sagal ma gǝtla, kǝm sǝrga bi kǝ vakavaki araa fǝga nǝ iitǝr biya.”
JOH 20:3 Kaa sagal kǝ Siman Bitrus ard mbǝrzǝn ar viyǝt kǝ ɗuula dagal damma gǝtla.
JOH 20:4 Kaa ǝmndǝra dagal kǝ iitǝr ba bǝrkuɗaatǝra, jighaarajig mbǝzǝn pallǝn kǝ Siman Bitrus dǝ ǝmndrǝga, dlaɓa dagha nǝ iin tǝghǝr kǝ Siman Bitrus da vaka gǝtla.
JOH 20:5 Ngǝghǝra kǝ iin vazanan damma vakaiya, kaa nǝghǝghgaanǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ kǝlpakan ɓǝlgana, amma dagha bi damma gǝtliin biya.
JOH 20:6 Kaa sagau kǝ Siman Bitrus tǝ halaana, kaa ba daas kǝ iin damma gǝtla, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ kǝlpakan ɗiigana.
JOH 20:7 Nǝghǝghanǝghǝg dlaɓ kǝ sǝɗavǝn kwa faɗavan dǝ ghǝra Yesu ɗiigaan vakavaki tlǝrǝn shah dǝ kǝlpakana.
JOH 20:8 Kaa dǝgaadǝg baz mbǝrzǝn kwa tsugwa ba zunngw tǝghǝr Siman Bitrus damma vakaiya. Nǝghǝgha ba nǝ iina, kaa fǝdǝghǝrǝtfǝga.
JOH 20:9 (Gwaastǝn nǝgharaaka bi kǝ dǝgiti vindava ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl kwa taakiya, barari da ciig Yesu dǝ shifǝga.)
JOH 20:10 Kaa gwiya daas kǝ mbǝrzahaan da vaka ndzǝganaatǝra.
JOH 20:11 Ghacaghacǝg Maryam tǝ ghaiya gǝtl gyǝmala, tuuga. Ba tuug nǝ iina, kaa ngǝghǝrangǝg zhara damma gǝtla,
JOH 20:12 Kaa nǝghǝghgaanǝghǝg kǝ inn kǝ zarha ɓǝlg buw ar ma sǝɗav maɗǝkw ar cǝhurgan vakavaki ndza dǝ tluwa vǝgha Yesu. Zǝrɓǝlǝg palla cǝhurga vaka ghǝra, kwah dlaɓ cǝhurga vaka shǝgahaana.
JOH 20:13 Kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg kǝ Zǝrha ɓǝlgah taakiya, “Uusǝna, au wagha tuug nǝngi?” Aiyama taa kǝ iitra, “Kǝsavuukǝssǝg Yaazhigǝlara, ǝn sǝrǝgai kǝ vakavaki aa fǝvva dǝ iin biya.”
JOH 20:14 Tagada ba nǝ iin kǝ ǝlbǝgna, kaa gwivǝtgwiga nǝghǝgha ba Yesu ghacǝgana, amma nǝghǝghaaka bi taakiya iin biya.
JOH 20:15 Kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Uusǝna, aaujilǝbǝg kǝskǝgh tuugi? War wagha gatǝg nǝnngi?” Ma tlǝg nǝ iin daddakwa ɓa tlǝr ma ɗyaghaara guhiina, aiyama taa kǝ iina, “Dadda hǝnnyaha, akwama kǝgh wagha kǝsǝgantkǝsǝga, tagwatag kǝ vakavaki agha fǝga nǝnnga, kwakyarvad ǝn kǝsanta.”
JOH 20:16 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Maryama!” Kaa gwivǝt kǝ iin da vak Yesu amaa kǝ iin dǝ ghaiya Yahudaha, “Rabboni!” Dǝgiti tuuk vakaiya nǝ iina, dadda tsaga dǝgita.
JOH 20:17 Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Hǝkykwa biya, aɗaba danǝti davak Daad ndan biya. Amma dǝg davak zaraabahar tagtǝrtag taakiya, ǝn dagat da vak Daadara, dlaɓa Daadaruwa, Daadamazhigǝlara, dlaɓa Daadamazhigǝlaruwa.”
JOH 20:18 Kaa dagal kǝ Maryam Magadala da tagtǝr kǝ mbǝrzaha, amaa “Nǝghananǝghǝg kǝ Yaazhigǝla.” Tagtǝr dlaɓ kǝ dǝgiti taghar Yesu.
JOH 20:19 Ɓǝlaa ba hwaas daghuvala hǝnnga zǝngw ma maaka, kaa dzahvǝtdzahǝg kǝ mbǝrzaha vak palla, dlaɓa ar ngahant kǝ ghaiya gudah mbakyarvad tlǝvuukwa Yahudaha. Kaa tsugwatsugw kǝ Yesu ma taatakaatǝr amaa, “Gabǝr tǝghǝr kǝskurama.”
JOH 20:20 Tǝhala kwa tagada nǝ iin kǝ kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga, kaa martǝrdamarǝg kǝ iin kǝ dǝvvahaan ard dlǝmbǝlaana. Kaa dlaiga kǝ mbǝrzah nǝghǝghara ba nǝ iitǝr kǝ Yazhigǝla.
JOH 20:21 Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iitǝr gwiya daala, “Gabǝr tǝghǝr kǝskurama! Bandkwa ɓǝlakut Daada, kai ndakwi ǝn ɓǝlkur bandkwaha.”
JOH 20:22 Tagada ba nǝ iin kwaha, kaa fǝrtǝrdǝm kǝ shifǝgaana, amaa taa kǝ iitǝra, “Dlǝghamdlǝghǝg kǝ Shǝɗkwa Daadamazhigǝla.
JOH 20:23 Baɗǝm dadda kwam ɓǝshgarnaa nǝ uuram kǝ haipahaana, ɓǝshavarnaɓǝshiga, dlaɓa baɗǝm dadda kwa ɓǝshamarnaa biya, ɓǝshvarnaa biya.”
JOH 20:24 Tuma kwa ɗahav dǝ ghwalaha, pall ma mbǝrzah kǝlaawa tar buwa, ndza, maay ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ iitǝr ma sartǝn sagha Yesu biya.
JOH 20:25 Am kyalǝma mbǝrzahan taa kǝ iina, “Nǝghamdanǝghǝg kǝ Yaazhigǝla!” Aiyam Tum taa kǝ iitǝra, “Akwama nǝghana bi kǝ ɗuula amsams ma dǝvvahaan biya, ǝn fǝm kǝ zǝra dǝvvar ma ɗuula amsams biya, dlaɓa ǝn fǝm kǝ dǝvvar ma dlǝmbǝlaan vaka ghuga guup biya, ǝn fǝdǝghǝrǝt biya.”
JOH 20:26 Tǝhala maaka, kaa gwiya dzahvǝtdzahǝg kǝ mbǝrzaha vak palla ma hǝnnyahiina, dlaɓa Tuma ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ iitǝra. Ghaiya gudah ndakwi ngahangahana, kaa tsugwatsugw Yesu ma taatakaatǝr amaa, “Gabǝr tǝghǝr kǝskurama.”
JOH 20:27 Tǝhala kwah amaa taa kǝ Tuma, “Faffǝg kǝ zǝra dǝvvagh vaakwana, vazǝg kǝ dǝvvahara. Vǝlǝg kǝ dǝvvagh faffǝg damma dlǝmbǝlara. Ɓag bi kǝ ndaundau biya, fǝdǝghǝrǝtfǝga.”
JOH 20:28 Am Tum taa kǝ iina, “Yaazhigǝlara ard Daadamazhigǝlara!”
JOH 20:29 Kaa tagartag Yesu taakiya, “Aɗaba aghaa nǝghǝkwadnǝghǝg iin wagha fǝghǝdǝghǝrǝt nǝnnga. Bark kǝ lii nǝgharkwa biya dlaɓa fardǝghǝrǝtfǝga.”
JOH 20:30 Ɓagaaɓag Yesu kǝ dǝga sǝrgah ba ɗyak ma gyiyaha mbǝrzahaana, kwa viindava bi ma kwanǝn kǝ kakkaɗ biya.
JOH 20:31 Vindavavindǝg wanahaan kwakyarvad am fǝdǝghǝrǝt taakiya Yesu iin Kǝristi, Zǝra Daadamazhigǝla. Dlaɓa tǝdvad fadghǝr ma ɗagaana am tlǝkǝna kǝ shiifǝga.
JOH 21:1 Tǝhala kwaha kaa gwiya tsǝgwatsǝgw kǝ Yesu vak mbǝrzahaan tǝ ghaiya dǝlva Tibariya. Dlaɓa wan ɗuuli marrada nǝ iin kǝ ghǝrana.
JOH 21:2 Siman Bitrus, ard Tum kwa ɗahav dǝ Ghwallaha, ard Nataniyel kwama Kana ma Galili, ard dǝ zarha Zabadi, ard kyalǝma mbǝrzah buwa baɗǝmma ar ǝmtaɗa.
JOH 21:3 Am Bitrusa, “Ən dagal da vaiya kilfa.” Aiyam kyǝlǝma mbǝrzaha, “Kǝmnd ndakwani kǝm dagal ǝmǝtaɗ dǝ kǝgha.” Kaa sagal kǝ iitǝr ar dǝm damma pɛrayuwa, kaa dagal kǝ iitǝra. Amma ma huɗa kwahiin kǝ avǝɗa, viyarǝti aanji ndau biya.
JOH 21:4 Dlakadur ba wurra, ghacǝgan Yesu tǝ ghaiya dǝlva, amma nǝghǝgharaaka bi mbǝrzahaan taakiya Yesu biya.
JOH 21:5 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Daala zarha, tlamkǝnatlǝg kǝ kilfa?” Kaa ngugwanguw kǝ iitǝr taakiya “Maaya.”
JOH 21:6 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Ɓǝlamɓǝlǝg kǝ amshi damma dǝvvaa kaffa pɛrayuwa, am da tlǝkǝnatlǝga.” Kaa ɓǝlgaan kǝ iitǝr bandkwa tagatǝr Yesu, ar vaiyit kǝ kilf ba ɗyaka, pelatǝrvaapelǝg baz tǝɗa amshi damma pɛrayuwa.
JOH 21:7 Am mbǝrzǝn waig Yesuwǝn taa kǝ Bitrusa, “Abi Yaazhigǝla!” Cinngha ba Siman Bitrus taakiya Yaazhigǝla, kǝsant kǝ sǝɗavan tsǝgwǝvva, aɗaba ndza ba dǝ kusǝgha. Tǝhalakwa, kaa dzǝva daay kǝ iin damma yuwa.
JOH 21:8 Kaa ba sagau kyalǝma mbǝrzah da tǝ ghaiya dǝlǝv ma pɛrayuwa, ar tǝɗa amshiya vaiya kilf righarighaan dǝ kilfa. Aɗaba ndzar maay bǝtky dǝ ghaiya dǝlviin biya, tamaha shig dǝrǝmǝk hǝkǝrɗa.
JOH 21:9 Ba dǝ sagalaatǝr wah sa tǝ ghaiya gardza, nǝghara ba ghuvǝra kaar dǝ kilf ɓǝlga tǝ vakai ard bruudiya.
JOH 21:10 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Anaagham kǝ kyalǝma kilf ma kwanahaan amaa vaigǝt nǝ uuram ndakwanǝnna.”
JOH 21:11 Kaa ba daas kǝ Siman Bitrus damma pɛrayuwa, tǝɗda kǝ amshiya vaiya kilf da tǝ ghaiya gardza. Amshiya vaiya kilfǝn dlaɓa righarighaan dǝ maandala kilf dǝrmǝk dǝ kuldlǝɓ tar hǝkǝrɗa. Bakǝvakwaha, ndzǝgana ɗyakǝra kilfǝna, tǝhghana bi kǝ amshiya biya.
JOH 21:12 Am Yesu taa kǝ iitǝra, “Asamasǝg naa ziyamzǝg kǝ kaffa dlakaduura.” Maay wa shughana gyi ma mbǝrzahaan kǝ ndavǝgarundavǝg taakiya ma war nǝ iin biya, aɗaba ar sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya Yaazhigǝla.
JOH 21:13 Kaa sagau kǝ Yesu kǝssant kǝ bruudiyin vǝlǝtǝra, ɓagaa band kwah dlaɓ dǝ kilfa.
JOH 21:14 Dǝga hǝkǝrɗ wan kǝ Yesu tsugwatsug vak mbǝrzahaan tǝhala ciigaan ma gǝtlaha.
JOH 21:15 Ghyǝnngara ba nǝ iitǝr za kaffa, kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg Yesu kǝ Siman Bitrus taakiya, “Siman zǝra Yuhwanna, agha waikwawaig juujig kǝ kwannahaana?” Kaa ngwarangug kǝ Bitrus amaa, “Aana, Yaazhigǝla, agha sǝrǝgasǝrǝg taakiya ǝn wayakwaiga.” Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Gǝlǝg kǝ tuughahara.”
JOH 21:16 Kaa gwiya ndavǝgarundavǝg Yesu kǝ dǝga buwa amaa, “Siman zǝra Yuhwanna, agha waikwawaiga?” Kaa ngugarangug kǝ iina, “Aana, Yaazhigǝla agha sǝrǝgasǝrǝg taakiya ǝn waiyakwaiga.” Am nǝ Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Faffǝg kǝ hyimi tuuk kǝ tuughahara.”
JOH 21:17 Kaa gwiya ndavgarundavǝg Yesu kǝ dǝga hǝkǝrɗ amaa, “Siman zǝra Yuhwanna, agha waikwawaiga.” Kaa badza huɗvǝg kǝ Bitrusa, aɗaba kwa ndavgharu Yesu kǝ dǝga hǝkǝrɗǝn taakiya, “Agha waikwawaiga?” Iin dlaɓ ngugharangug taakiya, “Yaazhigǝla, agha sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgitah ba ɗǝmma, agha sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya ǝn waiyakwaiga.” Am Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Gǝlǝg kǝ tuughahara.
JOH 21:18 Bak jiijiira, ǝn tagaktaga, ma sartǝn agha daalla zǝra agha fǝgaan kǝ sǝɗɗav bad ghǝragha agha dagal da vakavaki agha naaga nǝnnga, amma ma nǝghalnǝg kǝ malaha, agha talgaan kǝ dǝvvagh uudi tlǝrǝn wa fak sǝɗava, dǝkada da vakavaki agha naay kǝ dagal biya.”
JOH 21:19 Tagadatag Yesu kwannǝn kǝ ǝlbǝga kwakyarvad marvǝda hulfa ǝmǝtsǝgi da ǝmtsǝg Bitrus kwa da saa dǝ ndanngǝr kǝ Daadamazhigǝla. Tǝhala kwan kǝ ǝlbǝga, am Yesu taa kǝ Bitrus, “Gatǝkwagatǝga.”
JOH 21:20 Kaa gwivǝtgwig kǝ Bitrus vaza da tǝ halla, kaa nǝghǝganǝghǝg kǝ iin kǝ mbǝrzǝn kwa waig Yesu gata iitǝr tǝ halla. Kwan kǝ mbǝrz wandza dǝngǝzhiga tǝ Yesu ma sarta za kaffa hwaɗaga haarakǝssa dzava hǝnnyaha. Iin wa ndavǝgharu kǝ Yesu taakiya, “Yaazhigǝla, war wa da vǝla kǝghi?.”
JOH 21:21 Nǝghǝgha ba Bitrus kǝ iina, kaa ndavǝgarundavǝg kǝ iin kǝ Yesu amaa, “Yaazhigǝla, uudanǝn mi?”
JOH 21:22 Aiyam Yesu taa kǝ iina, “Akwaman naagaan ndzan dǝ shiifǝga bamma gwiyanghǝragwig saaya, auw lambaghi? Gatǝkwagatǝg aska nǝnnga.”
JOH 21:23 Aɗabad kwaha, kwannǝn kǝ ǝlbǝg kutalkutǝg ma yaa dadda gata Yesu taakiya, kwan kǝ mbǝrz da maay ǝmtsǝg biya. Amma tagada bi Yesu taakiya, da maay ǝmǝtsǝg biya, tagada ba taakiya, “Akwaman naagaan ndzan dǝ shiifǝg bamma gwiyanghǝragwig saaya, au lambaghi?”
JOH 21:24 Kwan kǝ mbǝrz wa ɓaga shiid tǝghǝr kǝ kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitaha, iin dlaɓ wa vindavindǝga. Kǝm sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya shiidaana ba jiijiira.
JOH 21:25 Mǝng nǝ dǝgitah ba ɗyak kwa ɓaga Yesu, akwama taakiya aa vindavvindǝg baɗǝmma, man tlǝg naiya aanji duni dǝ ghǝraana ma kǝssgant bi kǝ kakkaɗahaan akwama viindav biya.
ROM 1:1 Bulus, kwatnaha Kǝristi Yesu, kwa ɗahavant kiyava nǝg kǝ zǝr ɓǝlga Yesu, dlaɓa favan ba kǝrkangyakw kiyava taa ǝlbǝg Marawa Daadamazhigǝla.
ROM 1:2 Kwanǝn kǝ ǝlbǝg Maraw na, iin wa taa Daadamazhigǝl kǝ langiyaan ba wur tǝdvad tlayangngahaana, band kwa vinndǝga ma Kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl Cacuwanacacuwana.
ROM 1:3 Kwan kǝ Əlbǝg Maraw tǝghǝr kǝ Zǝraan na, kwa tǝdvad ndzǝganaan ma duniya, sǝghal ma hulfa Dauda,
ROM 1:4 amma tǝdvad ndzǝgana cacuwuraaan ma shiɗǝkwa, favdǝghǝrǝtfǝg taakiya Zǝra Daadamazhigǝl nǝ iin tǝdvad ciigaan ma gǝtlaha. Favdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Yesu Kǝristi dlaɓ taaki Yaazhigǝla miyam nǝ iina.
ROM 1:5 Tlankǝna tǝdvad Kǝristi Yesu nai kǝ hɛrǝr kiyava nǝg kǝ zǝr ɓǝlgaana, kwakyarvad fǝvaara ɗagaana, dlaɓa ǝn ɗahant kǝ kǝrdiyah baɗǝm ar hayant dǝ iina, ar faarana.
ROM 1:6 Kuram ndakwi am ma kǝrdiyahi ɗahavtǝrant kiyava nǝg kǝ dǝga Yesu Kǝristi.
ROM 1:7 Ən vindkur kǝskuram baɗǝmmaru lii ma Ruma, kurami waikur Daadamazhigǝla, dlaɓa kiyava nǝg kǝ uudahaan cacuwanacacuwana, hɛrǝrra, ard gabǝra Daadamazhigǝl Daada miyama ard dǝga Yaazhigǝl Yesu Kǝristi, aa ndzandzǝg tǝghǝr kǝskurama.
ROM 1:8 Ba zunngwa, ǝn tagar uus kǝ Daadamazhigǝlar tǝdvad Yesu Kǝristi mbakyarvad kuram baɗǝmma, aɗaba tagavdatag nǝ ǝlbǝga fadghǝraru tǝ iin aanji takwar ma duniya.
ROM 1:9 Daadamazhigǝl kwan ɓagar nai kǝ tlǝr bad ǝrvidmahuɗ pall tǝdvad taa ǝlbǝg marawa Zǝraana, iin shidar taakiya ǝn dzamkurdzamǝg ba kǝlaa hǝnnga,
ROM 1:10 ba tuuk sarti ǝn dzugw nai kǝ zhigǝla, ǝn ghalgaan kǝ Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, akwama haighanthaiga, ma ɓaga ndandara, ma naa tlǝkǝna kǝ ɗuula da vakaru ndakwana.
ROM 1:11 Ən naagaan ǝn nǝghǝkuraan mbakyarvad ǝn vǝlkur kǝ gyagyaan kwa tlǝvkǝna tǝdvad shiɗǝkw kiyava fǝkurna ndzǝɗa.
ROM 1:12 Naagara, iin taakiya, baɗǝmmamiyam ma kiyama faraa kǝ ndzǝɗ kǝ ghǝramiyama, ǝn fǝkura kǝ ndzǝɗ dǝ fadghǝrarra, kuram dlaɓa, am fǝwa kǝ ndzǝɗ dǝ dǝgaruwa.
ROM 1:13 Zaraabaha, ǝn naagaan am sǝran taakiya, shiga ngwǝn wana, ǝn naa da vakaruwa, bakǝvakwaha tsakwavatsǝg nǝ uuda, kwan naag nai kǝ da vakaruuna, aɗaba ma naa tlǝkǝna kǝ lii pǝla ghǝr ma kuram bandkwa ɓagana nai vakavakahi tlǝrǝn ma lii ar yahudah biya.
ROM 1:14 Dlaiyar kǝskai taa ǝlbǝg maraw ma gǝdǝrkǝsa ard gǝdzǝrkǝsa, kǝ lii ɗyamɗyam ard dlagaha.
ROM 1:15 Iin wa kǝman nai ba vaivai kǝ tagkur ǝlbǝg maraw kǝskuram lii ma Ruma.
ROM 1:16 Əlbǝg Maraw na dǝga zhǝru bi nǝ iin kǝskai biya, aɗaba iin ndzǝɗa Daadamazhigǝl kwa saa dǝ katǝg aanji kwar kǝ dadda fadǝghǝra, dǝga zunngwa Yahudaha, tǝhala kwaha lii ar Yahudah biya.
ROM 1:17 Aɗaba maradamarǝg nǝ Əlbǝg Maraw kǝ ɗulli ɓadlǝghana Daadamazhigǝl kǝ ndzǝganaan ǝmtaɗ dǝ uudaha, kwanna tlǝvkǝna ba tǝdvad fadǝghǝr kaltiya, bandkwa vindavindan ma Kakkaɗ taakiya, daddakwa ɓadlǝghanaɓadlǝg kǝ ndzǝganaan dǝ Daadamazhigǝla, da ndzǝga ba tǝ fadǝghǝra.
ROM 1:18 Aɗaba maradamarǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ badzǝga ǝrvidmahuɗaan sii ma ghǝrazhigǝl da tǝghǝr kǝ lii maay gǝdza Daadamazhigǝl biya, ar lii ɓa tlǝra kǝlaadǝr nǝ iitǝra, dlaɓa tsaraa kǝ shig kǝ jiir tǝdvad kalaadǝratǝra.
ROM 1:19 Dǝgiti maa sǝrvasǝrg tǝghǝr kǝ Daadamazhigǝl ba tǝ ɓalaɓal nǝ iin tsaw vakaatǝra, aɗaba maratǝrdamarǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ dǝgitaha.
ROM 1:20 Ndzǝgana Daadamazhigǝla ard ndzǝɗaan tangw damma zǝrazǝra dǝgitahi nǝghvanǝghǝg dǝ gyi biya. Aɗaba bamma sarti vǝrɗyava duniya maravdamarǝg wanahaan kǝ dǝgitah ba tǝ ɓalaɓala, nǝghǝvtraakanǝghǝg dlaɓ wanahaan tǝdvad dǝgitahi vǝrɗya nǝ iina. Mbakyarvad kwaha, ar maay nǝ uudah dǝ ɗuula farwut biya.
ROM 1:21 Aanji ba war sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, bakǝvakwaha faraara bi band Daadamazhigǝl biya, dlaɓa tagarar bi kǝ uus biya. Dlakulva kwaha dzamaghǝraatǝra nalnǝg ba gyaana, dlaɓa ǝrviɗmahuɗatǝra nalnǝg ba dǝkdǝka.
ROM 1:22 Aanji bar taakiya, ar yaa dadda dabariya, amma ar dlagaha.
ROM 1:23 Mbǝɗarnambǝɗǝg kǝ ndangǝra Daadamazhigǝl kwa maay ǝmtsǝg dǝ dzakǝva dǝgit band uud kwa ǝmtsǝga, ard ghǝlahi kwa dzakǝva ɗiikaha, ard almanaha ard azahulǝmba.
ROM 1:24 Mbakyarvad kwaha ɗuwatǝrnaaɗug Daadamazhigǝl kǝ kǝma dǝgaha kǝlaadǝri naghant nǝ ǝrvidmahuɗatǝr kǝ ɓagaana, dlaɓa ar ɓa dǝga tsa zhǝruw dǝ vǝghahaatǝra ma taatakatǝra.
ROM 1:25 Mbǝɗarnambǝɗǝg kǝ jiira Daadamazhigǝl kǝ fiida, ar ɓagar kwatnahǝr kǝ dǝgitahi vǝrɗya nǝ iina, baz ɓagar tlǝr kǝ iitǝr dlakulva kwa maraa ɓagar nǝ iitǝr kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, iin wa tlaltlǝg kǝ galǝg ba tangw damma zǝrazǝra. Aandz bandkwaha.
ROM 1:26 Mbakyarvad kwaha ɗuwatǝrnaaɗug Daadamazhigǝl kǝ kǝmma ɓaa dǝgaha tsa zhǝruwa. Ənghwasahaatǝr ndakwani ɗuuwarasɗug kǝ camarakav dǝ ghwalvah kwa iin tanngaraan ba sagalaan ma daadija, kaa ba caamarakav kǝ iitǝr dǝ vǝgahaatǝr kwa kalkal bi sagalaan bamma daati.
ROM 1:27 Ghwalvah ndakwi ɗuwarasɗuug kǝ camarakǝv dǝ ǝnghwasah kwa in wa kalkal sagalaan bamma daati. Ghwalǝva ard ghwalva ar ɓa dǝga tsa zhǝruwa, sardaa ndǝkwah nǝ iitǝr kǝ dlaɗ da tǝ ghǝraatǝr kwa ba kalkal dǝ tlǝraha kǝlaadǝraatǝra.
ROM 1:28 Larwalǝg tsau kǝ sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, kaa ɗuutǝrǝsɗug Daadamazhigǝl dǝ dzamaghǝra dlagǝraatǝr kiyava ɓa dǝgitahi kalkal bi kǝ ɓag biya.
ROM 1:29 Ar righarighan aanji dǝ hulfa kwar kǝ dǝga kǝlaadǝra, dǝ dlǝrmǝga, dauwa, ar righarighan dǝ shilga, tsa shifǝga, uushava, ard vala uuda, ard dangwǝra huɗa, ar yaa dadda hwatsa amaha,
ROM 1:30 lii badza ɗaaga, lii ɓa tlǝghum dǝ Daadamazhigǝla, lii ɗaava uuda, lii naa ghǝra, lii ar fǝgaara kǝ ghǝraatǝra, lii ɓa ba dǝga kǝlaadǝra, lii maay fǝgaara kǝ daddaatǝr ard babbaahaatǝr biya.
ROM 1:31 Lii nǝghǝgaaka biya, lii maay righa lanngyi biya, ar maay waiyakǝv biya, dlaɓa ar maay ɓa zhuwadaal biya.
ROM 1:32 Ar sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ adzahadzaha Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, baɗǝm lii ɓa kwanahaan kǝ dǝgita, dlaitǝrdlaig nǝ ǝmtsǝga, kwanahaan kǝ dǝgitah kalti bi war ɓag nǝ iitǝr biya, baz tlahtǝr ilǝg kǝ iitǝr kǝ lii ɓa kwanahaana.
ROM 2:1 Mbakyarvad kwaha, kǝgh dadda tǝgar shari kǝ uuda, aanji agha war nǝnga, agha maay dǝ farwut biya, ma sartǝn agha tǝgar nǝng kǝ shari kǝ uuda, agha ghaza ghǝragha, aɗaba haipǝn agha zharǝg nǝng kǝ uud dǝ vakaina, iin wa ɓag nǝng ghǝravagha.
ROM 2:2 Kiyam sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya shariya Daadamazhigǝl ba jiijiira tǝghǝr kǝ lii ar ɓa kwanahaan kǝ dǝgita.
ROM 2:3 Kǝgh uuda! ba kǝgh dǝ ghǝragh ndakwani agha ɓagan kǝ haipǝn kwa agha vazǝg nǝng kǝ uud dǝ vakaina! Ma tlǝg ghǝragh agha da ngǝdlǝgharwangǝdlǝg kǝ shariya Daadamazhigǝla?
ROM 2:4 Nii agha nenna dyakǝra hɛrǝrra Daadamazhigǝla, ard fa ǝrvidmahuɗaana, ard kwa maay nǝ iin nguɗa ǝrvidmahuɗ watswats dǝ kǝghǝn hi? Mbats, agha sǝrga bi taakiya, hɛrǝrra Daadamazhigǝl wa fakaafǝg kǝ pǝlaghǝr biya?
ROM 2:5 Amma mbakyarvad dǝkdǝka ghǝr ard dǝkdǝka ǝrvidmahuɗi agha dǝ vakai nǝnnga, agha dzagharu shari kǝ ghǝragha kwa paka kǝgh davala badzǝga ǝrvidmahuɗa Daadamazhigǝla, ma sartǝn da tav shari tǝdvad jiira Daadamazhigǝla.
ROM 2:6 Da vǝlgarvǝlǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ dǝg shigan aanji kwar kǝ uud kalkala dǝgiti ɓagaa nǝ iina
ROM 2:7 Kiyava lii ghularvaghulǝg kǝ ɓa tlǝra hɛrrǝr kǝ gata ndanngǝra ard ɗyakǝr ard shifǝga kwa maay ghyǝnng biya, da vǝltǝrvǝlǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ shifǝg tangw damma zǝrazǝra.
ROM 2:8 Amma lii naa ghǝraatǝra, ard lii naay kǝ jiir biya, dlaɓa ar ɓa tlǝra kǝlaadira, da ɗigaan Daadamazhigǝl kǝ ǝrviɗmahuɗaan tǝ iitǝra.
ROM 2:9 Dlaɗa ard mbahǝl wa paka aanji kwar kǝ uudi ɓa tlǝra kǝlaadǝra, ba zunngwa Yahudaha, tǝhala kwaha lii ar yahudah biya.
ROM 2:10 Baɗǝm daddakwa ɓa dǝgit marawa, da tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ ndanghǝra ard dyakǝra ard gabǝrǝra, ba zunngwa Yahudaha, tǝhalakwaha lii ar Yahudah biya.
ROM 2:11 Aɗaba maay Daadamazhigǝl fa dagar ma uud biya.
ROM 2:12 Baɗǝm lii ɓa haip kwal sǝrga adzahadzaha Muusa, ar da ruug ba kwal adzahadzaha, amma baɗǝm lii ɓa haip dǝ sǝrgasǝrgǝraatǝr kǝ adzahadzaha, da tǝvtǝr tǝdvad adzahadzaha shariya.
ROM 2:13 Aɗaba tǝdvad cinnga dǝgiti tag nǝ adzahadzah kalti bi wa da fǝgaraa uudah kǝ nǝg uudaha jiir tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl biya, bamma lii ɓa tlǝr dǝ dǝgiti tag nǝ adzahadzaha, iitǝr wada ɗahvǝtǝr dǝ uudaha jiirjiira.
ROM 2:14 Lii ar Yahudah biya, ar maay dǝ adzahadzaha Muus biya, bakǝvakwaha ar ɓagaan kǝ dǝgiti tag adzahadzaha ma ǝrvidmahuɗatǝr daghuvaliitlǝrna. Mbats lii tsagavtǝru bi nǝ adzahadzah biya, ar dǝ adzahadzaha ghǝraatǝra.
ROM 2:15 Marardamarǝg taakiya, dǝgiti naag nǝ adzahadzaha vindavindan ma ǝrviɗmahuɗaatǝra, dlaɓa dzamaghǝraatǝra nalnǝg kǝ shid kǝ iitǝra, davalitlǝrna dzamaghǝraatǝr tagtǝrtag taakiya ɓagara bi kalkal biya, davalitlǝrn dlaba dzamaghǝraatǝr tagtǝrtag taakiya ɓagarabag ba kalkala.
ROM 2:16 Mbakyarvad kwaha, bandkwa tag nǝ ǝlbǝg marawǝn kwan tag nai kǝ ǝlbǝgaanna, da nǝg bandkwah daghuvali da tǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ shariyaan tǝdvad Kǝristi Yesu tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgitahi shiɓashiɓan baɗǝm ma ǝrviɗmahuɗa uudaha.
ROM 2:17 Kǝgh ci dadda taakiya ǝn zhiil Yahud na, agha tsa ghǝr tǝ adzahadzaha Muusa, dlaɓa agha tsa kusǝgh taaki agha ba hweɗ dǝ Daadamazhigǝla,
ROM 2:18 agha taakiya, ǝn sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgiti tlatlǝg Daadamazhigǝl am nǝnnga, dlaɓa agha sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ adzahadzaha Muusa ard ɗuuli agha da kǝsgaaka nǝnng kǝ dǝgiti kalkallaana.
ROM 2:19 Akwama agha sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya, agha dadda taɗa gulfa, dlaɓa parak kǝ lii ma gurtla,
ROM 2:20 dadda kwartǝr degit kǝ dlagaha, dlaɓa dadda tsaga dǝgit kǝ zarha. Aɗaba fǝghǝdǝghǝrǝtfǝg nǝnng taakiya, agha sǝrgasǝrǝg kǝ dǝgit ba maraw ard jiir ma adzahadzaha Muusa.
ROM 2:21 Ai ciya, kǝgh dadda tsagtǝr kǝ uudaha, tsagarutsag kǝ ghǝragh ndana! Kǝgh dadda taa ǝlbǝg marawi agha taakiya aa ɓagav bi gǝl biya, agha maay ghǝravǝgh ɓa gǝl biya?
ROM 2:22 Kǝgh dadda taaki aa ɓagav bi gwaragwar biya, agha maay ghǝravǝgh ɓa gwaragwar biya? Kǝgh dadda caɗa ǝrviɗ tǝvǝgh kǝ ghǝla, agha maay ghǝravagh ɓa gǝl ma guda gǝliv biya?
ROM 2:23 Kǝgh dadda tsa kusǝgh dǝ adzahadzaha Muusa, agha maay badza ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝl tǝdvad kǝlgarwut adzahadzahaan biya?
ROM 2:24 Bandkwa vindava ma Kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, “Badzav mbakyarvad kuram Yahudah nǝ ɗaaga Daadamazhigǝl ma lii ar Yahudah biya.”
ROM 2:25 Akwama agha fǝgaarafǝg kǝ adzahadzaha Muusa, ɓa aguvacagh mǝng nǝ tlǝraana, akwama fǝghaara bi kǝ adzahadzaha Muus biya, nalnǝg bandǝgi ɓagaka bi nǝ uud kǝ aguvac biya.
ROM 2:26 Akwa mar tsuufǝgan lii ɓagavtǝra bi nǝ aguvac kǝ dǝgiti tag nǝ adzahaadzaha Muus taaki aa ɓagavɓaga, mbats da nǝtǝrdal bi Daadamazhigǝl band lii ɓagavtǝra nǝ aguvac biya?
ROM 2:27 Akwamar mar tsuufǝgan nǝ lii ɓagavtǝra bi nǝ aguvac kǝ dǝgiti tag nǝ adzahadzah taakiya aa ɓagavɓaga, ar da taktǝg kǝ shari kǝskǝghǝn agha dǝ aguvacǝn dlaɓa agha dǝ adzahadzaha Muus vindavindanna, aɗaba kǝlghǝdakǝlǝg kǝ adzahadzaha.
ROM 2:28 Agha nǝgal bi kǝ zhiil Yahuda jiijiir kwakyarvad ɓagakaɓag nǝ uud kǝ aguvac kalti biya, aguvaca jiijiira iin bi nǝ aguvaca vǝgh zhiilǝr biya.
ROM 2:29 Dlakulva kwaha, Zhiil Yahuda jiijiira iin Zhiil Yahuda kwama ǝrviɗmahuɗa, dlaɓa aguvaca jiijiira iin nǝ aguvaca ǝrviɗmahuɗa, dǝgiti ɓag Shiɗǝkwa Daadamazhigǝl tǝdvad adzahadzahi vindavindan biya, hulfa kwan kǝ uuda, Daadamazhigǝl kataghǝraan wa dlǝbgaana, uuda dǝgshig biya.
ROM 3:1 Au kaci tlǝra taakiya agha zhiil Yahudi? Au ci tlǝra ɓa guvaci?
ROM 3:2 Mǝng nǝ iin kǝ mǝnga, aanji ta kwar kǝ ɗuula! ba zunngwa, Yahudah wa vǝlatǝr Daadamazhigǝl ba dǝ ghǝraan kǝ langyiya ǝlbǝgaana.
ROM 3:3 Akwama mar dǝ maayra fadǝghǝr kyalmatǝr biyim? Da nǝgalnǝg kaci taakiya jiira Daadamazhigǝl maay tlǝran biya?
ROM 3:4 Maaya! Dzǝgaar dau ɗa! Daadamazhigǝl dadda jiira, bakvakwaha aanji kwar kǝ uuda ba dadda fiida. Bandkwa vindava ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝla taakiya, “Kiyava fǝvdǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ jiira ǝlbǝgagha, dlaɓa agha zǝgaan kǝ fiir akwama tak shari nǝ uuda.’’
ROM 3:5 Ai tsa, akwama maira jiira miyam wa nalnǝg kǝ ɗuula mara jiira Daadamazhigǝl ma, au wa kiyam da tag nǝ miyammi? Kiyam da taaki maay Daadamazhigǝl dǝ jiir akwama ɗiyadaɗiig kǝ ǝrviɗmahuɗaan tǝ kǝmiyami ciya? “Ən taa kwan naiya bandkwa tag tlǝmadauwa.”
ROM 3:6 Maaya! Dzǝgaar dau ɗa, ma bandkwaha, da tǝg ndandar ka ci Daadamazhigǝl kǝ shari kǝ duuniyi?
ROM 3:7 Akwama maira jiirar wa fǝghara jiira Daadamazhigǝl sagal da tǝ ɓalaɓal ba vaivaiya, nalnǝg dlaɓ kǝ dǝga fǝgara ndangǝr kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, iyau, kwakyarvadau ci gwastaan da vǝlgwa dlaɗ nǝ uud taakiya ǝn dadda haipi?
ROM 3:8 Akwama bandkwaha, ba kiyam zavukw dǝ ɓa kǝladǝr kiyava nǝg kǝ ɗuula tlǝkǝna hɛrǝr kǝskǝmiyam biya? kyalma uudah dlaɓa, ar taa ǝlbǝga badzaa ɗaaga miyama ar taakiya kiyam tag ndǝkwaha awarama. Da ghazǝvtǝrghazǝg nǝ uudahaan ba kalkal band kwa da ghazǝvǝtǝra.
ROM 3:9 Aitsa, auwa kiyam da tag nǝ miyami? jiyamuujig nǝ miyam Yahudah kǝ kyalma uudaha? Maaya! dzǝgaar dau ɗa! Tagiyamdatag taakiya baz Yahudaha ard lii Yahudah biya, baɗǝmmaatǝra tǝkaratǝkǝga, dlaɓa baɗǝmmaatǝra ar ba mizhangyil kǝ ndzǝɗa haipa.
ROM 3:10 Bandkwa vindavindan ma kkakaɗa Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, “maay dadda jiir biya, maay, aanji pall biya.
ROM 3:11 Maay daddakwa nǝghǝgakanǝghǝg biya, maay daddakwa gata Daadamazhigǝl biya.
ROM 3:12 Baɗǝmmaatǝr guyarardagwig kǝ ilǝg kǝ Daadamazhigǝla, ar madla bi tu kǝ ǝlbǝg biya, maay daddakwa ɓa dǝga jiijiir biya, maay aanji pall biya.
ROM 3:13 Mbakulyaraatǝr band gǝtl wurawurana, aryahatǝra nalnǝg kǝ dǝga vala uuda. Əlbǝgahi ar tag nǝ iitǝra, band gura ghaval kwa kǝlaada.
ROM 3:14 Əlbǝgahi sagal ma ghaiyahatǝra, ba ɗaava ard ǝlbǝg ɗyahɗyaha.
ROM 3:15 Ar ɓa watswats tǝdvad tsa shifǝga,
ROM 3:16 Ar dǝgal ba takwara, tlǝratǝr ba ciɓa uuda ard danngura huɗɗa.
ROM 3:17 Ar sǝrga bi kǝ ɗuula gabrǝr biya.
ROM 3:18 Maay gǝdza Daadamazhigǝl ma gyiyatǝr biya
ROM 3:19 Kiyam sǝrgasǝrǝg taakiya baɗǝm dǝgiti tag nǝ adzahadzaha Muusa, tagtǝr kǝ lii mizhanngyil kǝ adzahadzaha. Nalnǝg nǝ iin ǝndkwaha mbakyarvad tsǝtǝrva kǝ lii gata farwut baɗǝmma, dlaɓa marvǝdan taakiya baɗǝm duniya ar ba mizhanngyil kǝ shariya Daadamazhigǝla.
ROM 3:20 Aɗaba tǝ kwaha, maay wada tlǝvkǝnatlǝg kwal haip tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl tǝdvad tsufa dǝgiti tag nǝ adzahadzah taaki aa ɓagavɓag biya. Tlǝri ɓag nǝ adzahadzah iin taakiya, mararda kǝ haipaan kǝ uuda.
ROM 3:21 Ndakwan ciya, tagavdatag watlǝrin kǝ ɗuula tlǝkǝna jiira Daadamazhigǝla, kwan kǝ jiira tlǝfǝkǝna tǝ ɗuula adzahadzaha Muus biya, bakǝvakwaha tagadatag nǝ adzahadzaha Muusa ard tlayanngah kǝ shiid tǝghǝra.
ROM 3:22 Kwan kǝ jiira Daadamazhigǝl na, tlǝfkǝna tǝdvad fadǝghǝr tǝ Yesu Kǝristi kǝ lii fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg baɗǝmma. Maay wahazhawahazh ma taataka Yahudaha ard lii Yahudah biya,
ROM 3:23 Baɗǝm nǝ uudaha ɓagaraɓag kǝ haipa, dlaɓa hǝtsalarhǝtsǝg da tǝ ndangǝra Daadamazhigǝla,
ROM 3:24 Amma kwakyarvad hɛrǝrri ɓagaa Daadamazhigǝl ba gyagyaan aanji kǝ wara, ma ba war tlakǝnatlǝg kǝ ndzǝgan kwal haip tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl tǝdvad vargi varakiyama Kǝristi Yesu
ROM 3:25 Vǝladavǝlǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ Yesu kiyava kyuulǝg mbakyarvad kǝsa haipahamiyama, aɗaba tǝdvad avǝza kyuulǝgaan wada mɓishǝvǝtǝrna haipahatǝr kǝ uudah tǝdvad fadǝghǝraatǝra. Ɓagaaɓag Daadamazhigǝl kwan mbakyarvad marda kǝ jiiraana, ma sarta kwa ndza wura, faffǝg Daadamazhigǝl kǝ ǝrvidmahuɗ ɓǝlatǝrnaɓǝlǝg kǝ haipahatǝra. Marada ndǝkwah Daadamazhigǝl kǝ jiiran ma kwan kǝ sarta, vǝladavǝlǝg kǝ Yesu ǝmtsan mbakyarvad haipahamiyama, dlaɓa baɗǝm daddakwa fadǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Yesu da tlǝkǝnatlǝg kǝ ndzǝga kwal haip tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝla.
ROM 3:27 Aitsa, kiyam da tǝɗǝg tuuk au kaci kǝ fǝɗyavǝghi? Maaya, tsavda tǝ kwar kǝ ɗuul nǝ tǝɗa fǝɗyavǝghi? tsavda tǝdvad tsufa adzahadzaha Muusa? ǝndkwah biya, tsavda tǝdvad fadǝghǝra.
ROM 3:28 Aɗaba haiyamanthaig taakiya, tlǝfkǝna tǝdvad fadǝghǝr nǝ ndzǝga kwal haip tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝla, tǝdvad tsuufa adzahadzaha Muus biya.
ROM 3:29 Daadamazhigǝlǝn tsa, Daadamazhigǝl ba kǝ Yahudah kaltiya? Mbats maay Daadamazhigǝlaatǝr kǝ lii ar Yahudah biya? ba pakatta Daadamazhigǝl baz kǝ lii ar Yahudahǝn biya,
ROM 3:30 Aɗaba Daadamazhigǝl ba palla. Da fǝtǝraafǝg kǝ lii ɓagavtǝraɓag nǝ aguvac kǝ ndzǝga kwal haip tǝvuukwan tǝdvad fadǝghǝra, bandkwah dlaɓ lii ɓagavtǝra bi nǝ aguvac biya, ar da tlǝkǝna tǝdvad fadǝghǝr kǝ ndzǝga kwal haipa.
ROM 3:31 Aitsa, ɗiyamdaddaɗiigi kaci kǝ adzahadzaha Muus mbakyarvad kwan kǝ fadǝghǝra? ǝndkwah biya, dlakulva kwaha, hakyamdǝvǝthakyig tǝ vakaiya.
ROM 4:1 Kiyam da taaw kaci tǝghǝr kǝ Ibrahim, daadiija daadijamiyam tǝdvad ndzǝgana vǝghǝghi? auwa nǝghǝghaaka nǝ iin tǝghǝr kǝ ǝlbǝga fadǝghǝri?
ROM 4:2 Akwama tlakǝna tǝdvad tlǝraan nǝ Ibrahim kǝ ndzǝga kwal haip tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝla, mǝng dǝgiti da tǝɗǝg nǝ iin kǝ fǝɗyavǝgh dǝ vakaiya, amma tǝvuukwa Daadamazhigǝl biya.
ROM 4:3 Auwam kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝli? “Fadǝghǝrǝtfǝg nǝ Ibrahim tǝ Daadamazhigǝla, ka ba ɗagaan Daadamazhigǝl dǝ uuda jiijiira.”
ROM 4:4 Dadda kwa ɓa tlǝra, caug gyagyaan bi kǝ kwaɓ biya, cauwa dǝgshiga tlǝrana.
ROM 4:5 Daddakwa maay tsaghǝr tǝ tlǝraan biya, tsaghǝr ba tǝ Daadamazhigǝl kwa nǝdalnǝg kǝ yaa dadda haip ar tlǝkǝna kǝ ndzǝgan kwal haip tǝvuukana, da nǝdal kǝ fadǝghǝra uudanǝn kǝ jiira.
ROM 4:6 Daud ndakwi taga band kwah ma sarta kwa taga nǝ iin kǝ ǝlbǝg tǝghǝr kǝ barka, hayatǝrǝthaig Daadamazhigǝl ba kwal vaza dǝga jiijiiri ɓagara nǝ iitǝra,
ROM 4:7 “Dǝ bark nǝ uudi ɓishavarna dǝgitahi ɓaga nǝ iina, dlaɓa ɓishǝvarna haipahaana.
ROM 4:8 Dǝ bark nǝ uudani kwa madlai nǝ Yaazhigǝl fa haipahaan tuuk kǝ uupǝɗ biya,”
ROM 4:9 Kwan kǝ bark tsa, ba kǝ lii dǝ aguvac kalti nii baz lii maay dǝ aguvac hi? Abi dǝgiti kǝm tag nǝmnd ba vindavindan ma kakkaɗa Daadamazhigǝl taakiya, “Hayavaranthaig kǝ Ibrahim kwakyarvad fadǝghǝraan taakiya dadda jiir nǝ iina.”
ROM 4:10 Aitsa, ma sarta kwar wa tagavara kǝ Ibrahim taakiya dadda jiir nǝ iin ni? tǝhala kwa ɓagavara nǝ aguvac nii lakwuti ɓagǝvarɓag hi? lakwuti ɓagǝvarɓaga.
ROM 4:11 Ɓagavara ba nǝ aguvac kǝ Ibrahim, nalnǝg kǝ dǝga sǝrǝg kǝ iin taakiya, dadda jiir nǝ iin tǝdvad fadǝghǝraan lakwuti ɓagvarɓag nǝ aguvaca. Mbakyarvad kwaha nalnǝg nǝ Ibrahim kǝ Daad kǝ lii fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg tǝ Daadamazhigǝla, kiyava kǝdlǝvǝtǝrkǝdlǝg ma lii dǝ jiir aanji ba ɓagavtǝrabi nǝ aguvac biya.
ROM 4:12 Nal bandkwah dlaɓ nǝ Ibrahim kǝ Daad kǝ lii ɓagavtǝra nǝ aguvaca, kwa aguvac kalti bi war dǝvakai nǝ iitǝr biya, ar gatǝgaan baz hulfa garava fadǝghǝri dǝ vakai nǝ Ibrahim lakwuti ɓagvar nǝ aguvaca.
ROM 4:13 Langyi kwa tavara kǝ Ibrahim ard hulfaan taakiya da gwigaan kǝ duniya, tavara tǝdvad gata adzahadzaha Muus biya, tavara kwakyarvad jiira kwa tlǝvkena tǝ ɗuula fadǝghǝra.
ROM 4:14 Akwama lii gata adzahadzaha Muus wa da gwiya duniya, mbats fadǝghǝra uud nalnǝg ba gyaagyana, dlaɓa maay nǝ tlǝra langyiya Daadamazhigǝl biya.
ROM 4:15 Aɗaba adzahadzaha saa dǝ badzga ǝrvidmahuɗa Daadamazhigǝla, vakavaki maay nǝ adzahadzah biya, kǝlvarwut bi nǝ adzahadzah biya.
ROM 4:16 Mbakyarvad kwaha, sagau tǝdvad fadǝghǝra nǝ langyiya. Kwana nalnǝg kwakyarvad hɛrǝrra Daadamazhigǝla, dlaɓa kiyava haivǝtǝrant kǝ hulfa Ibrahim baɗǝmma, kiyava lii gata adzahadzaha Muus kalti biya, baz lii fardǝghǝrǝtfǝg bandkwa ɓagaa nǝ Ibrahim. Aɗaba Ibrahim nǝ daadamiyam baɗǝmma.
ROM 4:17 Bandkwa vindavindan ma kakkaɗ taakiya, “Nankadalnǝg kǝ Daad kǝ jibah ɗyakka,” Aɗaba righavantrighǝg langyi na.
